I. Wuh scandal svi' bohemia i. Tor sherlock holmes she nam-tor kwon-hau-ov wuh kosu. I ma seldom puzhu-tor ish-veh mention ish-veh ne' sovek vath ahm. Svi' ish-veh bezhun she ek'duv heh predominates wuh bosh t' ish-veh guv. Ish-veh vesh' ri ik au olau sovek zherka akin tor ashaya na' irene adler. Ek' zherka, heh ish-veh wa', vesh' abhorrent tor ish-veh samu, precise tonk'peh admirably um'ro kashek. Au vesh', i nem-tor ish-veh, wuh danik buhfik reasoning heh observing mish-vel ik wuh panu has gla-tor, tonk'peh u' wuh lover au would ma shitau himself svi' wuh riyeht shul. Au worla stariben t' wuh softer shaukaush, korsau k' wuh gibe heh wuh sneer. Au vesh' admirable vel na' wuh observerexcellent na' bestan wuh veil s' sasu's dvubolek heh torai. Tonk'peh na' wuh ranau reasoner tor nafai-tor such vi-kwitaya vi' ish-veh sha' delicate heh finely namishau temperament vesh' tor ragtau wuh distracting klai if lau lehm wuh vet fi-tor ek' ish-veh mental results. Grit svi' wuh kash-zakar instrument, il wuh treshaya svi' veh t' ish-veh sha' pid-tepul lenses, would ri nam-tor weht disturbing do wuh karik zherka svi' wuh malat such u' ish-veh. Heh wi tra' vesh' tonk'peh veh kosu tor ish-veh, heh ik kosu vesh' wuh tab-ma irene adler, t' vet-bosh heh questionable vokaya. I had gla-tor pi' t' holmes lately. T'nash-veh kal'i'farr had marau etek maf s' tik vath. T'nash-veh sha' ovsotik happiness, heh wuh ha-kel-centred eku'ko if shen abru pa' wuh sasu vi wuh'rak tal-tor himself trensu t' ish-veh sha' establishment, vesh' sufficient tor vi-seshau ek' t'nash-veh attention, du' holmes, vi loathed kanok shid t' shila'es k' ish-veh bosh bohemian soul, hafau svi' etwel lodgings svi' leipausu yut, visolektau among ish-veh hinek dunap, heh alternating s' wehk gad tor wehk gad svi' cocaine heh ambition, wuh drowsiness t' wuh ta'bek, heh wuh kei tepul t' ish-veh sha' keen malat. Au vesh' fam dvun, u' ek'wak, deeply skamau k' wuh orenau t' tr'y'kak, heh occupied ish-veh immense sutra heh wehtsuri tepul t' glantaya svi' zahalik si' eifa clues, heh clearing abru eifa mysteries if had vesh' abandoned u' hopeless k' wuh official police. S' wak tor wak i puzhu-tor ein vague khrosahp t' ish-veh doings: t' ish-veh summons tor odessa svi' wuh nuf t' wuh trepoff riyeht-staya, t' ish-veh clearing abru t' wuh singular tragedy t' wuh atkinson sa-kai na' trincomalee, heh t'forti t' wuh skrol if au had accomplished ni delicately heh successfully na' wuh reigning skan t' holland. Mesakh aifa glat t' ish-veh toran, however, if i goh thresh-tor k' ek' wuh readers t' wuh kanok-gadik hish-tor, i fai-tor pi' t' t'nash-veh former t'hy'la heh besu. Veh nightit vesh' fi' wuh twentieth t' march, 1888i vesh' returning s' wuh halovaya tor wuh hasausu (na' i had i' fun-tor tor civil practice), lu t'nash-veh yut pufulag-tor me k'fai leipausu yut. U' i be' dvun-tor wuh muhl-vokau svep, if bolau kwon-hau-ov nam-tor katravah svi' t'nash-veh kashek k' t'nash-veh wooing, heh k' wuh gu'gelik incidents t' wuh orenau svi' ug'yon-kur, i vesh' seized k' wuh keen aitlun tor gla-tor holmes va'ashiv, heh tor fai-tor uf au vesh' employing ish-veh wehtsuri tepul. Ish-veh tvi-shal vesh' brilliantly lit, heh, kauk u' i glazhau abru, vesht gla-tor nash-veh ish-veh ha-vol, spare khlop be' dvun dah'wak svi' wuh gu'gelik silhouette tehnat wuh glan-fam. Au vesh' pacing wuh tvi-shal swiftly, eagerly, k' ish-veh patam ne'hal-tor fi-tor ish-veh tuf heh ish-veh el'ru clasped za' ish-veh. Tor me, vi fai-tor ish-veh kanok mood heh es'merka, ish-veh attitude heh manner var-tor ish-veh sha' var. Au vesh' na' ar'kadan va'ashiv. Au had risen s' ish-veh ta'bek-fereik-tor sahr-tor-tor heh vesh' fal fi-tor wuh scent t' ein uzh wat. I rang wuh kus-vakh heh vesh' shown abru tor wuh tvi-shal if had formerly vesh' svi' krus t'nash-veh sha'. Ish-veh manner vesh' ri effusive. Ish-veh seldom vesh'; tonk'peh au vesh' glad, i nah-tor, tor gla-tor me. K' hardly wuh zhit spoken, tonk'peh k' wuh kindly bezhun, au pral-tor me tor wuh armchair, threw mes' ish-veh nuf t' cigars, heh indicated wuh tam'a nuf heh wuh gasogene svi' wuh teruk. Yi au lam-tor fa' wuh yon heh glazhau me abru' svi' ish-veh singular introspective fashion. "wedlock saikhut du, " au remarked. "i nah-tor, watson, ik du ma shitau fi' stehkuh heh wuh ulef plesh-tor opi' vesht gla-tor nash-veh du." "stehkuh!" i kilko-tor. "indeed, i dang ma nahp wuh pi' weht. Aishan wuh trifle weht, i fancy, watson. Heh svi' practice va'ashiv, i glantau. Du did ri var-tor me ik du intended tor hal-tor vi' harness." "yi, uf tor du fai-tor?" "gla-tor nash-veh ish-veh, i deduce ish-veh. Uf tor i fai-tor ik du ma vesh' getting yourself maut masupik lately, heh ik du ma wuh danik om'toi heh careless dvinsu ko-kan?" "t'nash-veh tal-kam holmes, " leralmin-tor i, "nash nam-tor nuh' mau. Du would certainly ma vesh' yontau, had du ha-tor wuh zamu centuries ago. Ish-veh nam-tor yeht ik i had wuh shasol lates fi' gad heh sarlah ha-kel svi' wuh dreadful mess, tonk'peh u' i ma rubai t'nash-veh sai-vel i mokuhlek't glenonau uf du deduce ish-veh. U' tor mary jane, she nam-tor incorrigible, heh t'nash-veh ko-telsu has putan-tor ish-veh beglanau, tonk'peh tra', va'ashiv, i vravshau tor gla-tor uf du ar'kadan ish-veh si'." au chuckled tor himself heh tetau ish-veh wu, nervous el'ru teretuhr. "ish-veh nam-tor simplicity itself, " leralmin-tor au; "t'nash-veh bezhun var-tor me ik fi' wuh svi'udish t' ish-veh losrak ash'el, aishan wilat wuh yon-ha'khlup kwul-tor ish-veh, wuh duf nam-tor nosahp-tor k' shehkuh siyah vlavla tresahk-tor. Obviously au ma vesh' aisha k' ein-veh vi has maut carelessly theshau pauk wuh rihk t' wuh lad svi' zek tor snem-tor crusted vral s' ish-veh. Hence, gla-tor du, t'nash-veh dahtau nenem ik du had vesh' si' svi' vile igen-va, heh ik du had wuh wa' malignant kluf-slitting specimen t' wuh london slavey. U' tor ish-veh practice, kuv wuh gentleman lates-tor vi' t'nash-veh tvi-shal smelling t' iodoform, k' wuh nesh-kur ulidar t' nitrate t' haul-tukh fi-tor ish-veh gas'rak kehr-oth, heh wuh bulge fi' wuh gas'rak vla t' ish-veh fik-taik tor gluvaya wilat au has secreted ish-veh stethoscope, i bolau nam-tor pasik, indeed, kuv i ri tor pronounce ish-veh tor nam-tor wuh torupik kisau t' wuh hasuk ha'yigal." i kupi ri gol'nev laughing na' wuh ease k' if au danau ish-veh torek t' nenem. "lu i zhu-tor du mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh utvau, " i remarked, "wuh vel kwon-hau-ov saudau tor me tor nam-tor ni ridiculously velik ik i kupi easily tor ish-veh myself, hi na' tik successive instance t' ish-veh reasoning i am hertak-tor abi' du danau ish-veh torek. Heh wi i dva-tor ik t'nash-veh bezhun nam-tor u' rom u' ish-veh." "ved ni, " au kilko-tor, ha'gelan wuh cigarette, heh throwing himself ne' vi' wuh armchair. "gla-tor du, tonk'peh du ri tor glantau. Wuh distinction nam-tor pa'shik. Na' li-fal, du ma frequently gla-tor wuh ash-tor if ras-tukh abru s' wuh tvur tor nash tvi-shal." "frequently." "uf k'ashiv?" "muhl, ein hundreds t' wak." "yi uf wehk nam-tor tra'?" "uf wehk? I ri tor fai-tor." "ved ni! Du ma ri glantau. Heh wi du ma gla-tor. Ik nam-tor aishan t'nash-veh sfek. I', i fai-tor ik tra' nam-tor leh- steh ash-tor, fai'ei i ma fi' gla-tor heh glantau. K' wuh yut, opi' du nam-tor interested svi' aifa pi' wat, heh opi' du nam-tor rom hiyet tor chronicle veh il dahkuh t' t'nash-veh trifling veshtau, du lau nam-tor interested svi' nash." au threw abru' wuh thalv t' bali, faf-kur-tinted notepaper if had vesh' lying tu'ash fi-tor wuh pasu. "sarlah ish-veh k' wuh kim-shah lehk, " leralmin-tor au. "telv-tor ish-veh aloud." wuh pitoh vesh' undated, heh rik' either signature il shi'yavekh. "tra' dungi vutau fi-tor du tor-mu-yor, na' wuh yonuk tor ohkuh o'wak-vel, " ish-veh leralmin-tor, "wuh gentleman vi aitlu tor consult du fi-tor wuh tukh t' wuh maut deepest moment. Ish-veh recent dvin tor veh t' wuh royal kelek t' europe ma shown ik du nam-tor veh vi lau safely nam-tor trusted k' tukh if nam-tor t' wuh importance if mokuhlek hardly nam-tor exaggerated. Nash khrosahp t' du etek ma s' ek' ha-shal poprah. Nam-tor svi' ish-veh tvi-shal yi na' ik wadan, heh ri tor nem-tor ish-veh amiss kuv ish-veh visitor sai-vel-tor wuh limein." "nash nam-tor indeed wuh mystery, " i remarked. "ra tor du glenonau ik ish-veh tvai?" "i ma rai faik wi. Ish-veh nam-tor wuh capital lafosh tor theorise fa' veh has faik. Insensibly veh palikau tor kuvoran kla-min tor saikhut wihka, instead t' wihka tor saikhut kla-min. Tonk'peh wuh pitoh itself. Ra tor du deduce s' ish-veh?" i carefully linisau wuh kitaun, heh wuh dun fi-tor if ish-veh vesh' written. "wuh sasu vi kitau ish-veh vesh' presumably muhl tor tor, " i remarked, endeavouring tor va'amau t'nash-veh besu's patorau. "such dun kupi ri nam-tor bought ne' ulef wuh tarkiv wuh packet. Ish-veh nam-tor peculiarly karik heh stegel." "peculiarthat nam-tor wuh maut zhit, " leralmin-tor holmes. "ish-veh nam-tor ri wuh eingelsu dun na' ek'. Meskaraya ish-veh abru tor wuh ta'hal." i did ni, heh gla-tor wuh suk "e" k' wuh pi' "g, " wuh "p, " heh wuh suk "g" k' wuh pi' "t" woven vi' wuh lef'es t' wuh dun. "ra tor du tor t' ik?" ya'akash holmes. "wuh ahm t' wuh maker, rai vet; il ish-veh monogram, rather." "mokov. Wuh 'g' k' wuh pi' 't' lam-tor na' 'gesellschaft, ' if nam-tor wuh german na' 'apc'koik.' ish-veh nam-tor wuh customary contraction spo' etwel 'co.' 'p, ' veling, lam-tor na' 'papier.' i' na' wuh 'eg.' kal-tor etek glance na' etwel continental gazetteer." au nem-tor ne' wuh ras khav-kur ral'es s' ish-veh nef. "eglow, eglonitzhere etek nam-tor, egria. Ish-veh nam-tor svi' wuh german-speaking countryin bohemia, ri irak s' carlsbad. 'remarkable u' hasu wuh scene t' wuh tevakh t' wallenstein, heh na' its numerous makh-zhuk-om heh dun-mills.' ha, ha, t'nash-veh sa-kan, ra tor du tor t' ik?" ish-veh bezhun sparkled, heh au satau abru wuh lo'uk pla-kur triumphant wan s' ish-veh cigarette. "wuh dun vesh' tor svi' bohemia, " i leralmin-tor. "precisely. Heh wuh sasu vi kitau wuh pitoh nam-tor wuh german. Tor du pitoh wuh peculiar torvaya t' wuh zhit-bal'nash khrosahp t' du etek ma s' ek' ha-shal poprah.' wuh frenchman il russian kupi ri ma written ik. Ish-veh nam-tor wuh german vi nam-tor ni uncourteous tor ish-veh tor-zhit. Ish-veh goh hafau, therefore, tor discover ra nam-tor aitlu k' nash german vi kitau fi-tor bohemian dun heh prefers sai-vel-tor wuh limein tor showing ish-veh limuk. Heh la' sarlah ish-veh, kuv i am ri mistaken, tor resolve ek' etwel vet-tor." u' au stariben tra' vesh' wuh nasik ralash t' jarel' hoofs heh grating halek tehnat wuh curb, zahal-tor k' wuh nasik seshaya na' wuh kus-vakh. Holmes whistled. "wuh shif, k' wuh ralash, " leralmin-tor au. "ha, " au fator, glancing s' wuh krani. "wuh nice pi' brougham heh wuh shif t' beauties. Wuh hundred heh kau-leh guineas apiece. Tra''s donku svi' nash nuf, watson, kuv tra' nam-tor nothing else." "i nah-tor ik i had weh-rom hal-tor, holmes." "ri wuh zeshau, hassu. Stay wilat du nam-tor. I am pakik rik' t'nash-veh boswell. Heh nash ugau tor nam-tor eku'ki. Ish-veh would nam-tor wuh pity tor din-tor ish-veh." "tonk'peh ish-veh client" "worla kashek ish-veh. I lau aitlun ish-veh gol'nev, heh ni lau au. La' sarlah ish-veh. Hayal-tor ne' svi' ik armchair, hassu, heh mazhiv-kur-tor etek ish-veh buhfik attention." wuh vohris heh ras ash, if had vesh' puzhu-tor fi-tor wuh kaiden heh svi' wuh tvur, svizh-tor iyi s'udish wuh svep. Yi tra' vesh' wuh ral heh authoritative sayumak. "sarlah svi'!" leralmin-tor holmes. Wuh sasu svi-tor vi kupi hardly ma vesh' lehkuh tor shehkuh ash'ya shehkuh inches svi' pidek, k' wuh tuf heh sikrus t' wuh hercules. Ish-veh sai-vel vesh' don-ka k' wuh richness if would, svi' england, nam-tor glazhau fi-tor u' akin tor rasahkos zahvan. Ras zhel t' astrakhan vesh' slashed mes' wuh sleeves heh fronts t' ish-veh dahtau-breasted tor-pal, du' wuh glu pla-kur tor-sai if vesh' lehm-tor abru' ish-veh tipan vesh' zehl-tor k' yai-kur-tor silk heh shar-tor na' wuh talu k' wuh brooch if consisted t' wuh single flaming beryl. Kluf if sadvun-tor halfway abru ish-veh vaukh, heh if vesh' trimmed na' wuh fik k' don-ka khav-kur ausachya, ovsoh wuh impression t' barbaric opulence if vesh' suggested k' ish-veh bosh appearance. Au lesh wuh sax'ksei-brimmed taik svi' ish-veh el'ru, du' au sai-vel-tor mes' wuh upper krus t' ish-veh limuk, extending ne' vesht wuh cheekbones, wuh nesh-kur vizard limein, if au had sauyaing namishau ik maut moment, na' ish-veh el'ru vesh' fam dvun ashenau tor ish-veh u' au svi-tor. S' wuh weh-neik krus t' wuh limuk au saudau tor nam-tor wuh sasu t' karik character, k' wuh bali, hanging bru, heh wuh wu, zehik chin suggestive t' resolution kwitau tor wuh wu-vath t' obstinacy. "du had t'nash-veh pitoh?" au ya'akash k' wuh glu harsh spes heh wuh strongly pu'ulidau german accent. "i var-tor du ik i would vutau." au glazhau s' veh tor wuh vath t' etek, u' kuv uncertain if tor shi'yavekh. "pray nem-tor wuh ku-san, " leralmin-tor holmes. "nash nam-tor t'nash-veh t'hy'la heh kazhuksu, dr. Watson, vi nam-tor occasionally rom hiyet tor gol'nev me svi' t'nash-veh nuf. Ik ma i wuh dor tor shi'yavekh?" "du lau shi'yavekh me u' wuh tum-tor von kramm, wuh bohemian nobleman. I ken-tor ik nash gentleman, ish-veh t'hy'la, nam-tor wuh sasu t' dor heh discretion, ik i lau sahrafel k' wuh tukh t' wuh danik mairik importance. Kuv ri, i dang mau prefer tor sviribau k' du sa'awek." i she-tor tor hal-tor, tonk'peh holmes kum-tor me k' wuh kar-nik heh kwitau me pla' vi' t'nash-veh ku-san. "ish-veh nam-tor fi', il rim, " leralmin-tor au. "du lau leralmin fa' nash gentleman sovek-vel if du lau leralmin tor me." wuh tum-tor shrugged ish-veh sax'ksei tipan. "yi i bolau palikau, " leralmin-tor au, "k' binding du fi' tor ek'esik secrecy na' dahkuh tevun; na' wuh shaht t' ik wak wuh tukh dungi nam-tor t' rai importance. Na' la' ish-veh nam-tor ri nuh' mau tor leralmin ik ish-veh nam-tor t' such rasath ish-veh lau ma wuh vi-yumuk fi-tor european vesht-var." "i ugaya, " leralmin-tor holmes. "heh i." "du dungi tobeg nash limein, " fator etwel flekh visitor. "wuh august person vi employs me istau ish-veh agent tor nam-tor ri-fainu tor du, heh i lau confess na' wuh'wak ik wuh title k' if i ma aishan puvutau myself nam-tor ri exactly t'nash-veh sha'." "i vesh' aware t' ish-veh, " leralmin-tor holmes dryly. "wuh circumstances nam-tor t' lo'uk delicacy, heh kanok precaution has tor nam-tor taken tor quench ra lau tor'ovau tor nam-tor wuh immense scandal heh seriously compromise veh t' wuh reigning skan t' europe. Tor stariben plainly, wuh tukh implicates wuh lo'uk kelek t' ormstein, samekhik sa-te'kru t' bohemia." "i vesh' isha aware t' ik, " murmured holmes, settling himself ne' svi' ish-veh armchair heh ikapik ish-veh bezhun. Etwel visitor glanced k' ein apparent ak'wikmun na' wuh languid, lounging khlop t' wuh sasu vi had vesh' rai vet depicted tor ish-veh u' wuh danik incisive reasoner heh danik energetic agent svi' europe. Holmes slowly reopened ish-veh bezhun heh glazhau impatiently na' ish-veh masuk' client. "kuv ish-veh majesty would condescend tor fupa s' ish-veh nuf, " au remarked, "i dang nam-tor weh-rom kup tor na'shikhau du." wuh sasu sprang s' ish-veh ku-san heh sahr-tor abru heh ne' wuh tvi-shal svi' uncontrollable agitation. Yi, k' wuh gesture t' desperation, au tore wuh limein s' ish-veh limuk heh hurled ish-veh fi-tor wuh solektra. "du nam-tor gas'rak, " au maf-tor; "i am wuh sa-te'kru. Po dang i attempt tor ip-sut ish-veh?" "po, indeed?" murmured holmes. "ish-veh majesty had ri spoken fa' i vesh' aware ik i vesh' addressing wilhelm gottsreich sigismond von ormstein, grand duke t' cassel-felstein, heh samekhik sa-te'kru t' bohemia." "tonk'peh du mokuhlek ken-tor, " leralmin-tor etwel flekh visitor, sitting ne' wuh'wak weht heh be' dvun-tor ish-veh el'ru abru' ish-veh pid wan-kur fa-patam, "du mokuhlek ken-tor ik i am ri accustomed tor doing such business svi' t'nash-veh sha' person. Wi wuh tukh vesh' ni delicate ik i kupi ri confide ish-veh tor wuh agent rik' putting myself svi' ish-veh tepul. Ki'sarlah nash-veh incognito s' prague na' wuh lof t' consulting du." "yi, pray consult, " leralmin-tor holmes, shutting ish-veh bezhun wuh'wak weht. "wuh kla-min nam-tor briefly aifa: ein kaukuh tevun ago, du' wuh lengthy yaret tor warsaw, i tor wuh acquaintance t' wuh muhl-fainu adventuress, irene adler. Wuh ahm nam-tor rai vet familiar tor du." "kindly glazhau ish-veh abru svi' t'nash-veh nakh, hassu, " murmured holmes rik' sharu ish-veh bezhun. Na' wehk tevun au had thanai wuh torektra t' docketing ek' paragraphs fundik sasu heh vel, ni ik ish-veh vesh' rihagik tor ahm wuh subject il wuh person fi' if au kupi ri na' wuh'wak furnish ro'fori. Svi' nash nuf i afer-tor ish-veh biography sandwiched svi' svi' ik t' wuh hebrew rabbi heh ik t' wuh suyu-commander vi had written wuh monograph fi-tor wuh glu-masutra aluk. "kal-tor me gla-tor!" leralmin-tor holmes. "hum! Pukeshta svi' uzh jersey svi' wuh tevun 1858. Contraltohum! La scala, hum! Prima donna imperial opera t' warsawyes! Retired s' operatic stageha! Living svi' londonquite ni! Ish-veh majesty, u' i ken-tor, became entangled k' nash nu'ri person, kitau ish-veh ein compromising nuhm, heh nam-tor i' desirous t' getting eifa nuhm pla'." "precisely ni. Tonk'peh uf" "vesh' tra' wuh tsat kal'i'farr?" "rim." "rai legal dun il tor-kisev?" "rim." "yi i vravshau tor zahal-tor ish-veh majesty. Kuv nash nu'ri person dang torvau ish-veh nuhm na' blackmailing il vath lof, uf nam-tor she tor skan-tor ish-veh authenticity?" "tra' nam-tor wuh kitaun." "pooh, pooh! Forgery." "t'nash-veh awek pitoh-dun." "stolen." "t'nash-veh sha' fen." "va'amau." "t'nash-veh ha'gel-bikuv." "bought." "etek vesh' fi' svi' wuh ha'gel-bikuv." "oh, tal-kam! Ik nam-tor maut rasahkos! Ish-veh majesty has indeed committed wuh indiscretion." "i vesh' madinsane." "du ma compromised yourself seriously." "i vesh' goh tarkiv prince yi. I vesh' nu'ri. I am tonk'peh reh-leh i'." "ish-veh bolau nam-tor recovered." "etek ma ar'kada heh vravshau." "ish-veh majesty bolau vlitau. Ish-veh bolau nam-tor bought." "she dungi ri makau." "stolen, yi." "kaukuh attempts ma vesh' tor. Dah'wak burglars svi' t'nash-veh vlitau ransacked ish-veh kelek. Wuh'wak etek matau ish-veh luggage lu she travelled. Dah'wak she has vesh' waylaid. Tra' has vesh' rai result." "rai glat t' ish-veh?" "absolutely rim." holmes abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor. "ish-veh nam-tor ved wuh takov pi' wat, " leralmin-tor au. "tonk'peh wuh maut serious veh tor me, " fun-tor wuh sa-te'kru reproachfully. "maut, indeed. Heh ra tor she propose tor tor k' wuh ha'gel-bikuv?" "tor ruin me." "tonk'peh uf?" "i am pa' tor nam-tor telik." "ni i ma puzhu-tor." "tor clotilde lothman von saxe-meningen, dahr ko-fu t' wuh sa-te'kru t' scandinavia. Du lau fai-tor wuh wonil dvatai t' ish-veh skan. She nam-tor herself wuh maut soul t' delicacy. Wuh duv t' wuh vet u' tor t'nash-veh spa-tor would katau wuh tukh tor wuh shaht." "heh irene adler?" "nan-tor tor satau au wuh ha'gel-bikuv. Heh she dungi tor ish-veh. I fai-tor ik she dungi tor ish-veh. Du ri tor fai-tor ish-veh, tonk'peh she has wuh soul t' pishek. She has wuh limuk t' wuh danik vaksurik t' kosu, heh wuh kashek t' wuh danik resolute t' sasu. Rather do i dang marry wuh'ashiv kosu, tra' nam-tor rai wu-vath tor if she would ri gonone." "du nam-tor sure ik she has ri satau ish-veh wi?" "i am sure." "heh po?" "fai'ei she has leralmin-tor ik she would satau ish-veh fi' wuh gad lu wuh betrothal vesh' publicly afsakau. Ik dungi nam-tor thurai gad." "oh, yi etek ma rehkuh gad wi, " leralmin-tor holmes k' wuh luvaya. "ik nam-tor maut fortunate, u' i ma veh il dahkuh tukh t' importance tor glazhau vi' aishan na' la'. Ish-veh majesty dungi, veling, stay svi' london na' wuh la'?" "certainly. Du dungi talal me na' wuh langham ne' wuh ahm t' wuh tum-tor von kramm." "yi i dungau eku du wuh zehl tor kal-tor du fai-tor uf etek progress." "pray tor ni. I dungau nam-tor ek' anxiety." "yi, u' tor donku?" "du ma carte blanche." "absolutely?" "i var-tor du ik i would mazhiv-kur-tor veh t' wuh provinces t' t'nash-veh kingdom tor ma ik ha'gel-bikuv." "heh na' la' kodona?" wuh sa-te'kru nem-tor wuh ras chamois duf sa'haf s' ne' ish-veh tor-sai heh laid ish-veh fi' wuh pasu. "tra' nam-tor rehkuh hundred plesh-tor svi' pi-maat-tukh heh stehkuh hundred svi' pitoh, " au leralmin-tor. Holmes scribbled wuh receipt fi-tor wuh thalv t' ish-veh pitoh-dunap heh handed ish-veh tor ish-veh. "heh mademoiselle's shi'yavekh?" au ya'akash. "nam-tor briony lodge, serpentine avenue, st. John's lapan." holmes nem-tor wuh pitoh t' ish-veh. "veh vath deshker, " leralmin-tor au. "vesh' wuh ha'gel-bikuv wuh tsorayek?" "ish-veh vesh'." "yi, rom-mu-yor, ish-veh majesty, heh i sahrafel ik etek dungau ak ma ein rom ro'fori na' du. Heh rom-mu-yor, watson, " au hau, u' wuh halek t' wuh royal brougham padukau ne' wuh yut. "kuv du dungi nam-tor rom hiyet tor vutau tor-morrow aru na' rehkuh o'wak-vel i dang spo' tor chat nash pi' tukh abru' k' du." ii. Na' rehkuh o'wak-vel precisely i vesh' na' leipausu yut, tonk'peh holmes had ri wi fun-tor. Wuh landlady informed me ik au had losrak wuh kelek shortly po' ohkuh o'wak-vel svi' wuh asal. I hayal-tor ne' be' wuh yon, however, k' wuh intention t' awaiting ish-veh, however wu au lau nam-tor. I vesh' already deeply interested svi' ish-veh inquiry, na', hi ish-veh vesh' vikuvau k' rim t' wuh grim heh flekh features if vesh' katravah k' wuh dahkuh tr'y'kak if i ma already vipladau, fam dvun, wuh malat t' wuh nuf heh wuh exalted wurzel t' ish-veh client mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh character t' its sha'. Indeed, k'wuhli s' wuh malat t' wuh investigation if t'nash-veh t'hy'la had fi' el'ru, tra' vesh' vel svi' ish-veh masterly ruskaraya t' wuh situation, heh ish-veh keen, incisive reasoning, if tor ish-veh wuh sanosh tor me tor orenau ish-veh torektra t' ar'kadan, heh tor zahal-tor wuh sahris, subtle methods k' if au disentangled wuh danik inextricable mysteries. Ni accustomed vesh' i tor ish-veh invariable navun ik wuh maut possibility t' ish-veh failing had ceased tor svi-tor vi' t'nash-veh patam. Ish-veh vesh' ikap-tor fi-tor kehkuh fa' wuh svep tu'ash, heh wuh drunken-looking groom, has-bosh-kempt heh vla-whiskered, k' wuh inflamed limuk heh disreputable sai-vel, lates-tor vi' wuh tvi-shal. Accustomed u' i vesh' tor t'nash-veh t'hy'la's taurauk tepul svi' wuh nam-tor-tor t' pastau, i had tor glazhau rehkuh wak fa' i vesh' ac'ruth ik ish-veh vesh' indeed au. K' wuh nod au vanished vi' wuh shi'yuk, whence au sasarlah svi' kaukuh minutes tweed-suited heh respectable, u' t' hinek. Putting ish-veh el'ru vi' ish-veh abru'lik, au sakadau si' ish-veh mal svi' khom t' wuh yon heh abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor heartily na' ein minutes. "muhl, really!" au maf-tor, heh yi au khluhkau heh abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor va'ashiv abi' au vesh' obliged tor ti pla', limp heh helpless, svi' wuh ku-san. "ra nam-tor ish-veh?" "ish-veh's ved nuh' funny. I am sure du kupi worla guess uf i employed t'nash-veh asal, il ra i shahtau k' doing." "i mokuhlek't glenonau. I suppose ik du ma vesh' watching wuh es'merka, heh sos'eh wuh kelek, t' din-tor irene adler." "ved ni; tonk'peh wuh sequel vesh' rather ritsuri. I dungi var-tor du, however. I losrak wuh kelek wuh pi' po' ohkuh o'wak-vel nash asal svi' wuh character t' wuh groom s' ar'kadan. Tra' nam-tor wuh wonderful sympathy heh freemasonry among horsey sasu. Nam-tor veh t' au, heh du dungi fai-tor ek' ik tra' nam-tor tor fai-tor. I ak afer-tor briony lodge. Ish-veh nam-tor wuh bijou villa, k' wuh bah-ker na' wuh pla', tonk'peh torvau si' svi' khom gas'rak abru tor wuh fau-yut, dahkuh var. Chubb klachek tor wuh svep. Suk sitting-tvi-shal fi' wuh gas'rak vla, muhl furnished, k' wu krani siyah tor wuh lan-tol, heh eifa preposterous eingelsu krani terayek if wuh kan kupi tu'ash. Za' tra' vesh' nothing remarkable, korsau ik wuh tvur krani kupi nam-tor pulau s' wuh fik t' wuh coach-kelek. I lates-tor pauk ish-veh heh linisau ish-veh closely s' kanok sfek t' zan-tor, tonk'peh rik' noting sovek-kitok t' eku'ko. "i yi lounged ne' wuh yut heh afer-tor, u' i gishu, ik tra' vesh' wuh mews svi' wuh lane if sahr-tor ne' k' veh temok t' wuh bah-ker. I lent wuh ostlers wuh el'ru svi' rubbing ne' ish-veh jarel, heh poprah svi' di'kizh twopence, wuh makh t' ulef-heh-ulef, dahkuh boshau t' shag tobacco, heh u' mau ro'fori u' i kupi aitlun pa' din-tor adler, tor leralmin nothing t' ulef wuh dozen vath sutra svi' wuh neighbourhood svi' ik i vesh' ri svi' wuh least interested, tonk'peh t'vi biographies i vesh' compelled tor shroi tor." "heh ra t' irene adler?" i ya'akash. "oh, she has da-tor ek' wuh sasu's patam ne' svi' ik krus. She nam-tor wuh daintiest vel ne' wuh bonnet fi' nash ek'tra. Ni leralmin wuh serpentine-mews, tor wuh sasu. She ha-tor quietly, uralau na' concerts, yetur si' na' kaukuh kanok gad, heh fun-tor na' stehkuh nasik na' aru-yem. Seldom hal-tor si' na' vath wak, kaula lu she uralau. Has goh veh sa visitor, tonk'peh wuh rom deal t' ish-veh. Au nam-tor gu'gelik, handsome, heh dashing, worla calls lehkuh tor wuh'wak wuh gad, heh k'ashiv dah'wak. Au nam-tor wuh mr. Godfrey norton, t' wuh tvik temple. Gla-tor wuh advantages t' wuh cabman u' wuh confidant. Au had driven ish-veh ha-kel wuh dozen wak s' serpentine-mews, heh fai-tor ek' pa' ish-veh. Lu i had shroi tor ek' au had tor var-tor, i began tor lates abru heh ne' be' briony lodge wuh'wak weht, heh tor nah-tor abru' t'nash-veh dotor t' campaign. "nash godfrey norton vesh' evidently wuh yauluhk klai svi' wuh tukh. Au vesh' wuh lawyer. Ik sounded ominous. Ra vesh' wuh relation svi' au, heh ra wuh vel t' ish-veh ashiv-tor yaretau? Vesh' she ish-veh client, ish-veh t'hy'la, il ish-veh mistress? Kuv wuh former, she had probably transferred wuh ha'gel-bikuv tor ish-veh keeping. Kuv wuh latter, ish-veh vesh' lehkuh kesik. Fi' wuh issue t' nash deshker nerau whether i dang fator t'nash-veh ar'kadan na' briony lodge, il da-tor t'nash-veh attention tor wuh gentleman's tvi-shal svi' wuh temple. Ish-veh vesh' wuh delicate sfek, heh ish-veh widened wuh vunai t' t'nash-veh inquiry. I pthak ik i spitau du k' aifa details, tonk'peh i ma tor kal-tor gla-tor du t'nash-veh pi' rihag'es, kuv du nam-tor tor ken-tor wuh situation." "i am zahalik du closely, " i kilko-tor. "i vesh' fam dvun balancing wuh tukh svi' t'nash-veh kashek lu wuh hansom cab drove abru tor briony lodge, heh wuh gentleman sprang si'. Au vesh' wuh remarkably handsome sasu, gu'gelik, aquiline, heh moustachedevidently wuh sasu t' ik i had puzhu-tor. Au saudau tor nam-tor svi' wuh lo'uk brax, saul-tor tor wuh cabman tor bek-tor, heh brushed vesht wuh maid vi tu'ash wuh svep k' wuh sov t' wuh sasu vi vesh' thoroughly na' ha-kel. "au vesh' svi' wuh kelek pa' ulef wuh wadan, heh i kupi kum glimpses t' ish-veh svi' wuh krani t' wuh sitting-tvi-shal, pacing abru heh ne', talking excitedly, heh pral-tor ish-veh kar. T' ish-veh kupi gla-tor nash-veh nothing. Presently au sasarlah, looking kauk weht flurried do fa'. U' au ash-tor abru tor wuh cab, au seshau wuh pi-maat-tukh glantau s' ish-veh abru'lik heh glazhau na' ish-veh earnestly, 'yetur spo' wuh e'shua, ' au saul-tor, 'wuh'rak tor gross & hankey's svi' regent yut, heh yi tor wuh church t' st. Monica svi' wuh edgeware fau-yut. Ulef wuh guinea kuv du tor ish-veh svi' dah-leh minutes!' "maf au went, heh i vesh' aishan wondering whether i dang ri tor muhl tor zahal-tor au lu abru wuh lane sarlah wuh pu pi' landau, wuh coachman k' ish-veh tor-pal goh ulef-buttoned, heh ish-veh tie ne' ish-veh kaluk, du' ek' wuh tags t' ish-veh harness vesh' sticking s' wuh tersek. Ish-veh hadn't seshau abru fa' she pohshaya s' wuh tvur svep heh vi' ish-veh. I goh kum-tor wuh glimpse t' ish-veh na' wuh moment, tonk'peh she vesh' wuh lovely kosu, k' wuh limuk ik wuh sasu lau tev-tor na'. "'wuh church t' st. Monica, john, ' she maf-tor, 'heh ulef wuh sovereign kuv du pulau ish-veh svi' dah-leh minutes.' "nash vesh' ved nuh' rom tor pak-tor, watson. I vesh' aishan balancing whether i dang sahr-tor na' ish-veh, il whether i dang perch za' ish-veh landau lu wuh cab sarlah k'fai wuh yut. Wuh yetursu glazhau dah'wak na' such wuh shabby panavau, tonk'peh i spen-tor svi' fa' au kupi vel. 'wuh church t' st. Monica, ' leralmin-tor i, 'heh ulef wuh sovereign kuv du pulau ish-veh svi' dah-leh minutes.' ish-veh vesh' dah-leh-kaukuh minutes tor leh-dah, heh veling ish-veh vesh' pa'shik hiyet ra vesh' svi' wuh salan. "t'nash-veh cabby drove sahris. I ri tor nah-tor i ek'wak drove faster, tonk'peh wuh vath vesh' tra' fa' etek. Wuh cab heh wuh landau k' ish-veh steaming jarel vesh' svi' khom t' wuh svep lu i lasha. I vlitau wuh sasu heh hurried vi' wuh church. Tra' vesh' ri wuh soul tra' korsau wuh dahkuh ik i had zahal-tor heh wuh surpliced clergyman, vi seemed tor nam-tor expostulating k' au. Au vesh' ek' rehkuh standing svi' wuh knot svi' khom t' wuh altar. I lounged abru wuh vla aisle spo' sovek vath idler vi has eku-tor vi' wuh church. Suddenly, tor t'nash-veh ak'wikmun, wuh rehkuh na' wuh altar limuk-tor pauk tor me, heh godfrey norton sarlah sahran u' lerash u' au kupi na' me. "'itaren oekon, ' au maf-tor. 'du'll tor. Sarlah! Sarlah!' "'ra yi?' i ya'akash. "'sarlah, sasu, sarlah, goh rehkuh minutes, il ish-veh skil-tor't nam-tor legal.' "i vesh' ulef-zaseshau abru tor wuh altar, heh fa' i fai-tor wilat i vesh' i afer-tor myself mumbling kesaya if vesh' zhal-tor svi' t'nash-veh kaluk, heh vouching na' vel t' if i fai-tor nothing, heh paik assisting svi' wuh shar tying abru t' irene adler, spinster, tor godfrey norton, bachelor. Ish-veh vesh' ek' ovsoh svi' wuh instant, heh tra' vesh' wuh gentleman thanking me fi' wuh veh vla heh wuh t'sai fi' wuh vath, du' wuh clergyman beamed fi' me svi' khom. Ish-veh vesh' wuh danik preposterous shul svi' if i ek'wak afer-tor myself svi' t'nash-veh ha'kiv, heh ish-veh vesh' wuh nahp t' ish-veh ik palikau me laughing aishan i'. Ish-veh seems ik tra' had vesh' ein informality pa' ish-veh license, ik wuh clergyman absolutely klee'fah tor marry au rik' wuh toglantausu t' ein wihfelau, heh ik t'nash-veh kunli appearance korsau wuh bridegroom s' having tor sally si' vi' wuh yut svi' psthan t' wuh buhfik sasu. Wuh bride mazhiv-kur-tor me wuh sovereign, heh i tvai sai-vel-tor ish-veh fi' t'nash-veh glantau naf-elakh svi' vokaya t' wuh occasion." "nash nam-tor wuh maut ri-gishu da-tor t' tek'ik, " leralmin-tor i; "heh ra yi?" "muhl, i afer-tor t'nash-veh dotoran maut seriously menaced. Ish-veh glazhau u' kuv wuh shif lau nem-tor wuh iyi trashan, heh ni necessitate maut prompt heh energetic thon-tor fi' t'nash-veh krus. Na' wuh church svep, however, au dahshau, au driving pla' tor wuh temple, heh she tor ish-veh sha' kelek. 'i dungau yetur si' svi' wuh shi'sochya na' kaukuh u' tsuri, ' she leralmin-tor u' she losrak ish-veh. I puzhu-tor rai weht. Au drove maf svi' natya kharat, heh i went ska' tor tor t'nash-veh sha' arrangements." "if nam-tor?" "ein samu kahm heh wuh makh t' naliveh, " au kilko-tor, ringing wuh kus-vakh. "i ma vesh' nuh' toranik tor nah-tor t' yem-tukh, heh i am kesik tor nam-tor busier fam dvun nash khru. K' wuh yut, hassu, i dungau aitlun ish-veh co-el'toraya." "i dungau nam-tor delighted." "du ri tor kashek breaking wuh tor-gav?" "ri svi' wuh least." "il sahran wuh pavesh t' pehkaya?" "ri svi' wuh rom aishan." "oh, wuh aishan nam-tor marom!" "yi i am ish-veh sasu." "i vesh' sure ik i lau rely fi' du." "tonk'peh ra nam-tor ish-veh du istaya?" "lu mrs. Turner has katau svi' wuh tray i dungi tor ish-veh pa'shik tor du. I', " au leralmin-tor u' au da-tor hungrily fi' wuh velik panavau ik etwel landlady had tanilau, "i bolau discuss ish-veh du' i yokul, na' i ma ri mau wak. Ish-veh nam-tor nearly kaukuh i'. Svi' dahkuh wadan etek bolau nam-tor fi' wuh scene t' torai. Din-tor irene, il madame, rather, fun-tor s' ish-veh yetur na' stehkuh. Etek bolau nam-tor na' briony lodge tor ragel-tor ish-veh." "heh ra yi?" "du bolau trasha ik tor me. I ma already arranged ra nam-tor tor paresh-tor. Tra' nam-tor goh veh sfek fi' if i bolau insist. Du bolau ri snertau, sarlah ra lau. Du ken-tor?" "i am tor nam-tor ta'raf?" "tor tor nothing whatever. Tra' dungi probably nam-tor ein pi' unpleasantness. Ri tor hau svi' ish-veh. Ish-veh dungi shaht svi' t'nash-veh hasu zhelesh vi' wuh kelek. Kehkuh il kaukuh minutes afterwards wuh sitting-tvi-shal krani dungi tu'ash. Du nam-tor tor wurzel yourself beyik ik tu'ash krani." "ha." "du nam-tor tor glantau me, na' i dungi nam-tor visible tor du." "ha." "heh lu i ashenau t'nash-veh handsoyou dungi lehm vi' wuh tvi-shal ra i mazhiv-kur-tor du tor lehm, heh dungi, na' wuh ka wak, ashenau wuh maf t' yon. Du ved zahal-tor me?" "entirely." "ish-veh nam-tor nothing maut formidable, " au leralmin-tor, taking wuh wu cigar-kushizhau padukau s' ish-veh abru'lik. "ish-veh nam-tor wuh ordinary plumber's vuzh-yon-hashek, fitted k' wuh taik na' either shaht tor tor ish-veh shal-ha'gelan. Ish-veh task nam-tor confined tor ik. Lu du ashenau ish-veh maf t' yon, ish-veh dungi nam-tor taken abru k' ved wuh su'etek t' sutra. Du lau yi lates tor wuh shaht t' wuh yut, heh i dungi rejoin du svi' lehkuh minutes. I rok ik i ma tor myself pa'shik?" "i am tor hafau ta'raf, tor prah be' wuh krani, tor glantau du, heh na' wuh glantokaya tor lehm svi' nash vel, yi tor ashenau wuh maf t' yon, heh tor bek-tor du na' wuh teruk t' wuh yut." "precisely." "yi du lau entirely rely fi' me." "ik nam-tor marom. I nah-tor, sos'eh, ish-veh nam-tor siyah wak ik i dator na' wuh uzh role i ma tor mavau." au sasaudau vi' ish-veh shi'yuk heh fun-tor svi' wuh zamu minutes svi' wuh character t' wuh amiable heh velik-minded nonconformist clergyman. Ish-veh sax'ksei nesh-kur taik, ish-veh baggy malanu, ish-veh wan-kur tie, ish-veh sympathetic abru'teruklar-ru'lut, heh paik glazhau t' peering heh benevolent curiosity vesh' such u' mr. John hare sa'awek kupi ma equalled. Ish-veh vesh' ri goh ik holmes rubai ish-veh costume. Ish-veh sagluvaya, ish-veh manner, ish-veh maut soul seemed tor vuhnau k' kanok sluk krus ik au assumed. Wuh skaf pakik wuh tok-ti fundauik-ithop, kauk u' ek'tal pakik wuh zat reasoner, lu au became wuh specialist svi' tr'y'kak. Ish-veh vesh' wuh yonuk vesht shehkuh lu etek losrak leipausu yut, heh ish-veh fam dvun aitlu lehkuh minutes tor wuh wadan lu etek afer-tor ourselves svi' serpentine avenue. Ish-veh vesh' already dusk, heh wuh ha'gelek vesh' aishan hasu lighted u' etek sahr-tor abru heh ne' svi' khom t' briony lodge, waiting na' wuh coming t' its occupant. Wuh kelek vesh' aishan such u' i had pictured ish-veh s' sherlock holmes' succinct kethelvaya, tonk'peh wuh locality saudau tor nam-tor lehkuh awek do i gishu. Fi' wuh contrary, na' wuh pi' yut svi' wuh hizhuk neighbourhood, ish-veh vesh' remarkably animated. Tra' vesh' wuh travek t' shabbily sai-vel-tor sasu smoking heh laughing svi' wuh teruk, wuh scissors-grazhayek k' ish-veh halek, dahkuh guardsmen vi vesh' flirting k' wuh nurse-ko-kan, heh several muhl-sai-vel-tor nu'ri sasu vi vesh' lounging abru heh ne' k' cigars svi' ish-veh ru'lut. "gla-tor du, " remarked holmes, u' etek sahr-tor tor heh fro svi' khom t' wuh kelek, "nash kal'i'farr rather simplifies tukh. Wuh ha'gel-bikuv shetau wuh dahtau-rihkau wun i'. Wuh pavesh nam-tor ik she would nam-tor u' averse tor its hasu gla-tor k' mr. Godfrey norton, u' etwel client nam-tor tor its coming tor wuh bezhun t' ish-veh princess. I' wuh deshker nam-tor, wilat nam-tor etek tor talal wuh ha'gel-bikuv?" "wilat, indeed?" "ish-veh nam-tor danik rikesik ik she lesh ish-veh pa' k' ish-veh. Ish-veh nam-tor tsorayek suk'es. Nuh' suk na' hagik concealment pa' wuh kosu's sai-vel. She fai-tor ik wuh sa-te'kru nam-tor capable t' having ish-veh waylaid heh pstha. Dahkuh attempts t' wuh wihfelau ma already vesh' tor. Etek lau nem-tor ish-veh, yi, ik she tor ri lesh ish-veh pa' k' ish-veh." "wilat, yi?" "ish-veh banker il ish-veh lawyer. Tra' nam-tor ik dahtau possibility. Tonk'peh i am vul-tor tor nah-tor neither. Kosu nam-tor naturally secretive, heh au spo' tor tor ish-veh sha' secreting. Po dang she el'ru ish-veh abru' tor sovek-veh else? She kupi sahrafel ish-veh sha' guardianship, tonk'peh she kupi ri var-tor ra indirect il political vi-yumuk lau nam-tor katau tor lesh fi-tor wuh business sasu. Isha, vokau ik she had resolved tor nam-tor-tor ish-veh k'svi wuh zamu gad. Ish-veh bolau nam-tor wilat she mokuhlek ti ish-veh el'ru fi-tor ish-veh. Ish-veh bolau nam-tor svi' ish-veh sha' kelek." "tonk'peh ish-veh has dah'wak vesh' burgled." "pshaw! Au did ri fai-tor uf tor glazhau." "tonk'peh uf dungi du glazhau?" "i dungi ri glazhau." "ra yi?" "i dungi prah ish-veh tor gluvaya me." "tonk'peh she dungi klee'fah." "she dungi ri nam-tor kup tor. Tonk'peh i zhu-tor wuh rumble t' halek. Ish-veh nam-tor ish-veh carriage. I' fitor t'nash-veh zek tor wuh nuhm." u' au stariben wuh gleam t' wuh sidelights t' wuh carriage sarlah pauk wuh curve t' wuh avenue. Ish-veh vesh' wuh klon pi' landau if rattled abru tor wuh svep t' briony lodge. U' ish-veh seshau abru, veh t' wuh loafing sasu na' wuh teruk dashed fa'rak tor tu'ash wuh svep svi' wuh rok t' earning wuh khaf-tukh, tonk'peh vesh' elbowed maf k' wuh'ashiv loafer, vi had rushed abru k' wuh ka intention. Wuh kei quarrel shau si', if vesh' increased k' wuh dahkuh guardsmen, vi nem-tor vla k' veh t' wuh loungers, heh k' wuh scissors-grazhayek, vi vesh' kaing fal fi-tor wuh vath vla. Wuh salur vesh' kwul-tor, heh svi' wuh instant wuh t'sai, vi had ash-tor s' ish-veh carriage, vesh' wuh centre t' wuh pi' knot t' kluhvau heh struggling sasu, vi kwul-tor savagely na' tik vath k' ish-veh ozh-dukal heh terpau. Holmes dashed vi' wuh patreitan tor protect wuh t'sai; tonk'peh, aishan u' au pulau ish-veh, au mazhiv-kur-tor wuh maf heh eku-tor tor wuh solektra, k' wuh khaf sahran freely ne' ish-veh limuk. Na' ish-veh tevan wuh guardsmen nem-tor tor ish-veh timut svi' veh kharat heh wuh loungers svi' wuh vath, du' wuh su'etek t' weh-rom sai-vel-tor sutra, vi had glantau wuh scuffle rik' taking krus svi' ish-veh, crowded svi' tor gol'nev wuh t'sai heh tor attend tor wuh dash-tor sasu. Irene adler, u' i dungi fam dvun vutau ish-veh, had hurried abru wuh ash-tor; tonk'peh she lam-tor na' wuh fik k' ish-veh superb khlop outlined tehnat wuh ha'ge t' wuh tvur, looking pla' vi' wuh yut. "nam-tor wuh ri donku-tor gentleman mau dash-tor?" she ya'akash. "au nam-tor tevik, " maf-tor several spes. "rai, rai, tra''s ha'kiv svi' ish-veh!" saul-tor wuh'ashiv. Nash yut, sanoi!" slowly heh solemnly au vesh' borne vi' briony lodge heh laid si' svi' wuh principal tvi-shal, du' i fam dvun glantau wuh proceedings s' t'nash-veh lehk k' wuh krani. Etek nam-tor tonk'peh preventing ish-veh s' injuring wuh'ashiv. Holmes had hayal-tor abru fi-tor wuh ku-san, heh vesht gla-tor nash-veh ish-veh dvunel spo' wuh sasu vi nam-tor svi' bolaya t' sov. Wuh maid rushed mes' heh threw tu'ash wuh krani. "nothing kupi ma vesh' weh-rom. Ish-veh nam-tor ek' gas'rak." "du ma wuh ha'gel-bikuv?" "i fai-tor wilat ish-veh nam-tor." "heh uf did du talal si'?" "she gluvau me, u' i var-tor du she would." She vesh' bound ki' me svi'. Ra else kupi she tor? Heh vi' ish-veh sitting-tvi-shal, if vesh' wuh maut tvi-shal if i suspected. Wuh vikayek t' yon vesh' admirably ovsoh. Wuh vuzh heh shouting vesh' hiyet tor hutau tor'tsu t' pishek. She kesau beautifully. Wuh pi' abru'-precipitance lau ruin ek'." "heh i'?" i ya'akash. "etwel psthan nam-tor practically shahtau. I dungau vutau k' wuh sa-te'kru tor-morrow, heh k' du, kuv du tun tor sarlah k' etek. She dungi ri nam-tor abru, ni ik etek dungau ma wuh pa'shik vunai. Isha, etek bolau nam-tor prompt, na' nash kal'i'farr lau tvai wuh ovsotik rubah svi' ish-veh ha'kiv heh es'merka. I yuk-tor na' leipausu yut ik mu-yor, heh etek vesh' engaged fi-tor etwel toast heh mon svi' wuh asal lu wuh sa-te'kru t' bohemia rushed vi' wuh tvi-shal. Sherlock holmes, i dva-tor?" leralmin-tor she. "i am mr. Holmes, " kilko-tor t'nash-veh besu, looking na' ish-veh k' wuh questioning heh rather startled gaze. "indeed! Tor nam-tor losrak till puvutau na'." t'nash-veh t'hy'la tore ish-veh tu'ash, heh etek ek' rehkuh telv-tor ish-veh teretuhr. Abi' po' wuh vikayek t' yon, i had ri wuh suspicion. Tonk'peh yi, lu i afer-tor uf i had pusvik-tor myself, i began tor nah-tor. I had vesh' vikau tehnat du tevun-krus ago. Wuh yon-kur-headed league i had puvutau fi-tor t'nash-veh t'hy'la, mr. "ra else mokuhlek nam-tor indicated k' ik gas'rak cuff ni maut shiny na' kaukuh inches, heh wuh losrak veh k' wuh mos patch be' wuh kar-nef wilat du shom ish-veh fi-tor wuh kitau-skaf?" I ma tor wuh pi' orenau t' tattoo ulidar heh ma kauk contributed tor wuh kitau-tanaf t' wuh subject. Ik trick t' staining wuh aluk' wef t' wuh delicate faf-kur nam-tor ved peculiar tor china. Lu, svi' haya, gla-tor nash-veh wuh chinese di'kaudj hanging s' ish-veh glantau-naf-elakh, wuh tukh shetau kauk weht velik." mr. Jabez wilson abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor heavily. "muhl, i worla!" leralmin-tor au. "i nahp palikauk ik du had ovsoh vel clever, tonk'peh gla-tor nash-veh ik tra' vesh' nothing svi' ish-veh po' ek'." "i palikau tor nah-tor, watson, " leralmin-tor holmes, "ik i tor wuh lafosh svi' explaining. 'omne ignotum pro magnifico, ' du fai-tor, heh t'nash-veh ri donku-tor pi' reputation, such u' ish-veh nam-tor, dungi dash shipwreck kuv i am ni candid. Mokuhlek du ri talal wuh advertisement, mr. Wilson?" "ha, i ma prah ish-veh i', " au kilko-tor k' ish-veh bali yon-kur ozh kastkau halfway ne' wuh tsek. "la' ish-veh nam-tor. Nash nam-tor ra began ish-veh ek'. Du aishan telv-tor ish-veh na' yourself, osu." i nem-tor wuh dun s' ish-veh heh telv-tor u' zahal-tor: "tor wuh yon-kur-headed league: fi' khrosahp t' wuh bequest t' wuh tab-ma ezekiah hopkins, t' lebanon, pennsylvania, u.s. Wuh, tra' nam-tor i' wuh'ashiv vacancy tu'ash if entitles wuh kisau t' wuh league tor wuh salary t' 4 wuh wehk gad na' purely nominal dvin. "ra fi' terra tor nash tvai?" i khrasau po' i had dah'wak telv-tor abru' wuh wehtsuri announcement. Holmes chuckled heh wriggled svi' ish-veh ku-san, u' vesh' ish-veh es'merka lu svi' pid tam'a. "muhl, ish-veh nam-tor aishan u' i ma vesh' telling du, mr. Sherlock holmes, " leralmin-tor jabez wilson, mopping ish-veh fa-patam; "i ma wuh pi' pawnbroker's business na' coburg keh-vla, be' wuh kahr. "ra nam-tor wuh ahm t' nash obliging youth?" ya'akash sherlock holmes. "ish-veh ahm nam-tor vincent spaulding, heh au's ri such wuh youth, either. Ish-veh's lerash tor leralmin ish-veh ya'shakhuv. I dang ri istaya wuh smarter assistant, mr. Holmes; heh i fai-tor maut muhl ik au kupi weh-rom himself heh pinkau dah'wak ra i am kup tor mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh. Ish-veh nam-tor ri wuh tsuri veshtaya among employers svi' nash ya'shakhuv. I ri tor fai-tor ik ish-veh assistant nam-tor ri u' remarkable u' ish-veh advertisement." "oh, au has ish-veh lafot, nuh', " leralmin-tor mr. Wilson. "worla vesh' such wuh katravahsu na' ha'gel-tanaf. Snapping maf k' wuh glayek lu au ought tor nam-tor improving ish-veh kashek, heh yi diving ne' vi' wuh cellar spo' wuh rabbit vi' its razh tor storau ish-veh bikuv. Ik nam-tor ish-veh nen lafot, tonk'peh fi' wuh bosh au's wuh rom worker. Tra''s rai vice svi' ish-veh." "au nam-tor fam dvun k' du, i presume?" "ha, osu. Au heh wuh ko-kan t' leh-keh, vi tor wuh zeshau t' velik fasan heh potau wuh shi cleanthat's ek' i ma svi' wuh kelek, na' i am wuh kir'an heh worla had sovek skan. Wilson, ik i vesh' wuh yon-kur-headed sasu.' "'po ik?' i ya'akash. "'po, ' leralmin-tor au, 'la''s wuh'ashiv vacancy fi' wuh league t' wuh yon-kur-headed sasu. "muhl, du mokuhlek easily nah-tor ik ik tor me prick abru t'nash-veh kaluk, na' wuh business has ri vesh' abru' rom na' ein tevun, heh wuh hayaik couple t' hundred would ma vesh' maut handy. "'var-tor me ek' pa' ish-veh, ' leralmin-tor i. "'muhl, ' leralmin-tor au, showing me wuh advertisement, 'du mokuhlek gla-tor na' yourself ik wuh league has wuh vacancy, heh tra' nam-tor wuh shi'yavekh wilat du dang apply na' particulars. U' irak u' i mokuhlek tor si', wuh league vesh' founded k' wuh american millionaire, ezekiah hopkins, vi vesh' maut peculiar svi' ish-veh yut. Au vesh' himself yon-kur-headed, heh au had wuh lo'uk sympathy na' ek' yon-kur-headed sasu; ni, lu au tev-tor, ish-veh vesh' afer-tor ik au had losrak ish-veh masuk' fortune svi' wuh el'ru t' trustees, k' instructions tor apply wuh eku'ko tor wuh providing t' hagik berths tor sasu t'vi isachya nam-tor t' ik kur. "'ri ni wehk u' du lau nah-tor, ' au kilko-tor. 'gla-tor du ish-veh nam-tor really confined tor londoners, heh tor grown sasu. Yi, va'ashiv, i ma puzhu-tor ish-veh nam-tor rai nam-tor-tor ish-veh applying kuv ish-veh isachya nam-tor ta'hal yon-kur, il gu'gelik yon-kur, il sovek-vel tonk'peh yeht ugelik, blazing, yonalik yon-kur. I', kuv du tun-tor tor apply, mr. "i', ish-veh nam-tor wuh kla-min, gentlemen, u' du lau gla-tor na' yourselves, ik t'nash-veh isachya nam-tor t' wuh maut bosh heh don-ka tint, ni ik ish-veh seemed tor me ik kuv tra' vesh' tor nam-tor sovek kuhlaya svi' wuh tukh i lam-tor u' rom wuh pavesh u' sovek sasu ik i had ek'wak ragel-tor. Uf au did ish-veh i kupi ri glenonau, tonk'peh au kwitau heh seshau heh butted abi' au prah me k'fai wuh patreitan, heh gas'rak abru tor wuh ash-tor if pufulag-tor tor wuh office. Tra' vesh' wuh dahtau pilash fi-tor wuh stair, ein going abru svi' rok, heh ein coming pla' dejected; tonk'peh etek wedged svi' u' muhl u' etek kupi heh ak afer-tor ourselves svi' wuh office." "ish-veh veshtaya has vesh' wuh danik entertaining veh, " remarked holmes u' ish-veh client svizh-tor heh uzhau ish-veh vokaya k' wuh masuk' k'hy t' snuff. "pray fator ish-veh maut eku'ki star-krus." "tra' vesh' nothing svi' wuh office tonk'peh wuh couple t' wooden ku-san heh wuh deal pasu, za' if hayal-tor wuh pi' sasu k' wuh patam ik vesh' kauk redder do t'nash-veh. Au leralmin-tor wuh zamu zhit tor tik candidate u' sarlah ish-veh abru, heh yi au kwon-hau-ov khartau tor talal ein lafot svi' au if would disqualify au. Getting wuh vacancy did ri seem tor nam-tor such wuh maut hagik tukh, po' ek'. However, lu etwel da-tor sarlah wuh pi' sasu vesh' mau weht favourable tor me do tor sovek t' wuh vath, heh au a'ing wuh svep u' etek svi-tor, ni ik au lau ma wuh awek zhit k' etek. "'nash nam-tor mr. Jabez wilson, ' leralmin-tor t'nash-veh assistant, 'heh au nam-tor willing tor boshaya wuh vacancy svi' wuh league.' "'heh au nam-tor admirably suited na' ish-veh, ' wuh vath kilko-tor. 'au has kanok requirement. I fam yehat recall lu ki'gla-tor nash-veh sovek-vel ni tok-ti.' au nem-tor wuh ash pla'rak, cocked ish-veh patam fi' veh vla, heh gazed na' t'nash-veh isachya abi' i olau ved fusik. Yi suddenly au taul-tor fa'rak, wrung t'nash-veh el'ru, heh congratulated me warmly fi' t'nash-veh navun. "'ish-veh would nam-tor injustice tor hesitate, ' leralmin-tor au. 'du dungi, however, i am sure, tobeg me na' taking wuh obvious precaution.' k' ik au seized t'nash-veh isachya svi' fi' ish-veh el'ru, heh seshau abi' i saul-tor k' wuh kusut. Ma du wuh skan?' "i kilko-tor ik i had ri. "ish-veh limuk tevan-tor iyi. "'tal-kam me!' au leralmin-tor gravely, 'ik nam-tor maut serious indeed! Ni'droi'ik nar-tor tor zhu-tor du leralmin ik. Wuh donketu-tor vesh', veling, na' wuh propagation heh sak-tor t' wuh yon-kur-patam u' muhl u' na' ish-veh rompotaya. Ish-veh nam-tor exceedingly unfortunate ik du dang nam-tor wuh bachelor.' "'svi' wuh nuf t' wuh'ashiv, ' leralmin-tor au, 'wuh objection lau nam-tor fatal, tonk'peh etek bolau sakadaya wuh sfek svi' favour t' wuh sasu k' such wuh patam t' isachya u' ish-veh. Wilson!' leralmin-tor vincent spaulding. 'i dang nam-tor kup tor glazhau po' ik na' du.' "'ra would nam-tor wuh wadan?' i ya'akash. "'lehkuh tor dahkuh.' "i' wuh pawnbroker's business nam-tor mostly ovsoh t' wuh khru, mr. "'nam-tor 4 wuh wehk gad.' "'heh wuh ar'kadan?' "'nam-tor purely nominal.' "'ra tor du vutau purely nominal?' "'muhl, du ma tor nam-tor svi' wuh office, il k'puu svi' wuh kelek, wuh bosh wak. "'ish-veh's goh kehkuh wadan wuh gad, heh i dang ri nah-tor t' leaving, ' leralmin-tor i. "'rai tobeg dungi avail, ' leralmin-tor mr. Duncan ross; 'neither has-mar il business il sovek-kitok. Du bolau talal ish-veh sha' neshuk, pens, heh blotting-dun, tonk'peh etek tanilau nash pasu heh ku-san. Dungi du nam-tor pok tor-morrow?' "'certainly, ' i kilko-tor. "'yi, rom-bye, mr. "muhl, i nahp abru' wuh tukh ek' gad, heh k' khru i vesh' svi' neik tam'a va'ashiv; na' i had ved persuaded myself ik wuh bosh tek'ik bolau nam-tor ein lo'uk tasadi il tehs, hi ra its vel lau nam-tor i kupi ri glenonau. Vincent spaulding did ra au kupi tor cheer me abru, tonk'peh k' bedtime i had reasoned myself s' wuh bosh vel. "muhl, tor t'nash-veh ak'wikmun heh delight, kanok-vei vesh' u' gas'rak u' tor-yehat. Wuh pasu vesh' eku si' pok na' me, heh mr. Duncan ross vesh' tra' tor gla-tor ik i prah fairly tor ar'kadan. Au palikau me ska' fi-tor wuh nuhm wuh, heh yi au losrak me; tonk'peh au would eku svi' s' wak tor wak tor gla-tor ik ek' vesh' gas'rak k' me. Na' dahkuh o'wak-vel au bade me rom-gad, complimented me fi-tor wuh nosahp ik i had written, heh klacha wuh svep t' wuh office po' me. "nash went fi' gad po' gad, mr. Holmes, heh fi' gad wuh khartausu sarlah svi' heh planked ne' kehkuh pi-maat-kur sovereigns na' t'nash-veh wehk gad's ar'kadan. Ish-veh vesh' wuh ka thurai wehk gad, heh wuh ka wuh wehk gad po'. Kanok asal i vesh' tra' na' lehkuh, heh kanok aru i losrak na' dahkuh. K' degrees mr. Duncan ross nem-tor tor coming svi' goh wuh'wak t' wuh asal, heh yi, po' wuh wak, au did ri sarlah svi' na' ek'. Fam dvun, veling, i worla dared tor trasha wuh tvi-shal na' wuh instant, na' i vesh' ri sure lu au lau sarlah, heh wuh billet vesh' such wuh rom veh, heh suited me ni muhl, ik i would ri risk wuh pak t' ish-veh. "ohkuh wehk gad be' dvun-tor maf spo' nash, heh i had written pa' abbots heh archery heh fo-wein heh te'koshif heh attica, heh rok-tor k' diligence ik i lau prah fi' tor wuh b's fa' maut wu. Ish-veh kodona me vel svi' foolscap, heh i had takov nearly boshau wuh nef k' t'nash-veh kitaun. Heh yi suddenly wuh bosh business sarlah tor wuh shaht." "tor wuh shaht?" "ha, osu. Heh rai later do nash asal. I went tor t'nash-veh ar'kadan u' tsuri na' lehkuh o'wak-vel, tonk'peh wuh svep vesh' ikap-tor heh klacha, k' wuh pi' keh-vla t' cardboard mah-tor fi' tor wuh svitan t' wuh gluvau-math k' wuh terp. La' ish-veh nam-tor, heh du mokuhlek telv-tor na' yourself." au meskarau abru wuh krus t' wan-kur cardboard pa' wuh suk'es t' wuh thalv t' pitoh-dun. October 9, 1890." sherlock holmes heh i skothon-tor nash curt announcement heh wuh rueful limuk za' ish-veh, abi' wuh comical vla t' wuh tek'ik ni completely overtopped kanok vath consideration ik etek fi' thorau si' vi' wuh roar t' laughter. "i fam yehat gla-tor ik tra' nam-tor sovek-vel maut funny, " maf-tor etwel client, flushing abru tor wuh gir t' ish-veh flaming patam. "kuv du mokuhlek tor nothing weh-rom do abru'teruklar-ru'lut na' me, i mokuhlek hal-tor kitok-wilat." "rai, rai, " maf-tor holmes, shoving ish-veh pla' vi' wuh ku-san s' if au had ulef risen. Pray ra ash-tor did du nem-tor lu du afer-tor wuh nop fi-tor wuh svep?" "i vesh' staggered, osu. I did ri fai-tor ra tor tor. Yi i puvutau na' wuh offices pauk, tonk'peh rim t' au seemed tor fai-tor sovek-vel pa' ish-veh. T'forti, i went tor wuh landlord, vi nam-tor wuh accountant living fi' wuh solektra lan-tol, heh i ya'akash ish-veh kuv au kupi var-tor me ra had shetau t' wuh yon-kur-headed league. Au leralmin-tor ik au had worla puzhu-tor t' sovek such ak'shem. Yi i ya'akash ish-veh vi mr. Duncan ross vesh'. Au kilko-tor ik wuh ahm vesh' uzh tor ish-veh. "'muhl, ' leralmin-tor i, 'wuh gentleman na' rai. 4.' "'ra, wuh yon-kur-headed sasu?' "'ha.' "'oh, ' leralmin-tor au, 'ish-veh ahm vesh' william morris. Au vesh' wuh solicitor heh vesh' using t'nash-veh tvi-shal u' wuh rikwonik convenience abi' ish-veh uzh premises vesh' pok. Au dvun-tor si' za-gad.' "'wilat sos talal ish-veh?' "'oh, na' ish-veh uzh offices. Au did var-tor me wuh shi'yavekh. Ha, 17 sa-te'kru edward yut, be' st. Paul's.' "i palikau ska', mr. Holmes, tonk'peh lu i prah tor ik shi'yavekh ish-veh vesh' wuh manufactory t' sutorik mal-nef-taik, heh kling svi' ish-veh had ek'wak puzhu-tor t' either mr. William morris il mr. Duncan ross." "heh ra did du tor yi?" ya'akash holmes. "i went ha-kel tor saxe-coburg keh-vla, heh i nem-tor wuh na'shikh t' t'nash-veh assistant. Tonk'peh au kupi ri gol'nev me svi' sovek yut. Au kupi goh leralmin ik kuv i bek-tor i dang zhu-tor k' lehk. Tonk'peh ik vesh' ri ved rom hiyet, mr. Holmes. I did ri istaya tor pak-tor such wuh shi rik' wuh struggle, ni, u' i had puzhu-tor ik du vesh' rom hiyet tor mazhiv-kur-tor na'shikh tor ri donku-tor sular vi vesh' svi' bolaya t' ish-veh, vesht sarlah nash-veh gas'rak maf tor du." "heh du did maut wisely, " leralmin-tor holmes. "ish-veh nuf nam-tor wuh exceedingly remarkable veh, heh i dungau nam-tor kunli tor glazhau vi' ish-veh. "po, i ma pakik kehkuh plesh-tor wuh wehk gad." "u' irak u' du nam-tor personally concerned, " remarked holmes, "i ri tor gla-tor ik du ma sovek grievance tehnat nash wehtsuri league. "rai, osu. Tonk'peh i aitlun tor talal si' pa' au, heh vi au nam-tor, heh ra ish-veh vel vesh' svi' mavaun nash prankif ish-veh vesh' wuh prankupon me. Ish-veh vesh' wuh takov kodonuhk kha'wal na' au, na' ish-veh kodona au dahkuh heh reh-leh plesh-tor." "etek dungau endeavour tor pa'shik abru aifa sfekau na' du. Heh, wuh'rak, veh il dahkuh deshkau, mr. Wilson. Nash assistant t' ish-veh vi wuh'rak puvutau ish-veh attention tor wuh advertisementhow wu had au vesh' k' du?" "pa' wuh tevun-krus yi." "na' ulef wages, svi' kla-min." "ha." "ra nam-tor au spo', nash vincent spaulding?" "pi', stout-torvau, maut sahris svi' ish-veh yut, rai isachya fi' ish-veh limuk, hi au's ri pen t' reh-leh. Has wuh wan-kur splash t' sash fi-tor ish-veh fa-patam." holmes hayal-tor abru svi' ish-veh ku-san svi' considerable tepor'es. "i nahp u' mau, " leralmin-tor au. Tonk'peh i bolau nam-tor prompt abru' nash tukh." "ra nam-tor du going tor tor, yi?" i ya'akash. "tor vuzh, " au kilko-tor. "ish-veh nam-tor ved wuh rehkuh mev wat, heh i eit'jae ik du skil-tor't stariben tor me na' kau-leh minutes." au tcha-tor himself abru svi' ish-veh ku-san, k' ish-veh wonil mal-nef drawn abru tor ish-veh hawk-spo' han, heh tra' au hayal-tor k' ish-veh bezhun a'ing heh ish-veh nesh-kur krizhiv mev thrusting si' spo' wuh dun t' ein flekh kushel. Ish-veh vesh' wuh poky, pi', shabby-genteel shi, wilat kehkuh zehl t' dingy dahkuh-storied dok kelek glazhau si' vi' wuh pi' railed-svi' enclosure, wilat wuh yartra t' weedy yar heh wuh zamu clumps t' spoh-tor laurel bushes tor wuh lerash puk tehnat wuh vuzh-laden heh uncongenial igen-tukh. Sherlock holmes pehkau svi' khom t' ish-veh k' ish-veh patam fi' veh vla heh glazhau ish-veh ek' abru', k' ish-veh bezhun shining brightly svi' puckered lids. "po did du kuhsh-tor wuh pavement?" "t'nash-veh tal-kam hassu, nash nam-tor wuh wak na' glantaya, ri na' variben. Etek nam-tor zamasu svi' wuh nemut's shasol. Etek fai-tor vel t' saxe-coburg keh-vla. Kal-tor etek i' explore wuh krus if ti za' ish-veh." wuh fau-yut svi' if etek afer-tor ourselves u' etek da-tor pauk wuh teruk s' wuh retired saxe-coburg keh-vla presented u' lo'uk wuh contrast tor ish-veh u' wuh khom t' wuh bikuv tor tor wuh pla'. Ish-veh vesh' veh t' wuh nen uzh-khaf-mev if zhelesh wuh traffic t' wuh kahr tor wuh desh'rak heh tev'rak. Wuh roadway vesh' klotau k' wuh immense pilash t' commerce flowing svi' wuh dahtau mashen inward heh outward, du' wuh lates-yut vesh' nesh-kur k' wuh hurrying bish t' pedestrians. Tra' nam-tor mortimer's, wuh tobacconist, wuh pi' newspaper mahr-kel, wuh coburg khlup t' wuh kahr heh suburban kutra, wuh kastik-goh-yokulsu restaurant, heh mcfarlane's carriage-kelek depot. Ik lesh etek gas'rak fi' tor wuh vath vihpan. Heh i', hassu, etek've ovsoh etwel ar'kadan, ni ish-veh's wak etek had ein mavau. Wuh sandwich heh wuh cup t' mon, heh yi ska' tor violin-solektra, wilat ek' nam-tor sweetness heh delicacy heh kril'es, heh tra' nam-tor rai yon-kur-headed clients tor smertau etek k' ish-veh conundrums." t'nash-veh t'hy'la vesh' wuh buhlik ralash-tanafsu, hasu himself ri goh wuh maut capable performer tonk'peh wuh tertitayek t' rai ordinary merit. Ek' wuh aru au hayal-tor svi' wuh stalls wrapped svi' wuh danik buhfik happiness, kogavik pral-tor ish-veh wu, wonil ozh svi' wak tor wuh ralash-tanaf, du' ish-veh kogavik smiling limuk heh ish-veh languid, dreamy bezhun vesh' u' rikes eifa t' holmes wuh sleuth-hound, holmes wuh relentless, keen-witted, pok-handed criminal agent, u' ish-veh vesh' tor-yehat tor conceive. Svi' ish-veh singular character wuh dual malat alternately asserted itself, heh ish-veh mairik exactness heh astuteness represented, u' i ma k'ashiv nahp, wuh rolaya tehnat wuh poetic heh contemplative mood if occasionally predominated svi' ish-veh. Wuh swing t' ish-veh malat nem-tor ish-veh s' mairik languor tor devouring tepul; heh, u' i fai-tor muhl, au vesh' worla ni truly formidable u' lu, na' gad fi' shaht, au had vesh' lounging svi' ish-veh armchair svi' ish-veh improvisations heh ish-veh nesh-kur-nuhm yadan. Yi ish-veh vesh' ik wuh lust t' wuh a'vesh' would suddenly sarlah fi-tor ish-veh, heh ik ish-veh maut-ugelik reasoning tepul would shen tor wuh volik t' intuition, abi' eifa vi vesh' unacquainted k' ish-veh methods would glazhau askance na' ish-veh u' fi' wuh sasu t'vi fai-tukh vesh' ri ik t' vath mortals. Lu vesht gla-tor nash-veh ish-veh ik aru ni enwrapped svi' wuh ralash-tanaf na' st. James's tvur i olau ik wuh ek'rasah wak lau nam-tor coming fi-tor eifa ik au had eku himself tor shi'kar ne'. "du aitlun tor hal-tor ha-kel, rai vet, hassu, " au remarked u' etek sasarlah. "ha, ish-veh would nam-tor u' muhl." "heh i ma ein business tor tor if dungi nem-tor ein wadan. I ma kanok utvau tor dva-tor ik etek dungau nam-tor svi' wak tor pehkaya ish-veh. Tonk'peh tor-gad hasu gad rather complicates tukh. I dungau aitlun ish-veh gol'nev tor-mu-yor." "na' ra wak?" "lehkuh dungi nam-tor lehkuh-mal hiyet." "i dungau nam-tor na' leipausu yut na' lehkuh." "maut muhl. Ek' au aitlu nam-tor wuh hinek dog tor gol'nev ish-veh tor tor wuh sahran ne'." "i rok wuh kwai kushel lau ri skan-tor tor nam-tor wuh shaht t' etwel a'vesh', " glantau mr. Merryweather gloomily. Merryweather, wuh stake dungi nam-tor ein 30,000; heh na' du, jones, ish-veh dungi nam-tor wuh sasu fi-tor ik du istaya tor ti ish-veh el'ru." "john krizhiv, wuh murderer, pi'tak, smasher, heh forger. Au's wuh nu'ri sasu, mr. Merryweather, tonk'peh au nam-tor na' wuh patam t' ish-veh ha'yigal, heh i would rather ma t'nash-veh kar-nik-zhel fi' ish-veh do fi' sovek criminal svi' london. Etek had occasion ein tevun-krus ago tor karik-tor etwel resources heh yahv-tor na' ik lof 30,000 napoleons s' wuh kutra t' france. Ish-veh has shetau fainu ik etek ma worla had occasion tor unpack wuh donku, heh ik ish-veh nam-tor fam dvun lying svi' etwel cellar. Wuh'wak goh had i fainu ish-veh tor vravshau, svi' wuh nuf t' wuh sa-te'kru t' bohemia heh t' wuh irene adler ha'gel-bikuv; tonk'peh lu i glazhau pla' tor wuh flekh business t' wuh glat t' kehkuh, heh wuh wehtsuri circumstances tersau k' wuh orenau svi' ug'yon-kur, i olau ik ish-veh would nam-tor wuh flekh tangle indeed if au kupi ri unravel. I losrak ish-veh yi, fam dvun puffing na' ish-veh nesh-kur krizhiv mev, k' wuh conviction ik lu vesht sarlah nash-veh va'ashiv fi' wuh thurai khru i would talal ik au meskarau svi' ish-veh el'ru ek' wuh clues if would ras-tukh abru tor wuh sha'es t' wuh disappearing bridegroom t' din-tor mary sutherland. Wuh professional nuf t' lo'uk ne-seshan vesh' engaging t'nash-veh sha' attention na' wuh wak, heh wuh bosh t' thurai gad i vesh' toranik na' wuh bedside t' wuh sufferer. Ish-veh vesh' ri abi' ikap-tor fi-tor shehkuh o'wak-vel ik i afer-tor myself elik heh vesh' kup tor sikar vi' wuh hansom heh yetur tor leipausu yut, ulef kwes ik i lau nam-tor nuh' tab-ma tor gol-tor na' wuh dénouement t' wuh pi' mystery. I afer-tor sherlock holmes sa'awek, however, ulef asleep, k' ish-veh wu, wonil shid tcha-tor abru svi' wuh sha'ti t' ish-veh armchair. "muhl, ma du kilau ish-veh?" i ya'akash u' i svi-tor. "ha. Ish-veh vesh' wuh bisulphate t' baryta." "rai, rai, wuh mystery!" i maf-tor. "oh, ik! I nahp t' wuh alem ik i ma vesh' working fi-tor. Tra' vesh' worla sovek mystery svi' wuh tukh, hi, u' i leralmin-tor za-gad, ein t' wuh details nam-tor t' eku'ko. Wuh goh drawback nam-tor ik tra' nam-tor rai tor-gav, i pthak, ik mokuhlek esta wuh scoundrel." I am kwes ik i am wuh pi' tab-ma, tonk'peh i am ri ved t'nash-veh sha' trensu, du fai-tor. I dungau nem-tor nothing na' vahl abi' i ma wuh opportunity t' looking personally vi' ish-veh. I dungi danau wuh fupa s' t' vel tor du, u' irak u' i ma vesh' kup tor ken-tor ish-veh, svi' wuh maut zamu zhit. "boscombe ku-li nam-tor wuh shasol kahkrus ri maut irak s' ross, svi' herefordshire. Wuh largest landed proprietor svi' ik krus nam-tor wuh mr. John turner, vi tor ish-veh donku svi' australia heh fun-tor ein tevun ago tor wuh hinek shasol.
