Mccarthy potau dahkuh servantsa sasu heh wuh ko-kan. Turner had wuh considerable household, ein ulef-dozen na' wuh least. Ik nam-tor u' mau u' i ma vesh' kup tor hoknau pa' wuh skan. I' na' wuh kla-min. "fi' belaar 3rd, ik nam-tor, fi' gad kim-shah, mccarthy losrak ish-veh kelek na' hatherley pa' rehkuh svi' wuh aru heh lates-tor ne' tor wuh boscombe patra, if nam-tor wuh pi' suk'muzh shidau k' wuh spreading s' wuh pilash if sahr-tor ne' wuh boscombe ku-li. Au had vesh' si' k' ish-veh serving-sasu svi' wuh asal na' ross, heh au had var-tor wuh sasu ik au bolau brax, u' au had wuh latva t' importance tor potau na' rehkuh. S' ik latva au worla sarlah pla' alive. "s' hatherley uroshal-kelek tor wuh boscombe patra nam-tor wuh yonuk t' wuh mile, heh dahkuh sutra gla-tor ish-veh u' au be' dvun-tor abru' nash solektra. Veh vesh' wuh hinek kosu, t'vi ahm nam-tor ri mentioned, heh wuh vath vesh' william crowder, wuh zhagra-keeper svi' wuh employ t' mr. Turner. Fi' aifa toglantausu depose ik mr. Mccarthy vesh' walking sa'awek. Wuh zhagra-keeper hau ik k'svi wuh zamu minutes t' ish-veh seeing mr. Mccarthy be' dvun au had gla-tor ish-veh sa-fu, mr. James mccarthy, going wuh ka yut k' wuh pohshayek ne' ish-veh kar. Tor wuh buhfik t' ish-veh dva, wuh sa-mekh vesh' actually svi' glan na' wuh wak, heh wuh sa-fu vesh' zahalik ish-veh. Au nahp rai weht t' wuh tukh abi' au puzhu-tor svi' wuh khru t' wuh tragedy ik had paresh-tor. "wuh dahkuh mccarthys vesh' gla-tor po' wuh wak lu william crowder, wuh zhagra-keeper, pakik glan t' au. Wuh boscombe patra nam-tor bali wooded pauk, k' aishan wuh geldel t' yar heh t' reeds pauk wuh rihk. Wuh ko-kan t' leh-keh, tranush moran, vi nam-tor wuh ko-fu t' wuh lodge-keeper t' wuh boscombe ku-li estate, vesh' svi' veh t' wuh lapan picking svai. She fupa s' ik du' she vesh' tra' gla-tor ish-veh, na' wuh ek'zehl t' wuh lapan heh beyik wuh suk'muzh, mr. Mccarthy heh ish-veh sa-fu, heh ik au saudau tor nam-tor having wuh khrashik quarrel. She puzhu-tor mr. Mccarthy wuh tela'at using maut karik gen-lis tor ish-veh sa-fu, heh gla-tor ish-veh wuh latter ashenau abru ish-veh el'ru u' kuv tor kwul ish-veh sa-mekh. She vesh' ni koltha k' ish-veh khrash ik she sahr-tor maf heh var-tor ish-veh ko-mekh lu she pulau ha-kel ik she had losrak wuh dahkuh mccarthys quarrelling be' boscombe patra, heh ik she vesh' kwes ik au vesh' going tor puk. She had hardly leralmin-tor wuh zhit lu nu'ri mr. Mccarthy sarlah sahran abru tor wuh lodge tor leralmin ik au had afer-tor ish-veh sa-mekh tevik svi' wuh lapan, heh tor ya'akash na' wuh gol'nev t' wuh lodge-keeper. Au vesh' mau teporilau, rik' either ish-veh pohshayek il ish-veh taik, heh ish-veh gas'rak el'ru heh sleeve vesh' glantau tor nam-tor kurau k' sluk khaf. Fi' zahalik ish-veh au afer-tor wuh tevik ak'shem sakadau si' fi-tor wuh yar be' wuh patra. Wuh patam had vesh' beaten svi' k' ashiv-tor salur t' ein ras heh pasik wun. Wuh dash vesh' such u' lau maut muhl ma vesh' inflicted k' wuh butt-shaht t' ish-veh sa-fu's pohshayek, if vesh' afer-tor lying fi' wuh yar k'svi wuh zamu sahr-tor t' wuh ak'shem. Ne' aifa circumstances wuh nu'ri sasu vesh' instantly pehkau, heh wuh verdict t' 'wilful riyeht-staya' having vesh' fun-tor na' wuh inquest fi' gad, au vesh' fi' gad katau fa' wuh magistrates na' ross, vi ma referred wuh nuf tor wuh thurai assizes. Eifa nam-tor wuh nen kla-min t' wuh nuf u' au sasarlah fa' wuh tevanu-talsu heh wuh police-kelek." "i kupi hardly glenonau wuh weht damning nuf, " i remarked. "kuv ek'wak circumstantial evidence sfekau tor wuh criminal ish-veh tor ni la'." "circumstantial evidence nam-tor wuh maut tricky vel, " kilko-tor holmes thoughtfully. "ish-veh lau seem tor sfek maut zehik tor veh vel, tonk'peh kuv du izaya ish-veh sha' sfek t' zan-tor wuh pi', du lau talal ish-veh pointing svi' wuh kaing uncompromising manner tor vel entirely natya. Ish-veh bolau nam-tor confessed, however, ik wuh nuf glazhau exceedingly shi'vukhut tehnat wuh nu'ri sasu, heh ish-veh nam-tor maut tor-yehat ik au nam-tor indeed wuh culprit. Tra' nam-tor several sutra svi' wuh neighbourhood, however, heh ekhlami din-tor turner, wuh ko-fu t' wuh neighbouring landowner, vi dva-tor svi' ish-veh innocence, heh vi ma retained lestrade, ik du lau recollect svi' tersaya k' wuh orenau svi' ug'yon-kur, tor ar'kadan si' wuh nuf svi' ish-veh eku'ko. Lestrade, hasu rather puzzled, has referred wuh nuf tor me, heh hence ish-veh nam-tor ik dahkuh svitan-aged gentlemen nam-tor hashan na'tev'rak na' kau-leh miles wuh wadan instead t' quietly digesting ish-veh asal-yem na' ha-kel." "i am kwes, " leralmin-tor i, "ik wuh kla-min nam-tor ni obvious ik du dungi talal pi' lit tor nam-tor nazh-tor s' nash nuf." "tra' nam-tor nothing weht deceptive do wuh obvious kla-min, " au kilko-tor, laughing. "isha, etek lau pavesh tor kwul fi-tor ein vath obvious kla-min if lau ma vesh' k' rai tvai obvious tor mr. Lestrade. Du fai-tor me nuh' muhl tor nah-tor ik i am boasting lu i leralmin ik i dungau either wugau il vashau ish-veh wihka k' tvai if au nam-tor ved incapable t' employing, il kauk t' understanding. Tor nem-tor wuh wuh'rak li-fal tor el'ru, i maut clearly pakashogau ik svi' ish-veh shi'yuk wuh krani nam-tor fi-tor wuh gas'rak-el'ru vla, heh wi i deshker whether mr. Lestrade would ma noted kauk ni shal-evident wuh vel u' ik." "uf fi' terra" "t'nash-veh tal-kam katravahsu, i fai-tor du muhl. I fai-tor wuh askital neatness if characterises du. Du hohl-tor kanok asal, heh svi' nash tevun-yonuk du hohl-tor k' wuh ug'yel-ha'gel; tonk'peh opi' ish-veh shaving nam-tor lehkuh heh lehkuh ovsotik u' etek prah weh-irak pla' fi' wuh losrak vla, abi' ish-veh shetau positively slovenly u' etek prah pauk wuh vulu t' wuh ahs, ish-veh nam-tor surely maut pa'shik ik ik vla nam-tor lehkuh illuminated do wuh vath. I kupi ri glenonau wuh sasu t' ish-veh es'merka looking na' himself svi' wuh kaik ta'hal heh hasu satisfied k' such wuh result. I goh quote nash u' wuh trivial li-fal t' glantaya heh inference. Therein ti t'nash-veh métier, heh ish-veh nam-tor aishan tor-yehat ik ish-veh lau nam-tor t' ein dvin svi' wuh investigation if ti fa' etek. Tra' nam-tor veh il dahkuh minor sfekau if vesh' katau si' svi' wuh inquest, heh if nam-tor don panahik." "ra nam-tor au?" "ish-veh saudau ik ish-veh pehkaya did ri nem-tor shi na' wuh'wak, tonk'peh po' wuh fun tor hatherley uroshal. Fi' wuh inspector t' constabulary informing ish-veh ik au vesh' wuh prisoner, au remarked ik au vesh' ri ak'wikmun tor zhu-tor ish-veh, heh ik ish-veh vesh' rai weht do ish-veh eshikh. Nash glantaya t' ish-veh had wuh malatik daya t' removing sovek zavikau t' vet if lau ma hafau svi' wuh kashkau t' wuh tevanu-talsu's jury." "ish-veh vesh' wuh confession, " i khrasau. "rai, na' ish-veh vesh' zahal-tor k' wuh protestation t' innocence." "coming fi' wuh fik t' such wuh damning weizehl t' pavek, ish-veh vesh' k'puu wuh danik suspicious remark." "fi' wuh contrary, " leralmin-tor holmes, "ish-veh nam-tor wuh brightest rift if i mokuhlek na' la' gla-tor svi' wuh wan. However innocent au lau nam-tor, au kupi ri nam-tor such wuh ek'esik imbecile u' ri tor gla-tor ik wuh circumstances vesh' maut nesh-kur tehnat ish-veh. Had au saudau ak'wikmun na' ish-veh sha' pehkaya, il vup-tor indignation na' ish-veh, i dang ma glazhau fi-tor ish-veh u' highly suspicious, fai'ei such ak'wikmun il reshan would ri nam-tor malatik ne' wuh circumstances, heh wi lau saudau tor nam-tor wuh buhfik policy tor wuh scheming sasu. Ish-veh frank acceptance t' wuh situation ulidar ish-veh u' either wuh innocent sasu, il else u' wuh sasu t' considerable shal-restraint heh firmness. U' tor ish-veh remark pa' ish-veh eshikh, ish-veh vesh' isha ri unnatural kuv du panah-tor ik au lam-tor be' wuh tevik ak'shem t' ish-veh sa-mekh, heh ik tra' nam-tor rai vet ik au had ik maut gad ni irak yen-tor ish-veh filial gu-vam u' tor bandy zhit k' ish-veh, heh kauk, fupa s' wuh pi' ko-kan t'vi evidence nam-tor ni yauluhk, tor ashenau ish-veh el'ru u' kuv tor kwul ish-veh. Wuh shal-reproach heh contrition if nam-tor gluvaya svi' ish-veh remark saudau tor me tor nam-tor wuh glat t' wuh muhl-bosh kashek rather do t' wuh guilty veh." i hutau t'nash-veh patam. "wehk sasu ma vesh' geldau fi' irak slighter evidence, " i remarked. "ni au ma. Heh wehk sasu ma vesh' wrongfully geldau." "ra nam-tor wuh nu'ri sasu's sha' khrosahp t' wuh tukh?" "ish-veh nam-tor, i am kwes, ri maut encouraging tor ish-veh supporters, hi tra' nam-tor veh il dahkuh sfekau svi' ish-veh if nam-tor suggestive. Du dungi talal ish-veh la', heh lau telv-tor ish-veh na' yourself." au picked si' s' ish-veh uzh'a'lek wuh va'asau t' wuh local herefordshire dun, heh having da-tor ne' wuh thalv au sasfekau wuh paragraph svi' if wuh unfortunate nu'ri sasu had putan-tor ish-veh sha' star-krus t' ra had paresh-tor. I settled myself ne' svi' wuh teruk t' wuh carriage heh telv-tor ish-veh maut carefully. Ish-veh sahr-tor svi' nash yut: "mr. James mccarthy, wuh goh sa-fu t' wuh tevik, vesh' yi puvutau heh mazhiv-kur-tor evidence u' zahal-tor: 'i had vesh' maf s' ha-kel na' rehkuh gad na' bristol, heh had goh aishan fun-tor fi-tor wuh asal t' kim-shah gad, wuh 3rd. T'nash-veh sa-mekh vesh' tadek-adir s' ha-kel na' wuh wak t' t'nash-veh lashan, heh i vesh' informed k' wuh maid ik au had driven abru' tor ross k' john cobb, wuh groom. Shortly po' t'nash-veh fun i puzhu-tor wuh halek t' ish-veh pash svi' wuh ker, heh, looking s' t'nash-veh krani, vesht gla-tor nash-veh ish-veh prah si' heh lates rapidly s' wuh ker, hi i vesh' ri aware svi' if kharat au vesh' going. I yi nem-tor t'nash-veh pohshayek heh strolled si' svi' wuh kharat t' wuh boscombe patra, k' wuh intention t' visiting wuh rabbit warren if nam-tor fi-tor wuh vath vla. Fi' t'nash-veh yut vesht gla-tor nash-veh william crowder, wuh zhagra-keeper, u' au had fupa s' svi' ish-veh evidence; tonk'peh au nam-tor mistaken svi' thinking ik i vesh' zahalik t'nash-veh sa-mekh. I had rai idea ik au vesh' svi' khom t' me. Lu pa' wuh hundred ker s' wuh patra i puzhu-tor wuh maf t' "cooee!" if vesh' wuh tsuri glantokaya svi' t'nash-veh sa-mekh heh myself. I yi hurried fa'rak, heh afer-tor ish-veh standing k' wuh patra. Au saudau tor nam-tor mau ak'wikmun na' seeing me heh ya'akash me rather roughly ra i vesh' doing tra'. Wuh conversation ensued if pufulag-tor tor pid zhit heh siyah tor salur, na' t'nash-veh sa-mekh vesh' wuh sasu t' wuh maut khrashik temper. Seeing ik ish-veh shaukaush vesh' becoming ungovernable, i losrak ish-veh heh fun-tor na' hatherley uroshal. I had ri hal-tor weht do 150 ker, however, lu i puzhu-tor wuh hideous outcry za' me, if aisha me tor sahr-tor pla' va'ashiv. I afer-tor t'nash-veh sa-mekh expiring fi-tor wuh solektra, k' ish-veh patam terribly dash-tor. I eku-tor t'nash-veh pohshayek heh meskarau ish-veh svi' t'nash-veh kar, tonk'peh au siyah instantly yausha. I knelt be' ish-veh na' ein minutes, heh yi tor t'nash-veh yut tor mr. Turner's lodge-keeper, ish-veh kelek hasu wuh nearest, tor ya'akash na' assistance. Vesht gla-tor nash-veh kling be' t'nash-veh sa-mekh lu i fun-tor, heh i ma rai idea uf sarlah ish-veh k' ish-veh dash. Au vesh' ri wuh popular sasu, hasu somewhat samu heh forbidding svi' ish-veh manners, tonk'peh au had, u' irak u' i fai-tor, rai torupik nemut. I fai-tor nothing further t' wuh tukh.' "wuh tevanu-talsu: did ish-veh sa-mekh tor sovek star-krus tor du fa' au tev-tor? "toglantausu: au mumbled wuh zamu zhit, tonk'peh i kupi goh kum ein allusion tor wuh rat. "wuh tevanu-talsu: ra did du ken-tor k' ik? "toglantausu: ish-veh zhelesh rai meaning tor me. I nahp ik au vesh' delirious. "wuh tevanu-talsu: ra vesh' wuh sfek fi-tor if du heh ish-veh sa-mekh had nash kim-shah quarrel? "toglantausu: i dang prefer ri tor kilko-srashiv. "wuh tevanu-talsu: i am kwes ik i bolau hish-tor ish-veh. "toglantausu: ish-veh nam-tor really impossible na' me tor var-tor du. I mokuhlek assure du ik ish-veh has nothing tor tor k' wuh maf tragedy if zahal-tor. "wuh tevanu-talsu: ik nam-tor na' wuh kelek tor klopau. I bolaya ri sasfekau tor du ik ish-veh refusal tor kilko-srashiv dungi prejudice ish-veh nuf considerably svi' sovek fa-wak proceedings if lau arise. "toglantausu: i bolau fam dvun klee'fah. "wuh tevanu-talsu: i ken-tor ik wuh maf t' 'cooee' vesh' wuh tsuri glantokaya svi' du heh ish-veh sa-mekh? "toglantausu: ish-veh vesh'. "wuh tevanu-talsu: uf vesh' ish-veh, yi, ik au uttered ish-veh fa' gla-tor ish-veh du, heh fa' au kauk fai-tor ik du had fun-tor s' bristol? "toglantausu (k' considerable confusion): i ri tor fai-tor. "wuh juryman: did gla-tor du nothing if aroused ish-veh suspicions lu du fun-tor fi' khaf-spol wuh maf heh afer-tor ish-veh sa-mekh fatally dash-tor? "toglantausu: nothing definite. "wuh tevanu-talsu: ra tor du tvai? "toglantausu: i vesh' ni ertau heh teporilau u' i rushed si' vi' wuh tu'ash, ik i kupi nah-tor t' nothing kaula t' t'nash-veh sa-mekh. Wi i ma wuh vague impression ik u' i sahr-tor fa'rak vel ti fi-tor wuh solektra tor wuh losrak t' me. Ish-veh seemed tor me tor nam-tor vel zhai-kur svi' kur, wuh tor-pal t' ein wihfelau, il wuh plaid sos'eh. Lu i she-tor s' t'nash-veh sa-mekh i glazhau pauk na' ish-veh, tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' hal-tor. "'tor du tvai ik ish-veh sasaudau fa' du went na' gol'nev?' "'ha, ish-veh vesh' hal-tor.' "'du fam yehat leralmin ra ish-veh vesh'?' "'rai, i had wuh olaya vel vesh' tra'.' "'uf irak s' wuh ak'shem?' "'wuh dozen ker il ni.' "'heh uf irak s' wuh rihk t' wuh lapan?' "'pa' wuh ka.' "'yi kuv ish-veh vesh' snem-tor ish-veh vesh' du' du vesh' k'svi wuh dozen ker t' ish-veh?' "'ha, tonk'peh k' t'nash-veh pla' na' ish-veh.' "nash concluded wuh linisaya t' wuh toglantausu." "gla-tor nash-veh, " leralmin-tor i u' i glanced ne' wuh tsek, "ik wuh tevanu-talsu svi' ish-veh concluding remarks vesh' rather severe fi-tor nu'ri mccarthy. Au calls attention, heh k' utvau, tor wuh discrepancy pa' ish-veh sa-mekh having signalled tor ish-veh fa' seeing ish-veh, isha tor ish-veh refusal tor mazhiv-kur-tor details t' ish-veh conversation k' ish-veh sa-mekh, heh ish-veh singular khrosahp t' ish-veh sa-mekh's dying zhit. Au nam-tor ek', u' au remarks, maut mau tehnat wuh sa-fu." holmes abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor softly tor himself heh sakadau himself si' fi-tor wuh cushioned ku-san. "fi' du heh wuh tevanu-talsu ma vesh' na' ein kusut-tor, " leralmin-tor au, "tor single si' wuh maut strongest sfekau svi' wuh nu'ri sasu's favour. Ri tor gla-tor du ik du alternately mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh lit na' having nuh' mau glenonaya heh nuh' pi'? Nuh' pi', kuv au kupi ri fereik-tor wuh aishan t' quarrel if would mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh sympathy t' wuh jury; nuh' mau, kuv au wakrubau s' ish-veh sha' tvik hokni'es sovek-vel ni outré u' wuh dying dzhinaya tor wuh rat, heh wuh incident t' wuh vanishing sai. Rai, osu, i dungau betaya nash nuf s' wuh sfek t' zan-tor ik ra nash nu'ri sasu leralmin-tor nam-tor yeht, heh etek dungau gla-tor whither ik ul-wihka dungi ras-tukh etek. Heh i' la' nam-tor t'nash-veh abru'lik petrarch, heh ri wuh'ashiv zhit dungau i leralmin t' nash nuf abi' etek nam-tor fi' wuh scene t' torai. Etek khi-gad-yem na' swindon, heh gla-tor nash-veh ik etek dungau nam-tor tra' svi' dah-leh minutes." ish-veh vesh' nearly kehkuh o'wak-vel lu etek na' kim-shah, po' be' dvun-tor k'fai wuh vaksurik stroud ku-li, heh abru' wuh sax'ksei gleaming severn, afer-tor ourselves na' wuh takov pi' shasol-kahr t' ross. Wuh galat, ferret-spo' sasu, furtive heh sly-looking, vesh' waiting na' etek fi-tor wuh skaf. Svi' spite t' wuh ta'hal khav-kur dustcoat heh duf-leggings if au sai-vel-tor svi' deference tor ish-veh rustic surroundings, i had rai rihag'es svi' recognising lestrade, t' scotland ker. K' ish-veh etek drove tor wuh hereford kar wilat wuh tvi-shal had already vesh' engaged na' etek. "i ma ordered wuh carriage, " leralmin-tor lestrade u' etek hayal-tor abru' wuh cup t' theris-masu. "i fai-tor ish-veh energetic malat, heh ik du would ri nam-tor kunli abi' du had vesh' fi' wuh scene t' wuh tr'y'kak." "ish-veh vesh' maut nice heh complimentary t' du, " holmes kilko-tor. "ish-veh nam-tor entirely wuh deshker t' barometric ne'hish." lestrade glazhau startled. "i ri tor ved zahal-tor, " au leralmin-tor. "uf nam-tor wuh makh? Dah-leh-naukuh, gla-tor nash-veh. Rai salan, heh ri wuh wan svi' wuh igen. I ma wuh caseful t' cigarettes la' if bolaya smoking, heh wuh ku-san nam-tor maut mau superior tor wuh tsuri shasol hotel abomination. I tor ri nah-tor ik ish-veh nam-tor yesik ik i dungau nam-tor-tor wuh carriage tor-mu-yor." lestrade abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor indulgently. "du ma, rai vet, already shidau ish-veh conclusions s' wuh newspapers, " au leralmin-tor. "wuh nuf nam-tor u' eiktra u' wuh pikestaff, heh wuh weht veh hal-tor vi' ish-veh wuh plainer ish-veh shetau. Fam dvun, veling, veh mokuhlek't klee'fah wuh t'sai, heh such wuh maut a'rak veh, nuh'. She has puzhu-tor t' du, heh would ma ish-veh opinion, hi i repeatedly var-tor ish-veh ik tra' vesh' nothing if du kupi tor if i had ri already ovsoh. Po, kudau t'nash-veh soul! La' nam-tor ish-veh carriage na' wuh svep." au had hardly spoken fa' tra' rushed vi' wuh tvi-shal veh t' wuh danik lovely nu'ri kosu ik i ma ek'wak gla-tor svi' t'nash-veh ha'kiv. Ish-veh mu'gahv-kur bezhun shining, ish-veh bru-lar parted, wuh faf-kur kluhvau fi-tor ish-veh nak, ek' nahp t' ish-veh malatik reserve pakik svi' ish-veh overpowering tepor'es heh concern. "oh, mr. Sherlock holmes!" she maf-tor, glancing s' veh tor wuh vath t' etek, heh t'forti, k' wuh kosu's sahris intuition, fastening fi-tor t'nash-veh besu, "i am ni glad ik du ma sarlah. I ma driven ne' tor var-tor du ni. I fai-tor ik james didn't tor ish-veh. I fai-tor ish-veh, heh i aitlun du tor palikaya fi-tor ish-veh ar'kadan fai-tor ish-veh, nuh'. Worla kal-tor yourself vet fi-tor ik sfek. Etek ma fainu tik vath opi' etek vesh' pi' kanu, heh i fai-tor ish-veh lafot u' kling else tor; tonk'peh au nam-tor nuh' sival-hearted tor dash-tor wuh hash-tor. Such wuh falun nam-tor absurd tor sovek-veh vi really fai-tor ish-veh." "i rok etek lau pa'shik ish-veh, din-tor turner, " leralmin-tor sherlock holmes. "du lau rely fi-tor t'nash-veh doing ek' ik i mokuhlek." "tonk'peh du ma telv-tor wuh evidence. Du ma shidau ein conclusion? Tor du ri gla-tor ein loophole, ein lafot? Tor du ri yourself nah-tor ik au nam-tor innocent?" "i nah-tor ik ish-veh nam-tor maut yesik." "tra', i'!" she maf-tor, throwing pla' ish-veh patam heh looking defiantly na' lestrade. "du zhu-tor! Au mazhiv-kur-tor me rok-tor." lestrade shrugged ish-veh tipan. "i am kwes ik t'nash-veh kazhuksu has vesh' wuh pi' sahris svi' forming ish-veh conclusions, " au leralmin-tor. "tonk'peh au nam-tor gas'rak. Oh! I fai-tor ik au nam-tor gas'rak. James worla did ish-veh. Heh pa' ish-veh quarrel k' ish-veh sa-mekh, i am sure ik wuh utvau po au would ri stariben pa' ish-veh tor wuh tevanu-talsu vesh' fai'ei i vesh' concerned svi' ish-veh." "svi' ra yut?" ya'akash holmes. "ish-veh nam-tor rai wak na' me tor ip-sut sovek-vel. James heh ish-veh sa-mekh had wehk disagreements pa' me. Mr. Mccarthy vesh' maut anxious ik tra' dang nam-tor wuh kal'i'farr svi' etek. James heh i ma kwon-hau-ov ashau tik vath u' sa-kai heh ko-kai; tonk'peh veling au nam-tor nu'ri heh has gla-tor maut pi' t' ha'kiv wi, andandwell, au naturally did ri istaya tor tor sovek-vel spo' ik wi. Ni tra' vesh' quarrels, heh nash, i am sure, vesh' veh t' au." "heh ish-veh sa-mekh?" ya'akash holmes. "vesh' au svi' favour t' such wuh union?" "rai, au vesh' averse tor ish-veh isha. Kling tonk'peh mr. Mccarthy vesh' svi' favour t' ish-veh." wuh sahris blush be' dvun-tor abru' ish-veh sluk nu'ri limuk u' holmes pohshaya veh t' ish-veh keen, questioning glances na' ish-veh. "nemaiyo na' nash ro'fori, " leralmin-tor au. "lau gla-tor nash-veh ish-veh sa-mekh kuv i vutau tor-morrow?" "i am kwes wuh hassu skil-tor't kal-tor ish-veh." "wuh hassu?" "ha, ma du ri puzhu-tor? Ri donku-tor sa-mekh has worla vesh' karik na' tevun pla', tonk'peh nash has pushau ish-veh ne' completely. Au has taken tor ish-veh sar-tak, heh dr. Willows leralmin-tor ik au nam-tor wuh vashau heh ik ish-veh nervous torektra nam-tor zarahk-tor. Mr. Mccarthy vesh' wuh goh sasu alive vi had fainu dad svi' wuh hinek gad svi' victoria." "ha! Svi' victoria! Ik nam-tor yauluhk." "ha, na' wuh ip-thorshek." "ved ni; na' wuh pi-maat-tukh-ip-thorshek, wilat, u' i ken-tor, mr. Turner tor ish-veh donku." "ha, certainly." "nemaiyo, din-tor turner. Du ma vesh' t' tukh assistance tor me." "du dungi var-tor me kuv du ma sovek ro'fori tor-morrow. Rai vet du dungi hal-tor tor wuh prison tor gla-tor james. Oh, kuv du tor, mr. Holmes, tor var-tor ish-veh ik i fai-tor ish-veh tor nam-tor innocent." "i dungi, din-tor turner." "i bolau hal-tor ha-kel i', na' dad nam-tor maut has-bosh, heh au din-tor me ni kuv i trasha ish-veh. Rom-bye, heh oekon gol'nev du svi' ish-veh undertaking." she hurried s' wuh tvi-shal u' impulsively u' she had svi-tor, heh etek puzhu-tor wuh halek t' ish-veh carriage rattle ska' ne' wuh yut. "i am kafusik t' du, holmes, " leralmin-tor lestrade k' dignity po' wuh zamu minutes' silence. "po dang du ashenau abru rok-tor if du nam-tor bound tor disappoint? Watson, i pthak ik du dungi talal ish-veh maut vohris, tonk'peh i dungau goh nam-tor maf wuh couple t' wadan." i lates-tor ne' tor wuh wurzel k' au, heh yi czar-tor k'fai wuh yut t' wuh pi' kahr, t'forti returning tor wuh hotel, wilat i ti fi-tor wuh ku-san heh ar'kada tor eku'ko myself svi' wuh kin-kur-backed dunap. Wuh puny besau t' wuh var vesh' ni wonil, however, lu tcok'at tor wuh glu mystery k'fai'ei etek vesh' groping, heh i afer-tor t'nash-veh attention czar ni continually s' wuh torai tor wuh kla-min, ik i na' kim-shah flung ish-veh mes' wuh tvi-shal heh mazhiv-kur-tor myself abru entirely tor wuh consideration t' wuh pavek t' wuh gad. Supposing ik nash unhappy nu'ri sasu's var vesh' absolutely yeht, yi ra hellish vel, ra absolutely unforeseen heh wehtsuri calamity kupi ma paresh-tor svi' wuh wak lu au parted s' ish-veh sa-mekh, heh wuh moment lu, drawn pla' k' ish-veh shei, au rushed vi' wuh glade? Ish-veh vesh' vel terrible heh tevalik. Ra kupi ish-veh nam-tor? Lau ri wuh malat t' wuh dash reveal vel tor t'nash-veh hasuk instincts? I rang wuh kus-vakh heh puvutau na' wuh weekly county dun, if tuhlau wuh verbatim khrosahp t' wuh inquest. Svi' wuh sharushsu's deposition ish-veh vesh' fupa s' ik wuh posterior wuh t' wuh losrak parietal hinek heh wuh losrak ulef t' wuh patam-pla-dor-hinek had vesh' zarahk-tor k' wuh ras salur s' wuh pasik wun. I pu'ulidau wuh gla-tor fi-tor t'nash-veh sha' patam. Clearly such wuh salur bolau ma vesh' kwul-tor s' za'. Ik vesh' tor ein sadvun svi' favour t' wuh accused, u' lu gla-tor quarrelling au vesh' limuk tor limuk k' ish-veh sa-mekh. Fam dvun, ish-veh did ri hal-tor na' maut mau, na' wuh older sasu lau ma da-tor ish-veh pla' fa' wuh salur tevan-tor. Fam dvun, ish-veh lau nam-tor don du' tor vutau holmes' attention tor ish-veh. Yi tra' vesh' wuh peculiar dying dzhinaya tor wuh rat. Ra kupi ik tvai? Ish-veh kupi ri nam-tor delirium. Wuh sasu dying s' wuh sudden salur tor ri commonly shetau delirious. Rai, ish-veh vesh' weht kesik tor nam-tor wuh attempt tor danau uf au ragel-tor ish-veh buk. Tonk'peh ra kupi ish-veh indicate? I cudgelled t'nash-veh shi'nahp tor talal ein tor-yehat danaya. Heh yi wuh incident t' wuh zhai-kur sai gla-tor k' nu'ri mccarthy. Kuv ik vesh' yeht wuh murderer bolau ma eku-tor ein krus t' ish-veh sai-vel, presumably ish-veh overcoat, svi' ish-veh hash, heh bolau ma had wuh hardihood tor fun heh tor lesh ish-veh maf na' wuh instant lu wuh sa-fu vesh' kneeling k' ish-veh pla' da-tor ri wuh dozen sahr-tor ska'. Ra wuh nalatra t' mysteries heh improbabilities wuh bosh vel vesh'! Ish-veh vesh' tab-ma fa' sherlock holmes fun-tor. Sarlah ish-veh pla' sa'awek, na' lestrade vesh' staying svi' lodgings svi' wuh kahr. Fi' wuh vath el'ru, wuh sasu dang nam-tor na' ish-veh maut buhfik heh keenest na' such nice ar'kadan u' ik, heh i did ri istaya tor tor ish-veh lu fagged k' wuh wu halovaya. Ki'gla-tor nash-veh nu'ri mccarthy." "heh ra did du oren-tor s' ish-veh?" "nothing." "kupi au lehm rai ta'hal?" "rim na' ek'. I vesh' vul-tor tor nah-tor na' veh wak ik au fai-tor vi had ovsoh ish-veh heh vesh' screening ish-veh il ish-veh, tonk'peh i am convinced i' ik au nam-tor u' puzzled u' kanok-veh else. Au nam-tor ri wuh maut sahris-witted youth, hi comely tor glazhau na' heh, i dang nah-tor, ralash na' khaf-spol." "i fam yehat krol-tor ish-veh zahvan, " i remarked, "kuv ish-veh nam-tor indeed wuh kla-min ik au vesh' averse tor wuh kal'i'farr k' ni sem-rik-tor wuh nu'ri t'sai u' nash din-tor turner." "ah, thereby geldau wuh rather kusut-tor var. Nash katravahsu nam-tor madly, insanely, svi' ashaya k' ish-veh, tonk'peh ein dahkuh tevun ago, lu au vesh' goh wuh lad, heh fa' au really fai-tor ish-veh, na' she had vesh' maf kaukuh tevun na' wuh boarding-shi'oren, ra tor wuh idiot tor tonk'peh prah vi' wuh clutches t' wuh barmaid svi' bristol heh marry ish-veh na' wuh registry office? Kling fai-tor wuh zhit t' wuh tukh, tonk'peh du mokuhlek glenonau uf maddening ish-veh bolau nam-tor tor ish-veh tor nam-tor upbraided na' ri doing ra au would mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh maut bezhun tor tor, tonk'peh ra au fai-tor tor nam-tor absolutely impossible. Ish-veh vesh' sheer frenzy t' nash wihfelau if tor ish-veh lehm ish-veh el'ru abru vi' wuh sov lu ish-veh sa-mekh, na' ish-veh kim-shah interview, vesh' goading ish-veh fi' tor propose tor din-tor turner. Rom has sasarlah t' ek'rasah, however, na' wuh barmaid, finding s' wuh dun ik au nam-tor svi' serious trouble heh kesik tor nam-tor geldau, has lehm-tor ish-veh abru' utterly heh has written tor ish-veh tor leralmin ik she has wuh sa-telsu already svi' wuh bermuda dockyard, ni ik tra' nam-tor really rai tie svi' au. I nah-tor ik ik zeshau t' ro'fori has consoled nu'ri mccarthy na' ek' ik au has dashau." "tonk'peh kuv au nam-tor innocent, vi has ovsoh ish-veh?" "ah! Vi? I would vutau ish-veh attention maut wa' tor dahkuh sfekau. Veh nam-tor ik wuh riyeht-stau sasu had wuh latva k' ein-veh na' wuh patra, heh ik wuh ein-veh kupi ri ma vesh' ish-veh sa-fu, na' ish-veh sa-fu vesh' maf, heh au did ri fai-tor lu au would fun. "ish-veh nam-tor leralmin-tor ik mr. Turner, t' wuh tvur, nam-tor ni has-bosh ik ish-veh ha'kiv nam-tor despaired t'." "wuh shakhupik sasu, i presume?" leralmin-tor holmes. "pa' sheh-leh; tonk'peh ish-veh constitution has vesh' zarahk-tor k' ish-veh ha'kiv abroad, heh au has vesh' svi' failing muhl'es na' ein wak. Ik nam-tor eku'ki, " leralmin-tor holmes. "oh, ha! Svi' wuh hundred vath yut au has gol-tor ish-veh. Kanok-veh pa' la' stariben t' ish-veh kindness tor ish-veh." "really! Tor ish-veh ri kwul du u' wuh pi' singular ik nash mccarthy, vi saudau ki' had pi' t' ish-veh sha', heh ki' vesh' ne' such obligations tor turner, dang fam dvun variben t' marrying ish-veh sa-fu tor turner's ko-fu, vi nam-tor, presumably, heiress tor wuh estate, heh ik svi' such wuh maut cocksure manner, u' kuv ish-veh vesh' goh wuh nuf t' wuh mnah heh ek' else would zahal-tor? Ish-veh nam-tor wuh weht flekh, opi' etek fai-tor ik turner himself vesh' averse tor wuh idea. Wuh ko-fu var-tor etek u' mau. Tor du ri deduce vel s' ik?" "ha, ik nam-tor ish-veh." ish-veh vesh' wuh widespread, kel'o-looking kelek, dahkuh-storied, kitau-kov-roofed, k' lo'uk kin-kur blotches t' lichen fi-tor wuh zhai-kur temok. Wuh drawn blinds heh wuh smokeless vuzh-mev, however, mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh stricken glazhau, u' hi wuh rasath t' nash horror fam dvun ti ras fi-tor ish-veh. Etek puvutau na' wuh svep, lu wuh maid, na' holmes' ya'akash, gluvau etek wuh kluf if ish-veh trensu sai-vel-tor na' wuh wak t' ish-veh tevakh, heh isha wuh shif t' wuh sa-fu's, hi ri wuh shif if au had yi had. Having thon-tor aifa maut carefully s' stehkuh il ohkuh natya sfekau, holmes aitlu pufulag-tor tor wuh kelek-ker, s' if etek ek' zahal-tor wuh kuvoran yut if pufulag-tor tor boscombe patra. Sherlock holmes vesh' mesuvulau lu au vesh' fal fi-tor such wuh scent u' nash. Sasu vi had goh fainu wuh hizhuk thinker heh logician t' leipausu yut would ma vravshau tor naglanshau ish-veh. Ish-veh limuk kluhvau heh mu'glau. Ish-veh meix'tem vesh' drawn vi' dahkuh lerash nesh-kur zehl, du' ish-veh bezhun min-tor si' s' ne'rak au k' wuh steely glitter. Ish-veh limuk vesh' keh'sei ne'le, ish-veh tipan ovalau, ish-veh bru-lar lerakhovau, heh wuh os-khaf-mev lam-tor si' spo' whipcord svi' ish-veh wu, sinewy talu. Ish-veh han-sharular seemed tor eiksha k' wuh purely aushfa lust na' wuh a'vesh', heh ish-veh kashek vesh' ni absolutely concentrated fi-tor wuh tukh fa' ish-veh ik wuh deshker il remark tevan-tor unheeded fi-tor ish-veh kaluk, il, na' wuh danik, goh provoked wuh sahris, impatient snarl svi' kilko. Swiftly heh silently au tor ish-veh yut bi' wuh yut if sahr-tor k'fai wuh ne-yartra, heh ni k' yut t' wuh lapan tor wuh boscombe patra. Ish-veh vesh' damp, marshy solektra, u' nam-tor ek' ik kahkrus, heh tra' vesh' ulidar t' wehk ash'ya, fi' fi-tor wuh yut heh svi' wuh pen yar if bounded ish-veh fi' either vla. Sometimes holmes would brax fi', sometimes pehkaya tevik, heh wuh'wak au tor ved wuh pi' pamutaya vi' wuh ne-yartra. Lestrade heh i lates-tor za' ish-veh, wuh detective indifferent heh contemptuous, du' i glantau t'nash-veh t'hy'la k' wuh eku'ko if sprang s' wuh conviction ik kanok veh t' ish-veh torai vesh' khartau na' wuh definite shaht. Wuh boscombe patra, if nam-tor wuh pi' reed-girt thalv t' masu ein kau-leh ker mes', nam-tor situated na' wuh krup svi' wuh hatherley uroshal heh wuh awek shi'sochya t' wuh wealthy mr. Turner. Abru' wuh lapan if zehl-tor ish-veh fi-tor wuh weh-irak vla etek kupi gla-tor wuh yon-kur, jutting kov-suk'fek if pu'ulidau wuh shi t' wuh don-ka landowner's kelek. Fi' wuh hatherley vla t' wuh patra wuh lapan grew maut bali, heh tra' vesh' wuh wonil san-zhel t' sodden yar dah-leh sahr-tor mes' svi' wuh rihk t' wuh lap heh wuh reeds if zehl-tor wuh suk'muzh. Lestrade gluvau etek wuh faikaik gla-tor na' if wuh ak'shem had vesh' afer-tor, heh, indeed, ni moist vesh' wuh solektra, ik i kupi plainly gla-tor wuh zavikau if had vesh' losrak k' wuh tevan t' wuh stricken sasu. Tor holmes, u' kupi gla-tor nash-veh k' ish-veh nayik limuk heh peering bezhun, maut wehk vath vel vesh' tor nam-tor telv-tor fi-tor wuh sahr-tor yar. Au sahr-tor pauk, spo' wuh dog vi nam-tor picking abru wuh scent, heh yi da-tor fi-tor t'nash-veh besu. "ra did du hal-tor vi' wuh patra na'?" au ya'akash. "i aluk-kum-tor pa' k' wuh dref. I nahp tra' lau nam-tor ein wun il vath zavikau. Tonk'peh uf fi' terra" "oh, tut, tut! I ma rai wak! Ik losrak ash'ya t' ish-veh k' its inward kuvoran nam-tor ek' abru' wuh shi. Wuh mole kupi zavikau ish-veh, heh tra' ish-veh vanishes among wuh reeds. Oh, uf velik ish-veh would ek' ma vesh' had i vesh' la' fa' sarlah au spo' wuh kuht t' buffalo heh wallowed ek' abru' ish-veh. La' nam-tor wilat wuh party k' wuh lodge-keeper sarlah, heh au ma wein-tor ek' ash'yaidar na' shehkuh il ohkuh ash'ya pauk wuh ak'shem. Tonk'peh la' nam-tor rehkuh dahshauk ash'yaidar t' wuh ka ash'ya." au drew si' wuh gelek heh ti ne' fi-tor ish-veh waterproof ki' wuh weh-rom zan-tor, talking ek' wuh wak rather tor himself do tor etek. "aifa nam-tor nu'ri mccarthy's ash'ya. Dah'wak au vesh' walking, heh wuh'wak au sahr-tor swiftly, ni ik wuh lad nam-tor deeply pu'ulidau heh wuh timut hardly visible. Ik bears si' ish-veh var. Au sahr-tor lu gla-tor ish-veh ish-veh sa-mekh fi' wuh solektra. Yi la' nam-tor wuh sa-mekh's ash'ya u' au sahr-tor abru heh ne'. Ra nam-tor nash, yi? Ish-veh nam-tor wuh butt-shaht t' wuh pohshayek u' wuh sa-fu lam-tor listening. Heh nash? Ha, ha! Ra ma etek la'? Tiptoes! Tiptoes! Keh-vla, nuh', ved ritsuri kluf! Sarlah au, au hal-tor, sarlah au againof rivak ik vesh' na' wuh tor-sai. I' wilat did au sarlah s'?" au sahr-tor abru heh ne', sometimes losing, sometimes finding wuh yut abi' etek vesh' muhl k'svi wuh rihk t' wuh lapan heh ne' wuh duv t' wuh lo'uk beech, wuh largest lap svi' wuh neighbourhood. "ish-veh has vesh' wuh nuf t' considerable eku'ko, " au remarked, returning tor ish-veh malatik manner. "i fancy ik nash zhai-kur kelek fi' wuh gas'rak bolau nam-tor wuh lodge. "nash lau eku'ko du, lestrade, " au remarked, holding ish-veh si'. "wuh riyeht-staya vesh' ovsoh k' ish-veh." "gla-tor nash-veh rai ulidar." "tra' nam-tor rim." "uf tor du fai-tor, yi?" "wuh yar vesh' growing ne' ish-veh. Ish-veh had goh lain tra' wuh zamu gad. Tra' vesh' rai glat t' wuh shi whence ish-veh had vesh' taken. Ish-veh corresponds k' wuh dash. Tra' nam-tor rai glat t' sovek vath wun." "heh wuh murderer?" "nam-tor wuh ha-vol sasu, losrak-handed, limps k' wuh gas'rak mal, sai-vel-tor bali-soled shooting-kluf heh wuh zhai-kur tor-sai, vuzh indian cigars, nam-tor-tor wuh cigar-holder, heh lesh wuh pasik pen-lipau svi' ish-veh abru'lik. Tra' nam-tor several vath indications, tonk'peh aifa lau nam-tor hiyet tor mamuk etek svi' etwel psthan." lestrade abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor. "du ar'kadan ish-veh sha' method, heh i dungau ar'kadan t'nash-veh. I dungau nam-tor toranik nash aru, heh dungau probably fun tor london k' wuh khru ranau." "heh trasha ish-veh nuf unfinished?" "rai, shahtau." "tonk'peh wuh mystery?" "ish-veh nam-tor kilau." "vi vesh' wuh criminal, yi?" "wuh gentleman i kethelvau." "tonk'peh vi nam-tor au?" "surely ish-veh would ri nam-tor rihagik tor talal si'. Nash nam-tor ri such wuh populous neighbourhood." lestrade shrugged ish-veh tipan. "i am wuh practical sasu, " au leralmin-tor, "heh i really fam yehat undertake tor hal-tor pa' wuh shasol looking na' wuh losrak-handed gentleman k' wuh zhagra mal. I dungau eku du wuh zehl fa' i trasha." having losrak lestrade na' ish-veh tvi-shal, etek drove tor etwel hotel, wilat etek afer-tor khi-gad-yem fi-tor wuh pasu. Holmes vesh' ralash-fam heh visolektau svi' nahp k' wuh kusut-tor sagluvaya fi-tor ish-veh limuk, u' veh vi tal-tor himself svi' wuh perplexing shul. "glazhau la', watson, " au leralmin-tor lu wuh sai vesh' pa'shu "aishan hayal-tor ne' svi' nash ku-san heh kal-tor me preach tor du na' wuh pi'. I ri tor fai-tor ved ra tor tor, heh i dang tala ish-veh na'shikh. Ta'hal wuh cigar heh kal-tor me expound." "pray tor ni." "muhl, i', svi' panahik nash nuf tra' nam-tor dahkuh sfekau pa' nu'ri mccarthy's narrative if kwul-tor etek fi' instantly, hi au impressed me svi' ish-veh favour heh du tehnat ish-veh. Veh vesh' wuh kla-min ik ish-veh sa-mekh dang, fupa s' ish-veh khrosahp, maf 'cooee!' fa' seeing ish-veh. Wuh vath vesh' ish-veh singular dying dzhinaya tor wuh rat. Au mumbled several zhit, du ken-tor, tonk'peh ik vesh' ek' ik kum-tor wuh sa-fu's kaluk. I' s' nash dahtau sfek etwel kla-hil bolau palikau, heh etek dungi palikau ish-veh k' presuming ik ra wuh lad leralmin-tor nam-tor absolutely yeht." "ra t' nash 'cooee!' yi?" "muhl, obviously ish-veh kupi ri ma vesh' tvai na' wuh sa-fu. Wuh sa-fu, u' irak u' au fai-tor, vesh' svi' bristol. Ish-veh vesh' mere pavesh ik au vesh' k'svi earshot. Wuh 'cooee!' vesh' tvai tor skamau wuh attention t' whoever ish-veh vesh' ik au had wuh latva k'. Tonk'peh 'cooee' nam-tor wuh distinctly australian maf, heh veh if nam-tor nam-tor-tor svi' australians. Tra' nam-tor wuh karik presumption ik wuh person ik mccarthy gishu tor ragel-tor ish-veh na' boscombe patra vesh' ein-veh vi had vesh' svi' australia." "ra t' wuh rat, yi?" sherlock holmes nem-tor wuh hesha dun s' ish-veh abru'lik heh flattened ish-veh si' fi' wuh pasu. "nash nam-tor wuh besan t' wuh sashila t' victoria, " au leralmin-tor. "i wired tor bristol na' ish-veh kim-shah mu-yor." au shitau ish-veh el'ru abru' krus t' wuh besan. "ra tor du telv-tor?" "arat, " i telv-tor. "heh i'?" au ashenau ish-veh el'ru. "ballarat." "ved ni. Ik vesh' wuh zhit wuh sasu uttered, heh t' if ish-veh sa-fu goh kum-tor wuh kim-shah dahkuh zhit-shaya. Au vesh' trying tor utter wuh ahm t' ish-veh murderer. Ni heh ni, t' ballarat." "ish-veh nam-tor wonderful!" i sporiben. "ish-veh nam-tor obvious. Heh i', gla-tor du, i had wonilau wuh vunai ne' considerably. Wuh mat t' wuh zhai-kur ain vesh' wuh wuh sfek if, granting wuh sa-fu's star-krus tor nam-tor yeht, vesh' wuh certainty. Etek ma sarlah i' s' mere vagueness tor wuh definite conception t' wuh australian s' ballarat k' wuh zhai-kur tor-sai." "certainly." "heh veh vi vesh' na' ha-kel svi' wuh kahkrus, na' wuh patra mokuhlek goh nam-tor betau k' wuh uroshal il k' wuh estate, wilat ri-fainusu kupi hardly czar." "ved ni." "yi sarlah etwel expedition t' tor-gad. K' wuh linisaya t' wuh solektra i nazh-tor wuh trifling details if i mazhiv-kur-tor tor ik imbecile lestrade, u' tor wuh nafu'es t' wuh criminal." "tonk'peh uf did du nazh-kap au?" "du fai-tor t'nash-veh method. Ish-veh nam-tor founded fi-tor wuh glantaya t' trifles." "ish-veh pidek i fai-tor ik du lau roughly judge s' wuh wu-vath t' ish-veh stride. Ish-veh kluf, nuh', lau nam-tor var-tor s' ish-veh zavikau." "ha, au vesh' peculiar kluf." "tonk'peh ish-veh lameness?" "wuh impression t' ish-veh gas'rak ash'ya vesh' kwon-hau-ov lehkuh natya do ish-veh losrak. Au shitau lehkuh rasath fi-tor ish-veh. Po? Fai'ei au limpedhe vesh' lame." "tonk'peh ish-veh losrak-handedness." "du vesh' yourself kwul-tor k' wuh malat t' wuh dash u' vipladau k' wuh sharushsu na' wuh inquest. Wuh salur vesh' kwul-tor s' iyi za', heh wi vesh' fi-tor wuh losrak vla. I', uf mokuhlek ik nam-tor vita ish-veh vesh' k' wuh losrak-handed sasu? Au had lam-tor za' ik lap du' wuh interview svi' wuh sa-mekh heh sa-fu. Au had kauk smoked tra'. I afer-tor wuh vitush t' wuh cigar, if t'nash-veh special fai-tukh t' tobacco vitush enables me tor pronounce u' wuh indian cigar. I ma, u' du fai-tor, vaikau ein attention tor nash, heh written wuh pi' monograph fi' wuh vitush t' 140 natya vuhna'es t' mev, cigar, heh cigarette tobacco. Having afer-tor wuh vitush, i yi glazhau pauk heh discovered wuh stump among wuh yekuhl wilat au had tossed ish-veh. Ish-veh vesh' wuh indian cigar, t' wuh vuhna'es if nam-tor padukau svi' rotterdam." "heh wuh cigar-holder?" "kupi gla-tor nash-veh ik wuh shaht had ri vesh' svi' ish-veh ru'lut. Therefore au nam-tor-tor wuh holder. Wuh um had vesh' tresahk ska', ri bitten ska', tonk'peh wuh tresahk vesh' ri wuh sok'i veh, ni i deduced wuh pasik pen-lipau." "holmes, " i leralmin-tor, "du ma drawn wuh vis pauk nash sasu s' if au fam yehat stron, heh du ma korsau wuh innocent komihn ha'kiv u' truly u' kuv du had tresahk wuh elakh if vesh' hanging ish-veh. Gla-tor nash-veh wuh kharat svi' if ek' nash sfekau. Wuh culprit nam-tor" "mr. John turner, " maf-tor wuh hotel waiter, sharu wuh svep t' etwel sitting-tvi-shal, heh ushering svi' wuh visitor. Wuh sasu vi svi-tor vesh' wuh flekh heh impressive khlop. Ish-veh vohris, limping ash heh ovalau tipan mazhiv-kur-tor wuh appearance t' decrepitude, heh wi ish-veh lerash, glu-zehl-tor, craggy features, heh ish-veh masuk' sikrus gluvau ik au vesh' ma t' ritsuri karik'es t' ak'shem heh t' character. Ish-veh tangled hisahk, grizzled isachya, heh outstanding, tevan-tor bezhun-zehl puterish-tor tor mazhiv-kur-tor wuh sov t' dignity heh tepul tor ish-veh appearance, tonk'peh ish-veh limuk vesh' t' wuh ashen wan-kur, du' ish-veh bru-lar heh wuh teruk t' ish-veh han-sharular vesh' kur-tor k' wuh duvek t' pla-kur. Ish-veh vesh' pa'shik tor me na' wuh glance ik au vesh' svi' wuh grip t' ein tevalik heh chronic has. "pray hayal-tor ne' fi' wuh ku-san, " leralmin-tor holmes kogavik. "du had t'nash-veh pitoh?" "ha, wuh lodge-keeper katau ish-veh abru. Du leralmin-tor ik du istau tor gla-tor me la' tor nan'woi scandal." "i nahp sutra would variben kuv i went tor wuh tvur." "heh po did du istaya tor gla-tor me?" au glazhau mes' na' t'nash-veh besu k' despair svi' ish-veh weary bezhun, u' hi ish-veh deshker vesh' already kilko-tor. "ha, " leralmin-tor holmes, answering wuh glazhau rather do wuh zhit. "ish-veh nam-tor ni. I fai-tor ek' pa' mccarthy." wuh hinek sasu sank ish-veh limuk svi' ish-veh el'ru. "oekon gol'nev me!" au maf-tor. "tonk'peh i would ri ma kal-tor wuh nu'ri sasu sarlah tor klau. I mazhiv-kur-tor du t'nash-veh zhit ik i would ma spoken si' kuv ish-veh went tehnat ish-veh na' wuh assizes." "i am glad tor zhu-tor du leralmin ni, " leralmin-tor holmes gravely. "i would ma spoken i' had ish-veh ri vesh' na' t'nash-veh tal-kam ko-kan. Ish-veh would shaya ish-veh heartit dungi shaya ish-veh khaf-spol lu she zhu-tor ik i am pehkau." "ish-veh lau ri sarlah tor ik, " leralmin-tor holmes. "ra?" "i am rai official agent. I ken-tor ik ish-veh vesh' ish-veh ko-fu vi required t'nash-veh la'es la', heh i am peran svi' ish-veh eku'ko. Nu'ri mccarthy bolau nam-tor prah ska', however." "i am wuh dying sasu, " leralmin-tor hinek turner. "i ma had ritsuri-nosh t'slor-dau-tukh na' tevun. T'nash-veh hassu leralmin-tor ish-veh nam-tor wuh deshker whether i dungau ha-tor wuh tevun-krus. Wi i would rather tev-tor ne' t'nash-veh sha' kamu do svi' wuh gaol." holmes she-tor heh hayal-tor ne' na' wuh pasu k' ish-veh pen svi' ish-veh el'ru heh wuh uzh'a'lek t' dun fa' ish-veh. "aishan var-tor etek wuh yeht'es, " au leralmin-tor. "i dungau jot ne' wuh kla-min. Du dungi glat ish-veh, heh watson la' mokuhlek toglantausu ish-veh. Yi i kupi torvau ish-veh confession na' wuh kim-shah si-vukhut-krus tor korsau nu'ri mccarthy. I ugaya du ik i dungau ri nam-tor-tor ish-veh vita ish-veh nam-tor absolutely bolau." "ish-veh's u' muhl, " leralmin-tor wuh hinek sasu; "ish-veh's wuh deshker whether i dungau ha-tor tor wuh assizes, ni ish-veh tukh pi' tor me, tonk'peh i dang istaya tor spare alice wuh kolaya. Heh i' i dungi tor wuh vel pa'shik tor du; ish-veh has vesh' wuh akarshif svi' wuh peran, tonk'peh dungi ri nem-tor me wu tor var-tor. "du didn't fai-tor nash tevik sasu, mccarthy. Au vesh' wuh e'shua incarnate. I var-tor du ik. Oekon potau du s' wuh clutches t' such wuh sasu u' au. Ish-veh grip has vesh' fi-tor me aifa dah-leh tevun, heh au has thorshau t'nash-veh ha'kiv. I'll var-tor du wuh'rak uf vesht sarlah nash-veh tor nam-tor svi' ish-veh tepul. "ish-veh vesh' svi' wuh lehkuh-mal '60's na' wuh diggings. I vesh' wuh nu'ri chap yi, fal-blooded heh reckless, pok tor da-tor t'nash-veh el'ru na' sovek-vel; i prah among rasahkos besu, nem-tor tor mon, had rai kunli k' t'nash-veh claim, nem-tor tor wuh bush, heh svi' wuh zhit became ra du would vutau abru' la' wuh yut robber. Tra' vesh' shehkuh t' etek, heh etek had wuh kwai, elik ha'kiv t' ish-veh, sticking abru wuh wurzel s' wak tor wak, il stopping wuh wagons fi' wuh fau-yut tor wuh diggings. Nesh-kur jack t' ballarat vesh' wuh ahm i went ne', heh etwel party nam-tor fam dvun vokau svi' wuh sashila u' wuh ballarat gang. "veh gad wuh pi-maat-tukh nik'el sarlah ne' s' ballarat tor melbourne, heh etek ti svi' bek-tor na' ish-veh heh nashiv ish-veh. Tra' vesh' shehkuh troopers heh shehkuh t' etek, ni ish-veh vesh' wuh ikap-tor vel, tonk'peh etek emptied kehkuh t' ish-veh saddles na' wuh wuh'rak volley. Rehkuh t' etwel sa-kan vesh' pustau, however, fa' etek prah wuh swag. I shitau t'nash-veh el'ru-pohshayek tor wuh patam t' wuh wagon-yetursu, vi vesh' nash maut sasu mccarthy. I istaya tor wuh s'haile ik i had pohshaya ish-veh yi, tonk'peh i spared ish-veh, hi vesht gla-tor nash-veh ish-veh wicked pi' bezhun teslau fi' t'nash-veh limuk, u' hi tor vokau kanok feature. Etek prah maf k' wuh pi-maat-tukh, became wealthy sasu, heh tor etwel yut abru' tor england rik' hasu suspected. Tra' i parted s' t'nash-veh hinek pals heh satalau tor settle ne' tor wuh hizhuk heh respectable ha'kiv. I bought nash estate, if chanced tor nam-tor svi' wuh mahr-kel, heh i eku myself tor tor wuh pi' rom k' t'nash-veh donku, tor tor abru na' wuh yut svi' if i had pinkau ish-veh. I telik, nuh', heh hi t'nash-veh ko-telsu tev-tor nu'ri she losrak me t'nash-veh tal-kam pi' alice. Kauk lu she vesh' aishan wuh kan-bu ish-veh wee el'ru seemed tor ras-tukh me ne' wuh gas'rak yut u' nothing else had ek'wak ovsoh. Svi' wuh zhit, i da-tor abru' wuh uzh mor heh did t'nash-veh buhfik tor tor abru na' wuh vesht. Ek' vesh' going muhl lu mccarthy laid ish-veh grip fi-tor me. "i had hal-tor abru tor kahr pa' wuh investment, heh i ragel-tor ish-veh svi' regent yut k' hardly wuh tor-pal tor ish-veh pla' il wuh kluf tor ish-veh ash'ya. "'la' etek nam-tor, jack, ' leralmin-tor au, touching me fi' wuh kar; 'etek'll nam-tor u' rom u' wuh skan tor du. Tra''s dahkuh t' etek, me heh t'nash-veh sa-fu, heh du mokuhlek ma wuh keeping t' etek. Kuv du don'tit's wuh tok-ti, tor-gav-abiding shasol nam-tor england, heh tra''s kwon-hau-ov wuh policeman k'svi masu-kov.' "muhl, ne' sarlah au tor wuh tev'rak shasol, tra' vesh' rai shaking au ska', heh tra' au ma ha-tor rent elik fi' t'nash-veh buhfik solektra ek'wak opi'. Tra' vesh' rai shom na' me, rai sochya, rai forgetfulness; da-tor wilat i would, tra' vesh' ish-veh cunning, grinning limuk na' t'nash-veh kar-nef. Ish-veh grew weh-rasahkos u' alice grew abru, na' au ak gla-tor i vesh' weht kwes t' ish-veh fai-tor t'nash-veh vesht do t' wuh police. Whatever au aitlu au bolau ma, heh whatever ish-veh vesh' i mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh rik' deshker, solektra, donku, kelek, abi' na' kim-shah au ya'akash wuh vel if i kupi ri mazhiv-kur-tor. Au ya'akash na' alice. "ish-veh sa-fu, gla-tor du, had grown abru, heh ni had t'nash-veh ko-kan, heh u' i vesh' fainu tor nam-tor svi' kobat muhl'es, ish-veh seemed wuh tok-ti shad-kisheya tor ish-veh ik ish-veh lad dang ash vi' wuh bosh veltra. Tonk'peh tra' i vesh' pesik. I would ri ma ish-veh cursed fek rish-tor k' t'nash-veh; ri ik i had sovek ritishaya tor wuh lad, tonk'peh ish-veh khaf vesh' svi' ish-veh, heh ik vesh' hiyet. I lam-tor pesik. Mccarthy threatened. I braved ish-veh tor tor ish-veh rasahkos. Etek vesh' tor ragel-tor na' wuh patra midway svi' etwel kelek tor variben ish-veh abru'. "lu i went ne' tra' i afer-tor ish-veh talking k' ish-veh sa-fu, ni i smoked wuh cigar heh bek-tor za' wuh lap abi' au dang nam-tor sa'awek. Tonk'peh u' i shroi tor ish-veh variben ek' ik vesh' nesh-kur heh sfith(-) svi' me seemed tor sarlah uppermost. Au vesh' urging ish-veh sa-fu tor marry t'nash-veh ko-fu k' u' pi' fudau na' ra she lau nah-tor u' kuv she vesh' wuh slut s' ska' wuh yut. Ish-veh drove me mad tor nah-tor ik i heh ek' ik i meskarau danik tal-kam dang nam-tor svi' wuh tepul t' such wuh sasu u' nash. Sos ri snap wuh tel-tor? I vesh' already wuh dying heh wuh desperate sasu. Hi pa'shik t' kashek heh fairly karik t' sikrus, i fai-tor ik t'nash-veh sha' buk vesh' fen-tor. Tonk'peh t'nash-veh vokaya heh t'nash-veh ko-kan! Fi' kupi nam-tor korsau kuv i kupi tonk'peh silence ik flalik lahv. I did ish-veh, mr. Holmes. I would tor ish-veh va'ashiv. Deeply u' i ma sinned, i ma pufulag-tor wuh ha'kiv t' martyrdom tor atone na' ish-veh. Tonk'peh ik t'nash-veh ko-kan dang nam-tor entangled svi' wuh ka meshes if meskarau me vesh' weht do i kupi dash. I kwul-tor ish-veh ne' k' rai weht compunction do kuv au had vesh' ein flalik heh venomous beast. Ish-veh maf katau pla' ish-veh sa-fu; tonk'peh i had nazh-tor wuh wein t' wuh lapan, hi i vesh' punekwitau tor hal-tor pla' tor zaprah wuh tor-sai if i had eku-tor svi' t'nash-veh hash. Ik nam-tor wuh yeht var, gentlemen, t' ek' ik paresh-tor." "muhl, ish-veh nam-tor ri na' me tor judge du, " leralmin-tor holmes u' wuh hinek sasu signed wuh star-krus if had vesh' drawn si'. "i pray ik etek lau worla nam-tor ko'nar tor such wuh temptation." "i pray ri, osu. Heh ra tor du intend tor tor?" "svi' zan-tor t' ish-veh muhl'es, nothing. Du nam-tor yourself aware ik du dungi ak ma tor kilko-srashiv na' ish-veh deed na' wuh higher kelek do wuh assizes. I dungi potau ish-veh confession, heh kuv mccarthy nam-tor condemned i dungau nam-tor punekwitau tor nam-tor-tor ish-veh. Kuv ri, ish-veh dungau worla nam-tor gla-tor k' mortal bezhun; heh ish-veh tsat, whether du nam-tor alive il tevik, dungau nam-tor safe k' etek." "rom-halan, yi, " leralmin-tor wuh hinek sasu solemnly. "ish-veh sha' deathbeds, lu sarlah au, dungi nam-tor wuh easier na' wuh nahp t' wuh sochya if du ma putan-tor tor t'nash-veh." tottering heh shaking svi' ek' ish-veh masuk'veh nentu, au stumbled slowly s' wuh tvi-shal. "oekon gol'nev etek!" leralmin-tor holmes po' wuh wu silence. "po tor buk mavau such tricks k' ri donku-tor, helpless worms? I worla zhu-tor t' such wuh nuf u' nash ik i ri tor nah-tor t' baxter's zhit, heh leralmin, 'tra', tonk'peh na' wuh takov t' oekon, hal-tor sherlock holmes.'" james mccarthy vesh' acquitted na' wuh assizes fi' wuh karik'es t' wuh su'etek t' objections if had vesh' drawn si' k' holmes heh submitted tor wuh defending counsel. Hinek turner ha-tor na' stehkuh tevun-krus po' etwel interview, tonk'peh au nam-tor i' tevik; heh tra' nam-tor kanok prospect ik wuh sa-fu heh ko-fu lau sarlah tor ha-tor kunling teretuhr svi' ignorance t' wuh nesh-kur wan if shom-tor fi-tor ish-veh vesht. V. Wuh kaukuh zhar-kur pips lu i glance abru' t'nash-veh pitoh heh vipladau t' wuh sherlock holmes nuf svi' wuh tevun '82 heh '90, i am limuk-tor k' ni wehk if la' flekh heh eku'ki features ik ish-veh nam-tor rai hagik tukh tor fai-tor if tor dvel-tor heh if tor trasha. Ein, however, ma already nazh-tor publicity k'fai wuh dun, heh vath ma ri nufau wuh vunai na' eifa peculiar qualities if t'nash-veh t'hy'la ma svi' ni pid wuh degree, heh if ish-veh nam-tor wuh vel t' aifa dun tor illustrate. Ein, nuh', ma hertak-tor ish-veh analytical renkup'es, heh would nam-tor, u' narratives, palikaya rik' wuh shahtan, du' vath ma vesh' tonk'peh partially pa'shu abru, heh ma ish-veh danaya founded rather fi-tor conjecture heh surmise do fi' ik ek'esik olozhikaik skan if vesh' ni tal-kam tor ish-veh. Tra' nam-tor, however, veh t' aifa kim-shah if vesh' ni remarkable svi' its details heh ni startling svi' its results ik i am tempted tor mazhiv-kur-tor ein khrosahp t' ish-veh svi' spite t' wuh kla-min ik tra' nam-tor sfekau svi' tersaya k' ish-veh if worla ma vesh', heh probably worla dungi nam-tor, entirely pa'shu abru. Wuh tevun '87 furnished etek k' wuh wu weizehl t' nuf t' greater il lehkuh eku'ko, t' if i retain wuh vipladau. Among t'nash-veh headings ne' nash-veh leh-dah tevun-krus i talal wuh khrosahp t' wuh adventure t' wuh paradol tvi-shal, t' wuh amateur mendicant shila'es, vi meskarau wuh luxurious muhd svi' wuh weh-neik vault t' wuh furniture warehouse, t' wuh kla-min tersau k' wuh pak t' wuh british barque sophy anderson, t' wuh singular adventures t' wuh grice patersons svi' wuh vikuvtra t' uffa, heh t'forti t' wuh camberwell poisoning nuf. Svi' wuh latter, u' lau nam-tor vokau, sherlock holmes vesh' kup, k' kuvoran abru wuh tevik sasu's glantau, tor skan-tor ik ish-veh had vesh' skek abru dahkuh wadan fa', heh ik therefore wuh tevik had hal-tor tor sar-tak k'svi ik timea nenem if vesh' t' wuh greatest importance svi' clearing abru wuh nuf. Ek' aifa i lau lubesan si' na' ein fa-wak kinuf, tonk'peh rim t' au la' such singular features u' wuh flekh ranau t' circumstances if i ma i' taken abru t'nash-veh pen tor kethelvau. Ish-veh vesh' svi' wuh latter gad t' september, heh wuh equinoctial karik salan had eku svi' k' exceptional khrash. Ek' gad wuh salan had shei heh wuh sov-masu had beaten tehnat wuh krani, ni ik kauk la' svi' wuh khaf-spol t' lo'uk, el'ru-tor london etek vesh' punekwitau tor ashenau etwel kashkau na' wuh instant s' wuh routine t' ha'kiv heh tor naglanshau wuh la'es t' eifa lo'uk elemental nekwitau if shriek na' mankind k'fai wuh mofek t' ish-veh civilisation, spo' untamed beasts svi' wuh kraisek. U' khru drew svi', wuh sahriv grew higher heh louder, heh wuh salan maf-tor heh sobbed spo' wuh kan svi' wuh vuzh-mev. Sherlock holmes hayal-tor moodily na' veh vla t' wuh yon-sha'ti tuhs-indexing ish-veh vipladau t' tr'y'kak, du' i na' wuh vath vesh' glu svi' veh t' clark russell's tok-ti masutra-var abi' wuh vlut t' wuh karik salan s' rik' seemed tor herish k' wuh text, heh wuh splash t' wuh sov-masu tor wuvau si' vi' wuh wu na-yumaya t' wuh masutra pral. T'nash-veh ko-telsu vesh' fi' wuh yaret tor ish-veh ko-mekh's, heh na' wuh zamu gad i vesh' wuh dweller wuh'wak weht svi' t'nash-veh hinek ha-shal na' leipausu yut. "po, " leralmin-tor i, glancing abru na' t'nash-veh besu, "ik vesh' surely wuh kus-vakh. Vi kupi sarlah tor-mu-yor? Ein t'hy'la t' ish-veh, sos'eh?" "kaula yourself i ma rim, " au kilko-tor. "i ri tor kastorau visitors." "wuh client, yi?" "kuv ni, ish-veh nam-tor wuh serious nuf. Nothing lehkuh would katau wuh sasu si' fi' such wuh gad heh na' such wuh wadan. Tonk'peh i nem-tor ish-veh ik ish-veh nam-tor weht kesik tor nam-tor ein crony t' wuh landlady's." sherlock holmes vesh' riyeht svi' ish-veh conjecture, however, na' tra' sarlah wuh ash svi' wuh tvur heh wuh tapping na' wuh svep. Au sakadau si' ish-veh wu kar tor da-tor wuh ha'gelek maf s' himself heh na' wuh vacant ku-san fi-tor if wuh newcomer bolau hayal-tor. "sarlah svi'!" leralmin-tor au. Wuh sasu vi svi-tor vesh' nu'ri, ein dahkuh-heh-dah-leh na' wuh s'udish, muhl-groomed heh trimly clad, k' vel t' refinement heh delicacy svi' ish-veh kuvish. Wuh streaming umbrella if au meskarau svi' ish-veh el'ru, heh ish-veh wu shining waterproof var-tor t' wuh kei igen-va k'fai'ei au had sarlah. Au glazhau pa' ish-veh anxiously svi' wuh glare t' wuh ha'gelek, heh i kupi gla-tor ik ish-veh limuk vesh' spoh heh ish-veh bezhun ras, spo' eifa t' wuh sasu vi nam-tor rasathau ne' k' ein lo'uk anxiety. "i owe du wuh apology, " au leralmin-tor, raising ish-veh pi-maat-kur pince-nez tor ish-veh bezhun. "i sahrafel ik i am ri intruding. I pthak ik i ma katau ein zavikau t' wuh sahriv heh sov-masu vi' ish-veh snug tvi-shal." "mazhiv-kur-tor me ish-veh tor-pal heh umbrella, " leralmin-tor holmes. "au lau shom la' fi' wuh kik heh dungi nam-tor pseth presently. Du ma sarlah abru s' wuh khu'rak-tev'rak, gla-tor nash-veh." "ha, s' horsham." "ik krizhiv heh gav rish if gla-tor nash-veh fi-tor ish-veh gof taik nam-tor ved distinctive." "ki'sarlah nash-veh na' na'shikh." "ik nam-tor easily prah." "heh gol'nev." "ik nam-tor ri kwon-hau-ov ni hagik." "i ma puzhu-tor t' du, mr. Holmes. I puzhu-tor s' tra-lan prendergast uf du korsau ish-veh svi' wuh tankerville muhd scandal." "ah, veling. Au vesh' wrongfully accused t' cheating na' nop." "au leralmin-tor ik du kupi kilau sovek-vel." "au leralmin-tor nuh' mau." "ik du nam-tor worla beaten." "i ma vesh' beaten kehkuh timesthree wak k' sasu, heh wuh'wak k' wuh kosu." "tonk'peh ra nam-tor ik tcok'at k' wuh su'etek t' ish-veh navun?" "ish-veh nam-tor yeht ik i ma vesh' paik successful." "yi du lau nam-tor ni k' me." "i eit'jae ik du dungi bes-tor ish-veh ku-san abru tor wuh yon heh favour me k' ein details u' tor ish-veh nuf." "ish-veh nam-tor rai ordinary veh." "rim t' eifa if sarlah tor me nam-tor. I am wuh kim-shah kelek t' appeal." "heh wi i deshker, osu, whether, svi' ek' ish-veh veshtaya, du ma ek'wak shroi tor wuh weht mysterious heh inexplicable naf-elakh t' pavek do eifa if ma pavesh-tor svi' t'nash-veh sha' skan." "du boshaya me k' eku'ko, " leralmin-tor holmes. "pray mazhiv-kur-tor etek wuh bolayatik kla-min s' wuh palikaya, heh i mokuhlek afterwards deshker du u' tor eifa details if seem tor me tor nam-tor danik yauluhk." wuh nu'ri sasu seshau ish-veh ku-san abru heh kwitau ish-veh masupik ash'ya si' na' wuh yon. "t'nash-veh ahm, " leralmin-tor au, "nam-tor john openshaw, tonk'peh t'nash-veh sha' tek'ik ma, u' irak u' i mokuhlek ken-tor, pi' tor tor k' nash awful business. Ish-veh nam-tor wuh samekhik tukh; ni svi' zek tor mazhiv-kur-tor du wuh idea t' wuh kla-min, i bolau hal-tor pla' tor wuh palikaya t' wuh tek'ik. "du bolau fai-tor ik t'nash-veh sa'mekh'al had dahkuh sonsmy sa-kuk elias heh t'nash-veh sa-mekh joseph. T'nash-veh sa-mekh had wuh pi' zhuk-om na' coventry, if au sukau na' wuh wak t' wuh fereik-vel t' bicycling. Au vesh' wuh patentee t' wuh openshaw unbreakable zung-tor, heh ish-veh business ragel-tor k' such navun ik au vesh' kup tor makau ish-veh heh tor retire fi-tor wuh handsome competence. "t'nash-veh sa-kuk elias emigrated tor america lu au vesh' wuh nu'ri sasu heh became wuh planter svi' florida, wilat au vesh' reported ki' ovsoh maut muhl. Na' wuh wak t' wuh t'naehm au fought svi' jackson's ya'akash'er, heh afterwards ne' fash, wilat au she-tor tor nam-tor wuh shal-lan. Lu lee laid ne' ish-veh kar t'nash-veh sa-kuk fun-tor tor ish-veh plantation, wilat au hafau na' rehkuh il kehkuh tevun. Pa' 1869 il 1870 sarlah ish-veh pla' tor europe heh nem-tor wuh pi' estate svi' sussex, be' horsham. Au had tor wuh maut considerable fortune svi' wuh fupa s', heh ish-veh utvau na' leaving au vesh' ish-veh aversion tor wuh negroes, heh ish-veh ritishaya t' wuh republican policy svi' extending wuh franchise tor au. Au vesh' wuh singular sasu, kei heh sahris-tempered, maut flalik-mouthed lu au vesh' reshnek, heh t' wuh danik retiring disposition. Du' ek' wuh tevun ik au ha-tor na' horsham, i vet kuv ek'wak au eku ash'ya svi' wuh kahr. Au had wuh bah-ker heh dahkuh il rehkuh vunai pauk ish-veh kelek, heh tra' au would nem-tor ish-veh tusok, hi maut k'ashiv na' wehk gad fi' shaht au would worla trasha ish-veh tvi-shal. Au drank wuh lo'uk deal t' brandy heh smoked maut heavily, tonk'peh au would gla-tor rai shila'es heh did ri aitlun sovek t'hylara, ri kauk ish-veh sha' sa-kai. "au didn't kashek me; svi' kla-min, au nem-tor wuh fancy tor me, na' na' wuh wak lu gla-tor ish-veh me wuh'rak i vesh' wuh youngster t' leh-dah il ni. Nash would nam-tor svi' wuh tevun 1878, po' au had vesh' ohkuh il naukuh tevun svi' england. Au eit'jae t'nash-veh sa-mekh tor kal-tor me ha-tor k' ish-veh heh au vesh' maut ves tor me svi' ish-veh yut. Lu au vesh' sober au nam-tor-tor tor nam-tor tishau t' mavaun nesh-kur heh yon-kur heh draughts k' me, heh au would tor me ish-veh representative fi' k' wuh dvinsu heh k' wuh tradespeople, ni ik k' wuh wak ik i vesh' leh-sheh i vesh' ved trensu t' wuh kelek. I potau ek' wuh tal-muv heh kupi hal-tor wilat i tishau heh tor ra i tishau, ni wu u' i did ri ertau ish-veh svi' ish-veh awek'es. Tra' vesh' veh singular kaulauf, however, na' au had wuh single tvi-shal, wuh lumber-tvi-shal abru among wuh fik tvi-shal, if vesh' invariably klacha, heh if au would worla permit either me il sovek-veh else tor svi-tor. K' wuh sa-kan's curiosity i ma peeped k'fai wuh keyhole, tonk'peh i vesh' worla kup tor gla-tor weht do such wuh tershaya t' hinek lap-fek heh uzh'a'lek u' would nam-tor gishu svi' such wuh tvi-shal. "veh dayit vesh' svi' march, 1883a nuhm k' wuh k'shatri stamp ti fi-tor wuh pasu svi' khom t' wuh shal-lan's math. Ish-veh vesh' ri wuh tsuri vel na' ish-veh tor poprah nuhm, na' ish-veh dun vesh' ek' vlitau svi' pok donku, heh au had rai t'hylara t' sovek wihfelau. 's' india!' leralmin-tor au u' au nem-tor ish-veh abru, 'pondicherry postmark! Ra mokuhlek nash nam-tor?' sharu ish-veh hurriedly, si' tra' spen-tor kaukuh pi' psethau zhar-kur pips, if lates-tor ne' fi-tor ish-veh math. I began tor abru'teruklar-ru'lut na' nash, tonk'peh wuh abru'teruklar-ru'lut vesh' kwul-tor s' t'nash-veh bru-lar na' wuh glan t' ish-veh limuk. Ish-veh bru had tevan-tor, ish-veh bezhun vesh' protruding, ish-veh wadi wuh kur t' putty, heh au glared na' wuh envelope if au fam dvun meskarau svi' ish-veh trembling el'ru, 'k. K. K!' au shrieked, heh yi, 't'nash-veh oekon, t'nash-veh oekon, t'nash-veh sins ma overtaken me!' "'ra nam-tor ish-veh, sa-kuk?' i maf-tor. "'tevakh, ' leralmin-tor au, heh rising s' wuh pasu au retired tor ish-veh tvi-shal, leaving me palpitating k' horror. I nem-tor abru wuh envelope heh gla-tor scrawled svi' yon-kur neshuk fi-tor wuh tvik pi'rala, aishan abru' wuh lag, wuh nuhm k rehkuh wak ashiv-tor. Tra' vesh' nothing else korsau wuh kaukuh psethau pips. Ra kupi nam-tor wuh utvau t' ish-veh overpowering vash? I losrak wuh asal-yem-pasu, heh u' i she-tor wuh stair i ragel-tor ish-veh coming ne' k' wuh hinek zhar-tor tal-muv, if bolau ma belonged tor wuh fik tvi-shal, svi' veh el'ru, heh wuh pi' dvesh-tukh natuhn, spo' wuh cashbox, svi' wuh vath. "'au lau tor ra au spo', tonk'peh i'll pash au fam dvun, ' leralmin-tor au k' wuh oath. 'var-tor mary ik i dungau aitlun wuh yon svi' t'nash-veh tvi-shal tor-gad, heh satau ne' tor fordham, wuh horsham lawyer.' "i did u' au ordered, heh lu wuh lawyer lasha i vesh' ya'akash tor ash abru tor wuh tvi-shal. Wuh yon vesh' yontau brightly, heh svi' wuh grate tra' vesh' wuh shivak t' nesh-kur, fluffy vitush, u' t' yontau dun, du' wuh dvesh-tukh natuhn lam-tor tu'ash heh herbosh be' ish-veh. U' i glanced na' wuh natuhn i pubeglanau, k' wuh palikaya, ik fi-tor wuh lid vesh' hish-tor wuh abralash k if i had telv-tor svi' wuh asal fi-tor wuh envelope. "'i istaya du, john, ' leralmin-tor t'nash-veh sa-kuk, 'tor toglantausu t'nash-veh dungi. I trasha t'nash-veh estate, k' ek' its advantages heh ek' its disadvantages, tor t'nash-veh sa-kai, ish-veh sa-mekh, whence ish-veh dungi, rai vet, tev-tor tor du. Kuv du mokuhlek tizh-tor ish-veh svi' sochya, muhl heh rom! Kuv du talal du fam yehat, nem-tor t'nash-veh na'shikh, t'nash-veh sa-kan, heh trasha ish-veh tor ish-veh deadliest nemut. Ni'droi'ik nar-tor tor mazhiv-kur-tor du such wuh dahkuh-rihkau vel, tonk'peh i mokuhlek't leralmin ra da-tor vel nam-tor going tor nem-tor. Kindly glat wuh dun wilat mr. Fordham gluvau du.' "i signed wuh dun u' khartau, heh wuh lawyer nem-tor ish-veh maf k' ish-veh. Wuh singular incident tor, u' du lau nah-tor, wuh deepest impression fi-tor me, heh i pondered abru' ish-veh heh da-tor ish-veh kanok yut svi' t'nash-veh kashek rik' hasu kup tor tor sovek-vel t' ish-veh. Wi i kupi ri hutau ska' wuh vague olaya t' dread if ish-veh losrak za', hi wuh kashan grew lehkuh keen u' wuh wehk gad be' dvun-tor heh nothing pavesh-tor tor ertau wuh tsuri routine t' etwel ha-tor. Kupi gla-tor nash-veh wuh rubah svi' t'nash-veh sa-kuk, however. Au drank weht do ek'wak, heh au vesh' lehkuh vul-tor na' sovek wihfelau t' shila'es. Danik t' ish-veh wak au would spend svi' ish-veh tvi-shal, k' wuh svep klacha fi-tor wuh svi'udish, tonk'peh sometimes au would sasarlah svi' wuh wihfelau t' drunken frenzy heh would thorau s' wuh kelek heh bezhun-masu pa' wuh bah-ker k' wuh revolver svi' ish-veh el'ru, screaming si' ik au vesh' kwes t' rai sasu, heh ik au vesh' ri tor nam-tor cooped abru, spo' wuh sheep svi' wuh pen, k' sasu il e'shua. Lu aifa fal nunau vesh' abru', however, au would rush tumultuously svi' na' wuh svep heh klachek heh mofek ish-veh za' ish-veh, spo' wuh sasu vi mokuhlek brazen ish-veh si' rai longer tehnat wuh vash if ti na' wuh gir t' ish-veh soul. Na' such wak ki'gla-tor nash-veh ish-veh limuk, kauk fi' wuh samu gad, glisten k' masu'es, u' hi ish-veh vesh' uzh ashenau s' wuh basin. "muhl, tor sarlah tor wuh shaht t' wuh tukh, mr. Holmes, heh ri tor abuse ish-veh tranush, tra' sarlah wuh mu-yor lu au tor veh t' eifa drunken sallies s' if au worla sarlah pla'. Etek afer-tor ish-veh, lu etek went tor psthan na' ish-veh, limuk ne'le svi' wuh pi' yar-kur-scummed patra, if ti na' wuh ash'ya t' wuh bah-ker. Tra' vesh' rai glat t' sovek khrash, heh wuh masu vesh' tonk'peh dahkuh ash'ya glu, ni ik wuh jury, having fudau tor ish-veh fainu risvitan'es, katau svi' wuh verdict t' 'suicide.' tonk'peh i, vi fai-tor uf au winced s' wuh maut nahp t' tevakh, had mau ado tor persuade myself ik au had hal-tor s' ish-veh yut tor ragel-tor ish-veh. Wuh tukh be' dvun-tor, however, heh t'nash-veh sa-mekh svi-tor vi' mat t' wuh estate, heh t' ein 14,000, if ti tor ish-veh lit na' wuh kutra." "veh moment, " holmes interposed, "ish-veh star-krus nam-tor, i fa-glan-tor, veh t' wuh danik remarkable tor if i ma ek'wak shroi. Kal-tor me ma wuh kinuf t' wuh reception k' ish-veh sa-kuk t' wuh nuhm, heh wuh kinuf t' ish-veh supposed suicide." "wuh nuhm lasha fi' march 10, 1883. Ish-veh tevakh vesh' stehkuh wehk gad later, fi-tor wuh mu-yor t' lau 2nd." "nemaiyo. Pray proceed." "lu t'nash-veh sa-mekh nem-tor abru' wuh horsham veltra, au, na' t'nash-veh ya'akash, tor wuh tun-bosh linisaya t' wuh fik tvi-shal, if had vesh' kwon-hau-ov klacha abru. Etek afer-tor wuh dvesh-tukh natuhn tra', hi its tuhllar had vesh' vashau. Fi' wuh svi' wuh wein vesh' wuh dun label, k' wuh initials t' k. K. K. Ashiv-tor fi-tor ish-veh, heh 'nuhm, memoranda, receipts, heh wuh register' written ne'rak. Aifa, etek presume, indicated wuh malat t' wuh dun if had vesh' vashau k' shal-lan openshaw. Na' wuh shom, tra' vesh' nothing t' mau importance svi' wuh fik tvi-shal korsau wuh lo'uk wehk scattered dun heh pitoh-dunap kuvish fi-tor t'nash-veh sa-kuk's ha'kiv svi' america. Ein t' au vesh' t' wuh t'naehm wak heh gluvau ik au had ovsoh ish-veh gu-vam muhl heh had borne wuh repute t' wuh kyi'i ask'ersu. Vath vesh' t' wuh kinuf du' wuh reconstruction t' wuh southern fupa s', heh vesh' mostly concerned k' politics, na' au had evidently taken wuh karik krus svi' opposing wuh la'y-sa'haf politicians vi had vesh' satau ne' s' wuh desh'rak. "muhl, ish-veh vesh' wuh palikaya t' '84 lu t'nash-veh sa-mekh sarlah tor ha-tor na' horsham, heh ek' went u' muhl u' tor-yehat k' etek abi' wuh january t' '85. Fi' wuh fourth gad po' wuh uzh tevun i puzhu-tor t'nash-veh sa-mekh mazhiv-kur-tor wuh nasik maf t' ak'wikmun u' etek hayal-tor teretuhr na' wuh asal-yem-pasu. Tra' au vesh', sitting k' wuh newly tu'ash envelope svi' veh el'ru heh kaukuh psethau zhar-kur pips svi' wuh outstretched ku t' wuh vath veh. Au had kwon-hau-ov abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor na' ra au puvutau t'nash-veh cock-heh-bull var pa' wuh shal-lan, tonk'peh au glazhau maut pahth-tor heh puzzled i' ik wuh ka vel had sarlah fi-tor himself. "'po, ra fi' terra tor nash tvai, john?' au stammered. "t'nash-veh khaf-spol had da-tor tor ras-tukh. 'ish-veh nam-tor k. K. K, ' leralmin-tor i. "au glazhau svi'udish wuh envelope. 'ni ish-veh nam-tor, ' au maf-tor. 'la' nam-tor wuh maut nuhm. Tonk'peh ra nam-tor nash written abru' au?' "'shitau wuh dun fi' wuh sundial, ' i telv-tor, peeping abru' ish-veh tipan. "'ra dun? Ra sundial?' au ya'akash. "'wuh sundial svi' wuh bah-ker. Tra' nam-tor rai vath, ' leralmin-tor i; 'tonk'peh wuh dun bolau nam-tor eifa ik nam-tor vashau.' "'pooh!' leralmin-tor au, gripping lerash na' ish-veh courage. 'etek nam-tor svi' wuh civilised solektra la', heh etek mokuhlek't ma tomfoolery t' nash ves. Wilat tor wuh vel sarlah s'?' "'s' dundee, ' i kilko-tor, glancing na' wuh postmark. "'ein preposterous practical kha'wal, ' leralmin-tor au. 'ra ma i tor tor k' sundials heh dun? I dungau nem-tor rai beglanau t' such nonsense.' "'i dang certainly stariben tor wuh police, ' i leralmin-tor. "'heh nam-tor abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor na' na' t'nash-veh kusut-tor. Nothing t' wuh wihfelau.' "'yi kal-tor me tor ni?' "'rai, i zadau du. I skil-tor't ma wuh fuss tor pa' such nonsense.' "ish-veh vesh' svi' vain tor gyirm'i k' ish-veh, na' au vesh' wuh maut obstinate sasu. I went pa', however, k' wuh khaf-spol if vesh' bosh t' forebodings. "fi' wuh wuh gad po' wuh coming t' wuh nuhm t'nash-veh sa-mekh went s' ha-kel tor yaret wuh hinek t'hy'la t' ish-veh, tra-lan freebody, vi nam-tor svi' a'fic t' veh t' wuh forts fi-tor portsdown kunel. I vesh' glad ik au dang hal-tor, na' ish-veh seemed tor me ik au vesh' weh-irak s' tehvar lu au vesh' maf s' ha-kel. Svi' ik, however, i vesh' svi' lafosh. Fi-tor wuh dahr gad t' ish-veh absence i poprah wuh telegram s' wuh tra-lan, imploring me tor sarlah na' wuh'wak. T'nash-veh sa-mekh had tevan-tor abru' veh t' wuh glu gav-pits if abound svi' wuh neighbourhood, heh vesh' lying senseless, k' wuh zarahk-tor grat. I hurried tor ish-veh, tonk'peh au be' dvun-tor maf rik' having ek'wak recovered ish-veh hokni'es. Au had, u' ish-veh saudau, vesh' returning s' fareham svi' wuh twilight, heh u' wuh shasol vesh' ri-fainu tor ish-veh, heh wuh gav-pit unfenced, wuh jury had rai vaunah svi' bringing svi' wuh verdict t' 'tevakh s' ur'kif aisha.' carefully u' i linisau kanok kla-min tersau k' ish-veh tevakh, i vesh' unable tor talal sovek-vel if kupi suggest wuh idea t' riyeht-staya. Tra' vesh' rai glat t' khrash, rai footmarks, rai robbery, rai vipladau t' ri-fainusu having vesh' gla-tor fi-tor wuh fau-yut. Heh wi i bolaya ri var-tor du ik t'nash-veh kashek vesh' irak s' na' ease, heh ik i vesh' muhl-nigh ac'ruth ik ein flalik besau had vesh' woven pauk ish-veh. "svi' nash sinister yut vesht sarlah nash-veh vi' t'nash-veh inheritance. Du dungi ya'akash me po i did ri sashitau t' ish-veh? I kilko-srashiv, fai'ei i vesh' muhl convinced ik etwel troubles vesh' svi' ein yut nerik fi-tor wuh incident svi' t'nash-veh sa-kuk's ha'kiv, heh ik wuh tehvar would nam-tor u' pressing svi' veh kelek u' svi' wuh'ashiv. "ish-veh vesh' svi' january, '85, ik t'nash-veh ri donku-tor sa-mekh ragel-tor ish-veh shaht, heh dahkuh tevun heh ohkuh tevun-krus ma veshau opi' yi. Du' ik wak i ma ha-tor kunling na' horsham, heh i had palikau tor rok ik nash curse had be' dvun-tor maf s' wuh skan, heh ik ish-veh had shahtau k' wuh kim-shah generation. I had palikau tor nem-tor comfort nuh' ak, however; za-gad asal wuh salur tevan-tor svi' wuh maut shid svi' if ish-veh had sarlah fi-tor t'nash-veh sa-mekh." wuh nu'ri sasu nem-tor s' ish-veh waistcoat wuh crumpled envelope, heh turning tor wuh pasu au hutau si' fi-tor ish-veh kaukuh pi' psethau zhar-kur pips. "nash nam-tor wuh envelope, " au fator. "wuh postmark nam-tor londoneastern dahsaya. K'svi nam-tor wuh maut zhit if vesh' fi-tor t'nash-veh sa-mekh's kim-shah skladan: 'k. K. K.'; heh yi 'shitau wuh dun fi' wuh sundial.'" "ra ma du ovsoh?" ya'akash holmes. "nothing." "nothing?" "tor var-tor wuh yeht'es"au sank ish-veh limuk vi' ish-veh wonil, wan-kur el'ru"i ma olau helpless. I ma olau spo' veh t' eifa ri donku-tor rabbits lu wuh oluhk nam-tor writhing na' ish-veh. I seem tor nam-tor svi' wuh ruskaraya t' ein resistless, inexorable ek'rasah, if rai fa-glan heh rai precautions mokuhlek klashausu tehnat." "tut! Tut!" maf-tor sherlock holmes. "du bolau bae'cok, sasu, il du nam-tor pakik. Nothing tonk'peh tepul mokuhlek korsau du. Nash nam-tor rai wak na' despair." "ki'gla-tor nash-veh wuh police." "ah!" "tonk'peh au shroi tor t'nash-veh var k' wuh abru'teruklar-ru'lut. I am convinced ik wuh inspector has shidau wuh opinion ik wuh nuhm nam-tor ek' practical kha'wal, heh ik wuh deaths t' t'nash-veh relations vesh' really kisheya, u' wuh jury fupa s', heh vesh' ri tor nam-tor tersau k' wuh warnings." holmes hutau ish-veh clenched el'ru svi' wuh sov. "incredible imbecility!" au maf-tor. "au ma, however, kal-tor me wuh policeman, vi lau hafau svi' wuh kelek k' me." "has au sarlah k' du tor-mu-yor?" "rai. Ish-veh zek vesh' tor stay svi' wuh kelek." va'ashiv holmes raved svi' wuh sov. "po did sarlah du tor me?" au leralmin-tor, "heh, abru' ek', po did du ri sarlah na' wuh'wak?" "i did ri fai-tor. Ish-veh vesh' goh tor-gad ik i stariben tor tra-lan prendergast pa' t'nash-veh troubles heh vesh' na'shikhau k' ish-veh tor sarlah tor du." "ish-veh nam-tor really dahkuh gad opi' du had wuh nuhm. Etek dang ma bae'cok fa' nash. Du ma rai further evidence, i suppose, do ik if du ma shitau fa' usno suggestive detail if lau gol'nev etek?" "tra' nam-tor veh vel, " leralmin-tor john openshaw. Au rummaged svi' ish-veh tor-pal abru'lik, heh, bestan si' wuh krus t' discoloured, pla-kur-tinted dun, au laid ish-veh si' fi-tor wuh pasu. "i ma ein remembrance, " leralmin-tor au, "ik fi' wuh gad lu t'nash-veh sa-kuk yontau wuh dun i glantau ik wuh pi', unburned rihkal if ti svi' wuh vitush vesh' t' nash particular kur. I afer-tor nash single thalv fi-tor wuh lan-tol t' ish-veh tvi-shal, heh i am vul-tor tor nah-tor ik ish-veh lau nam-tor veh t' wuh dun if has, sos'eh, nuv-tor si' s' among wuh vath, heh svi' ik yut has stron-tor vashaya. Mesakh wuh mention t' pips, i ri tor gla-tor ik ish-veh gol-tor etek mau. I nah-tor myself ik ish-veh nam-tor wuh thalv s' ein awek gad-dunap. Wuh kitaun nam-tor undoubtedly t'nash-veh sa-kuk's." holmes dvun-tor wuh ha'gelek, heh etek fi' keh'sei abru' wuh thalv t' dun, if gluvau k' its ragged rihk ik ish-veh had indeed vesh' torn s' wuh dunap. Ish-veh vesh' headed, "march, 1869, " heh ne'rak vesh' wuh zahalik enigmatical beglanau: "4th. Hudson sarlah. Ka hinek skaf. "7th. Eku wuh pips fi' mccauley, paramore, heh john swain t' st. Augustine. "9th. Mccauley pa'shu. "10th. John swain pa'shu. "12th. Yaretau paramore. Ek' muhl." "nemaiyo!" leralmin-tor holmes, folding abru wuh dun heh returning ish-veh tor etwel visitor. "heh i' du bolau fi' rai khrosahp pak-tor wuh'ashiv instant. Etek fam yehat spare wak kauk tor discuss ra du ma var-tor me. Du bolau prah ha-kel instantly heh bae'cok." "ra dungau i tor?" "tra' nam-tor tonk'peh veh vel tor tor. Ish-veh bolau nam-tor ovsoh na' wuh'wak. Du bolau shitau nash krus t' dun if du ma shown etek vi' wuh dvesh-tukh natuhn if du ma kethelvau. Du bolau isha shitau svi' wuh pitoh tor leralmin ik ek' wuh vath dun vesh' yontau k' ish-veh sa-kuk, heh ik nash nam-tor wuh goh veh if hafau. Du bolau seo'a ik svi' such zhit u' dungi lesh conviction k' au. Having ovsoh nash, du bolau na' wuh'wak shitau wuh natuhn si' fi-tor wuh sundial, u' khartau. Tor du ken-tor?" "entirely." "ri tor nah-tor t' revenge, il sovek-vel t' wuh wihfelau, na' la'. Wuh wuh'rak consideration nam-tor tor snem-tor wuh pressing tehvar if nan-tor du. Wuh dahr nam-tor tor pa'shik abru wuh mystery heh tor taflau wuh guilty parties." Heh, abru' ek', nem-tor tun t' yourself svi' wuh meanwhile, na' i ri tor nah-tor ik tra' mokuhlek nam-tor wuh vet ik du nam-tor threatened k' wuh maut yeht heh imminent tehvar. Uf tor du hal-tor pla'?" "k' ranau s' waterloo." "ish-veh nam-tor ri wi naukuh. Wuh yut dungi nam-tor crowded, ni i sahrafel ik du lau nam-tor svi' ek'manek. Heh wi du fam yehat klashausu yourself nuh' closely." "i am armed." "ik nam-tor muhl. Tor-morrow i dungau eku tor ar'kadan fi-tor ish-veh nuf." "dungau gla-tor nash-veh du na' horsham, yi?" I dungau nem-tor ish-veh na'shikh svi' kanok particular." au hutau el'ru k' etek heh nem-tor ish-veh trasha. S'udish wuh salan fam dvun shei heh wuh sov-masu splashed heh lates-tor tehnat wuh krani. Nash flekh, kwai var seemed ki' sarlah tor etek s' svi' wuh mad elementsblown svi' fi-tor etek spo' wuh thalv t' masutra-vedik svi' wuh galeand i' tor ma vesh' reabsorbed k' au wuh'wak weht. Vi nam-tor nash k. K. K, heh po tor au pursue nash unhappy skan?" sherlock holmes a'ing ish-veh bezhun heh shitau ish-veh kar-nef fi-tor wuh kar t' ish-veh ku-san, k' ish-veh ozh-um teretuhr. "wuh tangu reasoner, " au remarked, "would, lu au had wuh'wak vesh' shown wuh single kla-min svi' ek' its bearings, deduce s' ish-veh ri goh ek' wuh naf-elakh t' pavek if pufulag-tor abru tor ish-veh tonk'peh isha ek' wuh results if would zahal-tor s' ish-veh. U' cuvier kupi correctly kethelvau wuh bosh aushfa k' wuh contemplation t' wuh single hinek, ni wuh observer vi has thoroughly ken-tor veh naf svi' wuh weizehl t' incidents dang nam-tor kup tor accurately fupa s' ek' wuh vath ones, fi' fa' heh po'. Etek ma ri wi ruskarau wuh results if wuh utvau sa'awek mokuhlek attain tor. Wat lau nam-tor kilau svi' wuh orenau if ma hertak-tor ek' eifa vi ma sought wuh kilkaya k' wuh mamuk t' ish-veh kash-ral. Tor lesh wuh tanaf, however, tor its k'lek ralash, ish-veh nam-tor bolayatik ik wuh reasoner dang nam-tor kup tor utilise ek' wuh kla-min if ma sarlah tor ish-veh fai-tukh; heh nash svi' itself implies, u' du dungi readily gla-tor, wuh mat t' ek' fai-tukh, if, kauk svi' aifa gad t' elik education heh encyclopæskaf, nam-tor wuh somewhat ritsuri accomplishment. Ish-veh nam-tor ri ni impossible, however, ik wuh sasu dang ma ek' fai-tukh if nam-tor kesik tor nam-tor useful tor ish-veh svi' ish-veh ar'kadan, heh nash i ma endeavoured svi' t'nash-veh nuf tor tor. Kuv i vokau rightly, du fi' veh occasion, svi' wuh lehkuh-mal gad t' etwel friendship, mesprah t'nash-veh grei svi' wuh maut precise fashion." "ha, " i kilko-tor, laughing. "ish-veh vesh' wuh singular kisev. Ven-dol-leralmin, yel-tal, heh politics vesh' pu'ulidau na' ris, i vokau. Kastik-tal vuhnayek, solektra-tal profound u' fudau wuh vral-kurau s' sovek shal k'svi kau-leh miles t' kahr, meil-tal rivitanik, vukhut-tal unsystematic, sensational kitau-tanaf heh tr'y'kak vipladau wuhinik, violin-hahf, boxer, swordsman, lawyer, heh shal-poisoner k' cocaine heh tobacco. Eifa, i nah-tor, vesh' wuh nen sfekau t' t'nash-veh nisaya." holmes wa'limatau na' wuh kim-shah item. "muhl, " au leralmin-tor, "i leralmin i', u' i leralmin-tor yi, ik wuh sasu dang potau ish-veh pi' shi'nahp-fik tvi-shal stocked k' ek' wuh furniture ik au nam-tor kesik tor nam-tor-tor, heh wuh shom au mokuhlek shitau maf svi' wuh lumber-tvi-shal t' ish-veh shi'dunap, wilat au mokuhlek prah ish-veh kuv au aitlu ish-veh. I', na' such wuh nuf u' wuh veh if has vesh' submitted tor etek tor-mu-yor, etek bolaya certainly tor muster ek' etwel resources. Kindly el'ru me ne' wuh nuhm k t' wuh american encyclopædia if lam-tor fi-tor wuh nef be' du. Nemaiyo. I' kal-tor etek panah-tor wuh situation heh gla-tor ra lau nam-tor deduced s' ish-veh. Svi' wuh wuh'rak shi, etek lau palikaya k' wuh karik presumption ik shal-lan openshaw had ein maut karik utvau na' leaving america. Sasu na' ish-veh wak t' ha'kiv ri tor rubah ek' ish-veh es'merka heh di'kizh willingly wuh sem-rik-tor ek'nosh t' florida na' wuh lonely ha'kiv t' wuh eingelsu provincial kahr. Ish-veh mairik ashaya t' awek'es svi' england suggests wuh idea ik au vesh' svi' pthak t' ein-veh il vel, ni etek lau ngiq'e u' wuh working ul-wihka ik ish-veh vesh' pthak t' ein-veh il vel if drove ish-veh s' america. U' tor ra ish-veh vesh' au ptha, etek mokuhlek goh deduce ik k' panahik wuh formidable nuhm if vesh' poprah k' himself heh ish-veh successors. Did du remark wuh postmarks t' eifa nuhm?" "wuh wuh'rak vesh' s' pondicherry, wuh dahr s' dundee, heh wuh wuh s' london." "s' she'rak london. Ra tor du deduce s' ik?" "au nam-tor ek' seaports. Ik wuh kitausu vesh' fi' dohn t' wuh hali." "marom. Etek ma already wuh clue. Tra' mokuhlek nam-tor rai vet ik wuh probabilitythe karik probabilityis ik wuh kitausu vesh' fi' dohn t' wuh hali. Heh i' kal-tor etek panah-tor wuh'ashiv sfek. Svi' wuh nuf t' pondicherry, stehkuh wehk gad veshau svi' wuh nan heh its fulfilment, svi' dundee ish-veh vesh' goh ein rehkuh il kehkuh gad. Tor ik suggest sovek-vel?" "wuh greater ir tor haolvaya." "tonk'peh wuh nuhm had isha wuh greater ir tor sarlah." "yi i ri tor gla-tor wuh sfek." Ish-veh glazhau u' kuv au kwon-hau-ov satau ish-veh singular warning il token fa' au lu starting fi-tor ish-veh skrol. Gla-tor du uf sahris wuh deed zahal-tor wuh glat lu sarlah ish-veh s' dundee.
