I nah-tor ik eifa stehkuh wehk gad represented wuh natyan svi' wuh sakat-masu-hali if katau wuh nuhm heh wuh masu-halovaun hali if katau wuh kitausu." "ish-veh nam-tor tor-yehat." "weht do ik. Ish-veh nam-tor yesik. Heh i' gla-tor du wuh tevalik urgency t' nash uzh nuf, heh po i urged nu'ri openshaw tor yuzhat. Wuh salur has kwon-hau-ov tevan-tor na' wuh shaht t' wuh wak if ish-veh would nem-tor wuh senders tor haolvaya wuh ir. Tonk'peh nash-veh sarlah s' london, heh therefore etek fam yehat tum-tor fi-tor vohtaya." "rom oekon!" i maf-tor. "ra mokuhlek ish-veh tvai, nash relentless persecution?" "wuh dun if openshaw lesh nam-tor obviously t' bolik importance tor wuh person il persons svi' wuh masu-halovaun-hali. I nah-tor ik ish-veh nam-tor ved pa'shik ik tra' bolau nam-tor weht do veh t' au. Wuh single sasu kupi ri ma fitor dahkuh deaths svi' such wuh yut u' tor tehs-tor wuh tevanu-talsu's jury. Tra' bolau ma vesh' several svi' ish-veh, heh au bolau ma vesh' sasu t' resource heh determination. Ish-veh dun au tvai ki', nam-tor wuh holder t' au vi ish-veh lau. Svi' nash yut gla-tor du k. K. K. Ceases tor nam-tor wuh initials t' wuh wuhsu heh shetau wuh badge t' wuh shila'es." "tonk'peh t' ra shila'es?" "ma du worla" leralmin-tor sherlock holmes, bending fa'rak heh sinking ish-veh spes"ma du worla puzhu-tor t' wuh ku klux klan?" "i worla ma." holmes da-tor abru' wuh mor t' wuh dunap fi-tor ish-veh mal-nef. "la' ish-veh nam-tor, " leralmin-tor au presently: "'ku klux klan. Wuh ahm derived s' wuh fanciful resemblance tor wuh ralash torvau k' cocking wuh kar-pohshayek. Nash terrible tsat shila'es vesh' shidau k' ein ex-confederate ask'ersu svi' wuh southern fupa s' po' wuh civil t'naehm, heh ish-veh rapidly shidau local khlup svi' natya krus t' wuh shasol, notably svi' tennessee, louisiana, wuh carolinas, georgia, heh florida. Its tepul vesh' nam-tor-tor na' political lof, principally na' wuh terrorising t' wuh negro voters heh wuh murdering heh driving s' wuh shasol t' eifa vi vesh' opposed tor its zan-tor. Its outrages vesh' usually preceded k' wuh warning satau tor wuh pu'ulidau sasu svi' ein fantastic tonk'peh paik naglanshau shapea sprig t' oak-mor svi' ein krus, melon nei il zhar-kur pips svi' vath. Fi' receiving nash wuh shi-kar-tor lau either openly abjure ish-veh former yut, il lau hash-tor s' wuh shasol. Kuv au braved wuh tukh si', tevakh would unfailingly sarlah fi-tor ish-veh, heh usually svi' ein flekh heh unforeseen manner. Ni buhfik vesh' wuh organisation t' wuh shila'es, heh ni systematic its methods, ik tra' nam-tor hardly wuh nuf fi-tor vipladau wilat sovek sasu navau svi' braving ish-veh k' impunity, il svi' if sovek t' its outrages vesh' traced ha-kel tor wuh perpetrators. Na' ein tevun wuh organisation flourished svi' spite t' wuh urgam t' wuh kaunshuk fupa s' government heh t' wuh weh-rom mohrn t' wuh shila svi' wuh khu'rak. Eventually, svi' wuh tevun 1869, wuh dvun rather suddenly neshau, hi tra' ma vesh' sporadic outbreaks t' wuh ka wihfelau opi' ik kinuf.' "du dungi glantau, " leralmin-tor holmes, laying ne' wuh ral'es, "ik wuh sudden breaking abru t' wuh shila'es vesh' coincident k' wuh disappearance t' openshaw s' america k' ish-veh dun. Ish-veh lau muhl ma vesh' aishan heh daya. Ish-veh nam-tor rai wonder ik au heh ish-veh skan ma ein t' wuh weht implacable tam'a fi-tor ish-veh yut. Du mokuhlek ken-tor ik nash register heh gad-dunap lau implicate ein t' wuh wuh'rak sasu svi' wuh khu'rak, heh ik tra' lau nam-tor wehk vi dungi ri yuk hagik na' mu-yor abi' ish-veh nam-tor recovered." "yi wuh thalv gla-tor etek" "nam-tor such u' etek lau gish. Ish-veh sahr-tor, kuv i vokau gas'rak, 'satau wuh pips tor wuh, b, heh c'ik nam-tor, satau wuh shila'es's warning tor au. Yi tra' nam-tor successive svin ik wuh heh b pa'shu, il losrak wuh shasol, heh t'forti ik c vesh' yaretau, k', i pthak, wuh sinister result na' c. Muhl, i nah-tor, hassu, ik etek lau kal-tor ein ta'hal vi' nash gu'gelik shi, heh i dva-tor ik wuh goh pavesh nu'ri openshaw has svi' wuh meantime nam-tor tor tor ra i ma var-tor ish-veh. Tra' nam-tor nothing weht tor nam-tor leralmin-tor il tor nam-tor ovsoh tor-mu-yor, ni el'ru me abru' t'nash-veh violin heh kal-tor etek ar'kadan tor yen-tor na' ulef wuh wadan wuh miserable igen-va heh wuh fam dvun weht miserable yut t' etwel katravahsu sasu." ish-veh had pa'shu svi' wuh asal, heh wuh yel vesh' shining k' wuh nessau ugel'es k'fai wuh neik-ha'khlup veil if geldau abru' wuh lo'uk kahr. Sherlock holmes vesh' already na' asal-yem lu vesht sarlah nash-veh ne'. "du dungi tobeg me na' ri waiting na' du, " leralmin-tor au; "i ma, i fa-glan-tor, wuh maut toranik gad fa' me svi' looking vi' nash nuf t' nu'ri openshaw's." "ra ash-tor dungi du nem-tor?" i ya'akash. "ish-veh dungi maut mau nerau fi-tor wuh results t' t'nash-veh wuh'rak inquiries. I lau ma tor hal-tor ne' tor horsham, po' ek'." "du dungi ri hal-tor tra' wuh'rak?" "rai, i dungau palikau k' wuh kahr. Aishan mokov wuh kus-vakh heh wuh maid dungi katau abru ish-veh mon." u' i bek-tor, i abertau wuh unopened newspaper s' wuh pasu heh glanced t'nash-veh bezhun abru' ish-veh. Ish-veh shom-tor fi-tor wuh heading if satau wuh chill tor t'nash-veh khaf-spol. "holmes, " i maf-tor, "du nam-tor nuh' tab-ma." "ah!" leralmin-tor au, laying ne' ish-veh cup, "i ptha u' mau. Uf vesh' ish-veh ovsoh?" au stariben calmly, tonk'peh kupi gla-tor nash-veh ik au vesh' deeply dvun-tor. "t'nash-veh bezhun kum-tor wuh ahm t' openshaw, heh wuh heading 'tragedy be' waterloo mesut.' la' nam-tor wuh khrosahp: "'svi' naukuh heh lehkuh kim-shah mu-yor police-constable fas-tor, t' wuh h dahsaya, fi' gu-vam be' waterloo mesut, puzhu-tor wuh maf na' gol'nev heh wuh splash svi' wuh masu. Wuh mu-yor, however, vesh' extremely gu'gelik heh stormy, ni ik, svi' spite t' wuh gol'nev t' several passers-k', ish-veh vesh' ved impossible tor daya wuh rescue. Wuh vikayek, however, vesh' putan-tor, heh, k' wuh mamuk t' wuh masu-police, wuh ak'shem vesh' eventually recovered. Ish-veh skan-tor tor nam-tor ik t' wuh nu'ri gentleman t'vi ahm, u' ish-veh saudau s' wuh envelope if vesh' afer-tor svi' ish-veh abru'lik, vesh' john openshaw, heh t'vi residence nam-tor be' horsham. Ish-veh nam-tor conjectured ik au lau ma vesh' hurrying ne' tor kum wuh kim-shah ranau s' waterloo wurzel, heh ik svi' ish-veh haste heh wuh mairik mu'khlup'es au din-tor ish-veh yut heh lates-tor abru' wuh rihk t' veh t' wuh pi' landing-shitau na' pilash steamboats. "ik dash-tor t'nash-veh pride, watson, " au leralmin-tor na' kim-shah. "ish-veh nam-tor wuh petty olaya, rai vet, tonk'peh ish-veh dash-tor t'nash-veh pride. Ish-veh shetau wuh personal tukh k' me i', heh, kuv oekon satau me muhl'es, i dungau eku t'nash-veh el'ru fi-tor nash gang. Ik au dang sarlah tor me na' gol'nev, heh ik i dang satau ish-veh maf tor ish-veh tevakh!" au sprang s' ish-veh ku-san heh sahr-tor pa' wuh tvi-shal svi' uncontrollable agitation, k' wuh kluhvau fi-tor ish-veh sallow nak heh wuh nervous clasping heh unclasping t' ish-veh wu wonil el'ru. "rai; i dungau nam-tor t'nash-veh sha' police. "texas, i nah-tor." "i vesh' ri heh am ri sure if; tonk'peh i fai-tor ik wuh hali bolau ma wuh american tveshu." "ra yi?" "i pstha wuh dundee vipladau, heh lu i afer-tor ik wuh barque lone yel vesh' tra' svi' january, '85, t'nash-veh suspicion became wuh certainty. I yi inquired u' tor wuh hali if ti na' la' svi' wuh kif t' london." "ha?" "wuh lone yel had lasha la' kim-shah wehk gad. I went ne' tor wuh albert kif heh afer-tor ik she had vesh' taken ne' wuh pilash k' wuh lehkuh-mal mashen nash asal, homeward bound tor yartra. I wired tor gravesend heh oren-tor ik she had be' dvun-tor ein wak ago, heh u' wuh salan nam-tor easterly i ma rai vet ik she nam-tor i' vesht wuh goodwins heh ri maut irak s' wuh isle t' wight." "ra dungi du tor, yi?" "oh, i ma t'nash-veh el'ru fi-tor ish-veh. Au heh wuh dahkuh katelau, nam-tor u' i oren-tor, wuh goh salatik-pukeshta americans svi' wuh hali. Wuh vath nam-tor finns heh germans. I fai-tor, isha, ik au vesh' ek' rehkuh maf s' wuh hali kim-shah mu-yor. I had ish-veh s' wuh stevedore vi has vesh' loading ish-veh tusla. K' wuh wak ik ish-veh masu-halovaun-hali pulau yartra wuh sakat-masu-hali dungi ma lesh nash nuhm, heh wuh elakh dungi ma informed wuh police t' yartra ik aifa rehkuh gentlemen nam-tor badly aitlu la' fi-tor wuh falun t' riyeht-staya." tra' nam-tor ek'wak wuh lafot, however, svi' wuh buhfik laid t' komihn dotoran, heh wuh murderers t' john openshaw vesh' worla tor poprah wuh zhar-kur pips if would gluvaya au ik wuh'ashiv, u' cunning heh u' resolute u' themselves, vesh' fi-tor ish-veh yut. Maut wu heh maut severe vesh' wuh equinoctial karik salan ik tevun. Etek bek-tor wu na' ro'fori t' wuh lone yel t' yartra, tonk'peh rim ek'wak pulau etek. Etek did na' kim-shah zhu-tor ik ein-wilat irak si' svi' wuh atlantic wuh zarahk-tor harr-krus-lehk t' wuh masu-hali vesh' gla-tor swinging svi' wuh trough t' wuh pral, k' wuh nuhm "l. S." skrim-tor fi-tor ish-veh, heh ik nam-tor ek' if etek dungau ek'wak fai-tor t' wuh buk t' wuh lone yel. Vi. Wuh sasu k' wuh kuvoran-tor bru isa whitney, sa-kai t' wuh tab-ma elias whitney, d.d, principal t' wuh theological college t' st. George's, vesh' mau tessau tor opium. Wuh es'merka grew fi-tor ish-veh, u' i ken-tor, s' ein duhik freak lu au vesh' na' college; na' having telv-tor de quincey's kethelvaya t' ish-veh sahr-tor-tor heh kashan, au had drenched ish-veh tobacco k' laudanum svi' wuh attempt tor torvau wuh ka daya. Au afer-tor, u' ni wehk weht ma ovsoh, ik wuh practice nam-tor easier tor attain do tor prah rid t', heh na' wehk tevun au fator tor nam-tor wuh kafeh tor wuh ta'bek, wuh vel t' mingled horror heh pity tor ish-veh t'hylara heh tomasu. I mokuhlek gla-tor ish-veh i', k' kin-kur, pasty limuk, tevan-tor lids, heh pin-sfek glan-sharu, ek' huddled svi' wuh ku-san, wuh vashau heh ruin t' wuh thol sasu. Veh nightit vesh' svi' belaar, '89there sarlah wuh mokov tor t'nash-veh kus-vakh, pa' wuh wadan lu wuh sasu mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh'rak luvaya heh glances na' wuh wak-vel. I hayal-tor abru svi' t'nash-veh ku-san, heh t'nash-veh ko-telsu laid ish-veh og-lum-ar'kadan ne' svi' ish-veh lap heh tor wuh pi' limuk t' disappointment. "wuh hasausu!" leralmin-tor she. "du'll ma tor hal-tor si'." i groaned, na' i vesh' newly sarlah pla' s' wuh weary gad. Etek puzhu-tor wuh svep tu'ash, wuh zamu hurried zhit, heh yi sahris ash-tor fi-tor wuh linoleum. Etwel sha' svep flew tu'ash, heh wuh t'sai, clad svi' ein gu'gelik-kur-tor tukh, k' wuh nesh-kur veil, svi-tor wuh tvi-shal. "du dungi tobeg t'nash-veh calling ni tab-ma, " she began, heh yi, suddenly losing ish-veh shal-tash, she sahr-tor fa'rak, threw ish-veh kar pa' t'nash-veh ko-telsu's talu, heh sobbed fi-tor ish-veh tipan. "oh, i'm svi' such trouble!" she maf-tor; "i tor ni aitlun wuh pi' gol'nev." "po, " leralmin-tor t'nash-veh ko-telsu, pulling abru ish-veh veil, "ish-veh nam-tor kate whitney. Uf du startled me, kate! I had ri wuh idea vi du vesh' lu sarlah du svi'." "i didn't fai-tor ra tor tor, ni vesht sarlah nash-veh zehik tor du." ik vesh' kwon-hau-ov wuh yut. Sular vi vesh' svi' tushat sarlah tor t'nash-veh ko-telsu spo' kushel tor wuh masu-ha'zehl-kel. "ish-veh vesh' maut slor t' du tor sarlah. I', du bolau ma ein wine heh masu, heh hayal-tor la' comfortably heh var-tor etek ek' pa' ish-veh. Il dang du rather ik i satau james ska' tor sar-tak?" "oh, rai, rai! I aitlun wuh hassu's na'shikh heh gol'nev, nuh'. Ish-veh's pa' isa. Au has ri vesh' ha-kel na' dahkuh gad. I am ni koltha pa' ish-veh!" ish-veh vesh' ri wuh wuh'rak wak ik she had spoken tor etek t' ish-veh sa-telsu's trouble, tor me u' wuh hassu, tor t'nash-veh ko-telsu u' wuh hinek t'hy'la heh shi'oren besu. Etek soothed heh comforted ish-veh k' such zhit u' etek kupi talal. Did she fai-tor wilat ish-veh sa-telsu vesh'? Vesh' ish-veh tor-yehat ik etek kupi katau ish-veh pla' tor ish-veh? Ish-veh seems ik ish-veh vesh'. She had wuh surest ro'fori ik t' tab-ma au had, lu wuh nunau vesh' fi' ish-veh, tor nam-tor-tor t' wuh opium den svi' wuh dan-irak she'rak t' wuh kahr. Hitherto ish-veh orgies had kwon-hau-ov vesh' confined tor veh gad, heh au had sarlah pla', twitching heh zarahk-tor, svi' wuh khru. Tonk'peh i' wuh spell had vesh' fi-tor ish-veh ohkuh-heh-keh-leh wadan, heh au ti tra', doubtless among wuh dregs t' wuh kifau, eshan svi' wuh gisam il sleeping ska' wuh daya. Tra' au vesh' tor nam-tor afer-tor, she vesh' sure t' ish-veh, na' wuh mofek t' pi-maat-tukh, svi' upper swandam lane. Tonk'peh ra vesh' she tor tor? Uf kupi she, wuh nu'ri heh timid kosu, tor ish-veh yut vi' such wuh shi heh pluck ish-veh sa-telsu si' s' among wuh ruffians vi vikuvau ish-veh? Tra' vesh' wuh nuf, heh veling tra' vesh' tonk'peh veh yut s' ish-veh. Lau i ri escort ish-veh tor nash shi? Heh yi, u' wuh dahr nahp, po dang she sarlah na' ek'? I vesh' isa whitney's hasuk adviser, heh u' such i had vi-yumuk abru' ish-veh. I kupi khartau ish-veh weh-rom kuv i vesh' sa'awek. I ugau ish-veh fi' t'nash-veh zhit ik i would satau ish-veh ha-kel svi' wuh cab k'svi dahkuh wadan kuv au vesh' indeed na' wuh shi'yavekh if she had putan-tor me. Heh ni svi' lehkuh minutes i had losrak t'nash-veh armchair heh cheery sitting-tvi-shal za' me, heh vesh' speeding na'she'rak svi' wuh hansom fi' wuh flekh skrol, u' ish-veh seemed tor me na' wuh wak, hi wuh fa-wak goh kupi gluvaya uf flekh ish-veh vesh' tor nam-tor. Tonk'peh tra' vesh' rai lo'uk rihag'es svi' wuh wuh'rak skaf t' t'nash-veh adventure. Upper swandam lane nam-tor wuh vile alley lurking za' wuh pid wharves if zehl wuh desh'rak vla t' wuh pilash tor wuh she'rak t' london mesut. Svi' wuh slop-mahr-kel heh wuh gin-mahr-kel, betau k' wuh menal hash t' ash-tor leading ne' tor wuh nesh-kur haf spo' wuh ru'lut t' wuh tauk, i afer-tor wuh den t' if i vesh' svi' psthan. Ordering t'nash-veh cab tor bek-tor, i be' dvun-tor ne' wuh ash-tor, worn hollow svi' wuh centre k' wuh ceaseless tread t' drunken ash'ya; heh k' wuh ta'hal t' wuh flickering elmin-ha'gelek abru' wuh svep i afer-tor wuh kuhr heh tor t'nash-veh yut vi' wuh wu, neik tvi-shal, bali heh ras k' wuh khav-kur opium vuzh, heh terraced k' wooden berths, spo' wuh forecastle t' wuh emigrant hali. K'fai wuh gloom veh kupi dimly kum wuh glimpse t' ak'shem lying svi' flekh fantastic poses, ovalau tipan, keh'sei mal-nef, patam lehm-tor pla', heh chins pointing abru'le, k' la' heh tra' wuh gu'gelik, fam-lustre bezhun da-tor fi-tor wuh newcomer. S' wuh nesh-kur duv tra' glimmered pi' yon-kur da-kuv t' ta'hal, i' ugelik, i' faint, u' wuh yontau gisam waxed il waned svi' wuh yerak t' wuh mokev mev. Wuh danik ti ralash-fam, tonk'peh ein muttered tor themselves, heh vath variben teretuhr svi' wuh flekh, neik, monotonous spes, ish-veh conversation coming svi' gushes, heh yi suddenly tailing ska' vi' silence, tik mumbling si' ish-veh sha' nahp heh paying pi' heed tor wuh zhit t' ish-veh behsu. Na' wuh weh-irak shaht vesh' wuh pi' fas-nentu t' yontau yonol-tukh, be' if fi' wuh rehkuh-legged wooden stool tra' hayal-tor wuh ha-vol, wonil hinek sasu, k' ish-veh ahs resting fi-tor ish-veh dahkuh ozh-dukal, heh ish-veh kar-nef fi-tor ish-veh mal-nef, staring vi' wuh yon. U' i svi-tor, wuh sallow malay attendant had hurried abru k' wuh mev na' me heh wuh tanilau t' wuh ta'bek, beckoning me tor wuh herbosh berth. "nemaiyo. I ma ri sarlah tor stay, " leralmin-tor i. "tra' nam-tor wuh t'hy'la t' t'nash-veh la', mr. Isa whitney, heh i istaya tor stariben k' ish-veh." tra' vesh' wuh dvun heh wuh sporun s' t'nash-veh gas'rak, heh peering k'fai wuh gloom, vesht gla-tor nash-veh whitney, spoh, haggard, heh unkempt, staring si' na' me. "t'nash-veh oekon! Ish-veh's watson, " leralmin-tor au. Au vesh' svi' wuh pitiable fupa s' t' rolaya, k' kanok tor'tsu svi' wuh twitter. "i leralmin, watson, ra o'wak-vel nam-tor ish-veh?" "nearly leh-wun." "t' ra gad?" "t' gad, belaar 19th." "rom heavens! I nahp ish-veh vesh' gad. Ish-veh nam-tor gad. Ra d'du aitlun tor koltha wuh chap na'?" au sank ish-veh limuk fi-tor ish-veh kar heh began tor sob svi' wuh pid abralash tal-muv. "i var-tor du ik ish-veh nam-tor gad, sasu. Ish-veh ko-telsu has vesh' waiting nash dahkuh gad na' du. Du dang nam-tor kafusik t' yourself!" "ni i am. Tonk'peh du've prah rish-tor, watson, na' i ma goh vesh' la' wuh zamu wadan, rehkuh mev, kehkuh pipesi yen-tor uf wehk. Tonk'peh i'll hal-tor ha-kel k' du. I wouldn't koltha katepoor pi' kate. Mazhiv-kur-tor me ish-veh el'ru! Ma du wuh cab?" "ha, i ma veh waiting." "yi i dungau hal-tor svi' ish-veh. Tonk'peh i bolau owe vel. Talal ra i owe, watson. I am ek' ska' kur. I mokuhlek tor nothing na' myself." i lates-tor ne' wuh wonil tvur svi' wuh dahtau zehl t' sleepers, holding t'nash-veh esh tor potau si' wuh vile, stupefying panaz t' wuh ta'bek, heh looking pa' na' wuh khartausu. I glanced ne'. Au kupi goh ma sarlah s' wuh hinek sasu na' t'nash-veh vla, heh wi au hayal-tor i' u' absorbed u' ek'wak, maut wonil, maut wrinkled, keh'sei k' ya'shakhuv, wuh opium mev dangling ne' s' svi' ish-veh mal-nef, u' hi ish-veh had eku-tor svi' sheer lassitude s' ish-veh ozh. I nem-tor dahkuh ash-tor fa'rak heh glazhau pla'. Ish-veh nem-tor ek' t'nash-veh shal-tash tor prevent me s' breaking si' vi' wuh maf t' astonishment. Au had da-tor ish-veh pla' ni ik rim kupi gla-tor ish-veh tonk'peh i. Ish-veh shid had boshau si', ish-veh wrinkles vesh' hal-tor, wuh pasik bezhun had tabakau ish-veh yon, heh tra', sitting k' wuh yon heh grinning na' t'nash-veh ak'wikmun, vesh' rim vath do sherlock holmes. Au tor wuh slight dvunel tor me tor betaya ish-veh, heh instantly, u' au da-tor ish-veh limuk ulef pauk tor wuh apc'koik wuh'wak weht, subsided vi' wuh doddering, thal-lipped senility. "holmes!" i zhal-tor, "ra fi' terra nam-tor du doing svi' nash den?" "u' neik u' du mokuhlek, " au kilko-tor; "i ma marom kaluk. Kuv du would ma wuh lo'uk kindness tor prah rid t' ik sottish t'hy'la t' ish-veh i dang nam-tor exceedingly glad ki' wuh pi' variben k' du." "i ma wuh cab s'udish." "yi pray satau ish-veh ha-kel svi' ish-veh. Du lau safely sahrafel ish-veh, na' au saudau tor nam-tor nuh' limp tor prah vi' sovek mischief. I olau, however, ik lu whitney vesh' wuh'wak confined svi' wuh cab t'nash-veh skrol vesh' practically accomplished; heh na' wuh shom, i kupi ri istaya sovek-vel weh-rom do tor nam-tor katravah k' t'nash-veh t'hy'la svi' veh t' eifa singular adventures if vesh' wuh tsuri nosh t' ish-veh nam. Svi' wuh zamu minutes i had written t'nash-veh pitoh, vlitau whitney's dun, pufulag-tor ish-veh si' tor wuh cab, heh gla-tor ish-veh driven k'fai wuh mu'khlup'es. Svi' wuh maut pen wak wuh decrepit khlop had sasarlah s' wuh opium den, heh i vesh' walking ne' wuh yut k' sherlock holmes. Na' dahkuh yut au shuffled bi' k' wuh keh'sei pla' heh wuh uncertain ash'ya. Yi, glancing sahris pauk, au straightened himself si' heh thorau vi' wuh hearty nunau t' laughter. "i suppose, watson, " leralmin-tor au, "ik du glenonau ik i ma hau opium-smoking tor cocaine vipohshaya, heh ek' wuh vath pi' kobat'es fi' if du ma favoured me k' ish-veh hasuk zan-tor." "i vesh' certainly ak'wikmun tor talal du tra'." "tonk'peh ri weht ni do i tor talal du." "vesht sarlah nash-veh tor talal wuh t'hy'la." "heh i tor talal wuh nemut." "wuh nemut?" "ha; veh t' t'nash-veh malatik nemut, il, dungau i leralmin, t'nash-veh malatik shi-kar-tor. Briefly, watson, i am svi' wuh midst t' wuh maut remarkable inquiry, heh i ma rok-tor tor talal wuh clue svi' wuh incoherent ramblings t' aifa sots, u' i ma ovsoh fa' i'. Had i vesh' naglanshau svi' ik den t'nash-veh ha'kiv would ri ma vesh' don wuh wadan's purchase; na' i ma nam-tor-tor ish-veh fa' i' na' t'nash-veh sha' lof, heh wuh rascally lascar vi sahr-tor ish-veh has sworn tor ma vengeance fi-tor me. Du ri tor tvai ak'shem?" "ay, ak'shem, watson. Etek dang nam-tor don-ka sasu kuv etek had 1000 na' kanok ri donku-tor e'shua vi has vesh' ovsoh tor tevakh svi' ik den. Ish-veh nam-tor wuh vilest riyeht-staya-pash fi' wuh bosh riverside, heh i pthak ik neville st. Clair has svi-tor ish-veh worla tor trasha ish-veh weht. Tonk'peh etwel pash dang nam-tor la'." au shitau ish-veh dahkuh kehr-oth svi' ish-veh zud heh whistled shrillya glantokaya if vesh' kilko-tor k' wuh kahwa whistle s' wuh ir, zahal-tor shortly k' wuh rattle t' halek heh wuh clink t' jarel' hoofs. Mesakh ti wuh'ashiv pasik shi'kwai t' dok heh mortar, its silence pushau goh k' wuh ras, regular footfall t' wuh policeman, il wuh songs heh saul-tor t' ein belated party t' revellers. "ein tevun agoto nam-tor definite, svi' lau, 1884there sarlah tor lee wuh gentleman, neville st. Clair k' ahm, vi saudau ki' plenty t' donku. Au nem-tor wuh suk villa, laid si' wuh solektra maut nicely, heh ha-tor paik svi' rom style. K' degrees au tor t'hylara svi' wuh neighbourhood, heh svi' 1887 au telik wuh ko-fu t' wuh local brewer, k' ik au i' has dahkuh kanu. Au had rai occupation, tonk'peh vesh' interested svi' several apc'koik heh went vi' kahr u' wuh tor-go svi' wuh asal, returning k' wuh 5: 14 s' thorshun yut kanok mu-yor. Mr. St. Clair nam-tor i' reh-leh-stehkuh tevun t' ya'shakhuv, nam-tor wuh sasu t' temperate es'merka, wuh rom sa-telsu, wuh maut affectionate sa-mekh, heh wuh sasu vi nam-tor popular k' ek' vi fai-tor ish-veh. Clair went vi' kahr rather earlier do tsuri, remarking fa' au palikau ik au had dahkuh yauluhk kadvin-tor tor perform, heh ik au would katau ish-veh pi' sa-kan ha-kel wuh natuhn t' dok. Au pral-tor ish-veh el'ru." "tonk'peh ish-veh lau ma vesh' wuh maf t' ak'wikmun. Astonishment na' wuh ri-gishu glan t' du lau aishan ish-veh tor lehm abru ish-veh el'ru?" "ish-veh nam-tor tor-yehat." "heh du nahp au vesh' seshau pla'?" "au sasaudau ni suddenly." "au lau ma leaped pla'. Du did ri gla-tor sovek-veh else svi' wuh tvi-shal?" "rai, tonk'peh nash horrible sasu confessed tor having vesh' tra', heh wuh lascar vesh' na' wuh ash'ya t' wuh kaiden." "ved ni. Ish-veh sa-telsu, u' irak u' du kupi gla-tor, had ish-veh ordinary sai-vel fi'?" "tonk'peh rik' ish-veh hmoi'neks il tie. I distinctly gla-tor ish-veh sai-famik drahk." "had au ek'wak spoken t' swandam lane?" "worla." "had au ek'wak gluvau sovek glat t' having taken opium?" "worla." "nemaiyo, mrs. St. Clair. Eifa nam-tor wuh principal sfekau pa' if i istau tor nam-tor absolutely pa'shik. Etek dungau i' ma wuh pi' mu'yor-yem heh yi retire, na' etek lau ma wuh maut toranik gad tor-morrow." wuh suk heh kel'o dahtau-bedded tvi-shal had vesh' shitau na' etwel sashitaya, heh i vesh' sahris svi' wuh thalv, na' i vesh' weary po' t'nash-veh mu-yor t' adventure. Sherlock holmes vesh' wuh sasu, however, vi, lu au had wuh unsolved wat fi-tor ish-veh kashek, would hal-tor na' gad, heh kauk na' wuh wehk gad, rik' shom, turning ish-veh abru', rearranging ish-veh kla-min, looking na' ish-veh s' kanok sfek t' zan-tor abi' au had either fathomed ish-veh il convinced himself ik ish-veh faik vesh' insufficient. Ish-veh vesh' ak evident tor me ik au vesh' i' preparing na' wuh ek'-mu-yor sitting. Au nem-tor ska' ish-veh tor-pal heh waistcoat, shitau fi' wuh suk pla-kur sai-vel-tor-gown, heh yi czar-tor pa' wuh tvi-shal collecting trak s' ish-veh sar-tak heh an'kar s' wuh ku-san heh armchairs. K' aifa au torvau wuh wihfelau t' she'rakik divan, fi-tor if au perched himself tuhs-malik, k' wuh ounce t' shag tobacco heh wuh natuhn t' matches laid si' svi' khom t' ish-veh. Svi' wuh neik-ha'khlup ta'hal t' wuh ha'gelek vesht gla-tor nash-veh ish-veh sitting tra', wuh hinek briar mev svi' ish-veh bru-lar, ish-veh bezhun teslau vacantly fi-tor wuh teruk t' wuh abru-tol, wuh pla-kur vuzh tcha-tor abru s' ish-veh, ralash-fam, motionless, k' wuh ta'hal shining fi-tor ish-veh karik-eku aquiline features. Ni au hayal-tor u' i eku-tor ska' tor yuk, heh ni au hayal-tor lu wuh sudden khrasaya aisha me tor wake abru, heh i afer-tor wuh belaar yel shining vi' wuh ha-shal. Wuh mev vesh' fam dvun svi' ish-veh bru-lar, wuh vuzh fam dvun tcha-tor abru'le, heh wuh tvi-shal vesh' bosh t' wuh ihnik tobacco haze, tonk'peh nothing hafau t' wuh tuh t' shag if i had gla-tor fi-tor wuh previous mu-yor. "kum'i, watson?" au ya'akash. "ha." "zhagra na' wuh asal yetur?" "certainly." "yi sai-vel. Kling nam-tor stirring wi, tonk'peh i fai-tor wilat wuh tihet-sa-kan sleeps, heh etek dungau ak ma wuh pash si'." au chuckled tor himself u' au stariben, ish-veh bezhun twinkled, heh au seemed wuh natya sasu tor wuh sombre thinker t' wuh previous mu-yor. U' i sai-vel-tor i glanced na' t'nash-veh glantau. Ish-veh vesh' rai wonder ik kling vesh' stirring. Ish-veh vesh' dah-leh-kaukuh minutes vesht kehkuh. I had hardly shahtau lu holmes fun-tor k' wuh ro'fori ik wuh sa-kan vesh' putting svi' wuh jarel. "i aitlun tor nisan wuh pi' wihka t' t'nash-veh, " leralmin-tor au, pulling fi' ish-veh kluf. "i nah-tor, watson, ik du nam-tor i' standing svi' wuh la'es t' veh t' wuh danik ek'esik duhsu svi' europe. I nazh tor nam-tor kicked s' la' tor charing tuhs. Tonk'peh i nah-tor i ma wuh tal-muv t' wuh tek'ik i'." "heh wilat nam-tor ish-veh?" i ya'akash, smiling. "svi' wuh bathroom, " au kilko-tor. "oh, ha, i am ri joking, " au fator, seeing t'nash-veh glazhau t' incredulity. "i ma aishan vesh' tra', heh i ma taken ish-veh si', heh i ma prah ish-veh svi' nash gladstone sa'haf. Sarlah fi', t'nash-veh sa-kan, heh etek dungau gla-tor whether ish-veh dungi ri nunau wuh klachek." etek tor etwel yut downstairs u' quietly u' tor-yehat, heh si' vi' wuh ugelik asal sunshine. Svi' wuh fau-yut lam-tor etwel jarel heh pash, k' wuh ulef-clad tihet-sa-kan waiting na' wuh patam. Etek fi' sprang svi', heh maf etek dashed ne' wuh london fau-yut. Wuh zamu shasol hal vesh' stirring, kuvish svi' sazh tor wuh metropolis, tonk'peh wuh zehl t' villas fi' either vla vesh' u' ralash-fam heh lifeless u' ein kahr svi' wuh sahr-tor. "ish-veh has vesh' svi' ein sfekau wuh singular nuf, " leralmin-tor holmes, flicking wuh jarel fi' vi' wuh ausahr. "i confess ik i ma vesh' u' glan-fam u' wuh mole, tonk'peh ish-veh nam-tor weh-rom tor oren-tor kau tab-ma do worla tor oren-tor ish-veh na' ek'." svi' kahr wuh earliest risers vesh' aishan palikaya tor glazhau sleepily s' ish-veh krani u' etek drove k'fai wuh yut t' wuh surrey vla. Be' dvun-tor ne' wuh waterloo mesut fau-yut etek tuhsau abru' wuh pilash, heh dashing abru wellington yut halek-tor sharply tor wuh gas'rak heh afer-tor ourselves svi' kes-wun yut. Sherlock holmes vesh' muhl fainu tor wuh nekwitaya, heh wuh dahkuh constables na' wuh svep saluted ish-veh. Veh t' au meskarau wuh jarel's patam du' wuh vath pufulag-tor etek svi'. "vi nam-tor fi' gu-vam?" ya'akash holmes. "inspector bradstreet, osu." "ah, bradstreet, uf nam-tor du?" wuh ha-vol, stout official had sarlah ne' wuh kov-flagged tvur, svi' wuh peaked taik heh frogged jacket. "i istaya tor ma wuh hizhuk zhit k' du, bradstreet." "certainly, mr. Holmes. Ash vi' t'nash-veh tvi-shal la'." ish-veh vesh' wuh pi', office-spo' tvi-shal, k' wuh masuk' ledger fi-tor wuh pasu, heh wuh telephone projecting s' wuh temok. Wuh inspector hayal-tor ne' na' ish-veh kitau-skaf. "ra mokuhlek i tor na' du, mr. Holmes?" "i puvutau pa' ik beggarman, boonethe veh vi vesh' vifalunau k' hasu concerned svi' wuh disappearance t' mr. Neville st. Clair, t' lee." "ha. Au vesh' katau abru heh remanded na' further inquiries." "ni i puzhu-tor. Du ma ish-veh la'?" "svi' wuh nala." "nam-tor au hizhuk?" "oh, au mazhiv-kur-tor rai trouble. Tonk'peh au nam-tor wuh kitork scoundrel." "kitork?" "ha, ish-veh nam-tor ek' etek mokuhlek tor tor tor ish-veh pu-tor ish-veh el'ru, heh ish-veh limuk nam-tor u' nesh-kur u' wuh tinker's. Muhl, lu wuh'wak ish-veh nuf has vesh' settled, au dungi ma wuh regular prison wu'sibav; heh i nah-tor, kuv gla-tor du ish-veh, du would sep-wafikh k' me ik au bolau ish-veh." "i dang spo' tor gla-tor ish-veh maut mau." "would du? Ik nam-tor easily ovsoh. Sarlah nash yut. Du mokuhlek trasha ish-veh sa'haf." "rai, i nah-tor ik i'll nem-tor ish-veh." "maut rom. Sarlah nash yut, kuv du sanoi." au pufulag-tor etek ne' wuh tvur, tu'ash wuh barred svep, be' dvun-tor ne' wuh kuvoran stair, heh katau etek tor wuh whitewashed tvur k' wuh zehl t' svep fi' tik vla. "wuh wuh fi' wuh gas'rak nam-tor ish-veh, " leralmin-tor wuh inspector. "la' ish-veh nam-tor!" au quietly pohshaya pla' wuh gluvau-math svi' wuh upper krus t' wuh svep heh glanced k'fai. "au nam-tor asleep, " leralmin-tor au. "du mokuhlek gla-tor ish-veh maut muhl." etek fi' shitau etwel bezhun tor wuh grating. Wuh prisoner ti k' ish-veh limuk na' etek, svi' wuh maut glu yuk, eshan slowly heh heavily. Au vesh' wuh svitan-sized sasu, coarsely clad u' became ish-veh calling, k' wuh kur-tor sav'el protruding k'fai wuh rent svi' ish-veh tattered tor-pal. Au vesh', u' wuh inspector had leralmin-tor, extremely kitork, tonk'peh wuh grime if wein-tor ish-veh limuk kupi ri ip-sut its repulsive ugliness. Wuh sax'ksei wheal s' wuh hinek ulidar sahr-tor gas'rak mes' ish-veh s' bezhun tor chin, heh k' its contraction had da-tor abru veh vla t' wuh upper bru, ni ik rehkuh zud vesh' ko'nar svi' wuh perpetual snarl. Wuh kolaya t' maut ugelik yon-kur isachya grew neik abru' ish-veh bezhun heh fa-patam. "au's wuh vaksur, isn't au?" leralmin-tor wuh inspector. "au certainly bolau wuh pu-tor, " remarked holmes. "i had wuh idea ik au lau, heh i nem-tor wuh liberty t' bringing wuh raul k' me." au tu'ash wuh gladstone sa'haf u' au stariben, heh nem-tor si', tor t'nash-veh astonishment, wuh maut suk wu'sibav-sponge. "au! Au! Du nam-tor wuh funny veh, " chuckled wuh inspector. "i', kuv du dungi ma wuh lo'uk goodness tor tu'ash ik svep maut quietly, etek dungi ak tor ish-veh tresahk wuh mau weht respectable khlop." "muhl, i ri tor fai-tor po ri, " leralmin-tor wuh inspector. "au doesn't glazhau wuh lit tor wuh kes-wun yut nala, tor au?" au trel-tor ish-veh tal-muv vi' wuh klachek, heh etek ek' maut quietly svi-tor wuh nala. Wuh sleeper ulef da-tor, heh yi settled ne' wuh'wak weht vi' wuh glu slumber. Holmes stooped tor wuh masu-mashek, moistened ish-veh sponge, heh yi tetau ish-veh dah'wak vigorously mes' heh ne' wuh prisoner's limuk. "kal-tor me ragtau du, " au saul-tor, "tor mr. Neville st. Clair, t' lee, svi' wuh county t' kent." worla svi' t'nash-veh ha'kiv ma i gla-tor such wuh glan. Wuh sasu's limuk puhnk-tor ska' ne' wuh sponge spo' wuh kas-wadi s' wuh lap. Hal-tor vesh' wuh dirik khav-kur tint! Hal-tor, nuh', vesh' wuh horrid ulidar if had seamed ish-veh mes', heh wuh kuvoran-tor bru if had putan-tor wuh repulsive sneer tor wuh limuk! Wuh twitch katau maf wuh tangled yon-kur isachya, heh tra', sitting abru svi' ish-veh sar-tak, vesh' wuh spoh, maf-limuk-tor, refined-looking sasu, nesh-kur-haired heh mos-skinned, rubbing ish-veh bezhun heh staring pa' ish-veh k' sleepy bewilderment. Yi suddenly realising wuh sashavaya, au shau vi' wuh shei heh threw himself ne' k' ish-veh limuk tor wuh trak. "lo'uk heavens!" maf-tor wuh inspector, "ish-veh nam-tor, indeed, wuh missing sasu. I fai-tor ish-veh s' wuh ha'gel-bikuv." wuh prisoner da-tor k' wuh reckless sov t' wuh sasu vi abandons himself tor ish-veh buk. "nam-tor ish-veh ni, " leralmin-tor au. "heh pray ra am i vifalunau k'?" "k' tor maf k' mr. Neville st. Oh, sarlah, du mokuhlek't nam-tor vifalunau k' ik vita au tor wuh nuf t' attempted suicide t' ish-veh, " leralmin-tor wuh inspector k' wuh wa'limatau. "muhl, i ma vesh' dah-leh-stehkuh tevun svi' wuh nekwitaya, tonk'peh nash really nem-tor wuh cake." "kuv i am mr. Neville st. Clair, yi ish-veh nam-tor obvious ik rai tr'y'kak has vesh' committed, heh ik, therefore, i am illegally detained." "rai tr'y'kak, tonk'peh wuh maut lo'uk lafosh has vesh' committed, " leralmin-tor holmes. "du would ma ovsoh weh-rom ki' trusted ish-veh ko-telsu." "ish-veh vesh' ri wuh ko-telsu; ish-veh vesh' wuh kanu, " groaned wuh prisoner. "oekon gol'nev me, i would ri ma au kafusik t' ish-veh sa-mekh. T'nash-veh oekon! Ra wuh sashavaya! Ra mokuhlek i tor?" sherlock holmes hayal-tor ne' be' ish-veh fi' wuh ku-san heh patted ish-veh kindly fi' wuh tipan. "kuv du trasha ish-veh tor wuh kelek t' tor-gav tor pa'shik wuh tukh abru, " leralmin-tor au, "veling du mokuhlek hardly nan'woi publicity. Fi' wuh vath el'ru, kuv du convince wuh police ek'te'kru ik tra' nam-tor rai tor-yehat nuf tehnat du, i ri tor fai-tor ik tra' nam-tor sovek utvau ik wuh details dang talal ish-veh yut vi' wuh dun. Inspector bradstreet would, i am sure, tor pitoh fi-tor sovek-vel if du lau var-tor etek heh nekhau ish-veh tor wuh proper ek'te'kru. Wuh nuf would yi worla hal-tor vi' kelek na' ek'." "oekon kudau du!" maf-tor wuh prisoner passionately. "i would ma palesh-tor imprisonment, ay, kauk execution, rather do ma losrak t'nash-veh miserable tsat u' wuh skan blot tor t'nash-veh kanu. "du nam-tor wuh wuh'rak vi ma ek'wak puzhu-tor t'nash-veh var. T'nash-veh sa-mekh vesh' wuh schoolmaster svi' chesterfield, wilat i poprah wuh marom education. I travelled svi' t'nash-veh youth, nem-tor tor wuh skaf, heh t'forti became wuh reporter fi' wuh khru dun svi' london. Veh gad t'nash-veh versu istau tor ma wuh weizehl t' ua'mrki fi-tor begging svi' wuh metropolis, heh i volunteered tor tanilau au. Tra' vesh' wuh sfek s' if ek' t'nash-veh adventures palikau. Ish-veh vesh' goh k' trying begging u' wuh amateur ik i kupi prah wuh kla-min fi-tor if tor nen t'nash-veh ua'mrki. Lu wuh fundauik-ithop i had, veling, oren-tor ek' wuh tsat t' tor abru, heh had vesh' khinik svi' wuh yar-kur-tvi-shal na' t'nash-veh renkup'es. I nem-tor advantage i' t' t'nash-veh bai'elkhrul-akteiben. I kras-tor t'nash-veh limuk, heh tor tor myself u' pitiable u' tor-yehat i tor wuh rom ulidar heh teslau veh vla t' t'nash-veh bru svi' wuh kuvoran k' wuh mamuk t' wuh pi' trel t' kahm-kur-tor plaster. Yi k' wuh yon-kur patam t' isachya, heh wuh appropriate sai-vel, i nem-tor t'nash-veh wurzel svi' wuh business krus t' wuh kahr, ostensibly u' wuh match-seller tonk'peh really u' wuh beggar. Na' stehkuh wadan i plied t'nash-veh trade, heh lu i fun-tor ha-kel svi' wuh khru i afer-tor tor t'nash-veh ak'wikmun ik i had poprah rai lehkuh tor 26s. 4d. "i kitau t'nash-veh ua'mrki heh nahp pi' weht t' wuh tukh abi', ein wak later, i backed wuh dun na' wuh t'hy'la heh had wuh writ dvin-tor fi-tor me na' 25. I vesh' na' t'nash-veh wit's shaht wilat tor prah wuh donku, tonk'peh wuh sudden idea sarlah tor me. I eit'jae wuh fortnight's takov s' wuh creditor, ya'akash na' wuh holiday s' t'nash-veh employers, heh spent wuh wak svi' begging svi' wuh kahr ne' t'nash-veh pasut. Svi' lehkuh gad i had wuh donku heh had vlitau wuh sa'akh. "muhl, du mokuhlek glenonau uf lerash ish-veh vesh' tor settle ne' tor arduous ar'kadan na' 2 wuh wehk gad lu i fai-tor ik i kupi pinkau u' mau svi' wuh gad k' smearing t'nash-veh limuk k' wuh pi' kras, laying t'nash-veh taik fi' wuh solektra, heh sitting fam dvun. Ish-veh vesh' wuh wu puk svi' t'nash-veh pride heh wuh donku, tonk'peh wuh dollars skil-tor na' kim-shah, heh i threw abru reporting heh hayal-tor gad po' gad svi' wuh teruk if i had wuh'rak pudvel-tor, inspiring pity k' t'nash-veh ghastly limuk heh boshak t'nash-veh abru'lik k' coppers. Goh veh sasu fai-tor t'nash-veh tsat. Au vesh' wuh keeper t' wuh neik den svi' if i nam-tor-tor tor lodge svi' swandam lane, wilat i kupi kanok asal sasarlah u' wuh squalid beggar heh svi' wuh khru mesuvulau myself vi' wuh muhl-sai-vel-tor sasu pa' kahr. Nash katravahsu, wuh lascar, vesh' muhl vlitau k' me na' ish-veh tvi-shal, ni ik i fai-tor ik t'nash-veh tsat vesh' safe svi' ish-veh mat. "muhl, maut ak i afer-tor ik i vesh' saving considerable hau-ov t' donku. I ri tor tvai ik sovek beggar svi' wuh yut t' london kupi pinkau 700 wuh yearwhich nam-tor lehkuh tor t'nash-veh bov takingsbut i had exceptional advantages svi' t'nash-veh tepul t' tor abru, heh isha svi' wuh kebitra t' repartee, if improved k' practice heh tor me ved wuh naglanshau character svi' wuh kahr. Ek' gad wuh pilash t' qsu'lit, vuhnau k' haul-tukh, mukau svi' fi-tor me, heh ish-veh vesh' wuh maut rasahkos gad svi' if i vravshau tor nem-tor 2. "u' i grew richer i grew weht ambitious, nem-tor wuh kelek svi' wuh shasol, heh eventually telik, rik' sovek-veh having wuh suspicion u' tor t'nash-veh yeht occupation. T'nash-veh tal-kam ko-telsu fai-tor ik i had business svi' wuh kahr. She pi' fai-tor ra. "kim-shah gad i had shahtau na' wuh gad heh vesh' sai-vel-tor svi' t'nash-veh tvi-shal abru' wuh opium den lu i glazhau s' t'nash-veh krani heh gla-tor, tor t'nash-veh horror heh astonishment, ik t'nash-veh ko-telsu vesh' standing svi' wuh yut, k' ish-veh bezhun teslau bosh fi-tor me. I mazhiv-kur-tor wuh maf t' ak'wikmun, threw abru t'nash-veh kar tor wein t'nash-veh limuk, heh, rushing tor t'nash-veh confidant, wuh lascar, entreated ish-veh tor prevent sovek-veh s' coming abru tor me. I puzhu-tor ish-veh spes downstairs, tonk'peh i fai-tor ik she kupi ri she-tor. Swiftly i threw ska' t'nash-veh sai-vel, seshau fi' eifa t' wuh beggar, heh shitau fi' t'nash-veh kurek heh wig. Kauk wuh ko-telsu's bezhun kupi ri tilau ni ovsotik wuh pasut. Tonk'peh yi ish-veh paresh-tor tor me ik tra' lau nam-tor wuh psthan svi' wuh tvi-shal, heh ik wuh sai-vel lau svik-tor me. I threw tu'ash wuh krani, reopening k' t'nash-veh khrash wuh pi' tresahk if i had inflicted fi-tor myself svi' wuh shi'yuk ik asal. Yi i seized t'nash-veh tor-pal, if vesh' weighted k' wuh coppers if i had aishan transferred tor ish-veh s' wuh duf sa'haf svi' if i lesh t'nash-veh takings. I hurled ish-veh s' wuh krani, heh ish-veh sasaudau vi' wuh thames. Wuh vath sai-vel would ma zahal-tor, tonk'peh na' ik moment tra' vesh' wuh rush t' constables abru wuh stair, heh wuh zamu minutes po' i afer-tor, rather, i confess, tor t'nash-veh vas, ik instead t' hasu shasutan-tor u' mr. Neville st. Clair, i vesh' pehkau u' ish-veh murderer. "i ri tor fai-tor ik tra' nam-tor sovek-kitok na' me tor danau. I vesh' satalau tor korsau t'nash-veh pasut u' wu u' tor-yehat, heh hence t'nash-veh preference na' wuh kitork limuk. Fai-tor ik t'nash-veh ko-telsu would nam-tor terribly anxious, i trel-tor ska' t'nash-veh mokov heh confided ish-veh tor wuh lascar na' wuh moment lu rai constable vesh' watching me, teretuhr k' wuh hurried scrawl, telling ish-veh ik she had rai aishan tor pthak." "ik pitoh goh pulau ish-veh za-gad, " leralmin-tor holmes. "rom oekon! Ra wuh wehk gad she bolau ma spent!" "wuh police ma glantau nash lascar, " leralmin-tor inspector bradstreet, "heh i mokuhlek ved ken-tor ik au lau talal ish-veh rihagik tor lehk wuh nuhm unobserved. Probably au handed ish-veh tor ein masusu klepovausu t' ish-veh, vi forgot ek' pa' ish-veh na' ein gad." "ik vesh' ish-veh, " leralmin-tor holmes, nodding approvingly; "i ma rai vet t' ish-veh. Tonk'peh ma du worla vesh' prosecuted na' begging?" "wehk wak; tonk'peh ra vesh' wuh tok-ti tor me?" "ish-veh bolau pehkaya la', however, " leralmin-tor bradstreet. "kuv wuh police nam-tor tor hush nash vel abru, tra' bolau nam-tor rai weht t' hugh boone." "i ma sworn ish-veh k' wuh danik solemn oaths if wuh sasu mokuhlek nem-tor." "svi' ik nuf i nah-tor ik ish-veh nam-tor yesik ik rai further ash-tor lau nam-tor taken. Tonk'peh kuv du nam-tor afer-tor va'ashiv, yi ek' bolau sasarlah. I am sure, mr. Holmes, ik etek nam-tor maut mau indebted tor du na' having pa'shu wuh tukh abru. I istaya i fai-tor uf du pulau ish-veh results." "i pulau nash-veh, " leralmin-tor t'nash-veh t'hy'la, "k' sitting fi-tor kaukuh trak heh consuming wuh ounce t' shag. I nah-tor, watson, ik kuv etek yetur tor leipausu yut etek dungau aishan nam-tor svi' wak na' asal-yem." vii. Wuh adventure t' wuh pla-kur carbuncle i had puvutau fi-tor t'nash-veh t'hy'la sherlock holmes fi-tor wuh dahr asal po' christmas, k' wuh intention t' wishing ish-veh wuh compliments t' wuh tevun-yonuk. Au vesh' lounging fi-tor wuh ku-san svi' wuh gahv-kur sai-vel-tor-gown, wuh mev-rack k'svi ish-veh pulau fi-tor wuh gas'rak, heh wuh tuh t' crumpled asal dun, evidently newly orenau, be' na' el'ru. Be' wuh ku-san vesh' wuh wooden ku-san, heh fi' wuh vulu t' wuh pla' geldau wuh maut seedy heh disreputable lerash-olau taik, mau wuh weh-rasahkos na' sai-vel-tor, heh treshau svi' several shitau. "rai, rai. Rai tr'y'kak, " leralmin-tor sherlock holmes, laughing. "goh veh t' eifa whimsical pi' incidents if dungi pavesh-tor lu du ma kehkuh million komihn beings ek' jostling tik vath k'svi wuh ret t' wuh zamu keh-vla miles. Du allude tor t'nash-veh attempt tor recover wuh irene adler dun, tor wuh singular nuf t' din-tor mary sutherland, heh tor wuh adventure t' wuh sasu k' wuh kuvoran-tor bru. "ish-veh nam-tor ish-veh taik." "rai, rai, au afer-tor ish-veh. Its owner nam-tor ri-fainu. I eit'jae ik du dungi glazhau fi-tor ish-veh ri u' wuh battered billycock tonk'peh u' wuh intellectual wat. Heh, wuh'rak, u' tor uf sarlah ish-veh la'. Ish-veh lasha fi-tor christmas asal, svi' apc'koik k' wuh rom thelik kushel, if nam-tor, i ma rai vet, roasting i' svi' khom t' peterson's yon. Wuh kla-min nam-tor aifa: pa' kehkuh o'wak-vel fi' christmas asal, peterson, vi, u' du fai-tor, nam-tor wuh maut trau katravahsu, vesh' returning s' ein pi' jollification heh vesh' tor ish-veh yut homeward ne' tottenham kelek fau-yut. Veh t' wuh latter knocked ska' wuh sasu's taik, fi' if au ashenau ish-veh terpau tor fosh-tor himself heh, swinging ish-veh abru' ish-veh patam, smashed wuh mahr-kel krani za' ish-veh. Ish-veh vesh' wuh maut ordinary nesh-kur taik t' wuh tsuri pauk shid, lerash heh mau wuh weh-rasahkos na' sai-vel-tor. Wuh tvitaya had vesh' t' yon-kur silk, tonk'peh vesh' wuh rom deal discoloured. "ish-veh vesh' catherine cusack vi var-tor me t' ish-veh, " leralmin-tor au svi' wuh crackling spes. "i seeher ladyship's waiting-maid. Ish-veh seems tor me, ryder, ik tra' nam-tor wuh tor t' wuh maut takov villain svi' du. Du fai-tor ik nash sasu horner, wuh plumber, had vesh' concerned svi' ein such tukh fa', heh ik suspicion would shom wuh weht readily fi-tor ish-veh. Ra did du tor, yi? "ish-veh nam-tor maut muhl tor cringe heh ukrau i', tonk'peh du nahp pi' hiyet t' nash ri donku-tor horner svi' wuh kif na' wuh tr'y'kak t' if au fai-tor nothing." "i dungi hash-tor, mr. Holmes. I dungi trasha wuh shasol, osu. Yi wuh falun tehnat ish-veh dungi shaya ne'." "hum! Etek dungi variben pa' ik. Heh i' kal-tor etek zhu-tor wuh yeht khrosahp t' wuh thurai bae'cok. "i dungi var-tor du ish-veh aishan u' ish-veh pavesh-tor, osu, " leralmin-tor au. Tra' vesh' rai shi pa' wuh hotel wilat ish-veh would nam-tor safe. I went si', u' kuv fi' ein kadvin, heh i tor na' t'nash-veh ko-kai's kelek. She had telik wuh sasu ahmau oakshott, heh ha-tor svi' brixton fau-yut, wilat she fattened fowls na' wuh mahr-kel. Ek' wuh yut tra' kanok sasu i ragel-tor seemed tor me tor nam-tor wuh policeman il wuh detective; heh, na' ek' ik ish-veh vesh' wuh samu mu-yor, wuh wadashaya vesh' pouring ne' t'nash-veh limuk fa' vesht sarlah nash-veh tor wuh brixton fau-yut. "t'nash-veh ko-kai had var-tor me ein wehk gad fa' ik i lau ma wuh pick t' ish-veh kushel na' wuh christmas la', heh i fai-tor ik she vesh' kwon-hau-ov u' rom u' ish-veh zhit. "'whatever vesh' du doing k' ik kushel, jem?' leralmin-tor she. "'muhl, ' leralmin-tor i, 'du leralmin-tor du'd mazhiv-kur-tor me veh na' christmas, heh i vesh' olaya if vesh' wuh fattest.' Tra''s dah-leh-shehkuh t' au, if tor veh na' du, heh veh na' etek, heh dahkuh dozen na' wuh mahr-kel.' "'hal-tor tor wuh dealer's, jem.' "'if dealer's?' "'breckinridge, t' covent bah-ker.' "'tonk'peh vesh' tra' wuh'ashiv k' wuh barred harr?' i ya'akash, 'wuh ka u' wuh veh i dvel-tor?' "muhl, yi, veling vesht gla-tor nash-veh ish-veh ek', heh i sahr-tor ska' u' lerash u' t'nash-veh ash'ya would lesh me tor nash sasu breckinridge; tonk'peh au had makau wuh lot na' wuh'wak, heh ri veh zhit would au var-tor me u' tor wilat au had hal-tor. Du puzhu-tor ish-veh yourselves tor-mu-yor. Muhl, au has kwon-hau-ov kilko-tor me spo' ik. T'nash-veh ko-kai nah-tor ik i am going mad. Sometimes i nah-tor ik i am myself. I suppose ik i am commuting wuh felony, tonk'peh ish-veh nam-tor aishan tor-yehat ik i am saving wuh soul. Nash katravahsu dungi ri hal-tor riyeht va'ashiv; au nam-tor nuh' terribly koltha. Satau ish-veh tor gaol i', heh du tor ish-veh wuh gaol-kushel na' ha'kiv. Isha, ish-veh nam-tor wuh tevun-yonuk t' thrap-fam'es nufau. Wuh adventure t' wuh speckled zhel fi' glancing abru' t'nash-veh pitoh t' wuh steh-leh shaik nuf svi' if i ma du' wuh kim-shah ohkuh tevun orenau wuh methods t' t'nash-veh t'hy'la sherlock holmes, i talal wehk tragic, ein comic, wuh suk su'etek goh flekh, tonk'peh rim commonplace; na', working u' au did rather na' wuh ashaya t' ish-veh tanaf do na' wuh acquirement t' don-tak, au klee'fah tor katravahsu himself k' sovek investigation if did ri palutunau na' wuh ritsuri, heh kauk wuh fantastic. T' ek' aifa vuhnau nuf, however, i fam yehat recall sovek if presented weht singular features do ik if vesh' katravah k' wuh muhl-fainu surrey skan t' wuh roylotts t' stoke moran. Wuh pavek svi' deshker paresh-tor svi' wuh lehkuh-mal gad t' t'nash-veh katravek k' holmes, lu etek vesh' thresh-tor tvi-shal u' bachelors svi' leipausu yut. Ish-veh nam-tor sos'eh u' muhl ik wuh kla-min dang i' sarlah tor ta'hal, na' i ma utvau tor fai-tor ik tra' nam-tor widespread rumours u' tor wuh tevakh t' dr. Grimesby roylott if palutunau tor tor wuh tukh kauk weht terrible do wuh yeht'es. Ish-veh vesh' lehkuh-mal svi' april svi' wuh tevun '83 ik i woke veh asal tor talal sherlock holmes standing, fully sai-vel-tor, k' wuh vla t' t'nash-veh sar-tak. Au vesh' wuh tab-ma riser, u' wuh tor-go, heh u' wuh wak-vel fi' wuh mantelpiece gluvau me ik ish-veh vesh' goh wuh yonuk-vesht stehkuh, i blinked abru na' ish-veh svi' ein ak'wikmun, heh sos'eh aishan wuh pi' resentment, na' i vesh' myself regular svi' t'nash-veh es'merka. "maut sorry tor knock du abru, watson, " leralmin-tor au, "tonk'peh ish-veh's wuh tsuri lot nash asal. Mrs. Hudson has vesh' knocked abru, she retorted fi-tor me, heh i fi' du." She nam-tor waiting i' svi' wuh sitting-tvi-shal. "t'nash-veh ahm nam-tor sherlock holmes. Nash nam-tor t'nash-veh intimate t'hy'la heh katravahsu, dr. Watson, fa' ik du mokuhlek stariben u' freely u' fa' myself. Ha! I am glad tor gla-tor ik mrs. Ish-veh nam-tor vash." she ashenau ish-veh veil u' she stariben, heh etek kupi gla-tor ik she vesh' indeed svi' wuh pitiable fupa s' t' agitation, ish-veh limuk ek' drawn heh zhai-kur, k' restless koltha bezhun, spo' eifa t' ein shi'kar aushfa. "etek dungau ak eku tukh gas'rak, i ma rai vet. Du ma sarlah svi' k' ranau nash asal, gla-tor nash-veh." "du fai-tor me, yi?" "t'nash-veh ahm nam-tor helen stoner, heh i am living k' t'nash-veh stepfather, vi nam-tor wuh kim-shah survivor t' veh t' wuh oldest saxon skan svi' england, wuh roylotts t' stoke moran, fi' wuh western ek'zehl t' surrey." holmes nodded ish-veh patam. "wuh ahm nam-tor familiar tor me, " leralmin-tor au. "wuh skan vesh' na' veh wak among wuh richest svi' england, heh wuh estates sadvun-tor abru' wuh ek'zehl vi' berkshire svi' wuh desh'rak, heh hampshire svi' wuh tev'rak. Svi' wuh kim-shah century, however, kehkuh successive heirs vesh' t' wuh dissolute heh wasteful disposition, heh wuh skan ruin vesh' eventually ovsoh k' wuh gambler svi' wuh gad t' wuh regency. Nothing vesh' losrak korsau wuh zamu acres t' solektra, heh wuh dahkuh-hundred-tevun-hinek kelek, if nam-tor itself plesh-tor ne' wuh ras mortgage. Wuh kim-shah squire zaseshau si' ish-veh nam tra', living wuh horrible ha'kiv t' wuh aristocratic pauper; tonk'peh ish-veh goh sa-fu, t'nash-veh stepfather, seeing ik au bolau rubilau himself tor wuh uzh nosh, prah wuh storilaya s' wuh tomasu, if enabled ish-veh tor nem-tor wuh hasuk degree heh went si' tor calcutta, wilat, k' ish-veh professional renkup'es heh ish-veh nekwitaya t' character, au afer-tor wuh suk practice. Svi' wuh nunau t' reshan, however, aisha k' ein robberies if had vesh' perpetrated svi' wuh kelek, au kuhsh-tor ish-veh salatik butler tor tevakh heh narrowly stron-tor wuh capital zhit-bal. U' ish-veh vesh', au dashau wuh wu zhil t' imprisonment heh afterwards fun-tor tor england wuh morose heh disappointed sasu. "lu dr. Roylott vesh' svi' india au telik t'nash-veh ko-mekh, mrs. Stoner, wuh nu'ri kir'an t' tra-lan-paik stoner, t' wuh bengal artillery. T'nash-veh ko-kai julia heh i vesh' t'dahsu, heh etek vesh' goh dahkuh tevun hinek na' wuh wak t' t'nash-veh ko-mekh's re-kal'i'farr. She had wuh considerable hau-ov t' moneynot lehkuh do 1000 wuh yearand nash she bequeathed tor dr. Roylott entirely du' etek resided k' ish-veh, k' wuh provision ik wuh ac'ruth kanok-tevunik hau-ov dang nam-tor kal-tor tor tik t' etek svi' wuh pavek t' etwel kal'i'farr. Shortly po' etwel fun tor england t'nash-veh ko-mekh diedshe vesh' pustau ohkuh tevun ago svi' wuh railway kisheya be' crewe. Dr. Roylott yi abandoned ish-veh attempts tor afer-tor himself svi' practice svi' london heh nem-tor etek tor ha-tor k' ish-veh svi' wuh hinek ancestral kelek na' stoke moran. Wuh donku if t'nash-veh ko-mekh had losrak vesh' hiyet na' ek' etwel aitlu, heh tra' seemed tor nam-tor rai obstacle tor etwel happiness. "tonk'peh wuh terrible rubah sarlah abru' etwel stepfather pa' nash wak. Instead t' tor t'hylara heh exchanging yaretau k' etwel behsu, vi had palikauk vesh' overjoyed tor gla-tor wuh roylott t' stoke moran pla' svi' wuh hinek skan ku-san, au ikap-tor himself abru svi' ish-veh kelek heh seldom sarlah si' korsau tor indulge svi' keimen quarrels k' whoever lau tuhs ish-veh yut. Khrash t' temper approaching tor mania has vesh' samekhik svi' wuh sasu t' wuh skan, heh svi' t'nash-veh stepfather's nuf ish-veh had, i dva-tor, vesh' intensified k' ish-veh wu residence svi' wuh tropics. Wuh weizehl t' disgraceful brawls nem-tor shi, dahkuh t' if shahtau svi' wuh police-kelek, abi' na' kim-shah au became wuh vash t' wuh pi'kahr, heh wuh sular-ves would hash-tor na' ish-veh betaya, na' au nam-tor wuh sasu t' immense karik'es, heh absolutely uncontrollable svi' ish-veh reshan. "kim-shah wehk gad au hurled wuh local shek-zhuksu abru' wuh parapet vi' wuh pilash, heh ish-veh vesh' goh k' paying abru' ek' wuh donku if i kupi hoknau teretuhr ik i vesh' kup tor avert wuh'ashiv tsuri sashavaya. Au had rai t'hylara na' ek' korsau wuh wandering gipsies, heh au would mazhiv-kur-tor aifa vagabonds trasha tor encamp fi-tor wuh zamu acres t' bramble-wein-tor solektra if represent wuh skan estate, heh would nar-tor svi' fun wuh hospitality t' ish-veh ith'du, wandering maf k' au sometimes na' wehk gad fi' shaht. Au has wuh shaukaush isha na' indian animals, if nam-tor satau abru' tor ish-veh k' wuh correspondent, heh au has i' wuh cheetah heh wuh baboon, if czar freely abru' ish-veh solektra heh nam-tor ptha k' wuh villagers siyah u' mau u' ish-veh trensu. "du mokuhlek glenonau s' ra i leralmin ik t'nash-veh ri donku-tor ko-kai julia heh i had rai lo'uk sanosh svi' etwel ha-tor. Rai dvinsu would stay k' etek, heh na' wuh akarshif etek did ek' wuh ar'kadan t' wuh kelek. She vesh' tonk'peh reh-leh na' wuh wak t' ish-veh tevakh, heh wi ish-veh isachya had already palikau tor whiten, kauk u' t'nash-veh has." "ish-veh ko-kai nam-tor tevik, yi?" "she tev-tor aishan dahkuh tevun ago, heh ish-veh nam-tor t' ish-veh tevakh ik i istaya tor stariben tor du. Du mokuhlek ken-tor ik, living wuh ha'kiv if i ma kethelvau, etek vesh' pi' kesik tor gla-tor sovek-veh t' etwel sha' ya'shakhuv heh shul. Etek had, however, wuh ezyet, t'nash-veh ko-mekh's maiden ko-kai, din-tor honoria westphail, vi ha-tor be' harrow, heh etek vesh' occasionally kal-tor tor vlitau pen yaretau na' nash t'sai's kelek. Julia went tra' na' christmas dahkuh tevun ago, heh ragel-tor tra' wuh ulef-vlitau tra-lan t' marines, tor ik she became engaged. T'nash-veh stepfather oren-tor t' wuh engagement lu t'nash-veh ko-kai fun-tor heh nufau rai objection tor wuh kal'i'farr; tonk'peh k'svi wuh fortnight t' wuh gad if had vesh' teslau na' wuh wedding, wuh terrible pavek paresh-tor if has deprived me t' t'nash-veh goh besu." sherlock holmes had vesh' leaning pla' svi' ish-veh ku-san k' ish-veh bezhun a'ing heh ish-veh patam ne'hal-tor svi' wuh an'kar, tonk'peh au ulef tu'ash ish-veh lids i' heh glanced mes' na' ish-veh visitor. "pray nam-tor precise u' tor details, " leralmin-tor au. "ish-veh nam-tor hagik na' me tor nam-tor ni, na' kanok pavek t' ik dreadful wak nam-tor seared vi' t'nash-veh vokaya. Wuh manor-kelek nam-tor, u' i ma already leralmin-tor, maut hinek, heh goh veh rala nam-tor i' inhabited. Wuh shi'yuk svi' nash rala nam-tor fi' wuh solektra lan-tol, wuh sitting-tvi-shal hasu svi' wuh central vihpan t' wuh kelek. T' aifa shi'yuk wuh wuh'rak nam-tor dr. Roylott's, wuh dahr t'nash-veh ko-kai's, heh wuh wuh t'nash-veh sha'. Tra' nam-tor rai sviribaya svi' au, tonk'peh au ek' tu'ash si' vi' wuh ka tvur. Tor i tor myself eiktra?" "perfectly ni." "wuh krani t' wuh rehkuh tvi-shal tu'ash si' fi-tor wuh yartra. Ik fatal mu-yor dr. Roylott had hal-tor tor ish-veh tvi-shal lehkuh-mal, hi etek fai-tor ik au had ri retired tor shom, na' t'nash-veh ko-kai vesh' troubled k' wuh fnish-tor t' wuh karik indian cigars if ish-veh vesh' ish-veh custom tor vuzh. She losrak ish-veh tvi-shal, therefore, heh sarlah vi' t'nash-veh, wilat she hayal-tor na' ein wak, chatting pa' ish-veh approaching wedding. "'var-tor me, helen, ' leralmin-tor she, 'ma du ek'wak puzhu-tor sovek-veh whistle svi' wuh tevik t' wuh mu-yor?' "'worla, ' leralmin-tor i. "'i suppose ik du kupi ri possibly whistle, yourself, svi' ish-veh yuk?' "'certainly ri. Tonk'peh po?' "'fai'ei du' wuh kim-shah zamu mu-yor i ma kwon-hau-ov, pa' rehkuh svi' wuh asal, puzhu-tor wuh neik, pa'shik whistle. I am wuh ta'hal sleeper, heh ish-veh has awakened me. I fam yehat var-tor wilat sarlah ish-veh fromperhaps s' wuh thurai tvi-shal, sos'eh s' wuh yartra. I nahp ik i would aishan ya'akash du whether du had puzhu-tor ish-veh.' "'rai, i ma ri. Ish-veh bolau nam-tor eifa wretched gipsies svi' wuh plantation.' "'maut kesik. Heh wi kuv ish-veh vesh' fi' wuh yartra, i wonder ik du did ri zhu-tor ish-veh isha.' "'ah, tonk'peh i yuk weht heavily do du.' "'muhl, ish-veh nam-tor t' rai lo'uk consequence, na' sovek tav.' she abru'teruklar-ru'lut pla' na' me, a'ing t'nash-veh svep, heh wuh zamu moments later i puzhu-tor ish-veh tal-muv da-tor svi' wuh klachek." "indeed, " leralmin-tor holmes. "vesh' ish-veh ish-veh custom kwon-hau-ov tor klachek yourselves svi' na' mu-yor?" "kwon-hau-ov." "heh po?" "i nah-tor ik i mentioned tor du ik wuh hassu potau wuh cheetah heh wuh baboon. Etek had rai olaya t' shar'es vita etwel svep vesh' klacha." "ved ni. Pray proceed k' ish-veh star-krus." "i kupi ri yuk ik mu-yor. Wuh vague olaya t' impending misfortune impressed me. T'nash-veh ko-kai heh i, du dungi recollect, vesh' t'dahsu, heh du fai-tor uf subtle nam-tor wuh naf-tor if bind dahkuh souls if nam-tor ni closely puk'ai'la. Ish-veh vesh' wuh kwai mu-yor. Wuh salan vesh' howling s'udish, heh wuh sov-masu vesh' beating heh splashing tehnat wuh krani. Suddenly, svi' ek' wuh hubbub t' wuh karik salan, tra' thorau forth wuh kwai shei t' wuh terrified kosu. I fai-tor ik ish-veh vesh' t'nash-veh ko-kai's spes. I sprang s' t'nash-veh sar-tak, wrapped wuh shawl pauk me, heh rushed vi' wuh tvur. U' i tu'ash t'nash-veh svep i seemed tor zhu-tor wuh neik whistle, such u' t'nash-veh ko-kai kethelvau, heh wuh zamu moments later wuh clanging ralash, u' kuv wuh shivak t' mokev had tevan-tor. U' i sahr-tor ne' wuh tvur, t'nash-veh ko-kai's svep vesh' unlocked, heh revolved slowly fi-tor its tu'adayek. I nantau na' ish-veh horror-stricken, ri fai-tor ra vesh' pa' tor issue s' ish-veh. K' wuh ta'hal t' wuh tvur-ha'gelek i gla-tor t'nash-veh ko-kai saudau na' wuh sharu, ish-veh limuk blanched k' vash, ish-veh el'ru groping na' gol'nev, ish-veh bosh khlop swaying tor heh fro spo' ik t' wuh drunkard. She writhed u' veh vi nam-tor svi' terrible kusut, heh ish-veh sikrus vesh' dreadfully convulsed. Palikauk i nahp ik she had ri naglanshau me, tonk'peh u' i keh'sei abru' ish-veh she suddenly shrieked si' svi' wuh spes if i dungau worla yen-tor, 'oh, t'nash-veh oekon! Helen! Ish-veh vesh' wuh zhel! Wuh speckled zhel!' tra' vesh' vel else if she would fain ma leralmin-tor, heh she stabbed k' ish-veh ozh vi' wuh sov svi' wuh kharat t' wuh hassu's tvi-shal, tonk'peh wuh sluk mahai seized ish-veh heh khluhkau ish-veh zhit. Such vesh' wuh dreadful shaht t' t'nash-veh k'diwa ko-kai." "veh moment, " leralmin-tor holmes, "nam-tor du sure pa' nash whistle heh metallic ralash? Kupi du swear tor ish-veh?" "ik vesh' ra wuh county tevanu-talsu ya'akash me na' wuh inquiry. "vesh' ish-veh ko-kai sai-vel-tor?" "rai, she vesh' svi' ish-veh mu-yor-sai-vel. Svi' ish-veh gas'rak el'ru vesh' afer-tor wuh yonol-tor stump t' wuh match, heh svi' ish-veh losrak wuh match-natuhn." "showing ik she had kwul-tor wuh ta'hal heh glazhau pa' ish-veh lu wuh vikayek nem-tor shi. Ik nam-tor yauluhk. Heh ra conclusions did wuh tevanu-talsu sarlah tor?" "au sasu-hil-tor wuh nuf k' lo'uk tun, na' dr. Roylott's spa-tor had wu vesh' notorious svi' wuh county, tonk'peh au vesh' unable tor talal sovek satisfactory aishan t' tevakh. T'nash-veh evidence gluvau ik wuh svep had vesh' terau fi-tor wuh tvik vla, heh wuh krani vesh' klotau k' hinek-fashioned fe-wein k' sax'ksei shek-tukh mofek, if vesh' shar-tor kanok mu-yor. Wuh temok vesh' carefully sounded, heh vesh' shown tor nam-tor ved huhtik ek' pauk, heh wuh flooring vesh' isha thoroughly linisau, k' wuh ka result. Wuh vuzh-mev nam-tor eik, tonk'peh nam-tor barred abru k' kehkuh suk staples. Ish-veh nam-tor ac'ruth, therefore, ik t'nash-veh ko-kai vesh' ved sa'awek lu she ragel-tor ish-veh shaht. Isha, tra' vesh' rai ulidar t' sovek khrash fi-tor ish-veh." "uf pa' gisam?" "wuh hassu linisau ish-veh na' ish-veh, tonk'peh rik' navun." "ha, tra' nam-tor nearly kwon-hau-ov ein tra'." "ah, heh ra did du hoknau s' nash allusion tor wuh banda speckled zhel?" "sometimes i ma nahp ik ish-veh vesh' goh wuh kwai variben t' delirium, sometimes ik ish-veh lau ma referred tor ein zhel t' sutra, sos'eh tor aifa maut gipsies svi' wuh plantation. I ri tor fai-tor whether wuh gla-tor handkerchiefs if ni wehk t' au sai-vel-tor abru' ish-veh patam lau ma suggested wuh flekh tetaya-zhit if she nam-tor-tor." holmes hutau ish-veh patam spo' wuh sasu vi nam-tor irak s' hasu satisfied. "aifa nam-tor maut glu mashau, " leralmin-tor au; "pray hal-tor fi' k' ish-veh narrative." "dahkuh tevun ma be' dvun-tor opi' yi, heh t'nash-veh ha'kiv has vesh' abi' lately lonelier do ek'wak. Wuh tevun-krus ago, however, wuh tal-kam t'hy'la, ik i ma fainu na' wehk tevun, has ovsoh me wuh dor tor ya'akash t'nash-veh el'ru svi' kal'i'farr. Ish-veh ahm nam-tor armitagepercy armitagethe dahr sa-fu t' mr. Armitage, t' aberayek masu, be' telvan. I vesh' nuh' shaken tor hal-tor tor sar-tak va'ashiv, however, ni i sai-vel-tor, heh u' ak u' ish-veh vesh' gad-ha'khlup i trel-tor ne', prah wuh dog-hal na' wuh tarkiv ha-shal, if nam-tor mesyutik, heh drove tor leatherhead, s' whence ki'sarlah nash-veh fi' nash asal k' wuh veh vel t' seeing du heh asking ish-veh na'shikh." Wi etek ma ri wuh moment tor pak-tor. "gu'gelik hiyet heh sinister hiyet." "wi kuv wuh t'sai nam-tor yeht svi' taran ik wuh flooring heh temok nam-tor ralash, heh ik wuh svep, krani, heh vuzh-mev nam-tor impassable, yi ish-veh ko-kai bolau ma vesh' undoubtedly sa'awek lu she ragel-tor ish-veh mysterious shaht." Ish-veh nam-tor precisely na' ik utvau ik etek nam-tor going tor stoke moran nash gad. I aitlun tor gla-tor whether wuh objections nam-tor fatal, il kuv au lau nam-tor danau maf. Tonk'peh ra svi' wuh ahm t' wuh e'shua!" wuh khrasaya had vesh' drawn s' t'nash-veh besu k' wuh kla-min ik etwel svep had vesh' suddenly dashed tu'ash, heh ik wuh masuk' sasu had nentulau himself svi' wuh sharu. Ish-veh costume vesh' wuh peculiar rish t' wuh professional heh t' wuh agricultural, having wuh nesh-kur fik-taik, wuh wu pelal-tor-pal, heh wuh shif t' pid gaiters, k' wuh hunting-urozh swinging svi' ish-veh el'ru. Du shitau me ska', tor du?" leralmin-tor etwel uzh visitor, taking wuh ash fa'rak heh shaking ish-veh hunting-urozh. "i fai-tor du, du scoundrel! I ma puzhu-tor t' du fa'. "holmes, wuh scotland ker jack-svi'-office!" holmes chuckled heartily. "ish-veh conversation nam-tor danik entertaining, " leralmin-tor au. "lu du hal-tor si' ikap-tor wuh svep, na' tra' nam-tor wuh klopau draught." "i dungi hal-tor lu i ma had t'nash-veh leralmin. Ri tor du dare tor meddle k' t'nash-veh tek'ik. Gla-tor la'." au ash-tor swiftly fa'rak, seized wuh poker, heh keh'sei ish-veh vi' wuh curve k' ish-veh masuk' khav-kur el'ru. "fancy ish-veh having wuh insolence tor confound me k' wuh official detective nekwitaya!
