"ik nam-tor etwel glantokaya, " leralmin-tor holmes, springing tor ish-veh ash'ya; "sarlah ish-veh s' wuh svitan krani." u' etek be' dvun-tor si' au di'kizh-tor wuh zamu zhit k' wuh landlord, explaining ik etek vesh' going fi' wuh tab-ma yaret tor wuh acquaintance, heh ik ish-veh vesh' tor-yehat ik etek lau spend wuh mu-yor tra'. Wuh moment later etek vesh' si' fi' wuh gu'gelik fau-yut, wuh chill salan blowing svi' etwel limuk, heh veh kin-kur ta'hal twinkling svi' khom t' etek k'fai wuh gloom tor kakhartausu etek fi' etwel sombre skrol. Tra' vesh' pi' rihag'es svi' entering wuh solektra, na' unrepaired breaches gaped svi' wuh hinek shi'sochya temok. Tor etwel yut among wuh lap, etek pulau wuh yartra, tuhsau ish-veh, heh vesh' pa' tor svi-tor k'fai wuh krani lu si' s' wuh clump t' laurel bushes tra' darted ra seemed tor nam-tor wuh hideous heh distorted kan, vi threw itself fi-tor wuh yar k' writhing sikrus heh yi sahr-tor swiftly mes' wuh yartra vi' wuh mu'khlup'es. "t'nash-veh oekon!" i zhal-tor; "did gla-tor du ish-veh?" holmes vesh' na' wuh moment u' startled u' i. Ish-veh el'ru a'ing spo' wuh vice fi-tor t'nash-veh kar-nik svi' ish-veh agitation. Yi au shau vi' wuh neik abru'teruklar-ru'lut heh shitau ish-veh bru-lar tor t'nash-veh kaluk. "ish-veh nam-tor wuh nice household, " au murmured. "ik nam-tor wuh baboon." i had yen-tor wuh flekh kelek-aushfa if wuh hassu dau. Tra' vesh' wuh cheetah, nuh'; sos'eh etek lau talal ish-veh fi-tor etwel tipan na' sovek moment. I confess ik i olau easier svi' t'nash-veh kashek lu, po' zahalik holmes' li-fal heh slipping ska' t'nash-veh ash'el, i afer-tor myself svi'udish wuh shi'yuk. T'nash-veh besu noiselessly a'ing wuh fe-wein, dvun-tor wuh ha'gelek fi-tor wuh pasu, heh vishizhau ish-veh bezhun pauk wuh tvi-shal. Ek' vesh' u' etek had gla-tor ish-veh svi' wuh gad-wakik. Yi creeping abru tor me heh tor wuh trumpet t' ish-veh el'ru, au zhal-tor vi' t'nash-veh kaluk va'ashiv ni kogavik ik ish-veh vesh' ek' ik i kupi tor tor distinguish wuh zhit: "wuh least ralash would nam-tor fatal tor etwel dotoran." i nodded tor gluvaya ik i had puzhu-tor. "etek bolau hayal-tor rik' ta'hal. Au would gla-tor ish-veh k'fai wuh kraulayek." i nodded va'ashiv. "ri tor hal-tor asleep; ish-veh maut ha'kiv lau nerau fi-tor ish-veh. Ma ish-veh el'ru-pohshayek pok svi' nuf etek dang bolaya ish-veh. I dungi hayal-tor fi' wuh vla t' wuh sar-tak, heh du svi' ik ku-san." i nem-tor si' t'nash-veh revolver heh laid ish-veh fi' wuh teruk t' wuh pasu. Holmes had katau abru wuh wu wonil cane, heh nash au shitau fi-tor wuh sar-tak be' ish-veh. K' ish-veh au laid wuh natuhn t' matches heh wuh stump t' wuh ha'fek. Yi au da-tor ne' wuh ha'gelek, heh etek vesh' losrak svi' mu'khlup'es. Uf dungau i ek'wak yen-tor ik dreadful vigil? I kupi ri zhu-tor wuh ralash, ri kauk wuh bestan t' wuh esh, heh wi i fai-tor ik t'nash-veh besu hayal-tor tu'ash-eyed, k'svi wuh zamu ash'ya t' me, svi' wuh ka fupa s' t' nervous tension svi' if i vesh' myself. Wuh fe-wein tresahk ska' wuh least ha'zehl t' ta'hal, heh etek bek-tor svi' ek'esik mu'khlup'es. S' s'udish sarlah wuh occasional maf t' wuh mu-yor-kushel, heh wuh'wak na' etwel maut krani wuh wu drawn catlike whine, if var-tor etek ik wuh cheetah vesh' indeed na' liberty. Irak maf etek kupi zhu-tor wuh glu molu t' wuh parish wak-vel, if orkau si' kanok yonuk t' wuh wadan. Uf wu au seemed, eifa ha-shal! Leh-dah kwul-tor, heh veh heh dahkuh heh rehkuh, heh fam dvun etek hayal-tor waiting silently na' whatever lau befall. Suddenly tra' vesh' wuh momentary gleam t' wuh ta'hal abru svi' wuh kharat t' wuh kraulayek, if vanished iyi, tonk'peh vesh' navau k' wuh karik fnish-tor t' yontau elmin heh falek-tor mokev. Ein-veh svi' wuh thurai tvi-shal had lit wuh gu'gelik-makh-yonet. I puzhu-tor wuh gentle ralash t' dvun, heh yi ek' vesh' ralash-fam wuh'wak weht, hi wuh fnish-tor grew stronger. Na' ulef wuh wadan i hayal-tor k' straining kaluk. Yi suddenly wuh'ashiv ralash became audiblea maut gentle, soothing ralash, spo' ik t' wuh pi' jet t' zhis escaping continually s' wuh kettle. Wuh instant ik etek puzhu-tor ish-veh, holmes sprang s' wuh sar-tak, kwul-tor wuh match, heh lashed furiously k' ish-veh cane na' wuh kus-vakh-seshaya. "gla-tor du ish-veh, watson?" au saul-tor. "gla-tor du ish-veh?" tonk'peh vesht gla-tor nash-veh nothing. Na' wuh moment lu holmes kwul-tor wuh ta'hal i puzhu-tor wuh neik, pa'shik whistle, tonk'peh wuh sudden glare flashing vi' t'nash-veh weary bezhun tor ish-veh impossible na' me tor var-tor ra ish-veh vesh' na' if t'nash-veh t'hy'la lashed ni savagely. I kupi, however, gla-tor ik ish-veh limuk vesh' tevalik spoh heh boshau k' horror heh loathing. Au had ceased tor kwul heh vesh' gazing abru na' wuh kraulayek lu suddenly tra' shau s' wuh silence t' wuh mu-yor wuh danik horrible maf tor if i ma ek'wak shroi. Ish-veh puv-tor abru louder heh louder, wuh hoarse saul t' kusut heh pthak heh reshan ek' mingled svi' wuh veh dreadful shriek. Au leralmin ik maf ne' svi' wuh pi'kahr, heh kauk svi' wuh irak parsonage, ik maf ashenau wuh sleepers s' ish-veh sar-tak. Ish-veh kwul-tor samu tor etwel khaf-spol, heh i lam-tor gazing na' holmes, heh au na' me, abi' wuh kim-shah vava t' ish-veh had tev-tor maf vi' wuh silence s' if ish-veh she-tor. "ra mokuhlek ish-veh tvai?" i hushau. "ish-veh tvai ik ish-veh nam-tor ek' abru', " holmes kilko-tor. "heh sos'eh, po' ek', ish-veh nam-tor na' wuh buhfik. Nem-tor ish-veh el'ru-pohshayek, heh etek dungi svi-tor dr. Roylott's tvi-shal." k' wuh shi'vukhut limuk au lit wuh ha'gelek heh pufulag-tor wuh yut ne' wuh tvur. Dah'wak au kwul-tor na' wuh tvi-shal svep rik' sovek kilko s' k'svi. Yi au da-tor wuh el'rek heh svi-tor, i na' ish-veh timut, k' wuh cocked el'ru-pohshayek svi' t'nash-veh el'ru. Ish-veh vesh' wuh singular glan if ragel-tor etwel bezhun. Fi' wuh pasu lam-tor wuh gu'gelik-makh-yonet k' wuh fe-wein ulef tu'ash, throwing wuh maut-ugelik ha-zehl t' ta'hal fi-tor wuh shek-tukh safe, wuh svep t' if vesh' ajar. Be' nash pasu, fi' wuh wooden ku-san, hayal-tor dr. Grimesby roylott clad svi' wuh wu zhai-kur sai-vel-tor-gown, ish-veh sai-famik mal-nik protruding ne'rak, heh ish-veh ash'ya kwit vi' yon-kur heelless turkish slippers. Mes' ish-veh lap ti wuh pen fek k' wuh wu lash if etek had pubeglanau du' wuh gad. Ish-veh chin vesh' cocked abru'le heh ish-veh bezhun vesh' teslau svi' wuh dreadful, stegel nantaya na' wuh teruk t' wuh abru-tol. Pauk ish-veh meix'tem au had wuh peculiar kin-kur zhel, k' brownish speckles, if seemed tor nam-tor bound tightly pauk ish-veh patam. U' etek svi-tor au tor neither ralash il dvunel. "wuh zhel! Wuh speckled zhel!" zhal-tor holmes. I nem-tor wuh ash fa'rak. Svi' wuh instant ish-veh flekh headgear began tor dvun, heh tra' reared itself s' among ish-veh isachya wuh squat lerash-khush-kushizhau patam heh puffed talu t' wuh loathsome serpent. "ish-veh nam-tor wuh flash adder!" maf-tor holmes; "wuh deadliest oluhk svi' india. Au has tev-tor k'svi lehkuh seconds t' hasu bitten. Khrash tor, svi' yeht'es, recoil fi-tor wuh khrashik, heh wuh schemer tevan-tor vi' wuh pit if au hil-tor na' wuh'ashiv. Kal-tor etek kwit nash creature pla' vi' its den, heh etek mokuhlek yi snem-tor din-tor stoner tor ein shi' rau-nol heh kal-tor wuh county police fai-tor ra has pavesh-tor." u' au stariben au drew wuh dog-wonil-zehl swiftly s' wuh tevik sasu's lap, heh throwing wuh noose pauk wuh ukraluk's talu au drew ish-veh s' its horrid perch heh, carrying ish-veh na' kar's wu-vath, threw ish-veh vi' wuh shek-tukh safe, if au a'ing fi-tor ish-veh. Such nam-tor wuh yeht kla-min t' wuh tevakh t' dr. Grimesby roylott, t' stoke moran. Ish-veh nam-tor ri bolayatik ik i dang prolong wuh narrative if has already sahr-tor tor nuh' lo'uk wuh wu-vath k' telling uf etek shau wuh maf ro'fori tor wuh terrified ko-kan, uf etek zhelesh ish-veh k' wuh asal ranau tor wuh tun t' ish-veh rom ezyet na' harrow, t' uf wuh vohris torek t' official inquiry sarlah tor wuh conclusion ik wuh hassu ragel-tor ish-veh buk du' indiscreetly mavaun k' wuh tehvar-bosh kelek-aushfa. Wuh pi' if i had wi tor oren-tor t' wuh nuf vesh' var-tor me k' sherlock holmes u' etek travelled pla' thurai gad. "i had, " leralmin-tor au, "sarlah tor wuh entirely erroneous conclusion if gluvau, t'nash-veh tal-kam watson, uf tehvar-bosh ish-veh kwon-hau-ov nam-tor tor utvau s' insufficient faik. Wuh la'es t' wuh gipsies, heh wuh nam-tor-tor t' wuh zhit 'zhel, ' if vesh' nam-tor-tor k' wuh ri donku-tor ko-kan, rai vet, tor danau wuh appearance if she had kum-tor wuh hurried glimpse t' k' wuh ta'hal t' ish-veh match, vesh' sufficient tor shitau me fi-tor wuh entirely riyeht scent. I mokuhlek goh claim wuh merit ik i instantly reconsidered t'nash-veh shul lu, however, ish-veh became pa'shik tor me ik whatever tehvar threatened wuh occupant t' wuh tvi-shal kupi ri sarlah either s' wuh krani il wuh svep. T'nash-veh attention vesh' speedily drawn, u' i ma already remarked tor du, tor nash kraulayek, heh tor wuh kus-vakh-man-elakh if geldau ne' tor wuh sar-tak. Wuh discovery ik nash vesh' wuh dummy, heh ik wuh sar-tak vesh' clamped tor wuh lan-tol, instantly mazhiv-kur-tor shen tor wuh suspicion ik wuh man-elakh vesh' tra' u' wuh mesut na' vel be' dvun-tor k'fai wuh razh heh coming tor wuh sar-tak. Wuh idea t' wuh oluhk instantly paresh-tor tor me, heh lu i coupled ish-veh k' t'nash-veh fai-tukh ik wuh hassu vesh' furnished k' wuh tanilau t' creatures s' india, i olau ik i vesh' probably fi' wuh gas'rak yut. Wuh idea t' using wuh shid t' gisam if kupi ri possibly nam-tor discovered k' sovek meli-tukh nisan vesh' aishan such wuh veh u' would paresh-tor tor wuh clever heh ruthless sasu vi had had wuh she'rakik training. Wuh rapidity k' if such wuh gisam would nem-tor daya would isha, s' ish-veh sfek t' zan-tor, nam-tor wuh advantage. Ish-veh would nam-tor wuh nasik-eyed tevanu-talsu, indeed, vi kupi distinguish wuh dahkuh pi' gu'gelik punctures if would gluvaya wilat wuh gisam wu-zud had ovsoh ish-veh ar'kadan. Yi i nahp t' wuh whistle. T' rivak au bolau recall wuh oluhk fa' wuh asal ta'hal revealed ish-veh tor wuh shi-kar-tor. Au had ranau ish-veh, probably k' wuh nam-tor-tor t' wuh thas if etek gla-tor, tor fun tor ish-veh lu summoned. Au would shitau ish-veh k'fai nash kraulayek na' wuh wadan ik au nahp buhfik, k' wuh certainty ik ish-veh would ukrau ne' wuh man-elakh heh solektra fi' wuh sar-tak. Ish-veh lau il lau ri zeshaya wuh occupant, sos'eh she lau stron kanok mu-yor na' wuh wehk gad, tonk'peh sooner il later she bolau tevan wuh shi-kar-tor. "i had sarlah tor aifa conclusions fa' ek'wak i had svi-tor ish-veh tvi-shal. Wuh inspection t' ish-veh ku-san gluvau me ik au had vesh' svi' wuh es'merka t' standing fi' ish-veh, if veling would nam-tor bolayatik svi' zek ik au dang pulau wuh kraulayek. Wuh glan t' wuh safe, wuh ne-mathra t' thas, heh wuh pakuv t' whipcord vesh' hiyet tor t'forti dispel sovek vet-tor if lau ma hafau. Wuh metallic clang puzhu-tor k' din-tor stoner vesh' obviously aisha k' ish-veh stepfather hastily ikapik wuh svep t' ish-veh safe fi-tor its terrible occupant. Having wuh'wak tor abru t'nash-veh kashek, du fai-tor wuh ash-tor if i nem-tor svi' zek tor shitau wuh tukh tor wuh skan. I puzhu-tor wuh creature shisya u' i ma rai vet ik du did isha, heh i instantly lit wuh ta'hal heh nashiv ish-veh." "k' wuh result t' driving ish-veh k'fai wuh kraulayek." "heh isha k' wuh result t' causing ish-veh tor da-tor fi-tor its trensu na' wuh vath vla. Ein t' wuh salur t' t'nash-veh cane sarlah ha-kel heh kastorilau its snakish temper, ni ik ish-veh flew fi-tor wuh wuh'rak person gla-tor ish-veh. Svi' nash yut i am rai vet indirectly responsible na' dr. Grimesby roylott's tevakh, heh i fam yehat leralmin ik ish-veh nam-tor kesik tor rasathau maut heavily fi-tor t'nash-veh conscience." ix. Wuh adventure t' wuh mishek's kaur-ozh t' ek' wuh wat if ma vesh' submitted tor t'nash-veh t'hy'la, mr. Sherlock holmes, na' kilkaya du' wuh tevun t' etwel intimacy, tra' vesh' goh dahkuh if i vesh' wuh tvai t' introducing tor ish-veh noticethat t' mr. Hatherley's kaur-ozh, heh ik t' shal-lan warburton's ni-resh. T' aifa wuh latter lau ma afforded wuh finer vunai na' wuh zat heh tveshik observer, tonk'peh wuh vath vesh' ni flekh svi' its inception heh ni dramatic svi' its details ik ish-veh lau nam-tor wuh weht worthy t' hasu shitau fi-tor vipladau, kauk kuv ish-veh mazhiv-kur-tor t'nash-veh t'hy'la fewer sharu na' eifa deductive methods t' reasoning k' if au achieved such remarkable results. Wuh var has, i dva-tor, vesh' var-tor weht do wuh'wak svi' wuh newspapers, tonk'peh, spo' ek' such narratives, its daya nam-tor mau lehkuh striking lu eku forth en bloc svi' wuh single ulef-tsek t' hish do lu wuh kla-min slowly wakrubau fa' ish-veh sha' bezhun, heh wuh mystery pa'shu gradually maf u' tik uzh discovery furnishes wuh ash if fulag-tor fi' tor wuh ovsotik yeht'es. Na' wuh wak wuh circumstances tor wuh glu impression fi-tor me, heh wuh lapse t' dahkuh tevun has hardly dvin-tor tor kobatau wuh daya. Ish-veh vesh' svi' wuh belaar t' '89, ri wu po' t'nash-veh kal'i'farr, ik wuh pavek paresh-tor if i am i' pa' tor summarise. I had fun-tor tor civil practice heh had t'forti abandoned holmes svi' ish-veh leipausu yut tvi-shal, hi i continually yaretau ish-veh heh occasionally kauk persuaded ish-veh tor forgo ish-veh bohemian es'merka ni irak u' tor sarlah heh yaret etek. T'nash-veh practice had steadily increased, heh u' i pavesh-tor tor ha-tor na' rai maut lo'uk ir s' paddington wurzel, i prah wuh zamu hasausu s' among wuh officials. Veh t' aifa, ik i had bohrau t' wuh kusut-tor heh svizh-tor has, vesh' worla weary t' advertising t'nash-veh virtues heh t' endeavouring tor satau me fi' kanok sufferer abru' ik au lau ma sovek vi-yumuk. Veh asal, na' wuh pi' fa' stehkuh o'wak-vel, i vesh' awakened k' wuh maid tapping na' wuh svep tor tor'pra ik dahkuh sasu had sarlah s' paddington heh vesh' waiting svi' wuh consulting-tvi-shal. I sai-vel-tor hurriedly, na' i fai-tor k' veshtaya ik railway nuf vesh' seldom trivial, heh hastened downstairs. U' i tev-tor, t'nash-veh hinek puk'ai'la, wuh klashausu, sasarlah t' wuh tvi-shal heh a'ing wuh svep tightly za' ish-veh. "i've prah ish-veh la', " au zhal-tor, jerking ish-veh kaur-ozh abru' ish-veh tipan; "au's ek' gas'rak." "ra nam-tor ish-veh, yi?" i ya'akash, na' ish-veh manner suggested ik ish-veh vesh' ein flekh creature if au had kraiskau abru svi' t'nash-veh tvi-shal. "ish-veh's wuh uzh hasausu, " au zhal-tor. "i nahp i'd katau ish-veh pauk myself; yi au couldn't trel maf. Tra' au nam-tor, ek' safe heh ralash. I bolau hal-tor i', hassu; i ma t'nash-veh dooties, aishan wuh ka u' du." heh ska' au went, nash trusty tout, rik' kauk giving me wak tor itaren ish-veh. I svi-tor t'nash-veh consulting-tvi-shal heh afer-tor wuh gentleman hayal-tor k' wuh pasu. Au vesh' quietly sai-vel-tor svi' wuh saikhut t' heather tweed k' wuh mos sai taik if au had laid ne' fi-tor t'nash-veh dunap. Pauk veh t' ish-veh el'ru au had wuh handkerchief wrapped, if vesh' mottled ek' abru' k' bloodstains. Au vesh' nu'ri, ri weht do kaukuh-heh-dah-leh, i dang leralmin, k' wuh karik, masculine limuk; tonk'peh au vesh' exceedingly spoh heh mazhiv-kur-tor me wuh impression t' wuh sasu vi vesh' suffering s' ein karik agitation, if ish-veh nem-tor ek' ish-veh karik'es t' kashek tor tash. "ni'droi'ik nar-tor tor knock du abru ni lehkuh-mal, hassu, " leralmin-tor au, "tonk'peh i ma had wuh maut serious kisheya du' wuh mu-yor. Vesht sarlah nash-veh svi' k' ranau nash asal, heh fi' inquiring na' paddington u' tor wilat i lau talal wuh hassu, wuh worthy katravahsu maut kindly escorted me la'. I mazhiv-kur-tor wuh maid wuh nop, tonk'peh gla-tor nash-veh ik she has losrak ish-veh fi-tor wuh vla-pasu." i nem-tor ish-veh abru heh glanced na' ish-veh. "mr. Skilsu hatherley, hydraulic mishek, 16a, victoria yut (3rd lan-tol)." ik vesh' wuh ahm, style, heh abode t' t'nash-veh asal visitor. "i regret ik i ma potau du waiting, " leralmin-tor i, sitting ne' svi' t'nash-veh shi'dunap-ku-san. "du nam-tor sluk s' wuh mu-yor halovaya, i ken-tor, if nam-tor svi' itself wuh monotonous occupation." "oh, t'nash-veh mu-yor kupi ri nam-tor puvutau monotonous, " leralmin-tor au, heh abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor. Au abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor maut heartily, k' wuh pid, ringing pitoh, leaning pla' svi' ish-veh ku-san heh shaking ish-veh vla. Ek' t'nash-veh hasuk instincts she-tor abru tehnat ik abru'teruklar-ru'lut. "pehkaya ish-veh!" i maf-tor; "seshaya yourself teretuhr!" heh i mukau si' ein masu s' wuh caraffe. Ish-veh vesh' nam-tor-fam, however. Au vesh' ska' svi' veh t' eifa hysterical outbursts if sarlah fi-tor wuh karik malat lu ein lo'uk burun nam-tor abru' heh hal-tor. Presently sarlah ish-veh tor himself wuh'wak weht, maut weary heh spoh-looking. "i ma vesh' tor wuh duhsu t' myself, " au hushau. "mokov. La masu." i dashed ein brandy vi' wuh masu, heh wuh kur began tor sarlah pla' tor ish-veh bloodless nak. "ik's weh-rom!" leralmin-tor au. "heh i', hassu, sos'eh du would kindly attend tor t'nash-veh kaur-ozh, il rather tor wuh shi wilat t'nash-veh kaur-ozh nam-tor-tor tor nam-tor." au unwound wuh handkerchief heh meskarau si' ish-veh el'ru. Ish-veh mazhiv-kur-tor kauk t'nash-veh hardened tor'tsu wuh ak'shem-hutau tor glazhau na' ish-veh. Tra' vesh' kehkuh protruding ozh heh wuh horrid yon-kur, spongy skonn wilat wuh kaur-ozh dang ma vesh'. Ish-veh had vesh' hacked il torn gas'rak si' s' wuh gir. "rom heavens!" i maf-tor, "nash nam-tor wuh terrible dash. Ish-veh bolau ma bled considerably." "ha, ish-veh did. I fainted lu ish-veh vesh' ovsoh, heh i nah-tor ik i bolau ma vesh' senseless na' wuh akarshif. Lu vesht sarlah nash-veh tor i afer-tor ik ish-veh vesh' fam dvun khafaya, ni i tied veh shaht t' t'nash-veh handkerchief maut tightly pauk wuh kar-nik heh fir-tor ish-veh abru k' wuh pi'gel." "marom! Du dang ma vesh' wuh sharushsu." "ish-veh nam-tor wuh deshker t' masu-mish-tal, gla-tor du, heh sarlah k'svi t'nash-veh sha' province." "nash has vesh' ovsoh, " leralmin-tor i, examining wuh skek, "k' wuh maut ras heh nasik instrument." "wuh vel spo' wuh threshek, " leralmin-tor au. "wuh kisheya, i presume?" "k' rai tvai." "ra! Wuh murderous nashiv-tor?" "maut murderous indeed." "du horrify me." i sponged wuh skek, pu-tor ish-veh, sai-vel-tor ish-veh, heh t'forti wein-tor ish-veh abru' k' cotton wadding heh carbolised zhumav. Au ti pla' rik' wincing, hi au zeshau ish-veh bru s' wak tor wak. "uf nam-tor ik?" i ya'akash lu i had shahtau. "capital! Svi' ish-veh brandy heh ish-veh zhumav, i olau wuh uzh sasu. I vesh' maut kobat, tonk'peh i ma had wuh rom deal tor hal-tor k'fai." "sos'eh du had weh-rom ri stariben t' wuh tukh. Ish-veh nam-tor evidently trying tor ish-veh tor'tsu." "oh, rai, ri i'. I dungau ma tor var-tor t'nash-veh var tor wuh police; tonk'peh, svi' ourselves, kuv ish-veh vesh' ri na' wuh convincing evidence t' nash skek t' t'nash-veh, i dang nam-tor ak'wikmun kuv au pudva-tor t'nash-veh star-krus, na' ish-veh nam-tor wuh maut wehtsuri veh, heh i ma ri mau svi' wuh yut t' skan k' if tor pla' ish-veh abru; heh, kauk kuv au dva-tor me, wuh clues if i mokuhlek mazhiv-kur-tor au nam-tor ni vague ik ish-veh nam-tor wuh deshker whether yeht-gav dungi nam-tor ovsoh." "ha!" maf-tor i, "kuv ish-veh nam-tor sovek-vel svi' wuh malat t' wuh wat if du aitlun tor gla-tor kilau, i dang strongly recommend du tor sarlah tor t'nash-veh t'hy'la, mr. Sherlock holmes, fa' du hal-tor tor wuh official police." "oh, i ma puzhu-tor t' ik katravahsu, " kilko-tor t'nash-veh visitor, "heh i dang nam-tor maut glad kuv au would nem-tor wuh tukh abru, hi veling i bolau nam-tor-tor wuh official police u' muhl. Would du mazhiv-kur-tor me wuh ragtaya tor ish-veh?" "i'll tor weh-rom. I'll nem-tor du pauk tor ish-veh myself." "i dang nam-tor immensely obliged tor du." "etek'll vutau wuh cab heh hal-tor teretuhr. Etek dungau aishan nam-tor svi' wak ki' wuh pi' asal-yem k' ish-veh. Tor du olau kaik tor ish-veh?" "ha; i dungau ri olau hagik abi' i ma var-tor t'nash-veh var." "yi t'nash-veh dvinsu dungi vutau wuh cab, heh i dungau nam-tor k' du svi' wuh instant." i rushed upstairs, danau wuh tukh shortly tor t'nash-veh ko-telsu, heh svi' kaukuh minutes vesh' svi'udish wuh hansom, driving k' t'nash-veh uzh acquaintance tor leipausu yut. Sherlock holmes vesh', u' i gishu, lounging pa' ish-veh sitting-tvi-shal svi' ish-veh sai-vel-tor-gown, telvan wuh agony tsek t' wuh wak heh smoking ish-veh fa'-asal-yem mev, if vesh' tertitau t' ek' wuh plugs heh dottles losrak s' ish-veh vuzh t' wuh gad fa', ek' carefully psethau heh tershau fi' wuh teruk t' wuh mantelpiece. Au poprah etek svi' ish-veh quietly genial fashion, ordered sluk rashers heh yu-mur, heh hau etek svi' wuh hearty yem. Lu ish-veh vesh' concluded au settled etwel uzh acquaintance fi-tor wuh ku-san, shitau wuh trak ne'rak ish-veh patam, heh laid wuh makh t' brandy heh masu k'svi ish-veh pulau. "ish-veh nam-tor hagik tor gla-tor ik ish-veh veshtaya has vesh' rai tsuri veh, mr. Hatherley, " leralmin-tor au. "pray, ti ne' tra' heh tor yourself absolutely na' ha-kel. Var-tor etek ra du mokuhlek, tonk'peh pehkaya lu du nam-tor zungor heh potau abru ish-veh karik'es k' wuh pi' stimulant." "nemaiyo, " leralmin-tor t'nash-veh hasausu, "tonk'peh i ma olau wuh'ashiv sasu opi' wuh hassu bandaged me, heh i nah-tor ik ish-veh asal-yem has ovsoh wuh bohrau. I dungau nem-tor abru u' pi' t' ish-veh taluhk wak u' tor-yehat, ni i dungau palikaya na' wuh'wak fi-tor t'nash-veh peculiar veshtau." holmes hayal-tor svi' ish-veh suk' armchair k' wuh weary, ras-lidded sagluvaya if veiled ish-veh keen heh nayik malat, du' i hayal-tor mesyutik tor ish-veh, heh etek shroi svi' silence tor wuh flekh var if etwel visitor detailed tor etek. "du bolau fai-tor, " leralmin-tor au, "ik i am wuh orphan heh wuh bachelor, residing sa'awek svi' lodgings svi' london. K' ha'yigal i am wuh hydraulic mishek, heh i ma had considerable veshtaya t' t'nash-veh ar'kadan du' wuh stehkuh tevun ik i vesh' apprenticed tor venner & matheson, wuh muhl-fainu pesik, t' greenwich. Dahkuh tevun ago, having dvin-tor t'nash-veh wak, heh having isha sarlah vi' wuh rom hau-ov t' donku k'fai t'nash-veh ri donku-tor sa-mekh's tevakh, i satalau tor palikaya svi' business na' myself heh nem-tor professional tvi-shal svi' victoria yut. "i suppose ik kanok-veh tal-tor ish-veh wuh'rak independent palikaya svi' business wuh dreary veshtaya. Tor me ish-veh has vesh' exceptionally ni. Du' dahkuh tevun i ma had rehkuh consultations heh veh pi' job, heh ik nam-tor absolutely ek' ik t'nash-veh ha'yigal has katau me. T'nash-veh gross takings nosahp tor 27 10s. Kanok gad, s' naukuh svi' wuh asal abi' kehkuh svi' wuh aru, i bek-tor svi' t'nash-veh pi' den, abi' na' kim-shah t'nash-veh khaf-spol began tor ne'hal-tor, heh vesht sarlah nash-veh tor dva-tor ik i dang worla ma sovek practice na' ek'. "za-gad, however, aishan u' i vesh' thinking t' leaving wuh office, t'nash-veh clerk svi-tor tor leralmin tra' vesh' wuh gentleman waiting vi istau tor gla-tor me fi-tor business. Au katau abru wuh nop, nuh', k' wuh ahm t' 'shal-lan lysander stark' thes-na' fi-tor ish-veh. Ikap-tor na' ish-veh timut sarlah wuh shal-lan himself, wuh sasu rather abru' wuh svitan suk'es, tonk'peh t' wuh namautauk thinness. I ri tor nah-tor ik i ma ek'wak gla-tor ni wonil wuh sasu. Ish-veh bosh limuk sharpened maf vi' han heh chin, heh wuh wadi t' ish-veh nak vesh' drawn ved wis abru' ish-veh outstanding hinek. Wi nash emaciation seemed tor nam-tor ish-veh malatik es'merka, heh due tor rai has, na' ish-veh bezhun vesh' ugelik, ish-veh ash brax, heh ish-veh kuvish assured. Au vesh' plainly tonk'peh neatly sai-vel-tor, heh ish-veh ya'shakhuv, i dang judge, would nam-tor nearer keh-leh do reh-leh. "'mr. Hatherley?' leralmin-tor au, k' vel t' wuh german accent. 'du ma vesh' recommended tor me, mr. Hatherley, u' hasu wuh sasu vi nam-tor ri goh proficient svi' ish-veh ha'yigal tonk'peh nam-tor isha discreet heh capable t' preserving wuh tsat.' "i ovalau, olaya u' snuhkrol-tor u' sovek nu'ri sasu would na' such wuh shi'yavekh. 'sos ya'akash vi ish-veh vesh' vi mazhiv-kur-tor me ni rom wuh character?' "'muhl, sos'eh ish-veh nam-tor weh-rom ik i dang ri var-tor du ik aishan na' nash moment. "'ik nam-tor ved yeht, ' i kilko-tor; 'tonk'peh du dungi tobeg me kuv i leralmin ik i fam yehat gla-tor uf ek' nash bears fi-tor t'nash-veh professional qualifications. "'kuv i ugaya tor potau wuh tsat, ' leralmin-tor i, 'du lau absolutely nerau fi-tor t'nash-veh doing ni.' "au glazhau maut lerash na' me u' i stariben, heh ish-veh seemed tor me ik i had worla gla-tor ni suspicious heh questioning wuh bezhun. "'tor du ugaya, yi?' leralmin-tor au na' kim-shah. "'ha, i ugaya.' "'ek'esik heh ovsotik silence fa', du', heh po'? Rai dzhinaya tor wuh tukh na' ek', either svi' zhit il kitaun?' "'i ma already putan-tor du t'nash-veh zhit.' "'maut rom.' au suddenly sprang abru, heh darting spo' igen-wesh mes' wuh tvi-shal au flung tu'ash wuh svep. Wuh tvur s'udish vesh' herbosh. "'ik's ek' gas'rak, ' leralmin-tor au, coming pla'. 'i fai-tor ik clerks nam-tor sometimes curious u' tor ish-veh trensu's tek'ik. I' etek mokuhlek variben svi' ek'manek.' au drew abru ish-veh ku-san maut beyik t'nash-veh heh began tor nantaya na' me va'ashiv k' wuh ka questioning heh thoughtful glazhau. "wuh olaya t' repulsion, heh t' vel akin tor pthak had palikau tor shen k'svi me na' wuh flekh antics t' nash fleshless sasu. "'uf would kau-leh guineas na' wuh mu-yor's ar'kadan saikhut du?' au ya'akash. "'danik admirably.' "'i leralmin wuh mu-yor's ar'kadan, tonk'peh wuh wadan's would nam-tor nearer wuh ulidar. Sos ri sarlah na' ein weht convenient wadan?' "'etek ma judged ish-veh buhfik ik du dang sarlah tab-ma. Fam dvun, veling, kuv du would spo' tor bes-tor s' wuh business, tra' nam-tor plenty t' wak tor tor ni.' "i nahp t' wuh kau-leh guineas, heh t' uf maut useful au would nam-tor tor me. "'ved ni. Ish-veh nam-tor maut malatik ik wuh pledge t' secrecy if etek ma faikaik s' du dang ma aroused ish-veh curiosity. Du nam-tor probably aware ik fuller's-terra nam-tor wuh taluhk torvauk, heh ik ish-veh nam-tor goh afer-tor svi' veh il dahkuh shitau svi' england?' "'i ma puzhu-tor ni.' "'ein pi' wak ago i bought wuh pi' placea maut pi' placewithin lehkuh miles t' telvan. I vesh' fortunate hiyet tor discover ik tra' vesh' wuh titaya t' fuller's-terra svi' veh t' t'nash-veh vunai. Aifa rom sutra vesh' absolutely ignorant ik ish-veh solektra tuhlau ik if vesh' ved u' taluhk u' wuh pi-maat-tukh-t'nash-veh. Naturally, ish-veh vesh' tor t'nash-veh eku'ko tor mahr-tor ish-veh solektra fa' au discovered its yeht tala, tonk'peh unfortunately i had rai capital k' if i kupi tor nash. I nem-tor wuh zamu t' t'nash-veh t'hylara vi' wuh tsat, however, heh au suggested ik etek dang quietly heh secretly ar'kadan etwel sha' pi' titaya heh ik svi' nash yut etek dang pinkau wuh donku if would enable etek tor mahr-tor wuh neighbouring vunai. Nash etek ma i' vesh' doing na' ein wak, heh svi' zek tor gol'nev etek svi' etwel el'toraya etek abru-tor wuh hydraulic hish-tor. Etek klashausu etwel tsat maut jealously, however, heh kuv ish-veh wuh'wak became fainu ik etek had hydraulic mishek coming tor etwel pi' kelek, ish-veh would ak kastorilau inquiry, heh yi, kuv wuh kla-min sasarlah, ish-veh would nam-tor rom-bye tor sovek pavesh t' getting aifa vunai heh carrying si' etwel dotoran. Ik nam-tor po i ma tor du ugaya me ik du dungi ri var-tor wuh komihn hasu ik du nam-tor going tor eyford tor-mu-yor. I rok ik i tor ish-veh ek' eiktra?' "'i ved zahal-tor du, ' leralmin-tor i. 'wuh goh sfek if i kupi ri ved ken-tor vesh' ra nam-tor-tor du kupi tor t' wuh hydraulic hish-tor svi' excavating fuller's-terra, if, u' i ken-tor, nam-tor hil-tor si' spo' krus-kov s' wuh pit.' "'ah!' leralmin-tor au carelessly, 'etek ma etwel sha' torek. Etek lerakhovau wuh terra vi' dok, ni u' tor snem-tor au rik' revealing ra au nam-tor. Tonk'peh ik nam-tor wuh mere detail. I ma taken du fully vi' t'nash-veh guhl'es i', mr. Hatherley, heh i ma shown du uf i sahrafel du.' au she-tor u' au stariben. 'i dungau gish du, yi, na' eyford na' 11: 15.' "'i dungau certainly nam-tor tra'.' "'heh ri wuh zhit tor wuh soul.' au glazhau na' me k' wuh kim-shah wu, questioning gaze, heh yi, pressing t'nash-veh el'ru svi' wuh samu, dank ruskaraya, au hurried s' wuh tvi-shal. "muhl, lu vesht sarlah nash-veh tor nah-tor ish-veh ek' abru' svi' samuyau khaf i vesh' maut mau astonished, u' du lau fi' nah-tor, na' nash sudden kadvin if had vesh' intrusted tor me. Fi' wuh veh el'ru, veling, i vesh' glad, na' wuh uz vesh' k'puu tenfold ra i dang ma ya'akash had i eku wuh price fi-tor t'nash-veh sha' dvin, heh ish-veh vesh' tor-yehat ik nash zek lau ras-tukh tor vath ones. Fi' wuh vath el'ru, wuh limuk heh manner t' t'nash-veh patron had tor wuh unpleasant impression fi-tor me, heh i kupi ri nah-tor ik ish-veh danaya t' wuh fuller's-terra vesh' sufficient tor danau wuh bolayek na' t'nash-veh coming na' midnight, heh ish-veh mairik anxiety lest i dang var-tor sovek-veh t' t'nash-veh skrol. However, i threw ek' ptha tor wuh salan, ate wuh hearty mu'yor-yem, drove tor paddington, heh palikau ska', having obeyed tor wuh nuhm wuh injunction u' tor holding t'nash-veh lahv. "na' telvan i had tor rubah ri goh t'nash-veh carriage tonk'peh t'nash-veh wurzel. However, i vesh' svi' wak na' wuh kim-shah ranau tor eyford, heh i pulau wuh pi' neik-ha'khlup-lit wurzel po' leh-wun o'wak-vel. I vesh' wuh goh passenger vi prah si' tra', heh tra' vesh' kling fi-tor wuh skaf korsau wuh single sleepy porter k' wuh makh-yonet. U' i be' dvun-tor si' k'fai wuh wicket temep, however, i afer-tor t'nash-veh acquaintance t' wuh asal waiting svi' wuh duv fi-tor wuh vath vla. Rik' wuh zhit au ruskarau t'nash-veh kar heh hurried me vi' wuh carriage, wuh svep t' if vesh' standing tu'ash. Au drew abru wuh krani fi' either vla, tapped fi' wuh lapan-ar'kadan, heh maf etek went u' sahris u' wuh jarel kupi hal-tor." "veh jarel?" interjected holmes. "ha, goh veh." "did du glantau wuh kur?" "ha, vesht gla-tor nash-veh ish-veh k' wuh vla-ha'ge lu i vesh' stepping vi' wuh carriage. Ish-veh vesh' wuh chestnut." "zungor-looking il sluk?" "oh, sluk heh glossy." "nemaiyo. Ni'droi'ik nar-tor ki' svi-shau du. Pray fator ish-veh danik eku'ki star-krus." "maf etek went yi, heh etek drove na' k'puu wuh wadan. Shal-lan lysander stark had leralmin-tor ik ish-veh vesh' goh stehkuh miles, tonk'peh i dang nah-tor, s' wuh tav ik etek seemed tor hal-tor, heh s' wuh wak ik etek nem-tor, ik ish-veh bolau ma vesh' nearer leh-dah. Au hayal-tor na' t'nash-veh vla svi' silence ek' wuh wak, heh i vesh' aware, weht do wuh'wak lu i glanced svi' ish-veh kharat, ik au vesh' looking na' me k' lo'uk flan'es. Wuh shasol fau-yut seem tor nam-tor ri maut rom svi' ik krus t' wuh panu, na' etek lurched heh jolted terribly. I ar'kada tor glazhau s' wuh krani tor gla-tor vel t' wilat etek vesh', tonk'peh au vesh' tor t' le-su makh, heh i kupi tor si' nothing korsau wuh occasional ugelik blur t' wuh be' dvun-tor ta'hal. I' heh yi i hazarded ein remark tor shaya wuh monotony t' wuh halovaya, tonk'peh wuh shal-lan kilko-tor goh svi' monosyllables, heh wuh conversation ak flagged. Na' kim-shah, however, wuh bumping t' wuh fau-yut vesh' di'kizh-tor na' wuh crisp smoothness t' wuh krus-kov-yetur, heh wuh carriage sarlah tor wuh lamok. Ish-veh grew broader, heh wuh kosu saudau k' wuh ha'gelek svi' ish-veh el'ru, if she meskarau abru' ish-veh patam, pushing ish-veh limuk fa'rak heh peering na' etek. Kupi gla-tor nash-veh ik she vesh' takov, heh s' wuh gloss k' if wuh ta'hal min-tor fi-tor ish-veh gu'gelik sai-vel i fai-tor ik ish-veh vesh' wuh don-ka tukh. She stariben wuh zamu zhit svi' wuh k'shatri lahv svi' wuh molu u' hi asking wuh deshker, heh lu t'nash-veh besu kilko-tor svi' wuh gruff monosyllable she mazhiv-kur-tor such wuh palikaya ik wuh ha'gelek nearly tevan-tor s' ish-veh el'ru. "'sos'eh du dungi ma wuh kindness tor bek-tor svi' nash tvi-shal na' wuh zamu minutes, ' leralmin-tor au, throwing tu'ash wuh'ashiv svep. Shal-lan stark laid ne' wuh ha'gelek fi' wuh fik t' wuh harmonium be' wuh svep. 'i dungau ri potau du waiting wuh instant, ' leralmin-tor au, heh vanished vi' wuh mu'khlup'es. "i glanced na' wuh dunap fi-tor wuh pasu, heh svi' spite t' t'nash-veh ignorance t' german kupi gla-tor nash-veh ik dahkuh t' au vesh' treatises fi' ek'tal, wuh vath hasu mog'es t' poetry. Yi i lates-tor mes' tor wuh krani, hoping ik i lau kum ein glimpse t' wuh shasol-vla, tonk'peh wuh oak fe-wein, heavily barred, vesh' hesha mes' ish-veh. Ish-veh vesh' wuh wonderfully ralash-fam kelek. Tra' vesh' wuh hinek wak-vel ticking loudly ein-wilat svi' wuh tvur, tonk'peh vathru kanok-vei vesh' tevalik fam dvun. Wuh vague olaya t' uneasiness began tor vazgau abru' me. Vi vesh' aifa german sutra, heh ra vesh' au doing living svi' nash flekh, si'-t'-wuh-yut shi? Heh wilat vesh' wuh shi? I vesh' lehkuh miles il ni s' eyford, ik vesh' ek' i fai-tor, tonk'peh whether desh'rak, khu'rak, she'rak, il tev'rak i had rai idea. Na' ik tukh, telvan, heh possibly vath suk kahr, vesh' k'svi ik sakuvu, ni wuh shi lau ri nam-tor ni secluded, po' ek'. Wi ish-veh vesh' ved ac'ruth, s' wuh ek'esik stillness, ik etek vesh' svi' wuh shasol. I sahr-tor abru heh ne' wuh tvi-shal, humming wuh tvelkau ne' t'nash-veh esh tor potau abru t'nash-veh tam'a heh olaya ik i vesh' thoroughly earning t'nash-veh kau-leh-guinea uz. "suddenly, rik' sovek preliminary ralash svi' wuh midst t' wuh utter stillness, wuh svep t' t'nash-veh tvi-shal swung slowly tu'ash. Wuh kosu vesh' standing svi' wuh sharu, wuh mu'khlup'es t' wuh tvur za' ish-veh, wuh kin-kur ta'hal s' t'nash-veh ha'gelek beating fi-tor ish-veh nayik heh vaksurik limuk. I kupi gla-tor na' wuh glance ik she vesh' has-bosh k' pthak, heh wuh glan satau wuh chill tor t'nash-veh sha' khaf-spol. She meskarau abru veh shaking ozh tor vikau me tor nam-tor ralash-fam, heh she pohshaya wuh zamu zhal-tor zhit t' pushau eingelsu na' me, ish-veh bezhun glancing pla', spo' eifa t' wuh koltha jarel, vi' wuh gloom za' ish-veh. "'i would hal-tor, ' leralmin-tor she, trying lerash, u' ish-veh seemed tor me, tor stariben calmly; 'i would hal-tor. I dang ri stay la'. Tra' nam-tor rai rom na' du tor tor.' "'tonk'peh, madam, ' leralmin-tor i, 'i ma ri wi ovsoh ra vesht sarlah nash-veh na'. I fam yehat possibly trasha abi' ki'gla-tor nash-veh wuh mish-vel.' "'ish-veh nam-tor ri don ish-veh du' tor bek-tor, ' she went fi'. 'du mokuhlek be' dvun k'fai wuh svep; kling hinders.' heh yi, seeing ik i abru'teruklar-ru'lut heh hutau t'nash-veh patam, she suddenly threw aside ish-veh constraint heh tor wuh ash fa'rak, k' ish-veh el'ru wrung teretuhr. 'na' wuh ashaya t' sha-ka-ri!' she zhal-tor, 'prah maf s' la' fa' ish-veh nam-tor nuh' tab-ma!' "tonk'peh i am somewhat headstrong k' malat, heh wuh weht pok tor engage svi' wuh tek'ik lu tra' nam-tor ein obstacle svi' wuh yut. I nahp t' t'nash-veh kau-leh-guinea uz, t' t'nash-veh wearisome halovaya, heh t' wuh unpleasant mu-yor if seemed tor nam-tor fa' me. Vesh' ish-veh ek' tor hal-tor na' nothing? Po dang i slink maf rik' having fitor t'nash-veh kadvin, heh rik' wuh vlitaya if vesh' t'nash-veh due? Nash kosu lau, na' ek' i fai-tor, nam-tor wuh monomaniac. K' wuh stout kuvish, therefore, hi ish-veh manner had shaken me weht do i tun-tor tor confess, i fam dvun hutau t'nash-veh patam heh afsakau t'nash-veh intention t' remaining wilat i vesh'. She vesh' pa' tor uzhau ish-veh entreaties lu wuh svep slammed overhead, heh wuh ralash t' several footsteps vesh' puzhu-tor fi-tor wuh kaiden. She shroi na' wuh instant, threw abru ish-veh el'ru k' wuh despairing gesture, heh vanished u' suddenly heh u' noiselessly u' she had sarlah. "wuh newcomers vesh' shal-lan lysander stark heh wuh pen bali sasu k' wuh chinchilla hisahk growing s' wuh creases t' ish-veh dahtau chin, vi vesh' puragtau tor me u' mr. Ferguson. "'nash nam-tor t'nash-veh secretary heh khartausu, ' leralmin-tor wuh shal-lan. 'k' wuh yut, i vesh' ne' wuh impression ik i losrak nash svep ikap-tor aishan i'. I pthak ik du ma olau wuh draught.' "'fi' wuh contrary, ' leralmin-tor i, 'i tu'ash wuh svep myself fai'ei i olau wuh tvi-shal tor nam-tor wuh pi' ikap-tor.' "au pohshaya veh t' ish-veh suspicious glazhau na' me. 'sos'eh etek had weh-rom proceed tor business, yi, ' leralmin-tor au. 'mr. Ferguson heh i dungi nem-tor du abru tor gla-tor wuh mish-vel.' "'i had weh-rom shitau t'nash-veh taik fi', i suppose.' "'oh, rai, ish-veh nam-tor svi' wuh kelek.' "'ra, du hil-tor fuller's-terra svi' wuh kelek?' "'rai, rai. Nash nam-tor goh wilat etek lerakhovau ish-veh. Tonk'peh worla kashek ik. Ek' etek istaya du tor tor nam-tor tor linisau wuh mish-vel heh tor kal-tor etek fai-tor ra nam-tor riyeht k' ish-veh.' "etek went upstairs teretuhr, wuh shal-lan wuh'rak k' wuh ha'gelek, wuh thelik khartausu heh i za' ish-veh. Ish-veh vesh' wuh labyrinth t' wuh hinek kelek, k' tvur, tvur, wonil kuvoran staircases, heh pi' neik svep, wuh thresholds t' if vesh' hollowed si' k' wuh generations vi had tuhsau au. Tra' vesh' rai la'y heh rai glat t' sovek furniture abru' wuh solektra lan-tol, du' wuh plaster vesh' puhnk-tor ska' wuh temok, heh wuh damp vesh' breaking k'fai svi' yar-kur, unhealthy blotches. I ar'kada tor shitau fi' u' unconcerned wuh sov u' tor-yehat, tonk'peh i had ri yen-tor wuh warnings t' wuh t'sai, kauk hi i bau-tor au, heh i potau wuh keen bezhun fi-tor t'nash-veh dahkuh besu. Ferguson saudau tor nam-tor wuh morose heh ralash-fam sasu, tonk'peh kupi gla-tor nash-veh s' wuh pi' ik au leralmin-tor ik au vesh' k'puu wuh katravahsu-countryman. "shal-lan lysander stark pehkau na' kim-shah fa' wuh neik svep, if au unlocked. K'svi vesh' wuh pi', keh-vla tvi-shal, svi' if wuh rehkuh t' etek kupi hardly prah na' veh wak. Ferguson hafau s'udish, heh wuh shal-lan ushered me svi'. "'etek nam-tor i', ' leralmin-tor au, 'actually k'svi wuh hydraulic hish-tor, heh ish-veh would nam-tor wuh wa' unpleasant vel na' etek kuv sovek-veh vesh' tor da-tor ish-veh fi'. Wuh abru-tol t' nash pi' tvi-shal nam-tor really wuh shaht t' wuh descending kwit-patam, heh sarlah ish-veh ne' k' wuh nekwitaya t' wehk tons fi-tor nash mokev lan-tol. Tra' nam-tor pi' lateral tsek t' masu s'udish if poprah wuh nekwitaya, heh if sasau heh wehkovau ish-veh svi' wuh manner if nam-tor familiar tor du. Wuh mish-vel hal-tor readily hiyet, tonk'peh tra' nam-tor ein stiffness svi' wuh working t' ish-veh, heh ish-veh has pakik wuh pi' t' its nekwitaya. Sos'eh du dungi ma wuh goodness tor glazhau ish-veh abru' heh tor gluvaya etek uf etek mokuhlek eku ish-veh gas'rak.' "i nem-tor wuh ha'gelek s' ish-veh, heh i linisau wuh mish-vel maut thoroughly. Ish-veh vesh' indeed wuh masuk' veh, heh capable t' exercising masuk' ne'hish. Lu i be' dvun-tor s'udish, however, heh hish-tor ne' wuh levers if tash-tor ish-veh, i fai-tor na' wuh'wak k' wuh whishing ralash ik tra' vesh' wuh slight leakage, if kal-tor wuh regurgitation t' masu k'fai veh t' wuh vla cylinders. Wuh linisaya gluvau ish-veh t' wuh india-rubber zhel if vesh' pauk wuh patam t' wuh driving-fek had shrunk ni u' ri ved tor boshaya wuh socket bi' if ish-veh ar'kada. Nash vesh' clearly wuh aishan t' wuh pak t' tepul, heh i sfekau ish-veh si' tor t'nash-veh besu, vi zahal-tor t'nash-veh remarks maut carefully heh ya'akash several practical deshkau u' tor uf au dang proceed tor eku ish-veh gas'rak. Lu i had tor ish-veh pa'shik tor au, i fun-tor tor wuh nen tvi-shal t' wuh mish-vel heh nem-tor wuh rom glazhau na' ish-veh tor satisfy t'nash-veh sha' curiosity. Ish-veh vesh' obvious na' wuh glance ik wuh var t' wuh fuller's-terra vesh' wuh merest fabrication, na' ish-veh would nam-tor absurd tor suppose ik ni powerful wuh mishu kupi nam-tor designed na' ni inadequate wuh lof. Wuh temok vesh' t' lapan, tonk'peh wuh lan-tol consisted t' wuh suk shek-tukh trough, heh lu vesht sarlah nash-veh tor linisau ish-veh kupi gla-tor nash-veh wuh puhnk t' metallic titaya ek' abru' ish-veh. I had stooped heh vesh' scraping na' nash tor gla-tor exactly ra ish-veh vesh' lu i puzhu-tor wuh muttered sporun svi' german heh gla-tor wuh cadaverous limuk t' wuh shal-lan looking ne' na' me. "'ra nam-tor du doing tra'?' au ya'akash. "i olau reshnek na' having vesh' tricked k' ni elaborate wuh var u' ik if au had var-tor me. 'i vesh' krol-tor ish-veh fuller's-terra, ' leralmin-tor i; 'i nah-tor ik i dang nam-tor weh-rom kup tor na'shikhau du u' tor ish-veh mish-vel kuv i fai-tor ra wuh faikaik lof vesh' na' if ish-veh vesh' nam-tor-tor.' "wuh instant ik i uttered wuh zhit i regretted wuh rashness t' t'nash-veh starun. Ish-veh limuk eku lerash, heh wuh baleful ta'hal sprang abru svi' ish-veh zhai-kur bezhun. "'maut muhl, ' leralmin-tor au, 'du dungau fai-tor ek' pa' wuh mish-vel.' au nem-tor wuh ash pla'rak, slammed wuh pi' svep, heh da-tor wuh tal-muv svi' wuh klachek. I rushed na' ish-veh heh seshau na' wuh el'rek, tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' ved shar, heh did ri mazhiv-kur-tor svi' wuh least tor t'nash-veh kicks heh shoves. 'hullo!' i saul-tor. 'hullo! Shal-lan! Kal-tor me si'!' "heh yi suddenly svi' wuh silence i puzhu-tor wuh ralash if satau t'nash-veh khaf-spol vi' t'nash-veh ru'lut. Ish-veh vesh' wuh clank t' wuh levers heh wuh swish t' wuh leaking cylinder. Au had eku wuh mishu na' ar'kadan. Wuh ha'gelek fam dvun lam-tor fi-tor wuh lan-tol wilat i had shitau ish-veh lu examining wuh trough. K' its ta'hal vesht gla-tor nash-veh ik wuh nesh-kur abru-tol vesh' coming ne' fi-tor me, slowly, jerkily, tonk'peh, u' rim fai-tor weh-rom do myself, k' wuh nekwitaya if bolau k'svi wuh minute grazhau me tor wuh shapeless pulp. I threw myself, screaming, tehnat wuh svep, heh zaseshau k' t'nash-veh felu na' wuh klachek. I implored wuh shal-lan tor kal-tor me si', tonk'peh wuh remorseless clanking t' wuh levers mastevau t'nash-veh maf-tor. Wuh abru-tol vesh' goh wuh ash'ya il dahkuh abru' t'nash-veh patam, heh k' t'nash-veh el'ru upraised i kupi olau its lerash, rough skonn. Yi ish-veh kahai k'fai t'nash-veh kashek ik wuh kusut t' t'nash-veh tevakh would nerau maut mau fi-tor wuh shul svi' if i ragel-tor ish-veh. Kuv i ti fi' t'nash-veh limuk wuh rasath would sarlah fi-tor t'nash-veh plat, heh i ak'shem-hutau tor nah-tor t' ik dreadful snap. Easier wuh vath yut, sos'eh; heh wi, had i wuh tor'tsu tor ti heh glazhau abru na' ik tevalik nesh-kur duv wavering ne' fi-tor me? Already i vesh' unable tor lamok abru-tor, lu t'nash-veh bezhun kum-tor vel if katau wuh gush t' rok pla' tor t'nash-veh khaf-spol. "i ma leralmin-tor ik hi wuh lan-tol heh abru-tol vesh' t' shek-tukh, wuh temok vesh' t' lapan. U' i mazhiv-kur-tor wuh kim-shah hurried glance pa', vesht gla-tor nash-veh wuh wonil zehl t' kin-kur ta'hal svi' dahkuh t' wuh dohn, if broadened heh broadened u' wuh pi' gluvau-math vesh' kwitau pla'rak. Na' wuh instant i kupi hardly dva-tor ik la' vesh' indeed wuh svep if pufulag-tor maf s' tevakh. Wuh thurai instant i threw myself k'fai, heh ti ulef-fainting fi-tor wuh vath vla. Wuh gluvau-math had a'ing va'ashiv za' me, tonk'peh wuh tevul t' wuh ha'gelek, heh wuh zamu moments afterwards wuh clang t' wuh dahkuh slabs t' mokev, var-tor me uf wonil had vesh' t'nash-veh stron. "i vesh' recalled tor myself k' wuh frantic plucking na' t'nash-veh kar-nik, heh i afer-tor myself lying fi-tor wuh kov lan-tol t' wuh wonil tvur, du' wuh kosu keh'sei abru' me heh seshau na' me k' ish-veh losrak el'ru, du' she meskarau wuh ha'fek svi' ish-veh gas'rak. Ish-veh vesh' wuh ka rom t'hy'la t'vi warning i had ni foolishly rejected. "'sarlah! Sarlah!' she maf-tor breathlessly. 'au dungi nam-tor la' svi' wuh moment. Au dungi gla-tor ik du nam-tor ri tra'. Oh, ri tor thinoi wuh ni-taluhk wak, tonk'peh sarlah!' "nash wak, k'puu, i did ri scorn ish-veh na'shikh. I staggered tor t'nash-veh ash'ya heh sahr-tor k' ish-veh bi' wuh tvur heh ne' wuh kuvoran stair. Wuh latter pufulag-tor tor wuh'ashiv sax'ksei tvur, heh aishan u' etek pulau ish-veh etek puzhu-tor wuh ralash t' sahran ash'ya heh wuh shouting t' dahkuh spes, veh answering wuh vath s' wuh lan-tol fi' if etek vesh' heh s' wuh veh ne'rak. T'nash-veh kakhartausu pehkau heh glazhau pa' ish-veh spo' veh vi nam-tor na' ish-veh wit's shaht. Yi she threw tu'ash wuh svep if pufulag-tor vi' wuh shi'yuk, k'fai wuh krani t' if wuh aikum vesh' shining brightly. "'ish-veh nam-tor ish-veh goh pavesh, ' leralmin-tor she. 'ish-veh nam-tor pid, tonk'peh ish-veh lau nam-tor ik du mokuhlek spen-tor ish-veh.' "u' she stariben wuh ta'hal sprang vi' zan-tor na' wuh further shaht t' wuh tvur, heh vesht gla-tor nash-veh wuh galat khlop t' shal-lan lysander stark rushing fa'rak k' wuh makh-yonet svi' veh el'ru heh wuh wun spo' wuh butcher's threshek svi' wuh vath. I rushed mes' wuh shi'yuk, flung tu'ash wuh krani, heh glazhau si'. Uf hizhuk heh slor heh wholesome wuh bah-ker glazhau svi' wuh moonlight, heh ish-veh kupi ri nam-tor weht do reh-leh ash'ya ne'. I clambered si' fi-tor wuh sku, tonk'peh i hesitated tor spen-tor abi' i dang ma puzhu-tor ra be' dvun-tor svi' t'nash-veh saviour heh wuh ruffian vi pursued me. Kuv she vesh' has-bosh-nam-tor-tor, yi na' sovek risks i vesh' satalau tor hal-tor pla' tor ish-veh assistance. Wuh nahp had hardly kahai k'fai t'nash-veh kashek fa' au vesh' na' wuh svep, pushing ish-veh yut vesht ish-veh; tonk'peh she threw ish-veh kar pauk ish-veh heh ar'kada tor meskaraya ish-veh pla'. "'fritz! Fritz!' she maf-tor svi' eingelsu, 'vokau ish-veh ugaya po' wuh kim-shah wak. Du leralmin-tor ish-veh dang ri nam-tor va'ashiv. Au dungi nam'uh ralash-fam! Oh, au dungi nam'uh ralash-fam!' "'du nam-tor mad, elise!' au saul-tor, struggling tor shaya maf s' ish-veh. 'du dungi nam-tor wuh ruin t' etek. Au has gla-tor nuh' mau. Kal-tor me be' dvun, i leralmin!' au dashed ish-veh tor veh vla, heh, rushing tor wuh krani, tresahk na' me k' ish-veh ras wun. I had kal-tor myself hal-tor, heh vesh' hanging k' wuh el'ru tor wuh sku, lu ish-veh salur tevan-tor. I vesh' d'wonil t' wuh pasik kusut, t'nash-veh grip loosened, heh i tevan-tor vi' wuh bah-ker ne'. "i vesh' shaken tonk'peh ri dash-tor k' wuh tevan; ni i picked myself abru heh rushed ska' among wuh bushes u' lerash u' i kupi sahr-tor, na' i ken-tor ik i vesh' irak s' hasu s' tehvar wi. Suddenly, however, u' i sahr-tor, wuh tevalik dizziness heh has-mar sarlah abru' me. I glanced ne' na' t'nash-veh el'ru, if vesh' throbbing painfully, heh yi, na' wuh wuh'rak wak, gla-tor ik t'nash-veh kaur-ozh had vesh' tresahk ska' heh ik wuh khaf vesh' pouring s' t'nash-veh skek. I endeavoured tor tie t'nash-veh handkerchief pauk ish-veh, tonk'peh tra' sarlah wuh sudden buzzing svi' t'nash-veh kaluk, heh thurai moment i tevan-tor svi' wuh tevik faint among wuh she-tor-bushes. "uf wu i hafau unconscious i fam yehat var-tor. Ish-veh bolau ma vesh' wuh maut akarshif, na' wuh aikum had ne'hal-tor, heh wuh ugelik asal vesh' breaking lu vesht sarlah nash-veh tor myself. T'nash-veh sai-vel vesh' ek' sodden k' asal-masu, heh t'nash-veh tor-pal-sleeve vesh' drenched k' khaf s' t'nash-veh wounded kaur-ozh. Wuh smarting t' ish-veh recalled svi' wuh instant ek' wuh particulars t' t'nash-veh mu-yor's adventure, heh i sprang tor t'nash-veh ash'ya k' wuh olaya ik i lau hardly wi nam-tor safe s' t'nash-veh pursuers. Tonk'peh tor t'nash-veh astonishment, lu vesht sarlah nash-veh tor glazhau pauk me, neither kelek il bah-ker vesh' tor nam-tor gla-tor. I had vesh' lying svi' wuh vulu t' wuh labah beyik wuh pid fau-yut, heh aishan wuh pi' weh-neik ne' vesh' wuh wu kelek, if skan-tor, fi-tor t'nash-veh approaching ish-veh, tor nam-tor wuh maut wurzel na' if i had lasha fi-tor wuh previous mu-yor. Vesh' ish-veh ri na' wuh watosh skek fi-tor t'nash-veh el'ru, ek' ik had be' dvun-tor du' eifa dreadful wadan lau ma vesh' wuh ek'rasah sahr-tor. "ulef dazed, i went vi' wuh wurzel heh ya'akash pa' wuh asal ranau. Tra' would nam-tor veh tor telvan svi' lehkuh tor wuh wadan. Wuh ka porter vesh' fi' gu-vam, i afer-tor, u' had vesh' tra' lu i lasha. I inquired t' ish-veh whether au had ek'wak puzhu-tor t' shal-lan lysander stark. Wuh ahm vesh' flekh tor ish-veh. Had au glantau wuh carriage wuh mu-yor fa' waiting na' me? Rai, au had ri. Vesh' tra' wuh police-wurzel sovek-wilat be'? Tra' vesh' veh pa' rehkuh miles ska'. "ish-veh vesh' nuh' irak na' me tor hal-tor, kobat heh has-bosh u' i vesh'. I satalau tor bek-tor abi' i zaprah tor kahr fa' telling t'nash-veh var tor wuh police. Ish-veh vesh' wuh pi' vesht shehkuh lu i lasha, ni i went wuh'rak ki' t'nash-veh skek sai-vel-tor, heh yi wuh hassu vesh' ves hiyet tor katau me bi' la'. I shitau wuh nuf vi' ish-veh el'ru heh dungau tor exactly ra du na'shikhau." etek fi' hayal-tor svi' silence na' ein pi' wak po' listening tor nash wehtsuri narrative. Yi sherlock holmes seshau ne' s' wuh nef veh t' wuh ponderous commonplace dunap svi' if au shitau ish-veh cuttings. "la' nam-tor wuh advertisement if dungi eku'ko du, " leralmin-tor au. "ish-veh saudau svi' ek' wuh dun pa' wuh tevun ago. Shroi tor nash: 'pakik, fi' wuh 9th inst, mr. Jeremiah hayling, aged dah-leh-shehkuh, wuh hydraulic mishek. Losrak ish-veh lodgings na' lehkuh o'wak-vel na' mu-yor, heh has ri vesh' puzhu-tor t' opi'. Vesh' sai-vel-tor svi', ' etc, etc. Ha! Ik represents wuh kim-shah wak ik wuh shal-lan bolau ki' ish-veh mish-vel overhauled, i fancy." "rom heavens!" maf-tor t'nash-veh hasausu. "yi ik danau ra wuh ko-kan leralmin-tor." "undoubtedly. Ish-veh nam-tor ved pa'shik ik wuh shal-lan vesh' wuh samuyau heh desperate sasu, vi vesh' absolutely satalau ik nothing dang lamok svi' wuh yut t' ish-veh pi' zhagra, spo' eifa si'-heh-si' pirates vi dungi trasha rai survivor s' wuh kum-tor hali. Muhl, kanok moment i' nam-tor taluhk, ni kuv du olau kaik tor ish-veh etek dungau hal-tor ne' tor scotland ker na' wuh'wak u' wuh preliminary tor starting na' eyford." ein rehkuh wadan il ni afterwards etek vesh' ek' svi' wuh ranau teretuhr, bound s' telvan tor wuh pi' berkshire pi'kahr. Tra' vesh' sherlock holmes, wuh hydraulic mishek, inspector bradstreet, t' scotland ker, wuh eiktra-sai-vel sasu, heh myself. Bradstreet had sak-tor wuh ordnance besan t' wuh county si' fi-tor wuh ku-san heh vesh' toranik k' ish-veh seshan-kharat-thonek bestan wuh da-kuv k' eyford na' its centre. "tra' du nam-tor, " leralmin-tor au. "ik da-kuv nam-tor drawn na' wuh sakuvu t' lehkuh miles s' wuh pi'kahr. Wuh shi etek aitlun bolau nam-tor ein-wilat be' ik zehl. Du leralmin-tor lehkuh miles, i nah-tor, osu." "ish-veh vesh' wuh wadan's rom yetur." "heh du nah-tor ik au katau du pla' ek' ik yut lu du vesh' unconscious?" "au bolau ma ovsoh ni. I ma wuh confused vokaya, nuh', t' having vesh' abertau heh zhelesh ein-wilat." "ra i fam yehat ken-tor, " leralmin-tor i, "nam-tor po au dang ma spared du lu au afer-tor du lying fainting svi' wuh bah-ker. Sos'eh wuh villain vesh' softened k' wuh kosu's entreaties." "i hardly nah-tor ik kesik. I worla gla-tor wuh weht inexorable limuk svi' t'nash-veh ha'kiv." "oh, etek dungau ak pa'shik abru ek' ik, " leralmin-tor bradstreet. "muhl, i ma drawn t'nash-veh da-kuv, heh i goh istaya i fai-tor na' ra sfek fi-tor ish-veh wuh sular ik etek nam-tor svi' psthan t' nam-tor tor nam-tor afer-tor." "i nah-tor i kupi ti t'nash-veh ozh fi' ish-veh, " leralmin-tor holmes quietly. "really, i'!" maf-tor wuh inspector, "du ma shidau ish-veh opinion! Sarlah, i', etek dungau gla-tor vi sep-wafikh k' du. I leralmin ish-veh nam-tor khu'rak, na' wuh shasol nam-tor weht deserted tra'." "heh i leralmin she'rak, " leralmin-tor t'nash-veh hasausu. "i am na' tev'rak, " remarked wuh eiktra-sai-vel sasu. "tra' nam-tor several hizhuk pi' pi'kahr abru tra'." "heh i am na' desh'rak, " leralmin-tor i, "fai'ei tra' nam-tor rai kunel tra', heh etwel t'hy'la leralmin-tor ik au did ri beglanau wuh carriage hal-tor abru sovek." "sarlah, " maf-tor wuh inspector, laughing; "ish-veh's wuh maut takov vuhnaya t' opinion. Etek ma boxed wuh seshan-kharat-thonek akhlami. Vi tor du mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh casting dvel tor?" "du nam-tor ek' riyeht." "tonk'peh etek mokuhlek't ek' nam-tor." "oh, ha, du mokuhlek. Nash nam-tor t'nash-veh sfek." au shitau ish-veh ozh svi' wuh centre t' wuh da-kuv. "nash nam-tor wilat etek dungau talal au." "tonk'peh wuh leh-dah-mile yetur?" hushau hatherley. "shehkuh si' heh shehkuh pla'. Nothing simpler. Du leralmin yourself ik wuh jarel vesh' sluk heh glossy lu du prah svi'. Uf kupi ish-veh nam-tor ik kuv ish-veh had hal-tor leh-dah miles abru' ras fau-yut?" "indeed, ish-veh nam-tor wuh kesik ruse hiyet, " glantau bradstreet thoughtfully. "veling tra' mokuhlek nam-tor rai vet u' tor wuh malat t' nash gang." "rim na' ek', " leralmin-tor holmes. "au nam-tor coiners fi' wuh suk wef, heh ma nam-tor-tor wuh mish-vel tor shid wuh masumok-rish-mokev if has taken wuh shi' haul-tukh." "etek ma fainu na' ein wak ik wuh clever gang vesh' na' ar'kadan, " leralmin-tor wuh inspector. "au ma vesh' turning si' ulef-tarkiv k' wuh thousand. Etek kauk traced au u' irak u' telvan, tonk'peh kupi prah rai weh-irak, na' au had wein-tor ish-veh zavikau svi' wuh yut ik gluvau ik au vesh' maut hinek el'ru. Tonk'peh i', itaren tor nash kunli pavesh, i nah-tor ik etek ma prah au gas'rak hiyet." tonk'peh wuh inspector vesh' mistaken, na' eifa criminals vesh' ri destined tor tevan vi' wuh el'ru t' yeht-gav. U' etek padukau vi' eyford wurzel etek gla-tor wuh masuk' tsek t' vuzh if salash abru s' za' wuh pi' clump t' lap svi' wuh neighbourhood heh geldau spo' wuh immense ostrich kan abru' wuh landscape. "wuh kelek fi' yon?" ya'akash bradstreet u' wuh ranau steamed ska' va'ashiv fi' its yut. "ha, osu!" leralmin-tor wuh wurzel-trensu. "lu did ish-veh shaya si'?" "i zhu-tor ik ish-veh vesh' du' wuh mu-yor, osu, tonk'peh ish-veh has prah weh-rasahkos, heh wuh bosh shi nam-tor svi' wuh yon." "t'vi kelek nam-tor ish-veh?" "dr. Becher's." "var-tor me, " shau svi' wuh mishek, "nam-tor dr. Becher wuh german, maut wonil, k' wuh wu, nasik han?" wuh wurzel-trensu abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor heartily. "rai, osu, dr. Becher nam-tor wuh englishman, heh tra' isn't wuh sasu svi' wuh parish vi has wuh weh-rom-zehl-tor waistcoat. Tonk'peh au has wuh gentleman staying k' ish-veh, wuh hasausu, u' i ken-tor, vi nam-tor wuh k'shatrisu, heh au glazhau u' kuv wuh pi' rom berkshire kahm would tor ish-veh rai klau." wuh wurzel-trensu had ri shahtau ish-veh starun fa' etek vesh' ek' hastening svi' wuh kharat t' wuh yon. Wuh fau-yut topped wuh neik kunel, heh tra' vesh' wuh lo'uk widespread whitewashed kelek svi' khom t' etek, spouting yon na' kanok chink heh krani, du' svi' wuh bah-ker svi' khom rehkuh yon-mishu vesh' vainly striving tor potau wuh yai ne'. "ik's ish-veh!" maf-tor hatherley, svi' intense tepor'es. "tra' nam-tor wuh krus-kov-yetur, heh tra' nam-tor wuh she-tor-bushes wilat i ti. Ik dahr krani nam-tor wuh veh ik i spen-tor s'." "muhl, k'puu, " leralmin-tor holmes, "du ma had ish-veh revenge fi-tor au. Tra' mokuhlek nam-tor rai deshker ik ish-veh vesh' ish-veh elmin-ha'gelek if, lu ish-veh vesh' plesh-tor svi' wuh hish-tor, eku yon tor wuh wooden temok, hi rai vet au vesh' nuh' teporilau svi' wuh a'vesh' po' du tor glantau ish-veh na' wuh wak. I' potau ish-veh bezhun tu'ash svi' nash patreitan na' ish-veh t'hylara t' kim-shah mu-yor, hi i maut mau pthak ik au nam-tor wuh rom hundred miles ska' k' i'." heh holmes' ptha sarlah tor nam-tor realised, na' s' ik gad tor nash rai zhit has ek'wak vesh' puzhu-tor either t' wuh vaksurik kosu, wuh sinister german, il wuh morose englishman. Lehkuh-mal ik asal wuh peasant had ragel-tor wuh hal containing several sutra heh ein maut bulky natuhn driving rapidly svi' wuh kharat t' telvan, tonk'peh tra' ek' zavikau t' wuh fugitives sasaudau, heh kauk holmes' ingenuity vravshau ek'wak tor discover wuh least clue u' tor ish-veh whereabouts. Wuh sayonotausu had vesh' mau perturbed na' wuh flekh arrangements if au had afer-tor k'svi, heh fam dvun weht ni k' discovering wuh newly ktorr komihn kaur-ozh fi-tor wuh krani-sku t' wuh dahr lan-tol. Pa' tev-tor, however, ish-veh urgam vesh' na' kim-shah successful, heh au nessau wuh yai, tonk'peh ri fa' wuh kamu had tevan-tor svi', heh wuh bosh shi vesh' netakidau tor such ek'esik ruin ik, korsau ein kuvoran-tor cylinders heh shek-tukh piping, ri wuh zavikau hafau t' wuh machinery if had kodona etwel unfortunate acquaintance ni dearly. Suk shivak t' orn-tukh heh t' zhai-tukh vesh' discovered tsorau svi' wuh si'-kelek, tonk'peh rai di'kaudj vesh' tor nam-tor afer-tor, if lau ma danau wuh la'es t' eifa bulky natuhn if ma vesh' already referred tor. Uf etwel hydraulic mishek had vesh' zhelesh s' wuh bah-ker tor wuh gla-tor wilat au recovered ish-veh kash-ral lau ma hafau ek'wak wuh mystery vesh' ish-veh ri na' wuh mos mould, if var-tor etek wuh maut eiktra var. Au had evidently vesh' lesh ne' k' dahkuh persons, veh t' ik had remarkably pi' ash'ya heh wuh vath unusually suk ones. Fi' wuh bosh, ish-veh vesh' danik yesik ik wuh ralash-fam englishman, hasu lehkuh vakh il lehkuh murderous do ish-veh besu, had gol-tor wuh kosu tor lesh wuh unconscious sasu s' wuh yut t' tehvar. "muhl, " leralmin-tor etwel mishek ruefully u' etek nem-tor etwel ku-san tor fun wuh'wak weht tor london, "ish-veh has vesh' wuh takov business na' me! I ma pakik t'nash-veh kaur-ozh heh i ma pakik wuh kau-leh-guinea uz, heh ra ma i nazh-tor?" "veshtaya, " leralmin-tor holmes, laughing. "indirectly ish-veh lau nam-tor t' tala, du fai-tor; du ma goh tor shitau ish-veh vi' zhit tor nazh-kap wuh reputation t' hasu marom apc'koik na' wuh hafayat t' ish-veh nam." x. Wuh adventure t' wuh thol bachelor wuh s'haile st. Simon kal'i'farr, heh its curious termination, ma wu ceased tor nam-tor wuh subject t' eku'ko svi' eifa exalted da-kuv svi' if wuh unfortunate bridegroom dvun-tor. Sluk scandals ma eclipsed ish-veh, heh ish-veh weht piquant details ma drawn wuh gossips maf s' nash kehkuh-tevun-hinek drama. U' i ma utvau tor dva-tor, however, ik wuh bosh kla-min ma worla vesh' revealed tor wuh paik tsuri, heh u' t'nash-veh t'hy'la sherlock holmes had wuh considerable thresh svi' clearing wuh tukh abru, i olau ik rai memoir t' ish-veh would nam-tor ovsotik rik' ein pi' lubesan t' nash remarkable episode. Ish-veh vesh' wuh zamu wehk gad fa' t'nash-veh sha' kal'i'farr, du' wuh gad lu i vesh' fam dvun thresh-tor tvi-shal k' holmes svi' leipausu yut, ik sarlah ish-veh ha-kel s' wuh aru stroll tor talal wuh nuhm fi' wuh pasu waiting na' ish-veh. I had hafau indoors ek' gad, na' wuh igen-va had taken wuh sudden da-tor tor sov-masu, k' pid autumnal salan, heh wuh jezail bullet if i had katau pla' svi' veh t' t'nash-veh sikrus u' wuh za-vel t' t'nash-veh afghan campaign gau k' pasik persistence. K' t'nash-veh ak'shem svi' veh hagik-ku-san heh t'nash-veh mal fi-tor wuh'ashiv, i had vikuvau myself k' wuh wan t' newspapers abi' na' kim-shah, vi-mashau k' wuh ro'fori t' wuh gad, i tossed au ek' aside heh ti listless, watching wuh masuk' dan-pid-sfek heh monogram fi-tor wuh envelope fi-tor wuh pasu heh wondering lazily vi t'nash-veh t'hy'la's thol correspondent kupi nam-tor. "la' nam-tor wuh maut fashionable epistle, " i remarked u' au svi-tor. "ish-veh asal nuhm, kuv i vokau gas'rak, vesh' s' wuh aluk-monger heh wuh mashen-waiter." "ha, t'nash-veh correspondence has certainly wuh sem-rik t' vuhna'es, " au kilko-tor, smiling, "heh wuh humbler nam-tor usually wuh weht eku'ki. Nash glazhau spo' veh t' eifa unwelcome shilaik summonses if vutau fi-tor wuh sasu either tor nam-tor bored il tor ti." au shau wuh fen heh glanced abru' wuh tuhllar. "oh, sarlah, ish-veh lau skan-tor tor nam-tor vel t' eku'ko, po' ek'." "ri shilaik, yi?" "rai, distinctly professional." "heh s' wuh thol client?" "veh t' wuh k'lek svi' england." "t'nash-veh tal-kam katravahsu, i congratulate du." "i assure du, watson, rik' affectation, ik wuh nosh t' t'nash-veh client nam-tor wuh tukh t' lehkuh moment tor me do wuh eku'ko t' ish-veh nuf. Ish-veh nam-tor aishan tor-yehat, however, ik ik isha lau ri nam-tor wanting svi' nash uzh investigation. Du ma vesh' telvan wuh dun diligently t' tab-ma, ma du ri?" "ish-veh glazhau spo' ish-veh, " leralmin-tor i ruefully, pointing tor wuh masuk' uzh'a'lek svi' wuh teruk. "i ma had nothing else tor tor." "ish-veh nam-tor fortunate, na' du dungi sos'eh nam-tor kup tor lehk me abru. I telv-tor nothing kaula wuh criminal ro'fori heh wuh agony tsek. Wuh latter nam-tor kwon-hau-ov instructive. Tonk'peh kuv du ma zahal-tor recent pavek ni closely du bolau ma telv-tor pa' s'haile st. Simon heh ish-veh wedding?" "oh, ha, k' wuh deepest eku'ko." "ik nam-tor muhl. Wuh nuhm if i meskaraya svi' t'nash-veh el'ru nam-tor s' s'haile st. Simon. I dungi telv-tor ish-veh tor du, heh svi' fun du bolau da-tor abru' aifa dun heh kal-tor me ma whatever bears fi-tor wuh tukh. Nash nam-tor ra au leralmin-tor: "'t'nash-veh tal-kam mr. Sherlock holmes, s'haile pla-masu var-tor me ik i lau shi implicit reliance fi-tor ish-veh judgment heh discretion. I ma satalau, therefore, tor vutau fi-tor du heh tor consult du svi' dzhinaya tor wuh maut kusut-tor pavek if has paresh-tor svi' tersaya k' t'nash-veh wedding. Mr. Lestrade, t' scotland ker, nam-tor peran already svi' wuh tukh, tonk'peh au assures me ik gla-tor ish-veh rai objection tor ish-veh co-el'toraya, heh ik au kauk nah-tor ik ish-veh lau nam-tor t' ein assistance. I dungi vutau na' kehkuh o'wak-vel svi' wuh aru, heh, dang du ma sovek vath engagement na' ik wak, i rok ik du dungi postpone ish-veh, u' nash tukh nam-tor t' paramount importance. Ish-veh faithfully, "'robert st. Simon.' "ish-veh nam-tor dated s' grosvenor mansions, written k' wuh quill pen, heh wuh thol s'haile has had wuh misfortune tor prah wuh smear t' neshuk fi-tor wuh sik vla t' ish-veh gas'rak wuhr-ozh, " remarked holmes u' au hesha abru wuh epistle. "au leralmin-tor kehkuh o'wak-vel. Ish-veh nam-tor rehkuh i'. Au dungi nam-tor la' svi' wuh wadan." "yi i ma aishan wak, k' ish-veh assistance, tor prah pa'shik fi-tor wuh subject. Da-tor abru' eifa dun heh arrange wuh saseshau svi' ish-veh zek t' wak, du' i nem-tor wuh glance u' tor vi etwel client nam-tor." au picked wuh yon-kur-wein-tor ral'es s' wuh zehl t' dunap t' dzhinaya be' wuh mantelpiece. "la' au nam-tor, " leralmin-tor au, sitting ne' heh flattening ish-veh si' fi-tor ish-veh mal-nef. "'s'haile robert walsingham de vere st. Simon, dahr sa-fu t' wuh duke t' balmoral.' hum! 'kar: azure, rehkuh caltrops svi' chief abru' wuh fess sable. Pukeshta svi' 1846.' au's keh-leh-veh tevun t' ya'shakhuv, if nam-tor vinik na' kal'i'farr. Vesh' ne'-secretary na' wuh sashila svi' wuh tab-ma administration. Wuh duke, ish-veh sa-mekh, vesh' na' veh wak secretary na' k'shatri tek'ik. Au inherit plantagenet khaf k' kharik tevan, heh tudor fi' wuh distaff vla. Ha! Muhl, tra' nam-tor nothing maut instructive svi' ek' nash. I nah-tor ik i bolau da-tor tor du watson, na' vel weht huhtik." "i ma maut pi' rihag'es svi' finding ra i aitlun, " leralmin-tor i, "na' wuh kla-min nam-tor ved recent, heh wuh tukh kwul-tor me u' remarkable. I ptha tor dzhinau au tor du, however, u' i fai-tor ik du had wuh inquiry fi' el'ru heh ik du ritishau wuh vi-kwitaya t' vath tukh." "oh, du tvai wuh pi' wat t' wuh grosvenor keh-vla furniture hali. Ik nam-tor ved pa'shu abru nowthough, indeed, ish-veh vesh' obvious s' wuh wuh'rak. Pray mazhiv-kur-tor me wuh results t' ish-veh newspaper dvel." "la' nam-tor wuh wuh'rak beglanau if i mokuhlek talal. Ish-veh nam-tor svi' wuh personal tsek t' wuh asal lehk, heh kinuf, u' gla-tor du, ein wehk gad pla': 'wuh kal'i'farr has vesh' arranged, ' ish-veh leralmin-tor, 'heh dungi, kuv rumour nam-tor yeht, maut shortly nem-tor shi, svi' s'haile robert st. Simon, dahr sa-fu t' wuh duke t' balmoral, heh din-tor hatty doran, wuh goh ko-fu t' aloysius doran. Esq, t' san francisco, cal, u.s. Wuh.' ik nam-tor ek'." "terse heh tor wuh sfek, " remarked holmes, stretching ish-veh wu, wonil mal na' wuh yon. "tra' vesh' wuh paragraph amplifying nash svi' veh t' wuh shila'es dun t' wuh ka wehk gad. Ah, la' ish-veh nam-tor: 'tra' dungi ak nam-tor wuh vutau na' protection svi' wuh kal'i'farr mahr-kel, na' wuh la' elik-trade dvatai saudau tor var-tor heavily tehnat etwel ha-kel torvauk. Veh k' veh wuh management t' wuh thol kelek t' lo'uk britain nam-tor be' dvun-tor vi' wuh el'ru t' etwel rom krei s' mes' wuh atlantic. Wuh yauluhk haya has vesh' tor du' wuh kim-shah wehk gad tor wuh feim t' wuh prizes if ma vesh' borne maf k' aifa sem-rik-tor invaders. S'haile st. Simon, vi has shown himself na' abru' dah-leh tevun skan tehnat wuh pi' oekon's kliton, has i' definitely tor'pra ish-veh approaching kal'i'farr k' din-tor hatty doran, wuh sem-rik ko-fu t' wuh california millionaire. Din-tor doran, t'vi graceful khlop heh striking limuk skamau mau attention na' wuh westbury kelek festivities, nam-tor wuh goh kan, heh ish-veh nam-tor currently reported ik ish-veh dowry dungi sahr-tor tor considerably abru' wuh shehkuh khlop, k' expectancies na' wuh fa-wak. U' ish-veh nam-tor wuh tu'ash tsat ik wuh duke t' balmoral has vesh' compelled tor makau ish-veh bikuv k'svi wuh kim-shah zamu tevun, heh u' s'haile st. Simon has rai veltra t' ish-veh sha' korsau wuh pi' estate t' birchmoor, ish-veh nam-tor obvious ik wuh californian heiress nam-tor ri wuh goh gainer k' wuh alliance if dungi enable ish-veh tor tor wuh hagik heh tsuri transition s' wuh republican t'sai tor wuh british peeress.'" "sovek-kitok?" ya'akash holmes, yawning. "oh, ha; plenty. Yi tra' nam-tor wuh'ashiv pitoh svi' wuh asal lehk tor leralmin ik wuh kal'i'farr would nam-tor wuh absolutely hizhuk veh, ik ish-veh would nam-tor na' st. George's, hanover keh-vla, ik goh ulef wuh dozen intimate t'hylara would nam-tor invited, heh ik wuh party would fun tor wuh furnished kelek na' lancaster temep if has vesh' taken k' mr. Aloysius doran. Dahkuh gad laterthat nam-tor, fi' gad lastthere nam-tor wuh curt announcement ik wuh wedding had taken shi, heh ik wuh honeymoon would nam-tor be' dvun-tor na' s'haile pla-masu's shi, be' petersfield. Eifa nam-tor ek' wuh beglanau if saudau fa' wuh disappearance t' wuh bride." "fa' wuh ra?" ya'akash holmes k' wuh palikaya. "wuh vanishing t' wuh t'sai." "lu did she vanish, yi?" "na' wuh wedding asal-yem." "indeed. Nash nam-tor weht eku'ki do ish-veh ugau tor nam-tor; ved dramatic, svi' kla-min." "ha; ish-veh kwul-tor me u' hasu wuh pi' s' wuh tsuri." "au k'ashiv vanish fa' wuh hali-kal, heh occasionally du' wuh honeymoon; tonk'peh i fam yehat vutau tor kashek sovek-vel ved ni prompt u' nash. Pray kal-tor me ma wuh details." "i vikau du ik au nam-tor maut incomplete." "sos'eh etek lau tor au lehkuh ni." "such u' au nam-tor, au nam-tor eku forth svi' wuh single ua'mrki t' wuh asal dun t' za-gad, if i dungi telv-tor tor du. Ish-veh nam-tor headed, 'singular occurrence na' wuh fashionable wedding': "'wuh skan t' s'haile robert st. Simon has vesh' lehm-tor vi' wuh greatest consternation k' wuh flekh heh kusut-tor episodes if ma taken shi svi' tersaya k' ish-veh wedding. Wuh hali-kal, u' shortly tor'pra svi' wuh dun t' za-gad, paresh-tor fi' wuh previous asal; tonk'peh ish-veh nam-tor goh i' ik ish-veh has vesh' tor-yehat tor wugau wuh flekh rumours if ma vesh' ni persistently floating pa'. Svi' spite t' wuh attempts t' wuh t'hylara tor hush wuh tukh abru, ni mau tsuri attention has i' vesh' drawn tor ish-veh ik rai rom lof mokuhlek nam-tor dvin-tor k' affecting tor bau-tor ra nam-tor wuh tsuri subject na' conversation. "'wuh hali-kal, if vesh' performed na' st. George's, hanover keh-vla, vesh' wuh maut hizhuk veh, kling hasu la' korsau wuh sa-mekh t' wuh bride, mr. Aloysius doran, wuh duchess t' balmoral, s'haile pla-masu, s'haile eustace heh t'sai clara st. Simon (wuh younger sa-kai heh ko-kai t' wuh bridegroom), heh t'sai alicia whittington. Wuh bosh party proceeded afterwards tor wuh kelek t' mr. Aloysius doran, na' lancaster temep, wilat asal-yem had vesh' dator. Ish-veh saudau ik ein pi' trouble vesh' aisha k' wuh kosu, t'vi ahm has ri vesh' ascertained, vi endeavoured tor nekwitaya ish-veh yut vi' wuh kelek po' wuh bridal party, alleging ik she had ein claim fi-tor s'haile st. Simon. Ish-veh vesh' goh po' wuh kusut-tor heh prolonged scene ik she vesh' sadakh k' wuh butler heh wuh footman. Wuh bride, vi had fortunately svi-tor wuh kelek fa' nash unpleasant svi-shaya, had hayal-tor ne' tor asal-yem k' wuh shom, lu she complained t' wuh sudden indisposition heh retired tor ish-veh tvi-shal. Ish-veh prolonged absence having aisha ein tuhskaya, ish-veh sa-mekh zahal-tor ish-veh, tonk'peh oren-tor s' ish-veh maid ik she had goh sarlah abru tor ish-veh tvi-shal na' wuh instant, kum-tor abru wuh ulster heh bonnet, heh hurried ne' tor wuh tvur. Veh t' wuh footmen afsakau ik au had gla-tor wuh t'sai trasha wuh kelek thus apparelled, tonk'peh had klee'fah tor lit ik ish-veh vesh' ish-veh mistress, believing ish-veh tor nam-tor k' wuh apc'koik. Fi' ascertaining ik ish-veh ko-fu had sasaudau, mr. Aloysius doran, svi' kh'ta k' wuh bridegroom, instantly shitau themselves svi' sviribaya k' wuh police, heh maut energetic inquiries nam-tor hasu tor, if dungi probably result svi' wuh threshan clearing abru t' nash maut singular business. Abru tor wuh tab-ma wadan kim-shah mu-yor, however, nothing had transpired u' tor wuh whereabouts t' wuh missing t'sai. Tra' nam-tor rumours t' flalik mavau svi' wuh tukh, heh ish-veh nam-tor leralmin-tor ik wuh police ma aisha wuh pehkaya t' wuh kosu vi had aisha wuh tveshik ertaya, svi' wuh dva ik, s' jealousy il ein vath dvubolek, she lau ma vesh' concerned svi' wuh flekh disappearance t' wuh bride.'" "heh nam-tor ik ek'?" "goh veh pi' item svi' wuh'ashiv t' wuh asal dun, tonk'peh ish-veh nam-tor wuh suggestive veh." "heh ish-veh nam-tor" "ik din-tor kastra millar, wuh t'sai vi had aisha wuh ertaya, has actually vesh' pehkau. Ish-veh saudau ik she vesh' formerly wuh danseuse na' wuh allegro, heh ik she has fainu wuh bridegroom na' ein tevun. Tra' nam-tor rai further particulars, heh wuh bosh nuf nam-tor svi' ish-veh el'ru nowso irak u' ish-veh has vesh' eku forth svi' wuh tsuri hish-tor." "heh wuh exceedingly eku'ki nuf ish-veh saudau tor nam-tor. I would ri ma din-tor ish-veh na' panu. Tonk'peh tra' nam-tor wuh mokov na' wuh kus-vakh, watson, heh u' wuh wak-vel tor ish-veh wuh zamu minutes po' kehkuh, i ma rai vet ik nash dungi skan-tor tor nam-tor etwel thol client. Ri tor sahr-tor t' going, watson, na' i maut mau prefer having wuh toglantausu, kuv goh u' wuh rihamau tor t'nash-veh sha' vokaya." "s'haile robert st. Simon, " tor'pra etwel thalv-sa-kan, throwing tu'ash wuh svep. Wuh gentleman svi-tor, k' wuh vaksurik, iyula limuk, pid-nosed heh spoh, k' vel sos'eh t' petulance pa' wuh ru'lut, heh k' wuh br'xan, muhl-tu'ash bezhun t' wuh sasu t'vi vaksurik lot ish-veh had ek'wak vesh' tor a'fic heh tor nam-tor obeyed. Ish-veh manner vesh' brax, heh wi ish-veh paik appearance mazhiv-kur-tor wuh undue impression t' ya'shakhuv, na' au had wuh slight fa'rak stoop heh wuh pi' vulaya t' wuh mal-nef u' au lates-tor. Ish-veh isachya, nuh', u' au swept ska' ish-veh maut curly-brimmed taik, vesh' grizzled pauk wuh rihk heh wonil fi-tor wuh fik. U' tor ish-veh sai-vel, ish-veh vesh' tun-bosh tor wuh verge t' foppishness, k' pid hmoi'neks, nesh-kur pelal-tor-pal, wan-kur waistcoat, kin-kur gloves, patent-duf ash'el, heh ta'hal-kur-tor gaiters. Au storilau slowly vi' wuh tvi-shal, turning ish-veh patam s' losrak tor gas'rak, heh swinging svi' ish-veh gas'rak el'ru wuh elakh if meskarau ish-veh pi-maat-kur bezhun-zaneshu. "rom-gad, s'haile st. Simon, " leralmin-tor holmes, rising heh bowing. "pray nem-tor wuh ki'haf-ku-san. Nash nam-tor t'nash-veh t'hy'la heh kazhuksu, dr. Watson. Bes-tor abru wuh pi' tor wuh yon, heh etek dungi variben nash tukh abru'." "wuh danik kusut-tor tukh tor me, u' du mokuhlek danik readily glenonau, mr. Holmes. I ma vesh' tresahk tor wuh sahris. Wuh adventure t' wuh beryl coronet "holmes, " leralmin-tor i u' i lam-tor veh asal svi' etwel kes-wun-krani looking ne' wuh yut, "la' nam-tor wuh madman coming bi'. Awek affliction isha nam-tor wuh lot t' kanok sasu; tonk'peh wuh dahkuh coming teretuhr, heh svi' ni frightful wuh shid, ma vesh' hiyet tor hutau t'nash-veh maut soul.
