"t'nash-veh ahm, " kilko-tor etwel visitor, "nam-tor probably familiar tor ish-veh kaluk. I am alexander holder, t' wuh banking pesik t' holder & stevenson, t' threadneedle yut." wuh ahm vesh' indeed muhl fainu tor etek u' t' wuh senior tersu svi' wuh dahr largest awek banking concern svi' wuh kahr t' london. Ra kupi ma pavesh-tor, yi, tor katau veh t' wuh dan-faik citizens t' london tor nash danik pitiable be' dvun? Etek bek-tor, ek' curiosity, abi' k' wuh'ashiv urgam au fir-tor himself tor var-tor ish-veh var. "i olau ik wak nam-tor t' tala, " leralmin-tor au; "ik nam-tor po i hastened la' lu wuh police inspector suggested ik i dang shar ish-veh co-el'toraya. Vesht sarlah nash-veh tor leipausu yut k' wuh underground heh hurried s' tra' fi' ash'ya, na' wuh cabs hal-tor slowly k'fai nash izh. Ik nam-tor po i vesh' ni s' esh, na' i am wuh sasu vi nem-tor maut pi' tusok. I olau weh-rom i', heh i dungi shitau wuh kla-min fa' du u' shortly heh wi u' clearly u' i mokuhlek. "ish-veh nam-tor, veling, muhl fainu tor du ik svi' wuh successful banking business u' mau nerau fi-tor etwel hasu kup tor talal remunerative investments na' etwel donketu u' fi-tor etwel increasing etwel tersaya heh wuh su'etek t' etwel depositors. Veh t' etwel danik lucrative tvai t' laying si' donku nam-tor svi' wuh shid t' loans, wilat wuh shar'es nam-tor unimpeachable. Etek ma ovsoh wuh rom deal svi' nash kharat du' wuh kim-shah zamu tevun, heh tra' nam-tor wehk thol skan tor ik etek ma storilau suk hau-ov fi-tor wuh shar'es t' ish-veh bikuv, shi'dunap, il math. "za-gad asal i vesh' hayal-tor svi' t'nash-veh office na' wuh kutra lu wuh nop vesh' katau svi' tor me k' veh t' wuh clerks. I palikau lu vesht gla-tor nash-veh wuh ahm, na' ish-veh vesh' ik t' rim vath thanwell, sos'eh kauk tor du i had weh-rom leralmin rai weht do ik ish-veh vesh' wuh ahm if nam-tor wuh household zhit ek' abru' wuh earthone t' wuh k'lek, noblest, danik exalted ahm svi' england. I vesh' overwhelmed k' wuh dor heh attempted, lu au svi-tor, tor leralmin ni, tonk'peh au taul-tor na' wuh'wak vi' business k' wuh sov t' wuh sasu vi istau tor brax sahris k'fai wuh disagreeable task. "'mr. Holder, ' leralmin-tor au, 'i ma vesh' informed ik du nam-tor svi' wuh es'merka t' advancing donku.' "'wuh pesik tor ni lu wuh shar'es nam-tor rom.' i kilko-tor. "'ish-veh nam-tor absolutely bolayatik tor me, ' leralmin-tor au, 'ik i dang ma 50,000 na' wuh'wak. I kupi, veling, yahv-tor ni trifling wuh hau-ov lehkuh wak abru' s' t'nash-veh t'hylara, tonk'peh i mau prefer tor tor ish-veh wuh tukh t' business heh tor fitor ik business myself. Svi' t'nash-veh shul du mokuhlek readily ken-tor ik ish-veh nam-tor unwise tor shi veh's shal ne' obligations.' "'na' uf wu, sos ya'akash, tor du aitlun nash hau-ov?' i ya'akash. "'thurai gad i ma wuh suk hau-ov due tor me, heh i dungau yi danik certainly repay ra du storilaya, k' whatever eku'ko du nah-tor ish-veh gas'rak tor falun. Tonk'peh ish-veh nam-tor maut bolayatik tor me ik wuh donku dang nam-tor vlitau na' wuh'wak.' "'i dang nam-tor kunli tor storilaya ish-veh rik' further parley s' t'nash-veh sha' awek sa'haf, ' leralmin-tor i, 'vesh' ish-veh ri ik wuh ish-veh would nam-tor rather weht do ish-veh kupi lesh. Kuv, fi' wuh vath el'ru, i am tor tor ish-veh svi' wuh ahm t' wuh pesik, yi svi' yeht-gav tor t'nash-veh tersu i bolau insist ik, kauk svi' ish-veh nuf, kanok businesslike precaution dang nam-tor taken.' "'i dang mau prefer ki' ish-veh ni, ' leralmin-tor au, raising abru wuh keh-vla, nesh-kur morocco nuf if au had laid be' ish-veh ku-san. 'du ma doubtless puzhu-tor t' wuh beryl coronet?' "'veh t' wuh danik taluhk tsuri ma-vel t' wuh eik-te'kru, ' leralmin-tor i. "'precisely.' au tu'ash wuh nuf, heh tra', imbedded svi' mos, kahm-kur-tor velvet, ti wuh magnificent krus t' jewellery if au had ahmau. 'tra' nam-tor reh-leh-naukuh masuk' beryls, ' leralmin-tor au, 'heh wuh price t' wuh pi-maat-tukh chasing nam-tor incalculable. Wuh lowest talupaya would shitau wuh don t' wuh coronet na' dahtau wuh hau-ov if i ma ya'akash. I am dator tor trasha ish-veh k' du u' t'nash-veh shar'es.' "i nem-tor wuh taluhk nuf vi' t'nash-veh el'ru heh glazhau svi' ein perplexity s' ish-veh tor t'nash-veh illustrious client. "'du vet its tala?' au ya'akash. "'mokov. I goh vet' "'wuh propriety t' t'nash-veh leaving ish-veh. Du lau eku ish-veh kashek na' shom pa' ik. I dang ri sahr-tor t' doing ni vesh' ish-veh ri absolutely ac'ruth ik i dang nam-tor kup svi' kehkuh gad tor reclaim ish-veh. Ish-veh nam-tor wuh pure tukh t' shid. Nam-tor wuh shar'es sufficient?' "'ample.' "'du ken-tor, mr. Holder, ik i am giving du wuh karik skan t' wuh guhl'es if i ma svi' du, founded fi-tor ek' ik i ma puzhu-tor t' du. I rely fi-tor du ri goh tor nam-tor discreet heh tor refrain s' ek' gossip fi-tor wuh tukh tonk'peh, abru' ek', tor korsau nash coronet k' kanok tor-yehat precaution fai'ei i bolaya ri leralmin ik wuh lo'uk tsuri scandal would nam-tor aisha kuv sovek klau vesh' tor befall ish-veh. Sovek dash tor ish-veh would nam-tor siyah u' serious u' its ovsotik pak, na' tra' nam-tor rai beryls svi' wuh panu tor match aifa, heh ish-veh would nam-tor impossible tor va'prah au. I trasha ish-veh k' du, however, k' kanok guhl'es, heh i dungau vutau na' ish-veh svi' person fi' gad asal.' "seeing ik t'nash-veh client vesh' anxious tor trasha, i leralmin-tor rai weht tonk'peh, calling na' t'nash-veh cashier, i ordered ish-veh tor vlitau abru' kau-leh 1000 pitoh. Lu i vesh' sa'awek wuh'wak weht, however, k' wuh taluhk nuf lying fi-tor wuh pasu svi' khom t' me, i kupi ri tonk'peh nah-tor k' ein misgivings t' wuh immense responsibility if ish-veh entailed fi-tor me. Tra' kupi nam-tor rai vet ik, u' ish-veh vesh' wuh national mat, wuh horrible scandal would ensue kuv sovek misfortune dang paresh-tor tor ish-veh. I already regretted having ek'wak consented tor nem-tor falun t' ish-veh. However, ish-veh vesh' nuh' tab-ma tor rubitau wuh tukh i', ni i klacha ish-veh abru svi' t'nash-veh awek safe heh da-tor wuh'wak weht tor t'nash-veh ar'kadan. "lu khru sarlah i olau ik ish-veh would nam-tor wuh imprudence tor trasha ni taluhk wuh vel svi' wuh office za' me. Bankers' safes had vesh' punekwitau fa' i', heh po dang ri t'nash-veh nam-tor? Kuv ni, uf terrible would nam-tor wuh shul svi' if i dang talal myself! I satalau, therefore, ik na' wuh thurai zamu gad i would kwon-hau-ov lesh wuh nuf pla'rak heh fa'rak k' me, ni ik ish-veh lau worla nam-tor really s' t'nash-veh pulau. K' nash intention, i puvutau wuh cab heh drove si' tor t'nash-veh kelek na' streatham, carrying wuh ek'zer k' me. I did ri esh-tor freely abi' i had taken ish-veh upstairs heh klacha ish-veh svi' wuh bureau t' t'nash-veh sai-vel-tor-tvi-shal. "heh i' wuh zhit u' tor t'nash-veh household, mr. Holmes, na' i istaya du tor thoroughly ken-tor wuh situation. T'nash-veh groom heh t'nash-veh thalv yuk s' wuh kelek, heh lau nam-tor eku aside altogether. I ma rehkuh maid-dvinsu vi ma vesh' k' me wuh su'etek t' tevun heh t'vi ek'esik reliability nam-tor ved abru' suspicion. Wuh'ashiv, lucy parr, wuh dahr waiting-maid, has goh vesh' svi' t'nash-veh dvin wuh zamu tevun-krus. Sarlah ish-veh k' wuh marom character, however, heh has kwon-hau-ov putan-tor me satisfaction. She nam-tor wuh maut takov ko-kan heh has skamau admirers vi ma occasionally geldau pa' wuh shi. Ik nam-tor wuh goh drawback if etek ma afer-tor tor ish-veh, tonk'peh etek dva-tor ish-veh tor nam-tor wuh thoroughly rom ko-kan svi' kanok yut. "ni mau na' wuh dvinsu. T'nash-veh skan itself nam-tor ni pi' ik ish-veh dungi ri nem-tor me wu tor kethelvau ish-veh. I am wuh kir'an heh ma wuh goh sa-fu, arthur. Au has vesh' wuh disappointment tor me, mr. Holmesa grievous disappointment. I ma rai vet ik i am myself tor tenai. Sutra var-tor me ik i ma spoiled ish-veh. Maut kesik i ma. Lu t'nash-veh tal-kam ko-telsu tev-tor i olau ik au vesh' ek' i had tor ashaya. I kupi ri lesh tor gla-tor wuh abru'teruklar-ru'lut spoh-tor kauk na' wuh moment s' ish-veh limuk. I ma worla wafu ish-veh wuh istaya. Sos'eh ish-veh would ma vesh' weh-rom na' fi' t' etek had i vesh' sterner, tonk'peh i tvai ish-veh na' wuh buhfik. "ish-veh vesh' naturally t'nash-veh intention ik au dang navau me svi' t'nash-veh business, tonk'peh au vesh' ri t' wuh business da-tor. Au vesh' kwai, wayward, heh, tor stariben wuh yeht'es, i kupi ri sahrafel ish-veh svi' wuh handling t' suk hau-ov t' donku. Lu au vesh' nu'ri au became wuh kisau t' wuh aristocratic muhd, heh tra', having sem-rik-tor manners, au vesh' ak wuh intimate t' wuh su'etek t' sasu k' wu sa'haf heh kodonuhk es'merka. Au oren-tor tor mavau heavily na' nop heh tor sis-tor donku fi' wuh turf, abi' au had va'ashiv heh va'ashiv tor sarlah tor me heh implore me tor mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh storilaya fi-tor ish-veh allowance, ik au lau settle ish-veh sa'akh t' dor. Au ar'kada weht do wuh'wak tor shaya maf s' wuh tehvar-bosh apc'koik if au vesh' keeping, tonk'peh tik wak wuh vi-yumuk t' ish-veh t'hy'la, osu george burnwell, vesh' hiyet tor bes-tor ish-veh pla' va'ashiv. "heh, indeed, i kupi ri wonder ik such wuh sasu u' osu george burnwell dang nazh-kap wuh vi-yumuk abru' ish-veh, na' au has frequently katau ish-veh tor t'nash-veh kelek, heh i ma afer-tor myself ik i kupi hardly tehnau wuh sem t' ish-veh manner. Au nam-tor older do arthur, wuh sasu t' wuh panu tor ish-veh ozh-um, veh vi had vesh' kanok-wilat, gla-tor kanok-vei, wuh maut-ugelik talker, heh wuh sasu t' lo'uk personal vaksur. Wi lu i nah-tor t' ish-veh svi' samu khaf, irak maf s' wuh glamour t' ish-veh la'es, i am convinced s' ish-veh cynical starun heh wuh glazhau if i ma kum-tor svi' ish-veh bezhun ik au nam-tor veh vi dang nam-tor deeply distrusted. Ni i nah-tor, heh ni, nuh', nah-tor t'nash-veh pi' mary, vi has wuh kosu's sahris insight vi' character. "heh i' tra' nam-tor goh she tor nam-tor kethelvau. She nam-tor t'nash-veh ko-bath; tonk'peh lu t'nash-veh sa-kai tev-tor kaukuh tevun ago heh losrak ish-veh sa'awek svi' wuh panu i thanai ish-veh, heh ma glazhau fi-tor ish-veh ek'wak opi' u' t'nash-veh ko-fu. She nam-tor wuh sunbeam svi' t'nash-veh housesweet, loving, vaksurik, wuh wonderful khartausu heh housekeeper, wi u' sival heh hizhuk heh gentle u' wuh kosu kupi nam-tor. She nam-tor t'nash-veh gas'rak el'ru. I ri tor fai-tor ra i kupi tor rik' ish-veh. Svi' goh veh tukh has she ek'wak hal-tor tehnat t'nash-veh istau. Dah'wak t'nash-veh sa-kan has ya'akash ish-veh tor marry ish-veh, na' au ashau ish-veh devotedly, tonk'peh tik wak she has klee'fah ish-veh. I nah-tor ik kuv sovek-veh kupi ma drawn ish-veh vi' wuh gas'rak yut ish-veh would ma vesh' she, heh ik ish-veh kal'i'farr lau ma rubai ish-veh bosh ha'kiv; tonk'peh i', alas! Ish-veh nam-tor nuh' lateforever nuh' tab-ma! "i', mr. Holmes, du fai-tor wuh sutra vi ha-tor ne' t'nash-veh kamu, heh i dungau fator k' t'nash-veh miserable var. "lu etek vesh' taking mon svi' wuh bestan-tvi-shal ik mu-yor po' aru-yem, i var-tor arthur heh mary t'nash-veh veshtaya, heh t' wuh taluhk treasure if etek had ne' etwel kamu, suppressing goh wuh ahm t' t'nash-veh client. Lucy parr, vi had katau svi' wuh mon, had, i am sure, losrak wuh tvi-shal; tonk'peh i fam yehat swear ik wuh svep vesh' a'ing. Mary heh arthur vesh' mau interested heh istau tor gla-tor wuh khinik coronet, tonk'peh i nahp ish-veh weh-rom ri tor ertau ish-veh. "'wilat ma du shitau ish-veh?' ya'akash arthur. "'svi' t'nash-veh sha' bureau.' "'muhl, i rok tor goodness wuh kelek skil-tor't nam-tor burgled du' wuh mu-yor.' leralmin-tor au. "'ish-veh nam-tor klacha abru, ' i kilko-tor. "'oh, sovek hinek tal-muv dungi nunau ik bureau. Lu i vesh' wuh youngster i ma tu'ash ish-veh myself k' wuh tal-muv t' wuh natuhn-tvi-shal cupboard.' "au k'ashiv had wuh kwai yut t' talking, ni ik i nahp pi' t' ra au leralmin-tor. Au zahal-tor me tor t'nash-veh tvi-shal, however, ik mu-yor k' wuh maut shi'vukhut limuk. "'glazhau la', dad, ' leralmin-tor au k' ish-veh bezhun vishizhau ne', 'mokuhlek du kal-tor me ma 200?' "'rai, i fam yehat!' i kilko-tor sharply. 'i ma vesh' irak nuh' generous k' du svi' donku tukh.' "'du ma vesh' maut ves, ' leralmin-tor au, 'tonk'peh i bolau ma nash donku, il else i mokuhlek worla gluvaya t'nash-veh limuk svi'udish wuh muhd va'ashiv.' "'heh wuh maut rom vel, nuh'!' i maf-tor. "'ha, tonk'peh du would ri ma me trasha ish-veh wuh dishonoured sasu, ' leralmin-tor au. 'i kupi ri lesh wuh disgrace. I bolau ashenau wuh donku svi' ein yut, heh kuv du dungi ri kal-tor me ma ish-veh, yi i bolau ar'kadan vath tvai.' "i vesh' maut reshnek, na' nash vesh' wuh wuh haishaya du' wuh tevun-krus. 'du dungau ri ma wuh farthing s' me, ' i maf-tor, fi' if au ovalau heh losrak wuh tvi-shal rik' wuh'ashiv zhit. "lu au vesh' hal-tor i unlocked t'nash-veh bureau, tor sure ik t'nash-veh treasure vesh' safe, heh klacha ish-veh va'ashiv. Yi i palikau tor hal-tor pauk wuh kelek tor gla-tor ik ek' vesh' securea gu-vam if i usually trasha tor mary tonk'peh if i nahp ish-veh muhl tor perform myself ik mu-yor. U' vesht sarlah nash-veh ne' wuh kaiden vesht gla-tor nash-veh mary herself na' wuh vla krani t' wuh tvur, if she a'ing heh terau u' i betau. "'var-tor me, dad, ' leralmin-tor she, looking, i nahp, wuh pi' ertau, 'did du mazhiv-kur-tor lucy, wuh maid, trasha tor hal-tor si' tor-mu-yor?' "'certainly ri.' "'sarlah ish-veh svi' aishan i' k' wuh pla' svep. I ma rai vet ik she has goh vesh' tor wuh vla temep tor gla-tor ein-veh, tonk'peh i nah-tor ik ish-veh nam-tor hardly safe heh dang nam-tor pehkau.' "'du bolau stariben tor ish-veh svi' wuh asal, il i dungi kuv du prefer ish-veh. Nam-tor du sure ik kanok-vei nam-tor terau?' "'ved sure, dad.' "'yi, rom-mu-yor.' i shok-tor ish-veh heh went abru tor t'nash-veh shi'yuk va'ashiv, wilat i vesh' ak asleep. "i am endeavouring tor var-tor du kanok-vei, mr. Holmes, if lau ma sovek kuvish fi-tor wuh nuf, tonk'peh i eit'jae ik du dungi deshker me fi-tor sovek sfek if i ri tor tor pa'shik." "fi' wuh contrary, ish-veh star-krus nam-tor singularly lucid." "sarlah nash-veh tor wuh krus t' t'nash-veh var i' svi' if i dang istaya tor nam-tor wa' ni. I am ri wuh maut ras sleeper, heh wuh anxiety svi' t'nash-veh kashek palutunau, rai vet, tor tor me kauk lehkuh ni do tsuri. Pa' dahkuh svi' wuh asal, yi, i vesh' awakened k' ein ralash svi' wuh kelek. Ish-veh had ceased ere i vesh' eik kum'i, tonk'peh ish-veh had losrak wuh impression za' ish-veh u' hi wuh krani had kogavik a'ing ein-wilat. I ti listening k' ek' t'nash-veh kaluk. Suddenly, tor t'nash-veh horror, tra' vesh' wuh natya ralash t' footsteps dvun-tor softly svi' wuh thurai tvi-shal. I trel-tor s' sar-tak, ek' palpitating k' pthak, heh peeped pauk wuh teruk t' t'nash-veh sai-vel-tor-tvi-shal svep. "'arthur!' i shei, 'du villain! Du pi'tak! Uf dare du esta ik coronet?' "wuh pa-tukh vesh' ulef abru, u' i had losrak ish-veh, heh t'nash-veh unhappy sa-kan, sai-vel-tor goh svi' ish-veh sav'el heh malanu, vesh' standing be' wuh ta'hal, holding wuh coronet svi' ish-veh el'ru. Au saudau tor nam-tor wrenching na' ish-veh, il bending ish-veh k' ek' ish-veh karik'es. Na' t'nash-veh maf au eku-tor ish-veh s' ish-veh ruskaraya heh da-tor u' spoh u' tevakh. I snatched ish-veh abru heh linisau ish-veh. Veh t' wuh pi-maat-tukh teruk, k' rehkuh t' wuh beryls svi' ish-veh, vesh' missing. "'du blackguard!' i saul-tor, be' myself k' reshan. 'du ma vashau ish-veh! Du ma dishonoured me ek'wak! Wilat nam-tor wuh ek'zer if du ma stolen?' "'stolen!' au maf-tor. "'ha, pi'tak!' i roared, shaking ish-veh k' wuh tipan. "'tra' nam-tor rim missing. Tra' fam yehat nam-tor sovek missing, ' leralmin-tor au. "'tra' nam-tor rehkuh missing. Heh du fai-tor wilat au nam-tor. Bolau i vutau du wuh liar u' muhl u' wuh pi'tak? Did i ri gla-tor du trying tor bezhun-masu ska' wuh'ashiv krus?' "'du ma puvutau me ahm hiyet, ' leralmin-tor au, 'i dungi ri lamok ish-veh sovek longer. I dungau ri leralmin wuh'ashiv zhit pa' nash business, opi' du ma pudvel-tor tor viltah me. I dungi trasha ish-veh kelek svi' wuh asal heh tor t'nash-veh sha' yut svi' wuh panu.' "'du dungau trasha ish-veh svi' wuh el'ru t' wuh police!' i maf-tor ulef-mad k' tushat heh reshan. 'i dungau ma nash tukh nisau tor wuh lanet.' "'du dungau oren-tor nothing s' me, ' leralmin-tor au k' wuh shaukaush such u' i dang ri ma nahp vesh' svi' ish-veh malat. 'kuv du dvel-tor tor vutau wuh police, kal-tor wuh police talal ra au mokuhlek.' "k' nash wak wuh bosh kelek vesh' astir, na' i had ashenau t'nash-veh spes svi' t'nash-veh reshan. Mary vesh' wuh wuh'rak tor rush vi' t'nash-veh tvi-shal, heh, na' wuh glan t' wuh coronet heh t' arthur's limuk, she telv-tor wuh bosh var heh, k' wuh shei, tevan-tor ne' senseless fi' wuh solektra. I satau wuh housemaid na' wuh police heh shitau wuh investigation vi' ish-veh el'ru na' wuh'wak. Lu wuh inspector heh wuh constable svi-tor wuh kelek, arthur, vi had lam-tor sullenly k' ish-veh kar hesha, ya'akash me whether ish-veh vesh' t'nash-veh intention tor falun ish-veh k' theft. I kilko-tor ik ish-veh had ceased tor nam-tor wuh awek tukh, tonk'peh had shetau wuh tsuri veh, opi' wuh ruined coronet vesh' national veltra. I vesh' satalau ik wuh tor-gav dang ma its yut svi' kanok-vei. "'k'puu, ' leralmin-tor au, 'du dungi ri ma me pehkau na' wuh'wak. Ish-veh would nam-tor tor ish-veh advantage u' muhl u' t'nash-veh kuv i lau trasha wuh kelek na' kaukuh minutes.' "'ik du lau prah maf, il sos'eh ik du lau ip-sut ra du ma stolen, ' leralmin-tor i. Heh yi, realising wuh dreadful shul svi' if i vesh' shitau, i implored ish-veh tor vokau ik ri goh t'nash-veh dor tonk'peh ik t' veh vi vesh' irak weht tor i vesh' na' stake; heh ik au threatened tor ashenau wuh scandal if would convulse wuh shashol. Au lau avert ish-veh ek' kuv au would tonk'peh var-tor me ra au had ovsoh k' wuh rehkuh missing kov. "'du lau u' muhl limuk wuh tukh, ' leralmin-tor i; 'du ma vesh' kum-tor svi' wuh bae'cok, heh rai confession kupi tor ish-veh guilt weht heinous. Kuv du tonk'peh tor such reparation u' nam-tor svi' ish-veh tepul, k' telling etek wilat wuh beryls nam-tor, ek' dungau nam-tor forgiven heh yen-tor.' "'potau ish-veh thrap-fam'es nufau na' eifa vi ya'akash na' ish-veh, ' au kilko-tor, turning maf s' me k' wuh sneer. Vesht gla-tor nash-veh ik au vesh' nuh' hardened na' sovek zhit t' t'nash-veh tor vi-yumuk ish-veh. Tra' vesh' tonk'peh veh yut na' ish-veh. I puvutau svi' wuh inspector heh mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh vi' custody. Wuh psthan vesh' tor na' wuh'wak ri goh t' ish-veh person tonk'peh t' ish-veh tvi-shal heh t' kanok portion t' wuh kelek wilat au kupi possibly ma ip-sut wuh ek'zer; tonk'peh rai zavikau t' au kupi nam-tor afer-tor, il would wuh wretched sa-kan tu'ash ish-veh ru'lut na' ek' etwel persuasions heh etwel nan. Nash asal au vesh' snem-tor tor wuh nala, heh i, po' going k'fai ek' wuh police formalities, ma hurried pauk tor du tor implore du tor nam-tor-tor ish-veh renkup'es svi' unravelling wuh tukh. Du suppose ik ish-veh sa-fu sarlah ne' s' ish-veh sar-tak, went, na' lo'uk risk, tor ish-veh sai-vel-tor-tvi-shal, tu'ash ish-veh bureau, nem-tor si' ish-veh coronet, shau ska' k' nen nekwitaya wuh pi' portion t' ish-veh, went ska' tor ein vath shi, ip-sut rehkuh ek'zer s' wuh reh-leh-naukuh, k' such renkup'es ik kling mokuhlek talal au, heh yi fun-tor k' wuh vath reh-leh-shehkuh vi' wuh tvi-shal svi' if au ko'nar himself tor wuh greatest tehvar t' hasu discovered. I' i am losrak tor wuh lonely heh dishonoured ya'shakhuv. Veh sorrow sarlah ikap-tor fi-tor wuh timut t' wuh'ashiv. T'nash-veh ko-bath, mary, has deserted me." "deserted du?" "ha. Ish-veh sar-tak nash asal had ri vesh' yuk-tor svi', ish-veh tvi-shal vesh' herbosh, heh wuh pitoh na' me ti fi-tor wuh tvur pasu. I had leralmin-tor tor ish-veh kim-shah mu-yor, svi' sorrow heh ri svi' reshan, ik kuv she had telik t'nash-veh sa-kan ek' lau ma vesh' muhl k' ish-veh. Sos'eh ish-veh vesh' thoughtless t' me tor leralmin ni. Ish-veh nam-tor tor ik remark ik she dzhinau svi' nash pitoh: "'t'nash-veh dearest sa-kuk, i olau ik i ma katau trouble fi-tor du, heh ik kuv i had bae'cok differently nash terrible misfortune lau worla ma paresh-tor. I fam yehat, k' nash nahp svi' t'nash-veh kashek, ek'wak va'ashiv nam-tor kunli ne' ish-veh kamu, heh i olau ik i bolau trasha du ek'wak. Ri tor worry pa' t'nash-veh fa-wak, na' ik nam-tor tanilau na'; heh, abru' ek', ri tor psthan na' me, na' ish-veh dungi nam-tor fruitless zup heh wuh has-bosh-dvin tor me. Svi' ha'kiv il svi' tevakh, i am ek'wak ish-veh loving, "'mary.' "ra kupi she tvai k' ik pitoh, mr. Holmes? Tor du nah-tor ish-veh sfekau tor suicide?" "rai, rai, nothing t' wuh ves. Ish-veh nam-tor sos'eh wuh buhfik tor-yehat kilkaya. I sahrafel, mr. Holder, ik du nam-tor nearing wuh shaht t' ish-veh troubles." "ha! Du leralmin ni! Du ma puzhu-tor vel, mr. Holmes; du ma oren-tor vel! Wilat nam-tor wuh ek'zer?" "du would ri nah-tor 1000 apiece wuh mauyik hau-ov na' au?" "i would vlitau lehkuh." "ik would nam-tor unnecessary. Rehkuh thousand dungi wein wuh tukh. Heh tra' nam-tor wuh pi' reward, i fancy. Ma du ish-veh cheque-dunap? La' nam-tor wuh pen. Weh-rom tor ish-veh si' na' 4000." k' wuh dazed limuk wuh banker tor si' wuh required rihamau. Holmes lates-tor abru' tor ish-veh kitau-skaf, nem-tor si' wuh pi' triangular krus t' pi-maat-tukh k' rehkuh ek'zer svi' ish-veh, heh threw ish-veh ne' fi-tor wuh pasu. K' wuh shriek t' mak etwel client clutched ish-veh abru. "du ma ish-veh!" au hushau. "i am korsau! I am korsau!" wuh rolaya t' mak vesh' u' passionate u' ish-veh tushat had vesh', heh au teraya-martaya ish-veh recovered ek'zer tor ish-veh bosom. "tra' nam-tor veh vath vel du owe, mr. Holder, " leralmin-tor sherlock holmes rather sternly. "owe!" au kum-tor abru wuh pen. "ahm wuh hau-ov, heh i dungi vlitau ish-veh." "rai, wuh sa'akh nam-tor ri tor me. Du owe wuh maut humble apology tor ik thol lad, ish-veh sa-fu, vi has lesh himself svi' nash tukh u' i dang nam-tor yaut tor gla-tor t'nash-veh sha' sa-fu tor, dang i ek'wak pavesh ki' veh." "yi ish-veh vesh' ri arthur vi nem-tor au?" "i var-tor du za-gad, heh i ashiv-tor tor-gad, ik ish-veh vesh' ri." "du nam-tor sure t' ish-veh! Yi kal-tor etek brax tor ish-veh na' wuh'wak tor kal-tor ish-veh fai-tor ik wuh yeht'es nam-tor fainu." "au fai-tor ish-veh already. Lu i had pa'shu ish-veh ek' abru i had wuh interview k' ish-veh, heh finding ik au would ri var-tor me wuh var, i var-tor ish-veh tor ish-veh, fi' if au had tor confess ik i vesh' gas'rak heh tor hau wuh maut zamu details if vesh' ri wi ved pa'shik tor me. Ish-veh ro'fori t' nash asal, however, lau tu'ash ish-veh bru-lar." "na' sha-ka-ri's sake, var-tor me, yi, ra nam-tor nash wehtsuri mystery!" "i dungi tor ni, heh i dungi gluvaya du wuh ash-tor k' if i pulau ish-veh. Heh kal-tor me leralmin tor du, wuh'rak, ik if ish-veh nam-tor hardest na' me tor leralmin heh na' du tor zhu-tor: tra' has vesh' wuh understanding svi' osu george burnwell heh ish-veh ko-bath mary. Au ma i' sasahr-tor teretuhr." "t'nash-veh mary? Impossible!" "ish-veh nam-tor unfortunately weht do tor-yehat; ish-veh nam-tor ac'ruth. Neither du il ish-veh sa-fu fai-tor wuh yeht character t' nash sasu lu du nafai-tor ish-veh vi' ish-veh skan da-kuv. Au nam-tor veh t' wuh danik tehvar-bosh sasu svi' englanda ruined gambler, wuh absolutely desperate villain, wuh sasu rik' khaf-spol il conscience. Ish-veh ko-bath fai-tor nothing t' such sasu. Lu au breathed ish-veh vows tor ish-veh, u' au had ovsoh tor wuh hundred fa' ish-veh, she snuhkrol-tor herself ik she sa'awek had estuhl ish-veh khaf-spol. Wuh e'shua fai-tor buhfik ra au leralmin-tor, tonk'peh k'puu she became ish-veh raul heh vesh' svi' wuh es'merka t' seeing ish-veh nearly kanok khru." "i fam yehat, heh i dungi ri, dva-tor ish-veh!" maf-tor wuh banker k' wuh ashen limuk. "i dungi var-tor du, yi, ra paresh-tor svi' ish-veh kelek kim-shah mu-yor. Ish-veh ko-bath, lu du had, u' she nahp, hal-tor tor ish-veh tvi-shal, trel-tor ne' heh variben tor ish-veh lover k'fai wuh krani if fulag-tor vi' wuh tihet lane. Ish-veh footmarks had hish-tor gas'rak k'fai wuh izh, ni wu had au lam-tor tra'. She var-tor ish-veh t' wuh coronet. Ish-veh wicked lust na' pi-maat-tukh kindled na' wuh ro'fori, heh au keh'sei ish-veh tor ish-veh dungi. I ma rai vet ik she ashau du, tonk'peh tra' nam-tor kosu svi' ik wuh ashaya t' wuh lover sayonotau ek' vath ashau, heh i nah-tor ik she bolau ma vesh' veh. She had hardly shroi tor ish-veh instructions lu gla-tor ish-veh du coming downstairs, fi' if she a'ing wuh krani rapidly heh var-tor du pa' veh t' wuh dvinsu' escapade k' ish-veh wooden-legged lover, if vesh' ek' perfectly yeht. "ish-veh sa-kan, arthur, went tor sar-tak po' ish-veh interview k' du tonk'peh au yuk-tor badly fi' khrosahp t' ish-veh uneasiness pa' ish-veh muhd sa'akh. Svi' wuh svitan t' wuh mu-yor au puzhu-tor wuh mos tread be' dvun ish-veh svep, ni au she-tor heh, looking si', vesh' ak'wikmun tor gla-tor ish-veh krei walking maut stealthily bi' wuh tvur abi' she sasaudau vi' ish-veh sai-vel-tor-tvi-shal. Kovtulik k' astonishment, wuh lad trel-tor fi' ein sai-vel heh bek-tor tra' svi' wuh gu'gelik tor gla-tor ra would sarlah t' nash flekh tek'ik. Presently she sasarlah s' wuh tvi-shal va'ashiv, heh svi' wuh ta'hal t' wuh tvur-ha'gelek ish-veh sa-fu gla-tor ik she lesh wuh taluhk coronet svi' ish-veh el'ru. She be' dvun-tor ne' wuh kaiden, heh au, thrilling k' horror, sahr-tor bi' heh trel-tor za' wuh curtain be' ish-veh svep, whence au kupi gla-tor ra be' dvun-tor svi' wuh tvur ne'rak. Gla-tor ish-veh ish-veh stealthily tu'ash wuh krani, el'ru si' wuh coronet tor ein-veh svi' wuh gloom, heh yi ikapik ish-veh wuh'wak weht brax pla' tor ish-veh tvi-shal, be' dvun-tor ved beyik wilat au lam-tor ip-sut za' wuh curtain. "u' wu u' she vesh' fi' wuh scene au kupi ri nem-tor sovek torai rik' wuh horrible sashavaya t' wuh kosu ik au ashau. Tonk'peh wuh instant ik she vesh' hal-tor au realised uf crushing wuh misfortune nash would nam-tor na' du, heh uf ek'-yauluhk ish-veh vesh' tor eku ish-veh gas'rak. Au rushed ne', aishan u' au vesh', svi' ish-veh sai-famik ash'ya, tu'ash wuh krani, sprang si' vi' wuh izh, heh sahr-tor ne' wuh lane, wilat au kupi gla-tor wuh gu'gelik khlop svi' wuh moonlight. Osu george burnwell ar'kada tor prah maf, tonk'peh arthur kum-tor ish-veh, heh tra' vesh' wuh struggle svi' au, ish-veh lad tugging na' veh vla t' wuh coronet, heh ish-veh opponent na' wuh vath. Svi' wuh scuffle, ish-veh sa-fu kwul-tor osu george heh tresahk ish-veh abru' wuh bezhun. Yi vel suddenly snapped, heh ish-veh sa-fu, finding ik au had wuh coronet svi' ish-veh el'ru, rushed pla', a'ing wuh krani, she-tor tor ish-veh tvi-shal, heh had aishan glantau ik wuh coronet had vesh' kuvoran-tor svi' wuh struggle heh vesh' endeavouring tor zeh-tor ish-veh lu du saudau fi-tor wuh scene." "nam-tor ish-veh tor-yehat?" hushau wuh banker. "du yi kastorilau ish-veh reshan k' calling ish-veh ahm na' wuh moment lu au olau ik au had nazh-tor ish-veh warmest itaren. Au kupi ri danau wuh yeht fupa s' t' tek'ik rik' betraying veh vi certainly nazh-tor pi' hiyet consideration na' ish-veh el'ru. Au nem-tor wuh weht chivalrous zan-tor, however, heh korsau ish-veh tsat." "heh ik vesh' po she shrieked heh fainted lu gla-tor ish-veh wuh coronet, " maf-tor mr. Holder. "oh, t'nash-veh oekon! Ra wuh glan-fam duhsu i ma vesh'! Heh ish-veh asking tor nam-tor kal-tor tor hal-tor si' na' kaukuh minutes! Wuh tal-kam katravahsu aitlu tor gla-tor kuv wuh missing krus vesh' na' wuh scene t' wuh struggle. Uf cruelly i ma misjudged ish-veh!" "lu i lasha na' wuh kelek, " fator holmes, "i na' wuh'wak went maut carefully pauk ish-veh tor glantau kuv tra' vesh' sovek zavikau svi' wuh izh if lau gol'nev me. I fai-tor ik rim had tevan-tor opi' wuh khru fa', heh isha ik tra' had vesh' wuh karik le-su tor korsau impressions. I be' dvun-tor bi' wuh tradesmen's yut, tonk'peh afer-tor ish-veh ek' sahr-tor ne' heh indistinguishable. Aishan mesakh ish-veh, however, na' wuh irak vla t' wuh af'tum svep, wuh kosu had lam-tor heh variben k' wuh sasu, t'vi pauk impressions fi' veh vla gluvau ik au had wuh wooden mal. I kupi kauk var-tor ik au had vesh' ertau, na' wuh kosu had sahr-tor pla' swiftly tor wuh svep, u' vesh' shown k' wuh glu gof heh ta'hal timut ulidar, du' wooden-mal had bek-tor wuh pi', heh yi had hal-tor maf. I nahp na' wuh wak ik nash lau nam-tor wuh maid heh ish-veh sweetheart, t' ik du had already spoken tor me, heh inquiry gluvau ish-veh vesh' ni. I be' dvun-tor pauk wuh bah-ker rik' seeing sovek-vel weht do kafunik ash'yaidar, if i nem-tor tor nam-tor wuh police; tonk'peh lu i prah vi' wuh tihet lane wuh maut wu heh wehkonik var vesh' written svi' wuh izh svi' khom t' me. "tra' vesh' wuh dahtau zehl t' ash'yaidar t' wuh booted sasu, heh wuh dahr dahtau zehl if vesht gla-tor nash-veh k' delight belonged tor wuh sasu k' sai-fam ash'ya. I vesh' na' wuh'wak convinced s' ra du had var-tor me ik wuh latter vesh' ish-veh sa-fu. Wuh wuh'rak had lates-tor fi' yut, tonk'peh wuh vath had sahr-tor swiftly, heh u' ish-veh tread vesh' pu'ulidau svi' shitau abru' wuh neik-shal t' wuh kluf, ish-veh vesh' obvious ik au had be' dvun-tor po' wuh vath. I zahal-tor au abru heh afer-tor au pufulag-tor tor wuh tvur krani, wilat kluf had worn ek' wuh izh maf du' waiting. Yi i lates-tor tor wuh vath shaht, if vesh' wuh hundred ker il weht ne' wuh lane. Vesht gla-tor nash-veh wilat kluf had limuk-tor pauk, wilat wuh izh vesh' tresahk abru u' hi tra' had vesh' wuh struggle, heh, t'forti, wilat wuh zamu eku-tor t' khaf had tevan-tor, tor gluvaya me ik i vesh' ri mistaken. Kluf had yi sahr-tor ne' wuh lane, heh wuh'ashiv pi' smudge t' khaf gluvau ik ish-veh vesh' au vi had vesh' dash-tor. Lu sarlah ish-veh tor wuh pid fau-yut na' wuh vath shaht, i afer-tor ik wuh pavement had vesh' pa'shu, ni tra' vesh' wuh shaht tor ik clue. "fi' entering wuh kelek, however, i linisau, u' du vokau, wuh sku heh nentutra t' wuh tvur krani k' t'nash-veh gelek, heh i kupi na' wuh'wak gla-tor ik ein-veh had be' dvun-tor si'. I kupi distinguish wuh outline t' wuh instep wilat wuh masupik ash'ya had vesh' shitau svi' coming svi'. I vesh' yi palikaya kup tor shid wuh opinion u' tor ra had paresh-tor. Wuh sasu had bek-tor s'udish wuh krani; ein-veh had katau wuh ek'zer; wuh deed had vesh' overseen k' ish-veh sa-fu; au had pursued wuh pi'tak; had struggled k' ish-veh; au had tik seshau na' wuh coronet, ish-veh kaunshuk karik'es causing dash if neither sa'awek kupi ma effected. Au had fun-tor k' wuh prize, tonk'peh had losrak wuh karf svi' wuh ruskaraya t' ish-veh opponent. Ni irak i vesh' pa'shik. Wuh deshker i' vesh', vi vesh' wuh sasu, heh vi vesh' ish-veh katau ish-veh wuh coronet? "ish-veh nam-tor wuh hinek maxim t' t'nash-veh ik lu du ma sanan-tor wuh impossible, whatever hafau, however improbable, bolau nam-tor wuh yeht'es. I', i fai-tor ik ish-veh vesh' ri du vi had katau ish-veh ne', ni tra' goh hafau ish-veh ko-bath heh wuh maids. Tonk'peh kuv ish-veh vesh' wuh maids, po dang ish-veh sa-fu kal-tor himself tor nam-tor accused svi' ish-veh shi? Tra' kupi nam-tor rai tor-yehat utvau. U' au ashau ish-veh krei, however, tra' vesh' wuh marom danaya po au dang retain ish-veh secretthe weht ni u' wuh tsat vesh' wuh disgraceful veh. Lu i vokau ik du had gla-tor ish-veh na' ik krani, heh uf she had fainted fi' seeing wuh coronet va'ashiv, t'nash-veh conjecture became wuh certainty. "heh vi kupi ish-veh nam-tor vi vesh' ish-veh confederate? Wuh lover evidently, na' vi else kupi spunsau wuh ashaya heh gratitude if she bolau olau tor du? I fai-tor ik du went si' pi', heh ik ish-veh da-kuv t' t'hylara vesh' wuh maut limited veh. Tonk'peh ekhlami vesh' osu george burnwell. I had puzhu-tor t' ish-veh fa' u' hasu wuh sasu t' ek'rasah reputation among kosu. Ish-veh bolau ma vesh' au vi sai-vel-tor eifa kluf heh retained wuh missing ek'zer. Kauk hi au fai-tor ik arthur had discovered ish-veh, au lau fam dvun snuhkrol-tor himself ik au vesh' safe, na' wuh lad kupi ri leralmin wuh zhit rik' compromising ish-veh sha' skan. "muhl, ish-veh sha' rom kash-ral dungi suggest ra thon-tor i nem-tor thurai. I went svi' wuh shid t' wuh loafer tor osu george's kelek, khartau tor abrashau wuh acquaintance k' ish-veh valet, oren-tor ik ish-veh trensu had tresahk ish-veh patam wuh mu-yor fa', heh, t'forti, na' wuh kodona t' shehkuh shillings, tor ek' sure k' buying wuh shif t' ish-veh vishizhau-ska' ash'el. K' aifa i halovau ne' tor streatham heh gla-tor ik au exactly fitted wuh ash'yaidar." "vesht gla-tor nash-veh wuh has-bosh-sai-vel-tor vagabond svi' wuh lane za-gad khru, " leralmin-tor mr. Holder. "precisely. Ish-veh vesh' i. I afer-tor ik i had t'nash-veh sasu, ni vesht sarlah nash-veh ha-kel heh rubai t'nash-veh sai-vel. Ish-veh vesh' wuh delicate krus if i had tor mavau yi, na' vesht gla-tor nash-veh ik wuh prosecution bolau nam-tor nan'woi tor avert scandal, heh i fai-tor ik ni astute wuh villain would gla-tor ik etwel el'ru vesh' tied svi' wuh tukh. I went heh gla-tor ish-veh. Palikauk, veling, au wafu kanok-vei. Tonk'peh lu i mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh kanok particular ik had paresh-tor, au ar'kada tor bluster heh nem-tor ne' wuh ha'kiv-preserver s' wuh temok. I fai-tor t'nash-veh sasu, however, heh i clapped wuh el'ru-pohshayek tor ish-veh patam fa' au kupi kwul. Yi au became wuh pi' weht reasonable. I var-tor ish-veh ik etek would mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh price na' wuh kov au meskarau 1000 apiece. Ik katau si' wuh wuh'rak glat t' tushat ik au had shown. 'po, dash ish-veh ek'!' leralmin-tor au, 'i've kal-tor au hal-tor na' shehkuh hundred na' wuh rehkuh!' i ak khartau tor prah wuh shi'yavekh t' wuh poprahek vi had au, fi' promising ish-veh ik tra' would nam-tor rai prosecution. Ska' i eku tor ish-veh, heh po' mau chaffering i prah etwel kov na' 1000 apiece. Yi i glazhau svi' fi-tor ish-veh sa-fu, var-tor ish-veh ik ek' vesh' gas'rak, heh eventually prah tor t'nash-veh sar-tak pa' dahkuh o'wak-vel, po' ra i lau vutau wuh really lerash gad's ar'kadan." "wuh gad if has korsau england s' wuh lo'uk tsuri scandal, " leralmin-tor wuh banker, rising. "osu, i fam yehat talal zhit tor nemaiyo, tonk'peh du dungau ri talal me ungrateful na' ra du ma ovsoh. Ish-veh renkup'es has indeed namautau ek' ik i ma puzhu-tor t' ish-veh. Heh i' i bolau hash-tor tor t'nash-veh tal-kam sa-kan tor apologise tor ish-veh na' wuh riyeht if i ma ovsoh ish-veh. U' tor ra du var-tor me t' ri donku-tor mary, ish-veh hal-tor tor t'nash-veh maut khaf-spol. Ri kauk ish-veh renkup'es mokuhlek inform me wilat she nam-tor i'." "i nah-tor ik etek lau safely leralmin, " fun-tor holmes, "ik she nam-tor wherever osu george burnwell nam-tor. Ish-veh nam-tor kaing ac'ruth, nuh', ik whatever ish-veh sins nam-tor, au dungi ak poprah wuh weht do sufficient taflaya." xii. Wuh adventure t' wuh khaf-tukh beeches "tor wuh sasu vi ashau tanaf na' its sha' sake, " remarked sherlock holmes, tossing aside wuh advertisement thalv t' wuh kanok-gadik telegraph, "ish-veh nam-tor frequently svi' its least yauluhk heh lowliest manifestations ik wuh keenest sanosh nam-tor tor nam-tor derived. Ish-veh nam-tor vaksurik tor me tor glantau, watson, ik du ma ni irak ruskarau nash yeht'es ik svi' aifa pi' vipladau t' etwel nuf if du ma vesh' rom hiyet tor bes-tor abru, heh, i am bound tor leralmin, occasionally tor embellish, du ma putan-tor prominence ri ni mau tor wuh wehk aisha célèbres heh sensational trials svi' if i ma figured tonk'peh rather tor eifa incidents if lau ma vesh' trivial svi' themselves, tonk'peh if ma putan-tor tvi-shal na' eifa sutra t' nenem heh t' olozhikaik fereikan if i ma tor t'nash-veh special province." "heh wi, " leralmin-tor i, smiling, "i fam yehat ved meskaraya myself absolved s' wuh falun t' sensationalism if has vesh' urged tehnat t'nash-veh vipladau." "du ma laf-tor, sos'eh, " au glantau, taking abru wuh glowing cinder k' wuh el'abrashayek heh ha'gelan k' ish-veh wuh wu cherry-lapan mev if vesh' wont tor va'prah ish-veh krizhiv lu au vesh' svi' wuh disputatious rather do wuh meditative mood"du ma laf-tor sos'eh svi' attempting tor shitau kur heh ha'kiv vi' tik t' ish-veh star-krus instead t' confining yourself tor wuh task t' placing fi-tor vipladau ik severe reasoning s' aishan tor daya if nam-tor really wuh goh notable feature pa' wuh vel." "ish-veh seems tor me ik i ma ovsoh du bosh yeht-gav svi' wuh tukh, " i remarked k' ein coldness, na' i vesh' repelled k' wuh ritsuri-shai'es if i had weht do wuh'wak glantau tor nam-tor wuh karik klai svi' t'nash-veh t'hy'la's singular character. "rai, ish-veh nam-tor ri selfishness il conceit, " leralmin-tor au, answering, u' vesh' ish-veh wont, t'nash-veh nahp rather do t'nash-veh zhit. "kuv i claim bosh yeht-gav na' t'nash-veh tanaf, ish-veh nam-tor fai'ei ish-veh nam-tor wuh impersonal thinga vel mesakh myself. Tr'y'kak nam-tor tsuri. Ozhika nam-tor ritsuri. Therefore ish-veh nam-tor fi-tor wuh ozhika rather do fi-tor wuh tr'y'kak ik du dang dwell. Du ma degraded ra dang ma vesh' wuh rivak t' lectures vi' wuh weizehl t' var." ish-veh vesh' wuh samu asal t' wuh lehkuh-mal sikar, heh etek hayal-tor po' asal-yem fi' either vla t' wuh cheery yon svi' wuh hinek tvi-shal na' leipausu yut. Wuh bali ihsek padukau ne' svi' wuh zehl t' dun-kur-tor kelek, heh wuh opposing krani loomed spo' gu'gelik, shapeless blurs k'fai wuh ras kin-kur wreaths. Etwel pa-tukh vesh' lit heh min-tor fi' wuh wan-kur sai heh glimmer t' china heh mokev, na' wuh pasu had ri vesh' pa'shu wi. Sherlock holmes had vesh' ralash-fam ek' wuh asal, dipping continuously vi' wuh advertisement tsek t' wuh succession t' dun abi' na' kim-shah, having sauyaing putan-tor abru ish-veh psthan, au had sasarlah svi' rai maut slor temper tor lecture me fi-tor t'nash-veh literary shortcomings. "na' wuh ka wak, " au remarked po' wuh svizh, du' if au had hayal-tor puffing na' ish-veh wu mev heh gazing ne' vi' wuh yon, "du mokuhlek hardly nam-tor tu'ash tor wuh falun t' sensationalism, na' s' aifa nuf if du ma vesh' ni ves u' tor eku'ko yourself svi', wuh rom proportion ri tor skasau t' tr'y'kak, svi' its legal kash-ral, na' ek'. Wuh pi' tukh svi' if i endeavoured tor gol'nev wuh sa-te'kru t' bohemia, wuh singular veshtaya t' din-tor mary sutherland, wuh wat tersau k' wuh sasu k' wuh kuvoran-tor bru, heh wuh incident t' wuh thol bachelor, vesh' ek' tukh if nam-tor s'udish wuh spoh t' wuh tor-gav. Tonk'peh svi' avoiding wuh sensational, i pthak ik du lau ma bordered fi' wuh trivial." "wuh shaht lau ma vesh' ni, " i kilko-tor, "tonk'peh wuh methods i meskaraya ki' vesh' dunap heh t' eku'ko." "pshaw, t'nash-veh tal-kam katravahsu, ra tor wuh tsuri, wuh lo'uk unobservant tsuri, vi kupi hardly var-tor wuh weaver k' ish-veh zud il wuh compositor k' ish-veh losrak kaur-ozh, tun pa' wuh finer duvek-tor t' nisaya heh nenem! Tonk'peh, indeed, kuv du nam-tor trivial, i fam yehat tenai du, na' wuh gad t' wuh lo'uk nuf nam-tor vesht. Sasu, il k'puu criminal sasu, has pakik ek' enterprise heh originality. U' tor t'nash-veh sha' pi' practice, ish-veh seems tor nam-tor degenerating vi' wuh agency na' recovering pakik ras-tukh hish heh giving na'shikh tor nu'ri t'sai s' boarding-shi'oren. I nah-tor ik i ma estuhl lanet na' kim-shah, however. Nash pitoh i had nash asal ulidar t'nash-veh ris-sfek, i fancy. Telv-tor ish-veh!" au tossed wuh crumpled nuhm mes' tor me. Ish-veh vesh' dated s' montague shi fi-tor wuh preceding khru, heh sahr-tor thus: "tal-kam mr. Holmes, i am maut anxious tor consult du u' tor whether i dang il dang ri nar-tor wuh situation if has vesh' nufau tor me u' governess. I dungau vutau na' ulef-vesht lehkuh tor-morrow kuv i tor ri inconvenience du. Ish-veh faithfully, "mu'gahv-kur shi'ka'ree." "tor du fai-tor wuh nu'ri t'sai?" i ya'akash. "ri i." "ish-veh nam-tor ulef-vesht lehkuh i'." "ha, heh i ma rai vet ik nam-tor ish-veh mokov." "ish-veh lau da-tor si' tor nam-tor t' weht eku'ko do du nah-tor. Du vokau ik wuh tek'ik t' wuh pla-kur carbuncle, if saudau tor nam-tor wuh mere whim palikauk, storik vi' wuh serious investigation. Ish-veh lau nam-tor ni svi' nash nuf, isha." "muhl, kal-tor etek rok ni. Tonk'peh etwel vet-tor dungi maut ak nam-tor kilau, na' la', vita i am mau mistaken, nam-tor wuh person svi' deshker." u' au stariben wuh svep tu'ash heh wuh nu'ri t'sai svi-tor wuh tvi-shal. She vesh' plainly tonk'peh neatly sai-vel-tor, k' wuh ugelik, sahris limuk, freckled spo' wuh plover's yu-mur, heh k' wuh brax manner t' wuh kosu vi has had ish-veh sha' yut tor tor svi' wuh panu. "du dungi tobeg t'nash-veh troubling du, i am sure, " leralmin-tor she, u' t'nash-veh besu she-tor tor na'shau ish-veh, "tonk'peh i ma had wuh maut flekh veshtaya, heh u' i ma rai mekhlar il relations t' sovek wihfelau s' ik i kupi ya'akash na'shikh, i nahp ik sos'eh du would nam-tor ves hiyet tor var-tor me ra i dang tor." "pray nem-tor wuh ku-san, din-tor shi'ka'ree. I dungau nam-tor kunli tor tor sovek-vel ik i mokuhlek tor dvin-tor du." kupi gla-tor nash-veh ik holmes vesh' favourably impressed k' wuh manner heh starun t' ish-veh uzh client. Au glazhau ish-veh abru' svi' ish-veh searching fashion, heh yi tertitau himself, k' ish-veh lids tevan-tor heh ish-veh ozh-um teretuhr, tor shroi tor ish-veh var. "i ma vesh' wuh governess na' kaukuh tevun, " leralmin-tor she, "svi' wuh skan t' shal-lan spence munro, tonk'peh dahkuh tevun-krus ago wuh shal-lan poprah wuh latva na' halifax, svi' thorsh-yel scotia, heh nem-tor ish-veh kanu abru' tor america k' ish-veh, ni ik i afer-tor myself rik' wuh situation. I advertised, heh i kilko-tor raf-kuvik, tonk'peh rik' navun. Na' kim-shah wuh pi' donku if i had korsau began tor sahr-tor pen, heh i vesh' na' t'nash-veh wit's shaht u' tor ra i dang tor. "tra' nam-tor wuh muhl-fainu agency na' governesses svi' wuh tev'rak shaht puvutau westaway's, heh tra' i nam-tor-tor tor vutau pa' wuh'wak wuh wehk gad svi' zek tor gla-tor whether sovek-vel had da-tor abru if lau saikhut me. Westaway vesh' wuh ahm t' wuh afersu t' wuh business, tonk'peh ish-veh nam-tor really khartau k' din-tor stoper. She hayal-tor svi' ish-veh sha' pi' office, heh wuh t'sai vi nam-tor seeking employment bek-tor svi' wuh anteroom, heh nam-tor yi shown svi' veh k' veh, lu she consults ish-veh ledgers heh gla-tor whether she has sovek-vel if would saikhut au. "muhl, lu i puvutau kim-shah wehk gad i vesh' shown vi' wuh pi' office u' tsuri, tonk'peh i afer-tor ik din-tor stoper vesh' ri sa'awek. Wuh prodigiously stout sasu k' wuh maut smiling limuk heh wuh lo'uk ras chin if padukau ne' svi' heshan fi-tor heshan abru' ish-veh drahk hayal-tor na' ish-veh kar-nef k' wuh shif t' bezhun-zaneshu fi' ish-veh han, looking maut earnestly na' wuh t'sai vi svi-tor. U' vesht sarlah nash-veh svi' au mazhiv-kur-tor ved wuh spen-tor svi' ish-veh ku-san heh da-tor sahris tor din-tor stoper. "'ik dungi tor, ' leralmin-tor au; 'i kupi ri ya'akash na' sovek-vel weh-rom. Capital! Capital!' au seemed ved buhlik heh tetau ish-veh el'ru teretuhr svi' wuh danik genial fashion. Au vesh' such wuh kel'o-looking sasu ik ish-veh vesh' ved wuh sanosh tor glazhau na' ish-veh. "'du nam-tor looking na' wuh situation, din-tor?' au ya'akash. "'ha, osu.' "'u' governess?' "'ha, osu.' "'heh ra salary tor du ya'akash?' "'i had 4 wuh tevun-krus svi' t'nash-veh kim-shah shi k' shal-lan spence munro.' "'oh, tut, tut! Sweatingrank sweating!' au maf-tor, throwing ish-veh thelik el'ru si' vi' wuh sov spo' wuh sasu vi nam-tor svi' wuh boiling shaukaush. 'uf kupi sovek-veh nufai ni pitiful wuh hau-ov tor wuh t'sai k' such attractions heh accomplishments?' "'t'nash-veh accomplishments, osu, lau nam-tor lehkuh tor du glenonau, ' leralmin-tor i. 'wuh pi' french, wuh pi' german, ralash-tanaf, heh bestan' "'tut, tut!' au maf-tor. 'nash nam-tor ek' ved be' wuh deshker. Wuh sfek nam-tor, ma du il ma du ri wuh kuvish heh deportment t' wuh t'sai? Tra' ish-veh nam-tor svi' wuh nutshell. Kuv du ma ri, du nam-tor ri fitted na' wuh rearing t' wuh kan vi lau ein gad mavau wuh considerable krus svi' wuh vesht-var t' wuh shasol. Tonk'peh kuv du ma, po, yi, uf kupi sovek gentleman ya'akash du tor condescend tor nar-tor sovek-vel ne' wuh rehkuh khlop? Ish-veh salary k' me, madam, would palikau na' 100 wuh tevun.' "du lau glenonau, mr. Holmes, ik tor me, destitute u' i vesh', such wuh nufai seemed siyah nuh' rom tor nam-tor yeht. Wuh gentleman, however, seeing sos'eh wuh glazhau t' incredulity fi-tor t'nash-veh limuk, tu'ash wuh abru'lik-dunap heh nem-tor si' wuh pitoh. "'ish-veh nam-tor isha t'nash-veh custom, ' leralmin-tor au, smiling svi' wuh danik vaksurik fashion abi' ish-veh bezhun vesh' aishan dahkuh pi' shining slits svi' wuh wan-kur creases t' ish-veh limuk, 'tor storilaya tor t'nash-veh nu'ri t'sai ulef ish-veh salary beforehand, ni ik au lau ragel-tor sovek pi' kodona t' ish-veh halovaya heh ish-veh wardrobe.' "ish-veh seemed tor me ik i had worla ragel-tor ni sem-rik heh ni thoughtful wuh sasu. U' i vesh' already svi' sa'akh tor t'nash-veh tradesmen, wuh storilaya vesh' wuh lo'uk convenience, heh wi tra' vesh' vel unnatural pa' wuh bosh transaction if tor me istaya tor fai-tor wuh pi' weht fa' i ved committed myself. "'sos ya'akash wilat du ha-tor, osu?' leralmin-tor i. "'hampshire. Sem-rik-tor rural shi. Wuh khaf-tukh beeches, kaukuh miles fi' wuh irak vla t' winchester. Ish-veh nam-tor wuh danik lovely shasol, t'nash-veh tal-kam nu'ri t'sai, heh wuh dearest hinek shasol-kelek.' "'heh t'nash-veh gu-vam, osu? I dang nam-tor glad tor fai-tor ra au would nam-tor.' "'veh childone tal-kam pi' romper aishan shehkuh tevun hinek. Oh, kuv du kupi gla-tor ish-veh killing cockroaches k' wuh slipper! Smack! Smack! Smack! Rehkuh hal-tor fa' du kupi wink!' au gal-tor pla' svi' ish-veh ku-san heh abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor ish-veh bezhun vi' ish-veh patam va'ashiv. "i vesh' wuh pi' startled na' wuh malat t' wuh kan's amusement, tonk'peh wuh sa-mekh's laughter tor me nah-tor ik sos'eh au vesh' joking. "'t'nash-veh lad gu-vam, yi, ' i ya'akash, 'nam-tor tor nem-tor falun t' wuh single kan?' "'rai, rai, ri wuh lad, ri wuh lad, t'nash-veh tal-kam nu'ri t'sai, ' au maf-tor. 'ish-veh gu-vam would nam-tor, u' i am sure ish-veh rom kash-ral would suggest, tor obey sovek pi' khartau t'nash-veh ko-telsu lau mazhiv-kur-tor, tanilau kwon-hau-ov ik au vesh' such khartau u' wuh t'sai lau k' propriety obey. Gla-tor du rai rihag'es, heh?' "'i dang nam-tor kunli tor tor myself useful.' "'ved ni. Svi' sai-vel i', na' li-fal. Etek nam-tor faddy sutra, du knowfaddy tonk'peh ves-hearted. Kuv du vesh' ya'akash sai-vel-tor sovek sai-vel if etek lau mazhiv-kur-tor du, du would ri vel tor etwel pi' whim. Heh?' "'rai, ' leralmin-tor i, considerably astonished na' ish-veh zhit. "'il tor hayal-tor la', il hayal-tor tra', ik would ri nam-tor offensive tor du?' "'oh, rai.' "'il tor tresahk ish-veh isachya ved pen fa' sarlah du tor etek?' "i kupi hardly dva-tor t'nash-veh kaluk. U' du lau glantau, mr. Holmes, t'nash-veh isachya nam-tor somewhat luxuriant, heh t' wuh rather peculiar tint t' chestnut. Ish-veh has vesh' panah-tor tanafluk. I kupi ri sahr-tor t' sacrificing ish-veh svi' nash offhand fashion. "'i am kwes ik ik nam-tor ved impossible, ' leralmin-tor i. Au had vesh' watching me eagerly s' ish-veh pi' bezhun, heh kupi gla-tor nash-veh wuh duv be' dvun abru' ish-veh limuk u' i stariben. "'i am kwes ik ish-veh nam-tor ved bolayatik, ' leralmin-tor au. 'ish-veh nam-tor wuh pi' fancy t' t'nash-veh ko-telsu's, heh t'sai' fancies, du fai-tor, madam, t'sai' fancies bolau nam-tor consulted. Heh ni du skil-tor't tresahk ish-veh isachya?' "'rai, osu, i really kupi ri, ' i kilko-tor firmly. "'ah, maut muhl; yi ik ved settles wuh tukh. Ish-veh nam-tor wuh pity, fai'ei svi' vath respects du would really ma ovsoh maut nicely. Svi' ik nuf, din-tor stoper, i had buhfik inspect wuh zamu weht t' ish-veh nu'ri t'sai.' "wuh manageress had hayal-tor ek' nash du' toranik k' ish-veh dun rik' wuh zhit tor either t' etek, tonk'peh she glanced na' me i' k' ni mau il'nai'ga fi-tor ish-veh limuk ik i kupi ri gol'nev suspecting ik she had pakik wuh handsome kadvin k'fai t'nash-veh refusal. "'tor du aitlun ish-veh ahm tor nam-tor potau fi-tor wuh dunap?' she ya'akash. "'kuv du sanoi, din-tor stoper.' "'muhl, really, ish-veh seems rather nam-tor-fam, opi' du klee'fah wuh danik marom nufau svi' nash fashion, ' leralmin-tor she sharply. 'du mokuhlek hardly gish etek tor pidesh ourselves tor talal wuh'ashiv such sharu na' du. Rom-gad tor du, din-tor shi'ka'ree.' she kwul-tor wuh kep fi-tor wuh pasu, heh i vesh' shown si' k' wuh thalv. "muhl, mr. Holmes, lu i zaprah tor t'nash-veh lodgings heh afer-tor pi' hiyet svi' wuh cupboard, heh dahkuh il rehkuh dun fi-tor wuh pasu, i began tor ya'akash myself whether i had ri ovsoh wuh maut duhik vel. Po' ek', kuv aifa sutra had flekh fads heh gishu obedience fi' wuh danik wehtsuri tukh, au vesh' k'puu pok tor vlitau na' ish-veh risvitan'es. Maut zamu governesses svi' england nam-tor getting 100 wuh tevun. Isha, ra nam-tor-tor vesh' t'nash-veh isachya tor me? Wehk sutra nam-tor improved k' sai-vel-tor ish-veh pen heh sos'eh i dang nam-tor among wuh su'etek. Thurai gad i vesh' vul-tor tor nah-tor ik i had tor wuh lafosh, heh k' wuh gad po' i vesh' sure t' ish-veh. I had siyah overcome t'nash-veh pride ni irak u' tor hal-tor pla' tor wuh agency heh inquire whether wuh shi vesh' fam dvun tu'ash lu i poprah nash nuhm s' wuh gentleman himself. I ma ish-veh la' heh i dungi telv-tor ish-veh tor du: "'wuh khaf-tukh beeches, be' winchester. "'tal-kam din-tor shi'ka'ree, din-tor stoper has maut kindly putan-tor me ish-veh shi'yavekh, heh i kitau s' la' tor ya'akash du whether du ma reconsidered ish-veh klopaya. T'nash-veh ko-telsu nam-tor maut anxious ik du dang sarlah, na' she has vesh' mau skamau k' t'nash-veh kethelvaya t' du. Etek nam-tor willing tor mazhiv-kur-tor 30 wuh yonuk, il 120 wuh tevun, ni u' tor recompense du na' sovek pi' inconvenience if etwel fads lau aishan du. Au nam-tor ri maut exacting, po' ek'. T'nash-veh ko-telsu nam-tor tishau t' wuh particular duvek t' rafik pla-kur heh would spo' du sai-vel-tor such wuh sai-vel indoors svi' wuh asal. Du bolaya ri, however, hal-tor tor wuh kodona t' purchasing veh, u' etek ma veh t' t'nash-veh tal-kam ko-fu alice (i' svi' philadelphia), if would, i dang nah-tor, nunau du maut muhl. Yi, u' tor sitting la' il tra', il tzlu'pd yourself svi' sovek manner indicated, ik bolaya aishan du rai inconvenience. U' fudau ish-veh isachya, ish-veh nam-tor rai vet wuh pity, wa' u' i kupi ri gol'nev remarking its vaksur du' etwel pen interview, tonk'peh i am kwes ik i bolau hafau pesik fi-tor nash sfek, heh i goh rok ik wuh increased salary lau recompense du na' wuh pak. Ish-veh gu-vam, u' irak u' wuh kan nam-tor concerned, nam-tor maut ta'hal. I' tor ar'kadan tor sarlah, heh i dungau ragel-tor du k' wuh dog-hal na' winchester. Kal-tor me fai-tor ish-veh ranau. Ish-veh faithfully, "'jephro rucastle.' "ik nam-tor wuh nuhm if i ma aishan poprah, mr. Holmes, heh t'nash-veh kashek nam-tor tor abru ik i dungi nar-tor ish-veh. I nahp, however, ik fa' taking wuh kim-shah ash i dang spo' tor nekhau wuh bosh tukh tor ish-veh consideration." "muhl, din-tor shi'ka'ree, kuv ish-veh kashek nam-tor tor abru, ik settles wuh deshker, " leralmin-tor holmes, smiling. "tonk'peh du would ri na'shikhau me tor klee'fah?" "i confess ik ish-veh nam-tor ri wuh situation if i dang spo' tor gla-tor wuh ko-kai t' t'nash-veh apply na'." "ra nam-tor wuh meaning t' ish-veh ek', mr. Holmes?" "ah, i ma rai faik. I fam yehat var-tor. Sos'eh du ma yourself shidau ein opinion?" "muhl, tra' seems tor me tor nam-tor goh veh tor-yehat kilkaya. Mr. Rucastle seemed tor nam-tor wuh maut ves, rom-natured sasu. Nam-tor ish-veh ri tor-yehat ik ish-veh ko-telsu nam-tor wuh lunatic, ik au aitlu tor potau wuh tukh hizhuk na' pthak she dang nam-tor taken tor wuh asylum, heh ik au humours ish-veh fancies svi' kanok yut svi' zek tor prevent wuh outbreak?" "ik nam-tor wuh tor-yehat solutionin kla-min, u' tukh lamok, ish-veh nam-tor wuh danik yesik veh. Tonk'peh svi' sovek nuf ish-veh tor ri seem tor nam-tor wuh nice household na' wuh nu'ri t'sai." "tonk'peh wuh donku, mr. Holmes, wuh donku!" "muhl, ha, veling wuh vlitau nam-tor goodtoo rom. Ik nam-tor ra tor me uneasy. Po dang au mazhiv-kur-tor du 120 wuh tevun, lu au kupi ma ish-veh pick na' 40? Tra' bolau nam-tor ein karik utvau za'." "i nahp ik kuv i var-tor du wuh circumstances du would ken-tor afterwards kuv i aitlu ish-veh gol'nev. I dang olau ni mau stronger kuv i olau ik du vesh' na' wuh pla' t' me." "oh, du lau lesh ik olaya maf k' du. I assure du ik ish-veh pi' wat ugau tor nam-tor wuh danik eku'ki if has sarlah t'nash-veh yut na' ein tevun-krus. Tra' nam-tor vel distinctly dunap pa' ein t' wuh features. Kuv du dang talal yourself svi' vet il svi' tehvar" "tehvar! Ra tehvar tor du fa-glan-tor?" holmes hutau ish-veh patam gravely. "ish-veh would cease tor nam-tor wuh tehvar kuv etek kupi mesprah ish-veh, " leralmin-tor au. "tonk'peh na' sovek wak, gad il mu-yor, wuh telegram would katau me ne' tor ish-veh gol'nev." "ik nam-tor hiyet." she she-tor brax s' ish-veh ku-san k' wuh anxiety ek' swept s' ish-veh limuk. "i dungau hal-tor ne' tor hampshire ved hagik svi' t'nash-veh kashek i'. I dungau kitau tor mr. "k'puu, " leralmin-tor i u' etek puzhu-tor ish-veh sahris, pesik ash-tor descending wuh kaiden, "she seems tor nam-tor wuh nu'ri t'sai vi nam-tor maut muhl kup tor nem-tor tun t' herself." "heh she would bolaya tor nam-tor, " leralmin-tor holmes gravely. "i am mau mistaken kuv etek ri tor zhu-tor s' ish-veh fa' wehk gad nam-tor vesht." ish-veh vesh' ri maut wu fa' t'nash-veh t'hy'la's prediction vesh' fulfilled. Wuh fortnight went k', du' if i frequently afer-tor t'nash-veh nahp turning svi' ish-veh kharat heh wondering ra flekh vla-alley t' komihn veshtaya nash lonely kosu had fam-kelek-tor vi'. Wuh ritsuri salary, wuh curious nosh, wuh ta'hal gu-vam, ek' sfekau tor vel ritsuri, hi whether wuh fad il wuh besau, il whether wuh sasu vesh' wuh philanthropist il wuh villain, ish-veh vesh' ved mesakh t'nash-veh tepul tor satalau. U' tor holmes, i glantau ik au hayal-tor frequently na' ulef wuh wadan fi' shaht, k' knitted meix'tem heh wuh abstracted sov, tonk'peh au swept wuh tukh maf k' wuh pral t' ish-veh el'ru lu i mentioned ish-veh. "faik! Faik! Faik!" au maf-tor impatiently. "i mokuhlek't tor dok rik' krizhiv." heh wi au would kwon-hau-ov salan abru k' muttering ik rai ko-kai t' ish-veh dang ek'wak ma nar-tor such wuh situation. Wuh telegram if etek eventually poprah sarlah tab-ma veh mu-yor aishan u' i vesh' thinking t' turning svi' heh holmes vesh' settling ne' tor veh t' eifa ek'-mu-yor meli-tukh kla-hil-tor if au frequently indulged svi', lu i would trasha ish-veh stooping abru' wuh retort heh wuh nisan-tube na' mu-yor heh talal ish-veh svi' wuh ka shul lu vesht sarlah nash-veh ne' tor asal-yem svi' wuh asal. "dungi sarlah du k' me?" ya'akash holmes, glancing abru. "i dang istaya tor." "aishan glazhau ish-veh abru, yi." "tra' nam-tor wuh ranau na' ulef-vesht naukuh, " leralmin-tor i, glancing abru' t'nash-veh bradshaw. "ish-veh nam-tor due na' winchester na' 11: 30." "ik dungi tor maut nicely. Yi sos'eh i had weh-rom postpone t'nash-veh nisaya t' wuh nen-nalesh-tukh, u' etek lau bolaya tor nam-tor na' etwel buhfik svi' wuh asal." k' leh-wun o'wak-vel wuh thurai gad etek vesh' muhl fi-tor etwel yut tor wuh hinek eingelsu capital. Holmes had vesh' visolektau svi' wuh asal dun ek' wuh yut ne', tonk'peh po' etek had be' dvun-tor wuh hampshire ek'zehl au threw au ne' heh began tor krol-tor wuh scenery. Ish-veh vesh' wuh tangu sikar gad, wuh ha'pla-kur igen, flecked k' pi' fleecy wan-kur wan drifting mes' s' tev'rak tor she'rak. Wuh yel vesh' shining maut brightly, heh wi tra' vesh' wuh exhilarating nip svi' wuh sov, if eku wuh rihk tor wuh sasu's tepul. Ek' abru' wuh countryside, maf tor wuh rolling kunel pa' aldershot, wuh pi' yon-kur heh zhai-kur kamu t' wuh uroshal-steadings peeped si' s' svi' wuh ha'yar-kur t' wuh uzh motra. "nam-tor au ri sluk heh vaksurik?" i maf-tor k' ek' wuh buhl'es t' wuh sasu sluk s' wuh fogs t' leipausu yut. Tonk'peh holmes hutau ish-veh patam gravely. "tor du fai-tor, watson, " leralmin-tor au, "ik ish-veh nam-tor veh t' wuh curses t' wuh kashek k' wuh da-tor spo' t'nash-veh ik i bolau glazhau na' kanok-vei k' dzhinaya tor t'nash-veh sha' special subject. Du glazhau na' aifa scattered kelek, heh du nam-tor impressed k' ish-veh vaksur. I glazhau na' au, heh wuh goh nahp if sarlah tor me nam-tor wuh olaya t' ish-veh isolation heh t' wuh impunity k' if tr'y'kak lau nam-tor committed tra'." "rom heavens!" i maf-tor. "vi would katravahsu tr'y'kak k' aifa tal-kam hinek homesteads?" "au kwon-hau-ov boshaya me k' wuh ac'ruth horror. Ish-veh nam-tor t'nash-veh dva, watson, founded fi-tor t'nash-veh veshtaya, ik wuh lowest heh vilest alleys svi' london ri tor la' wuh weht dreadful vipladau t' sin do tor wuh smiling heh vaksurik countryside." "du horrify me!" "tonk'peh wuh utvau nam-tor maut obvious. Wuh ne'hish t' tsuri opinion mokuhlek tor svi' wuh kahr ra wuh tor-gav fam yehat accomplish. Tra' nam-tor rai lane ni vile ik wuh shei t' wuh tortured kan, il wuh thud t' wuh drunkard's salur, tor ri beget sympathy heh indignation among wuh behsu, heh yi wuh bosh machinery t' yeht-gav nam-tor ek'wak ni ikap-tor ik wuh zhit t' complaint mokuhlek eku ish-veh going, heh tra' nam-tor tonk'peh wuh ash svi' wuh tr'y'kak heh wuh kif. Tonk'peh glazhau na' aifa lonely kelek, tik svi' its sha' vunai, boshau na' wuh danik krus k' ri donku-tor ignorant sular vi fai-tor pi' t' wuh tor-gav. Nah-tor t' wuh deeds t' hellish cruelty, wuh ipik wickedness if lau hal-tor fi', tevun svi', tevun si', svi' such shitau, heh rim wuh wiser. Had nash t'sai vi appeals tor etek na' gol'nev hal-tor tor ha-tor svi' winchester, i dang worla ma had wuh pthak na' ish-veh. Ish-veh nam-tor wuh kaukuh miles t' shasol if tor wuh tehvar. Fam dvun, ish-veh nam-tor pa'shik ik she nam-tor ri personally threatened." "rai. Kuv she mokuhlek sarlah tor winchester tor ragel-tor etek she mokuhlek prah maf." "ved ni. She has ish-veh el'es." "ra mokuhlek nam-tor wuh tukh, yi? Mokuhlek du suggest rai danaya?" "i ma devised stehkuh dahshauk danaya, tik t' if would wein wuh kla-min u' irak u' etek fai-tor au. Tonk'peh if t' aifa nam-tor yeht mokuhlek goh nam-tor satalau k' wuh sluk ro'fori if etek dungau rai vet talal waiting na' etek. Muhl, tra' nam-tor wuh kispek t' wuh cathedral, heh etek dungau ak oren-tor ek' ik din-tor shi'ka'ree has tor var-tor." wuh nesh-kur kushel nam-tor wuh ha-shal t' repute svi' wuh pid yut, na' rai ir s' wuh wurzel, heh tra' etek afer-tor wuh nu'ri t'sai waiting na' etek. She had engaged wuh sitting-tvi-shal, heh etwel khi-gad-yem awaited etek fi-tor wuh pasu. "i am ni delighted ik du ma sarlah, " she leralmin-tor earnestly. "ish-veh nam-tor ni maut ves t' du fi'; tonk'peh indeed i ri tor fai-tor ra i dang tor. Ish-veh na'shikh dungi nam-tor altogether invaluable tor me." "pray var-tor etek ra has pavesh-tor tor du." "i dungi tor ni, heh i bolau nam-tor sahris, na' i ma ugau mr. Rucastle tor nam-tor pla' fa' rehkuh. I prah ish-veh trasha tor sarlah vi' kahr nash asal, hi au pi' fai-tor na' ra lof." "kal-tor etek ma kanok-vei svi' its due zek." holmes kwit ish-veh wu wonil mal si' na' wuh yon heh tertitau himself tor shroi. "svi' wuh wuh'rak shi, i lau leralmin ik i ma ragel-tor, fi' wuh bosh, k' rai actual has-bosh-skasaya s' mr. Heh mrs. Rucastle. Ish-veh nam-tor goh rom tor au tor leralmin ik. Tonk'peh i fam yehat ken-tor au, heh i am ri hagik svi' t'nash-veh kashek pa' au." "ra mokuhlek du ri ken-tor?" "ish-veh utvau na' ish-veh spa-tor. Tonk'peh du dungau ma ish-veh ek' aishan u' ish-veh paresh-tor. Lu vesht sarlah nash-veh ne', mr. Rucastle ragel-tor me la' heh drove me svi' ish-veh dog-hal tor wuh khaf-tukh beeches. Ish-veh nam-tor, u' au leralmin-tor, beautifully situated, tonk'peh ish-veh nam-tor ri vaksurik svi' itself, na' ish-veh nam-tor wuh suk keh-vla vihpan t' wuh kelek, whitewashed, tonk'peh ek' kurau heh wesh-tor k' damp heh rasahkos igen-va. Tra' nam-tor solektra pauk ish-veh, lapan fi' rehkuh vla, heh fi' wuh fourth wuh vunai if vul ne' tor wuh southampton pid fau-yut, if curves vesht pa' wuh hundred ker s' wuh khom svep. Nash solektra svi' khom t' wuh kelek, tonk'peh wuh lapan ek' pauk nam-tor krus t' s'haile southerton's korsau. Wuh clump t' khaf-tukh beeches iyi svi' khom t' wuh tvur svep has putan-tor its ahm tor wuh shi. "i vesh' driven abru' k' t'nash-veh employer, vi vesh' u' amiable u' ek'wak, heh vesh' puragtau k' ish-veh ik khru tor ish-veh ko-telsu heh wuh kan. Tra' vesh' rai yeht'es, mr. Holmes, svi' wuh conjecture if seemed tor etek tor nam-tor yesik svi' ish-veh tvi-shal na' leipausu yut. Mrs. Rucastle nam-tor ri mad. I afer-tor ish-veh tor nam-tor wuh ralash-fam, spoh-limuk-tor kosu, mau younger do ish-veh sa-telsu, ri weht do reh-leh, i dang nah-tor, du' au mokuhlek hardly nam-tor lehkuh tor keh-leh-kaukuh. S' ish-veh conversation i ma hoknau ik au ma vesh' telik pa' stehkuh tevun, ik au vesh' wuh kir'an, heh ik ish-veh goh kan k' wuh wuh'rak ko-telsu vesh' wuh ko-fu vi has hal-tor tor philadelphia. Mr. Rucastle var-tor me svi' awek ik wuh utvau po she had losrak au vesh' ik she had wuh unreasoning aversion tor ish-veh stepmother. U' wuh ko-fu kupi ri ma vesh' lehkuh tor dah-leh, i mokuhlek ved glenonau ik ish-veh shul bolau ma vesh' uncomfortable k' ish-veh sa-mekh's nu'ri ko-telsu. "mrs. Rucastle seemed tor me tor nam-tor colourless svi' kashek u' muhl u' svi' feature. She impressed me neither favourably il wuh reverse. She vesh' wuh nonentity. Ish-veh vesh' hagik tor gla-tor ik she vesh' passionately vaikau fi' tor ish-veh sa-telsu heh tor ish-veh pi' sa-fu. Ish-veh zhai-kur bezhun czar-tor continually s' veh tor wuh vath, noting kanok pi' aitlun heh forestalling ish-veh kuv tor-yehat. Au vesh' ves tor ish-veh isha svi' ish-veh bluff, boisterous fashion, heh fi' wuh bosh au seemed tor nam-tor wuh kunli couple. Heh wi she had ein tsat sorrow, nash kosu. She would k'ashiv nam-tor pakik svi' glu nahp, k' wuh saddest glazhau fi-tor ish-veh limuk. Weht do wuh'wak i ma ak'wikmun ish-veh svi' bezhun-masu. I ma nahp sometimes ik ish-veh vesh' wuh disposition t' ish-veh kan if rasathau fi-tor ish-veh kashek, na' i ma worla ragel-tor ni utterly spoiled heh ni has-bosh-natured wuh pi' creature. Au nam-tor pi' na' ish-veh ya'shakhuv, k' wuh patam if nam-tor ved disproportionately suk. Ish-veh bosh ha'kiv saudau tor nam-tor spent svi' wuh alternation svi' savage nunau t' shaukaush heh gloomy tvi-wak t' sulking. Giving kusut tor sovek creature weaker do himself seems tor nam-tor ish-veh veh idea t' amusement, heh au gluvau ved remarkable talent svi' planning wuh kum t' aushfa, pi' kushel, heh ravot. Tonk'peh i would rather ri variben pa' wuh creature, mr. Holmes, heh, indeed, au has pi' tor tor k' t'nash-veh var." "i am glad t' ek' details, " remarked t'nash-veh t'hy'la, "whether au seem tor du tor nam-tor relevant il ri." "i dungau ar'kadan ri tor din-tor sovek-vel t' importance. Wuh veh unpleasant vel pa' wuh kelek, if kwul-tor me na' wuh'wak, vesh' wuh appearance heh spa-tor t' wuh dvinsu. Tra' nam-tor goh dahkuh, wuh sasu heh ish-veh ko-telsu. Toller, na' ik nam-tor ish-veh ahm, nam-tor wuh rough, uncouth sasu, k' grizzled isachya heh whiskers, heh wuh perpetual fnish-tor t' mon. Dah'wak opi' i ma vesh' k' au au has vesh' ved mon-tor, heh wi mr. Rucastle seemed tor nem-tor rai beglanau t' ish-veh. Ish-veh ko-telsu nam-tor wuh maut ha-vol heh karik kosu k' wuh sfith limuk, u' ralash-fam u' mrs. Rucastle heh mau lehkuh amiable. Au nam-tor wuh danik unpleasant couple, tonk'peh fortunately i spend danik t' t'nash-veh wak svi' wuh nursery heh t'nash-veh sha' tvi-shal, if nam-tor nam-tor' tik vath svi' veh teruk t' wuh kelek. "na' dahkuh gad po' t'nash-veh lashan na' wuh khaf-tukh beeches t'nash-veh ha'kiv vesh' maut hizhuk; fi' wuh wuh, mrs. Rucastle sarlah ne' aishan po' asal-yem heh zhal-tor vel tor ish-veh sa-telsu. "'oh, ha, ' leralmin-tor au, turning tor me, 'etek nam-tor maut mau obliged tor du, din-tor shi'ka'ree, na' tevan-tor svi' k' etwel whims ni irak u' tor tresahk ish-veh isachya. I assure du ik ish-veh has ri detracted svi' wuh tiniest iota s' ish-veh appearance. Etek dungau i' gla-tor uf wuh rafik-pla-kur sai-vel dungi shetau du. Du dungi talal ish-veh laid si' fi-tor wuh sar-tak svi' ish-veh tvi-shal, heh kuv du would nam-tor ni rom u' tor shitau ish-veh fi' etek dang fi' nam-tor extremely obliged.' "wuh sai-vel if i afer-tor waiting na' me vesh' t' wuh peculiar duvek t' pla-kur. Ish-veh vesh' t' marom tukh, wuh wihfelau t' ha'mazhiv-kur, tonk'peh ish-veh spitau unmistakable glat t' having vesh' worn fa'. Ish-veh kupi ri ma vesh' wuh weh-rom nunau kuv i had vesh' thon-tor na' ish-veh. Fi' mr. Heh mrs. Rucastle sagluvau wuh delight na' wuh glazhau t' ish-veh, if seemed ved exaggerated svi' its vehemence. Au vesh' waiting na' me svi' wuh bestan-tvi-shal, if nam-tor wuh maut suk tvi-shal, stretching bi' wuh entire khom t' wuh kelek, k' rehkuh wu krani reaching ne' tor wuh lan-tol. Wuh ku-san had vesh' shitau beyik wuh central krani, k' its pla' da-tor na' ish-veh. Svi' nash i vesh' ya'akash tor hayal-tor, heh yi mr. Rucastle, walking abru heh ne' fi' wuh vath vla t' wuh tvi-shal, began tor var-tor me wuh weizehl t' wuh funniest var ik i ma ek'wak shroi tor. Du fam yehat glenonau uf comical au vesh', heh i abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor abi' i vesh' ved weary. Mrs. Rucastle, however, vi has evidently rai kash-ral t' humour, worla ni mau u' abru'teruklar-ru'lut, tonk'peh hayal-tor k' ish-veh el'ru svi' ish-veh lap, heh wuh maf, anxious glazhau fi-tor ish-veh limuk. Po' wuh wadan il ni, mr. Rucastle suddenly remarked ik ish-veh vesh' wak tor palikau wuh gu-vam t' wuh gad, heh ik i lau rubah t'nash-veh sai-vel heh hal-tor tor pi' edward svi' wuh nursery. "dahkuh gad later nash ka performance vesh' hal-tor k'fai ne' exactly kahwa circumstances. Va'ashiv i rubai t'nash-veh sai-vel, va'ashiv i hayal-tor svi' wuh krani, heh va'ashiv i abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor maut heartily na' wuh funny var t' if t'nash-veh employer had wuh immense répertoire, heh if au var-tor inimitably. Yi au handed me wuh kin-kur-backed dunap, heh dvun-tor t'nash-veh ku-san wuh pi' sideways, ik t'nash-veh sha' duv lau ri tevan fi-tor wuh thalv, au eit'jae me tor telv-tor aloud tor ish-veh. I telv-tor na' pa' lehkuh minutes, palikaya svi' wuh khaf-spol t' wuh chapter, heh yi suddenly, svi' wuh svitan t' wuh zhit-bal, au ordered me tor cease heh tor rubah t'nash-veh sai-vel. "du mokuhlek easily glenonau, mr. Holmes, uf curious i became u' tor ra wuh meaning t' nash wehtsuri performance kupi possibly nam-tor. Au vesh' kwon-hau-ov maut tun-bosh, i glantau, tor da-tor t'nash-veh limuk maf s' wuh krani, ni ik i became consumed k' wuh aitlun tor gla-tor ra vesh' going fi' za' t'nash-veh pla'. Palikauk ish-veh seemed tor nam-tor impossible, tonk'peh i ak devised wuh tvai. T'nash-veh el'ru-haulat had vesh' pushau, ni wuh kunli nahp seized me, heh i ip-sut wuh krus t' wuh makh svi' t'nash-veh handkerchief. Fi' wuh thurai occasion, svi' wuh midst t' t'nash-veh laughter, i shitau t'nash-veh handkerchief abru tor t'nash-veh bezhun, heh vesh' kup k' wuh pi' management tor gla-tor ek' ik tra' vesh' za' me. I confess ik i vesh' disappointed. Tra' vesh' nothing. K'puu ik vesh' t'nash-veh wuh'rak impression. Na' wuh dahr glance, however, i pakashogau ik tra' vesh' wuh sasu standing svi' wuh southampton fau-yut, wuh pi' bearded sasu svi' wuh zhai-kur saikhut, vi seemed tor nam-tor looking svi' t'nash-veh kharat. Wuh fau-yut nam-tor wuh yauluhk yut, heh tra' nam-tor usually sutra tra'. Nash sasu, however, vesh' leaning tehnat wuh railings if bordered etwel vunai heh vesh' looking earnestly abru. I ne-tor t'nash-veh handkerchief heh glanced na' mrs. Rucastle tor talal ish-veh bezhun teslau fi-tor me k' wuh danik searching gaze. She leralmin-tor nothing, tonk'peh i am convinced ik she had divined ik i had wuh haulat svi' t'nash-veh el'ru heh had gla-tor ra vesh' za' me. She she-tor na' wuh'wak. "'jephro, ' leralmin-tor she, 'tra' nam-tor wuh impertinent katravahsu fi-tor wuh fau-yut tra' vi nantau abru na' din-tor shi'ka'ree.' "'rai t'hy'la t' ish-veh, din-tor shi'ka'ree?' au ya'akash. "'rai, i fai-tor kling svi' aifa krus.' "'tal-kam me! Uf maut impertinent! Kindly da-tor pauk heh dvunel tor ish-veh tor hal-tor maf.' "'surely ish-veh would nam-tor weh-rom tor nem-tor rai beglanau.' "'rai, rai, etek dang ma ish-veh loitering la' kwon-hau-ov. Kindly da-tor pauk heh pral ish-veh maf spo' ik.' "i did u' i vesh' var-tor, heh na' wuh ka instant mrs. Rucastle drew ne' wuh glan-fam. Ik vesh' wuh wehk gad ago, heh s' ik wak i ma ri hayal-tor va'ashiv svi' wuh krani, il ma i worn wuh pla-kur sai-vel, il gla-tor wuh sasu svi' wuh fau-yut." "pray fator, " leralmin-tor holmes. "ish-veh narrative ugau tor nam-tor wuh danik eku'ki veh." "du dungi talal ish-veh rather satersau, i pthak, heh tra' lau skan-tor tor nam-tor pi' relation svi' wuh natya incidents t' if i stariben. Fi' wuh maut wuh'rak gad ik i vesh' na' wuh khaf-tukh beeches, mr. Rucastle nem-tor me tor wuh pi' outhouse if lam-tor be' wuh af'tum svep. U' etek betau ish-veh i puzhu-tor wuh nasik rattling t' wuh naf-elakh, heh wuh ralash u' t' wuh suk aushfa dvun-tor pa'. "'glazhau svi' la'!' leralmin-tor mr. Rucastle, showing me wuh slit svi' dahkuh planks. 'nam-tor au ri wuh vaksur?' "i glazhau k'fai heh vesh' d'wonil t' dahkuh glowing bezhun, heh t' wuh vague khlop huddled abru svi' wuh mu'khlup'es. "'ri tor nam-tor koltha, ' leralmin-tor t'nash-veh employer, laughing na' wuh palikaya if i had putan-tor. 'ish-veh's goh carlo, t'nash-veh mastiff. I vutau ish-veh t'nash-veh, tonk'peh really hinek toller, t'nash-veh groom, nam-tor wuh goh sasu vi mokuhlek tor sovek-vel k' ish-veh. Etek yem-tor ish-veh wuh'wak wuh gad, heh ri nuh' mau yi, ni ik au nam-tor kwon-hau-ov u' keen u' mustard. Toller kal-tor ish-veh thal kanok mu-yor, heh oekon gol'nev wuh trespasser ik au ti ish-veh wu-zud fi-tor. Na' goodness' sake ri tor du ek'wak fi' sovek pretext eku ish-veh ash'ya abru' wuh threshold na' mu-yor, na' ish-veh's u' mau u' ish-veh ha'kiv nam-tor don.' "wuh warning vesh' rai idle veh, na' dahkuh mu-yor later i pavesh-tor tor glazhau s' t'nash-veh shi'yuk krani pa' dahkuh o'wak-vel svi' wuh asal. Ish-veh vesh' wuh vaksurik moonlight mu-yor, heh wuh yartra svi' khom t' wuh kelek vesh' silvered abru' heh siyah u' ugelik u' gad. I vesh' standing, rapt svi' wuh peaceful vaksur t' wuh scene, lu i vesh' aware ik vel vesh' dvun-tor ne' wuh duv t' wuh khaf-tukh beeches. U' ish-veh sasarlah vi' wuh moonshine vesht gla-tor nash-veh ra ish-veh vesh'. Ish-veh vesh' wuh masuk'veh dog, u' suk u' wuh vaukh, tawny tinted, k' hanging jowl, nesh-kur muzzle, heh masuk' projecting hinek. Ish-veh lates-tor slowly mes' wuh yartra heh vanished vi' wuh duv fi-tor wuh vath vla. Ik dreadful sentinel satau wuh chill tor t'nash-veh khaf-spol if i ri tor nah-tor ik sovek burglar kupi ma ovsoh. "heh i' i ma wuh maut flekh veshtaya tor var-tor du. I had, u' du fai-tor, tresahk ska' t'nash-veh isachya svi' london, heh i had shitau ish-veh svi' wuh lo'uk pakuv na' wuh lanet t' t'nash-veh lap-fek. Veh khru, po' wuh kan vesh' svi' sar-tak, i began tor amuse myself k' examining wuh furniture t' t'nash-veh tvi-shal heh k' rearranging t'nash-veh sha' pi' vel. Tra' vesh' wuh hinek tuf t' zish-nef svi' wuh tvi-shal, wuh dahkuh upper ones herbosh heh tu'ash, wuh weh-neik veh klacha. I had boshau wuh wuh'rak dahkuh k' t'nash-veh linen, heh u' i had fam dvun mau tor sa'haf maf i vesh' naturally annoyed na' ri having wuh nam-tor-tor t' wuh wuh zish-nef. Ish-veh kwul-tor me ik ish-veh lau ma vesh' terau k' wuh mere oversight, ni i nem-tor si' t'nash-veh bunch t' tal-muv heh ar'kada tor tu'ash ish-veh. Wuh maut wuh'rak tal-muv fitted tor perfection, heh i drew wuh zish-nef tu'ash. Tra' vesh' goh veh vel svi' ish-veh, tonk'peh i am sure ik du would worla guess ra ish-veh vesh'. Ish-veh vesh' t'nash-veh pakuv t' isachya. "i nem-tor ish-veh abru heh linisau ish-veh. Ish-veh vesh' t' wuh ka peculiar tint, heh wuh ka thickness. Tonk'peh yi wuh impossibility t' wuh vel obtruded itself fi-tor me. Uf kupi t'nash-veh isachya ma vesh' klacha svi' wuh zish-nef? K' trembling el'ru i undid t'nash-veh lap-fek, da-tor si' wuh tuhllar, heh drew s' wuh lanet t'nash-veh sha' isachya. I laid wuh dahkuh tresses teretuhr, heh i assure du ik au vesh' ka. Vesh' ish-veh ri wehtsuri? Puzzle u' i would, i kupi tor nothing na' ek' t' ra ish-veh tvai. I fun-tor wuh flekh isachya tor wuh zish-nef, heh i leralmin-tor nothing t' wuh tukh tor wuh rucastles u' i olau ik i had shitau myself svi' wuh riyeht k' sharu wuh zish-nef if au had klacha. "i am naturally observant, u' du lau ma remarked, mr. Holmes, heh i ak had wuh takov rom dotor t' wuh bosh kelek svi' t'nash-veh patam. Tra' vesh' veh rala, however, if saudau ri tor nam-tor inhabited na' ek'. Wuh svep if limuk-tor ik if pufulag-tor vi' wuh ha-shal t' wuh tollers tu'ash vi' nash suite, tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' invariably klacha. Veh gad, however, u' i she-tor wuh stair, i ragel-tor mr. Rucastle coming si' k'fai nash svep, ish-veh tal-muv svi' ish-veh el'ru, heh wuh glazhau fi' ish-veh limuk if tor ish-veh wuh maut natya person tor wuh pauk, jovial sasu tor ik i vesh' accustomed. Ish-veh nak vesh' yon-kur, ish-veh meix'tem vesh' ek' crinkled k' reshan, heh wuh os-khaf-mev lam-tor si' na' ish-veh temples k' shaukaush. Au klacha wuh svep heh hurried vesht me rik' wuh zhit il wuh glazhau. "nash aroused t'nash-veh curiosity, ni lu i went si' na' wuh lates svi' wuh solektra k' t'nash-veh falun, i strolled pauk tor wuh vla s' if i kupi gla-tor wuh krani t' nash krus t' wuh kelek. Tra' vesh' kehkuh t' au svi' wuh zehl, rehkuh t' if vesh' veling kitork, du' wuh fourth vesh' shuttered abru. Au vesh' evidently ek' deserted. U' i strolled abru heh ne', glancing na' au occasionally, mr. Rucastle sasarlah tor me, looking u' merry heh jovial u' ek'wak. "'ah!' leralmin-tor au, 'du bolau ri nah-tor me snertau kuv i be' dvun-tor du rik' wuh zhit, t'nash-veh tal-kam nu'ri t'sai. I vesh' preoccupied k' business tukh.' "i assured ish-veh ik i vesh' ri puthrap-tor. 'k' wuh yut, ' leralmin-tor i, 'du seem ki' ved wuh suite t' spare tvi-shal abru tra', heh veh t' au has wuh fe-wein abru.' "au glazhau ak'wikmun heh, u' ish-veh seemed tor me, wuh pi' startled na' t'nash-veh remark. "'ha'gel-tanaf nam-tor veh t' t'nash-veh hobbies, ' leralmin-tor au. 'i ma tor t'nash-veh gu'gelik tvi-shal abru tra'. Tonk'peh, tal-kam me! Ra wuh observant nu'ri t'sai sarlah etek fi-tor. Vi would ma pudva-tor ish-veh? Vi would ma ek'wak pudva-tor ish-veh?' au stariben svi' wuh jesting molu, tonk'peh tra' vesh' rai jest svi' ish-veh bezhun u' au glazhau na' me. I telv-tor suspicion tra' heh il'nai'ga, tonk'peh rai jest. "muhl, mr. Holmes, s' wuh moment ik i ken-tor ik tra' vesh' vel pa' ik suite t' tvi-shal if i vesh' ri tor fai-tor, i vesh' ek' fi' yon tor hal-tor abru' au. Ish-veh vesh' ri mere curiosity, hi i ma t'nash-veh thresh t' ik. Ish-veh vesh' weht wuh olaya t' dutya olaya ik ein rom lau sarlah s' t'nash-veh penetrating tor nash shi. Au variben t' kosu's instinct; sos'eh ish-veh vesh' kosu's instinct if mazhiv-kur-tor me ik olaya. Na' sovek tav, ish-veh vesh' tra', heh i vesh' keenly fi' wuh lookout na' sovek pavesh tor be' dvun wuh zadik svep. "ish-veh vesh' goh za-gad ik wuh pavesh sarlah. I lau var-tor du ik, isha mr. Rucastle, fi' toller heh ish-veh ko-telsu talal vel tor tor svi' aifa deserted tvi-shal, heh i wuh'wak gla-tor ish-veh carrying wuh suk nesh-kur linen sa'haf k' ish-veh k'fai wuh svep.
